File Summary

Purpose:
--------
This file contains a packed representation of a subset of the repository's contents that is considered the most important context.
It is designed to be easily consumable by AI systems for analysis, code review,
or other automated processes.

File Format:
------------
The content is organized as follows:
1. This summary section
2. Repository information
3. Directory structure
4. Repository files (if enabled)
5. Multiple file entries, each consisting of:
  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)
  c. Another separator line
  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with
  the same level of security as you would the original repository.
- Pay special attention to the Repository Description. These contain important context and guidelines specific to this project.

Notes:
------
- Some files may have been excluded based on .gitignore rules and Repomix's configuration
- Binary files are not included in this packed representation. Please refer to the Repository Structure section for a complete list of file paths, including binary files
- Only files matching these patterns are included: **/*
- Files matching patterns in .gitignore are excluded
- Files matching default ignore patterns are excluded
- Line numbers have been added to the beginning of each line
- Files are sorted by Git change count (files with more changes are at the bottom)

================
File: public/sw.js
================
 1: /**
 2:  * RA Syncbot Service Worker
 3:  *
 4:  * Minimal service worker — required for Android Chrome to fire the
 5:  * 'beforeinstallprompt' event (PWA installability check).
 6:  *
 7:  * Strategy: network-first for everything (we don't cache offline yet).
 8:  * This keeps the app simple while satisfying the PWA installability
 9:  * criteria. If you want true offline support later, add runtime caching
10:  * here.
11:  */
12: 
13: const SW_VERSION = 'ra-syncbot-v1'
14: 
15: self.addEventListener('install', (event) => {
16:   self.skipWaiting()
17: })
18: 
19: self.addEventListener('activate', (event) => {
20:   event.waitUntil(self.clients.claim())
21: })
22: 
23: // Network-first fetch handler (falls back to network on cache miss)
24: self.addEventListener('fetch', (event) => {
25:   // Only handle GET requests
26:   if (event.request.method !== 'GET') return
27: 
28:   // Skip cross-origin requests (analytics, fonts, etc.)
29:   const url = new URL(event.request.url)
30:   if (url.origin !== self.location.origin) return
31: 
32:   // Skip API requests — always hit the network
33:   if (url.pathname.startsWith('/api/')) return
34: 
35:   // Network-first: try the network, fall back to cache if offline
36:   event.respondWith(
37:     fetch(event.request).catch(() => caches.match(event.request))
38:   )
39: })

File: src/app/api/auth/update-email-prefs/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: // POST /api/auth/update-email-prefs — toggle emailNotifications for the current user
 6: // Body: { emailNotifications: boolean }
 7: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 8:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 9:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
10: 
11:   const body = await req.json()
12:   const { emailNotifications } = body as { emailNotifications: boolean }
13: 
14:   try {
15:     await db.execute({
16:       sql: 'UPDATE User SET emailNotifications = ? WHERE id = ?',
17:       args: [emailNotifications ? 1 : 0, user.id],
18:     })
19:   } catch (e: any) {
20:     // Column might not exist yet — try ALTER TABLE first
21:     try {
22:       await db.execute({ sql: 'ALTER TABLE User ADD COLUMN emailNotifications INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1' })
23:       await db.execute({
24:         sql: 'UPDATE User SET emailNotifications = ? WHERE id = ?',
25:         args: [emailNotifications ? 1 : 0, user.id],
26:       })
27:     } catch (e2: any) {
28:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to update preferences' }, { status: 500 })
29:     }
30:   }
31: 
32:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, emailNotifications })
33: }

================
File: src/app/api/event-equipment/route.ts
================
  1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
  2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
  3: import { getAuthUser, requireAdmin } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
  4: 
  5: // GET /api/event-equipment?eventId=<id> — list equipment items + claims for an event
  6: // POST /api/event-equipment — add an equipment item to an event (admin only)
  7: // DELETE /api/event-equipment?id=<itemId> — remove an equipment item (admin only, cascades to claims)
  8: // PATCH /api/event-equipment?id=<itemId> — update quantity/notes (admin only)
  9: 
 10: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 11:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 12:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
 13: 
 14:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
 15:   const eventId = searchParams.get('eventId')
 16:   if (!eventId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing eventId' }, { status: 400 })
 17: 
 18:   try {
 19:     const items = await db.execute({
 20:       sql: `SELECT * FROM EventEquipment WHERE eventId = ? ORDER BY createdAt ASC`,
 21:       args: [eventId],
 22:     })
 23: 
 24:     const result = []
 25:     for (const item of items.rows as any[]) {
 26:       const claims = await db.execute({
 27:         sql: `SELECT c.*, p.name as profileName FROM EquipmentClaim c
 28:               LEFT JOIN Profile p ON c.profileId = p.id
 29:               WHERE c.equipmentItemId = ? ORDER BY c.createdAt ASC`,
 30:         args: [item.id],
 31:       })
 32:       result.push({
 33:         id: item.id,
 34:         eventId: item.eventId,
 35:         name: item.name,
 36:         quantity: item.quantity,
 37:         notes: item.notes,
 38:         claims: claims.rows.map((c: any) => ({
 39:           id: c.id,
 40:           equipmentItemId: c.equipmentItemId,
 41:           profileId: c.profileId,
 42:           profileName: c.profileName ?? 'Unknown',
 43:           quantityClaimed: c.quantityClaimed,
 44:           transportOffered: !!c.transportOffered,
 45:           notes: c.notes,
 46:           createdAt: c.createdAt,
 47:         })),
 48:       })
 49:     }
 50: 
 51:     return NextResponse.json(result)
 52:   } catch (e: any) {
 53:     return NextResponse.json([])
 54:   }
 55: }
 56: 
 57: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 58:   const auth = await requireAdmin(req); if (auth) return auth
 59:   const body = await req.json()
 60:   const { eventId, name, quantity, notes } = body as {
 61:     eventId: string; name: string; quantity?: number; notes?: string
 62:   }
 63: 
 64:   if (!eventId || !name || !name.trim()) {
 65:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'eventId and name are required' }, { status: 400 })
 66:   }
 67: 
 68:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
 69:   try {
 70:     await db.execute({
 71:       sql: `INSERT INTO EventEquipment (id, eventId, name, quantity, notes, createdAt, updatedAt)
 72:             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
 73:       args: [id, eventId, name.trim(), quantity ?? 1, notes ?? null],
 74:     })
 75:   } catch (e: any) {
 76:     try {
 77:       await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EventEquipment (
 78:         id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 79:         eventId TEXT NOT NULL,
 80:         name TEXT NOT NULL,
 81:         quantity INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
 82:         notes TEXT,
 83:         createdAt TEXT NOT NULL,
 84:         updatedAt TEXT NOT NULL,
 85:         FOREIGN KEY (eventId) REFERENCES Event(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
 86:       )` })
 87:       await db.execute({
 88:         sql: `INSERT INTO EventEquipment (id, eventId, name, quantity, notes, createdAt, updatedAt)
 89:               VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
 90:         args: [id, eventId, name.trim(), quantity ?? 1, notes ?? null],
 91:       })
 92:     } catch (e2: any) {
 93:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to add equipment' }, { status: 500 })
 94:     }
 95:   }
 96: 
 97:   return NextResponse.json({ id, eventId, name: name.trim(), quantity: quantity ?? 1, notes: notes ?? null, claims: [] }, { status: 201 })
 98: }
 99: 
100: export async function PATCH(req: NextRequest) {
101:   const auth = await requireAdmin(req); if (auth) return auth
102:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
103:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
104:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
105: 
106:   const body = await req.json()
107:   const updates: string[] = []
108:   const args: unknown[] = []
109: 
110:   if (typeof body.quantity === 'number') { updates.push('quantity = ?'); args.push(body.quantity) }
111:   if ('notes' in body) { updates.push('notes = ?'); args.push(body.notes ?? null) }
112:   if (typeof body.name === 'string') { updates.push('name = ?'); args.push(body.name) }
113: 
114:   if (updates.length === 0) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No fields to update' }, { status: 400 })
115: 
116:   updates.push("updatedAt = datetime('now')")
117:   args.push(id)
118: 
119:   try {
120:     await db.execute({ sql: `UPDATE EventEquipment SET ${updates.join(', ')} WHERE id = ?`, args })
121:   } catch (e: any) {
122:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to update' }, { status: 500 })
123:   }
124: 
125:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
126: }
127: 
128: export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
129:   const auth = await requireAdmin(req); if (auth) return auth
130:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
131:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
132:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
133: 
134:   try {
135:     await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM EquipmentClaim WHERE equipmentItemId = ?', args: [id] })
136:   } catch (e: any) {}
137:   try {
138:     await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM EventEquipment WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
139:   } catch (e: any) {}
140: 
141:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
142: }

File: src/app/api/notifications/read/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: // POST /api/notifications/read?id=<notificationId> — mark a single notification as read
 6: // POST /api/notifications/read (no id) — mark ALL of the user's notifications as read
 7: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 8:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 9:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
10: 
11:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
12:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
13: 
14:   try {
15:     if (id) {
16:       await db.execute({
17:         sql: "UPDATE Notification SET readAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ? AND userId = ?",
18:         args: [id, user.id],
19:       })
20:     } else {
21:       await db.execute({
22:         sql: "UPDATE Notification SET readAt = datetime('now') WHERE userId = ? AND readAt IS NULL",
23:         args: [user.id],
24:       })
25:     }
26:     return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
27:   } catch (e: any) {
28:     return NextResponse.json({ ok: true }) // table might not exist yet
29:   }
30: }

================
File: scripts/migrate.ts
================
  1: /**
  2:  * Migration script — adds new tables and columns to an existing database.
  3:  *
  4:  * Safe to run multiple times — uses IF NOT EXISTS / IF NOT EXISTS patterns.
  5:  *
  6:  * Run with:
  7:  *   bun run scripts/migrate.ts
  8:  *
  9:  * Or set up a package.json script:
 10:  *   "migrate": "bun run scripts/migrate.ts"
 11:  */
 12: 
 13: import { createClient } from '@libsql/client'
 14: 
 15: const tursoUrl = process.env.TURSO_URL
 16: const tursoAuthToken = process.env.TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN
 17: 
 18: const db = tursoUrl
 19:   ? createClient({ url: tursoUrl, authToken: tursoAuthToken })
 20:   : createClient({ url: process.env.DATABASE_URL || 'file:./db/custom.db' })
 21: 
 22: async function migrate() {
 23:   console.log('Running migrations...')
 24: 
 25:   // ── New columns on existing tables ──────────────────────────────────────
 26: 
 27:   // User.emailNotifications (defaults to 1 = on)
 28:   try {
 29:     await db.execute({ sql: 'ALTER TABLE User ADD COLUMN emailNotifications INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1' })
 30:     console.log('  ✓ User.emailNotifications added')
 31:   } catch (e: any) {
 32:     if (String(e.message).includes('duplicate column')) {
 33:       console.log('  · User.emailNotifications already exists')
 34:     } else {
 35:       console.error('  ✗ Failed to add User.emailNotifications:', e.message)
 36:     }
 37:   }
 38: 
 39:   // Assignment.ackStatus + acknowledgedAt
 40:   try {
 41:     await db.execute({ sql: 'ALTER TABLE Assignment ADD COLUMN ackStatus TEXT' })
 42:     console.log('  ✓ Assignment.ackStatus added')
 43:   } catch (e: any) {
 44:     if (String(e.message).includes('duplicate column')) {
 45:       console.log('  · Assignment.ackStatus already exists')
 46:     } else {
 47:       console.error('  ✗ Failed to add Assignment.ackStatus:', e.message)
 48:     }
 49:   }
 50:   try {
 51:     await db.execute({ sql: 'ALTER TABLE Assignment ADD COLUMN acknowledgedAt TEXT' })
 52:     console.log('  ✓ Assignment.acknowledgedAt added')
 53:   } catch (e: any) {
 54:     if (String(e.message).includes('duplicate column')) {
 55:       console.log('  · Assignment.acknowledgedAt already exists')
 56:     } else {
 57:       console.error('  ✗ Failed to add Assignment.acknowledgedAt:', e.message)
 58:     }
 59:   }
 60: 
 61:   // ── New tables ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 62: 
 63:   // Skill catalog (reusable across events + profiles)
 64:   await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Skill (
 65:     id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 66:     name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
 67:     createdAt TEXT NOT NULL
 68:   )` })
 69:   console.log('  ✓ Skill table ready')
 70: 
 71:   // Equipment catalog (reusable equipment items)
 72:   await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquipmentCatalog (
 73:     id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 74:     name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
 75:     description TEXT,
 76:     createdAt TEXT NOT NULL
 77:   )` })
 78:   console.log('  ✓ EquipmentCatalog table ready')
 79: 
 80:   // Per-event equipment (what's needed for a specific event)
 81:   await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EventEquipment (
 82:     id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 83:     eventId TEXT NOT NULL,
 84:     name TEXT NOT NULL,
 85:     quantity INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
 86:     notes TEXT,
 87:     createdAt TEXT NOT NULL,
 88:     updatedAt TEXT NOT NULL,
 89:     FOREIGN KEY (eventId) REFERENCES Event(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
 90:   )` })
 91:   console.log('  ✓ EventEquipment table ready')
 92: 
 93:   // Equipment claims (instructor says "I'll bring this")
 94:   await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquipmentClaim (
 95:     id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 96:     equipmentItemId TEXT NOT NULL,
 97:     profileId TEXT NOT NULL,
 98:     quantityClaimed INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
 99:     transportOffered INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
100:     notes TEXT,
101:     createdAt TEXT NOT NULL,
102:     updatedAt TEXT NOT NULL,
103:     FOREIGN KEY (equipmentItemId) REFERENCES EventEquipment(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
104:   )` })
105:   console.log('  ✓ EquipmentClaim table ready')
106: 
107:   // Unique index: one claim per instructor per equipment item (prevents TOCTOU race)
108:   try {
109:     await db.execute({ sql: 'CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_equipmentclaim_item_profile ON EquipmentClaim (equipmentItemId, profileId)' })
110:     console.log('  ✓ EquipmentClaim unique index ready')
111:   } catch (e: any) {
112:     console.log('  · EquipmentClaim unique index already exists or failed:', e.message)
113:   }
114: 
115:   // Notifications (in-app bell)
116:   await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Notification (
117:     id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
118:     userId TEXT NOT NULL,
119:     type TEXT NOT NULL,
120:     title TEXT NOT NULL,
121:     body TEXT,
122:     eventId TEXT,
123:     assignmentId TEXT,
124:     readAt TEXT,
125:     createdAt TEXT NOT NULL,
126:     FOREIGN KEY (userId) REFERENCES User(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
127:   )` })
128:   console.log('  ✓ Notification table ready')
129: 
130:   // Email queue (digest system)
131:   await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EmailQueue (
132:     id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
133:     userId TEXT NOT NULL,
134:     type TEXT NOT NULL,
135:     subject TEXT NOT NULL,
136:     body TEXT NOT NULL,
137:     eventId TEXT,
138:     urgency TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'digest',
139:     sentAt TEXT,
140:     createdAt TEXT NOT NULL,
141:     FOREIGN KEY (userId) REFERENCES User(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
142:   )` })
143:   console.log('  ✓ EmailQueue table ready')
144: 
145:   // ── Seed skill catalog from existing data ──────────────────────────────
146: 
147:   console.log('\nSeeding skill catalog from existing skills...')
148:   const profiles = await db.execute({ sql: "SELECT skills FROM Profile WHERE skills IS NOT NULL AND skills != ''" })
149:   const events = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT skillName FROM EventSkill' })
150:   const skillSet = new Set<string>()
151:   for (const p of profiles.rows as any[]) {
152:     String(p.skills).split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean).forEach(s => skillSet.add(s))
153:   }
154:   for (const e of events.rows as any[]) {
155:     if (e.skillName) skillSet.add(e.skillName)
156:   }
157:   let seeded = 0
158:   for (const name of Array.from(skillSet).sort()) {
159:     try {
160:       await db.execute({
161:         sql: "INSERT INTO Skill (id, name, createdAt) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))",
162:         args: [crypto.randomUUID(), name],
163:       })
164:       seeded++
165:     } catch (e: any) {
166:       // Already exists — skip
167:     }
168:   }
169:   console.log(`  ✓ Seeded ${seeded} skills into catalog`)
170: 
171:   console.log('\n✓ Migration complete.')
172: }
173: 
174: migrate()
175:   .catch((e) => { console.error(e); process.exit(1) })
176:   .finally(() => db.close())

================
File: src/app/api/equipment/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: // GET /api/equipment — list all equipment catalog items (any authenticated user)
 6: // POST /api/equipment — create a new equipment catalog item (admin only)
 7: // DELETE /api/equipment?id=<id> — remove from catalog (admin only)
 8: 
 9: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
10:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
11:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
12: 
13:   try {
14:     const result = await db.execute({
15:       sql: 'SELECT * FROM EquipmentCatalog ORDER BY name ASC',
16:     })
17:     return NextResponse.json(result.rows.map((e: any) => ({
18:       id: e.id,
19:       name: e.name,
20:       description: e.description,
21:       createdAt: e.createdAt,
22:     })))
23:   } catch (e: any) {
24:     // Table doesn't exist yet — return empty
25:     return NextResponse.json([])
26:   }
27: }
28: 
29: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
30:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
31:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
32:   if (user.role !== 'admin') return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Admin only' }, { status: 403 })
33: 
34:   const body = await req.json()
35:   const { name, description } = body as { name: string; description?: string }
36:   if (!name || !name.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Name is required' }, { status: 400 })
37: 
38:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
39:   try {
40:     await db.execute({
41:       sql: "INSERT INTO EquipmentCatalog (id, name, description, createdAt) VALUES (?, ?, ?, datetime('now'))",
42:       args: [id, name.trim(), description ?? null],
43:     })
44:   } catch (e: any) {
45:     if (String(e.message).includes('UNIQUE')) {
46:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Equipment already exists' }, { status: 409 })
47:     }
48:     // Table doesn't exist — create it then retry
49:     try {
50:       await db.execute({ sql: 'CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquipmentCatalog (id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, description TEXT, createdAt TEXT NOT NULL)' })
51:       await db.execute({
52:         sql: "INSERT INTO EquipmentCatalog (id, name, description, createdAt) VALUES (?, ?, ?, datetime('now'))",
53:         args: [id, name.trim(), description ?? null],
54:       })
55:     } catch (e2: any) {
56:       if (String(e2.message).includes('UNIQUE')) {
57:         return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Equipment already exists' }, { status: 409 })
58:       }
59:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to create equipment' }, { status: 500 })
60:     }
61:   }
62: 
63:   return NextResponse.json({ id, name: name.trim(), description: description ?? null }, { status: 201 })
64: }
65: 
66: export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
67:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
68:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
69:   if (user.role !== 'admin') return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Admin only' }, { status: 403 })
70: 
71:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
72:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
73:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
74: 
75:   try {
76:     await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM EquipmentCatalog WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
77:   } catch (e: any) {
78:     // Table doesn't exist — nothing to delete
79:   }
80: 
81:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
82: }

================
File: src/app/api/equipment-claims/route.ts
================
  1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
  2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
  3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
  4: 
  5: // GET /api/equipment-claims?equipmentItemId=<id> — list claims for an equipment item
  6: // POST /api/equipment-claims — create or update a claim (instructor says "I'll bring this")
  7: //   Body: { equipmentItemId, quantityClaimed, transportOffered, notes }
  8: // DELETE /api/equipment-claims?id=<claimId> — release a claim
  9: 
 10: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 11:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 12:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
 13: 
 14:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
 15:   const equipmentItemId = searchParams.get('equipmentItemId')
 16: 
 17:   try {
 18:     if (equipmentItemId) {
 19:       const result = await db.execute({
 20:         sql: `SELECT c.*, p.name as profileName FROM EquipmentClaim c
 21:               LEFT JOIN Profile p ON c.profileId = p.id
 22:               WHERE c.equipmentItemId = ? ORDER BY c.createdAt ASC`,
 23:         args: [equipmentItemId],
 24:       })
 25:       return NextResponse.json(result.rows.map((c: any) => ({
 26:         id: c.id,
 27:         equipmentItemId: c.equipmentItemId,
 28:         profileId: c.profileId,
 29:         profileName: c.profileName ?? 'Unknown',
 30:         quantityClaimed: c.quantityClaimed,
 31:         transportOffered: !!c.transportOffered,
 32:         notes: c.notes,
 33:         createdAt: c.createdAt,
 34:       })))
 35:     }
 36:     return NextResponse.json([])
 37:   } catch (e: any) {
 38:     return NextResponse.json([])
 39:   }
 40: }
 41: 
 42: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 43:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 44:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
 45:   if (!user.profileId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No staff profile linked' }, { status: 400 })
 46: 
 47:   const body = await req.json()
 48:   const { equipmentItemId, quantityClaimed, transportOffered, notes } = body as {
 49:     equipmentItemId: string; quantityClaimed: number; transportOffered?: boolean; notes?: string
 50:   }
 51: 
 52:   if (!equipmentItemId || typeof quantityClaimed !== 'number' || quantityClaimed < 1) {
 53:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid request' }, { status: 400 })
 54:   }
 55: 
 56:   // Server-side check: don't allow claiming more than what's needed minus already-claimed
 57:   try {
 58:     const itemResult = await db.execute({
 59:       sql: 'SELECT quantity FROM EventEquipment WHERE id = ?',
 60:       args: [equipmentItemId],
 61:     })
 62:     if (itemResult.rows.length === 0) {
 63:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Equipment item not found' }, { status: 404 })
 64:     }
 65:     const needed = (itemResult.rows[0] as any).quantity as number
 66: 
 67:     const allClaims = await db.execute({
 68:       sql: 'SELECT profileId, quantityClaimed FROM EquipmentClaim WHERE equipmentItemId = ?',
 69:       args: [equipmentItemId],
 70:     })
 71:     const claimedByOthers = (allClaims.rows as any[])
 72:       .filter(c => c.profileId !== user.profileId)
 73:       .reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.quantityClaimed as number), 0)
 74:     const available = needed - claimedByOthers
 75: 
 76:     if (quantityClaimed > available) {
 77:       return NextResponse.json(
 78:         { error: `Only ${available} available (you can't claim ${quantityClaimed})` },
 79:         { status: 400 },
 80:       )
 81:     }
 82:   } catch (e: any) {
 83:     // Tables might not exist yet — proceed; the create-table fallback below handles it
 84:   }
 85: 
 86:   // Check for existing claim by this user on this equipment item.
 87:   // Wrapped in its own try/catch so a missing table is treated as "no existing claim"
 88:   // rather than a 500 (the table is created on-demand below).
 89:   let existingId: string | null = null
 90:   try {
 91:     const existing = await db.execute({
 92:       sql: 'SELECT id FROM EquipmentClaim WHERE equipmentItemId = ? AND profileId = ?',
 93:       args: [equipmentItemId, user.profileId],
 94:     })
 95:     if (existing.rows.length > 0) {
 96:       existingId = (existing.rows[0] as any).id
 97:     }
 98:   } catch {
 99:     // Table doesn't exist yet — treat as no existing claim
100:   }
101: 
102:   if (existingId) {
103:     // Update existing claim
104:     try {
105:       await db.execute({
106:         sql: `UPDATE EquipmentClaim SET quantityClaimed = ?, transportOffered = ?, notes = ?, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?`,
107:         args: [quantityClaimed, transportOffered ? 1 : 0, notes ?? null, existingId],
108:       })
109:       return NextResponse.json({ id: existingId, updated: true })
110:     } catch (e: any) {
111:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to update claim' }, { status: 500 })
112:     }
113:   }
114: 
115:   // Create new claim (with on-demand table creation)
116:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
117:   try {
118:     await db.execute({
119:       sql: `INSERT INTO EquipmentClaim (id, equipmentItemId, profileId, quantityClaimed, transportOffered, notes, createdAt, updatedAt)
120:             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
121:       args: [id, equipmentItemId, user.profileId, quantityClaimed, transportOffered ? 1 : 0, notes ?? null],
122:     })
123:   } catch (e: any) {
124:     // Table doesn't exist — create it then retry the insert
125:     try {
126:       await db.execute({ sql: `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquipmentClaim (
127:         id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
128:         equipmentItemId TEXT NOT NULL,
129:         profileId TEXT NOT NULL,
130:         quantityClaimed INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
131:         transportOffered INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
132:         notes TEXT,
133:         createdAt TEXT NOT NULL,
134:         updatedAt TEXT NOT NULL,
135:         FOREIGN KEY (equipmentItemId) REFERENCES EventEquipment(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
136:       )` })
137:       await db.execute({
138:         sql: `INSERT INTO EquipmentClaim (id, equipmentItemId, profileId, quantityClaimed, transportOffered, notes, createdAt, updatedAt)
139:               VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
140:         args: [id, equipmentItemId, user.profileId, quantityClaimed, transportOffered ? 1 : 0, notes ?? null],
141:       })
142:     } catch (e2: any) {
143:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to create claim' }, { status: 500 })
144:     }
145:   }
146: 
147:   return NextResponse.json({ id, created: true }, { status: 201 })
148: }
149: 
150: export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
151:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
152:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
153: 
154:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
155:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
156:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
157: 
158:   try {
159:     // Instructors can only release their own claims; admins can release any
160:     if (user.role === 'admin') {
161:       await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM EquipmentClaim WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
162:     } else {
163:       await db.execute({
164:         sql: 'DELETE FROM EquipmentClaim WHERE id = ? AND profileId = ?',
165:         args: [id, user.profileId],
166:       })
167:     }
168:   } catch (e: any) {
169:     // Table might not exist
170:   }
171: 
172:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
173: }

File: src/app/api/notifications/send-now/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { requireAdmin } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 3: import { sendAllPending } from '@/lib/email'
 4: 
 5: // POST /api/notifications/send-now — admin manually sends all pending digest emails.
 6: // Useful when Jelani has finished iterating and wants to flush the queue immediately.
 7: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 8:   const auth = await requireAdmin(req); if (auth) return auth
 9:   try {
10:     const result = await sendAllPending()
11:     return NextResponse.json(result)
12:   } catch (e: any) {
13:     console.error('Send-now error:', e.message)
14:     return NextResponse.json({ sent: 0, error: e.message }, { status: 500 })
15:   }
16: }

================
File: src/app/api/reminders/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { sendReminders, sendDigests } from '@/lib/email'
 3: 
 4: // POST /api/reminders — sends email reminders for assignments 2 days away,
 5: // AND sends the daily digest of pending notifications.
 6: // Called automatically when the schedule loads (fire-and-forget) or by Vercel Cron.
 7: export async function POST() {
 8:   try {
 9:     const [reminders, digests] = await Promise.all([
10:       sendReminders(),
11:       sendDigests(),
12:     ])
13:     return NextResponse.json({
14:       reminders: reminders.sent,
15:       digests: digests.sent,
16:       skipped: reminders.skipped || digests.skipped,
17:     })
18:   } catch (e: any) {
19:     console.error('Reminders/digest error:', e.message)
20:     return NextResponse.json({ reminders: 0, digests: 0, error: e.message })
21:   }
22: }

================
File: src/app/api/skills/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: // GET /api/skills — list all skills in the catalog (any authenticated user)
 6: // POST /api/skills — create a new skill in the catalog (admin only)
 7: // DELETE /api/skills?id=<id> — remove a skill from the catalog (admin only)
 8: 
 9: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
10:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
11:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
12: 
13:   try {
14:     const result = await db.execute({
15:       sql: 'SELECT * FROM Skill ORDER BY name ASC',
16:     })
17:     return NextResponse.json(result.rows.map((s: any) => ({
18:       id: s.id,
19:       name: s.name,
20:       createdAt: s.createdAt,
21:     })))
22:   } catch (e: any) {
23:     // Table doesn't exist yet — derive from existing skills in use
24:     const profiles = await db.execute({ sql: "SELECT skills FROM Profile WHERE skills IS NOT NULL AND skills != ''" })
25:     const events = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT skillName FROM EventSkill' })
26:     const skillSet = new Set<string>()
27:     for (const p of profiles.rows as any[]) {
28:       String(p.skills).split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean).forEach(s => skillSet.add(s))
29:     }
30:     for (const e of events.rows as any[]) {
31:       if (e.skillName) skillSet.add(e.skillName)
32:     }
33:     return NextResponse.json(Array.from(skillSet).sort().map((name, i) => ({
34:       id: `legacy-${i}`,
35:       name,
36:       createdAt: null,
37:     })))
38:   }
39: }
40: 
41: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
42:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
43:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
44:   if (user.role !== 'admin') return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Admin only' }, { status: 403 })
45: 
46:   const body = await req.json()
47:   const { name } = body as { name: string }
48:   if (!name || !name.trim()) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Name is required' }, { status: 400 })
49: 
50:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
51:   try {
52:     await db.execute({
53:       sql: "INSERT INTO Skill (id, name, createdAt) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))",
54:       args: [id, name.trim()],
55:     })
56:   } catch (e: any) {
57:     // UNIQUE constraint = skill already exists
58:     if (String(e.message).includes('UNIQUE')) {
59:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Skill already exists' }, { status: 409 })
60:     }
61:     // Table doesn't exist — create it then retry the insert
62:     try {
63:       await db.execute({ sql: 'CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Skill (id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, createdAt TEXT NOT NULL)' })
64:       await db.execute({
65:         sql: "INSERT INTO Skill (id, name, createdAt) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))",
66:         args: [id, name.trim()],
67:       })
68:     } catch (e2: any) {
69:       if (String(e2.message).includes('UNIQUE')) {
70:         return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Skill already exists' }, { status: 409 })
71:       }
72:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to create skill' }, { status: 500 })
73:     }
74:   }
75: 
76:   return NextResponse.json({ id, name: name.trim() }, { status: 201 })
77: }

85:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
86:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
87:

89:     await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM Skill WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
90:   } catch (e: any) {
91:     // Table doesn't exist — nothing to delete
92:   }
93: 
94:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })

================
File: src/components/scheduler/EquipmentSection.tsx
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState } from 'react'
  4: import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import { toast } from 'sonner'
  6: import { Plus, Trash2, X, Truck, Package, Check } from 'lucide-react'
  7: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
  8: import type { EventView, EquipmentItem } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
  9: 
 10: type Props = {
 11:   event: EventView
 12:   /** 'admin' = admin can add/remove items; 'instructor' = instructor can claim */
 13:   mode: 'admin' | 'instructor'
 14:   /** For instructor mode, the profileId of the current user */
 15:   myProfileId?: string | null
 16: }
 17: 
 18: async function fetchEquipment(eventId: string): Promise<EquipmentItem[]> {
 19:   const r = await fetch(`/api/event-equipment?eventId=${eventId}`)
 20:   if (!r.ok) return []
 21:   return r.json()
 22: }
 23: 
 24: export function EquipmentSection({ event, mode, myProfileId }: Props) {
 25:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 26:   const { data: equipment, isLoading } = useQuery({
 27:     queryKey: ['event-equipment', event.id],
 28:     queryFn: () => fetchEquipment(event.id),
 29:   })
 30: 
 31:   const [newItemName, setNewItemName] = useState('')
 32:   const [newItemQty, setNewItemQty] = useState(1)
 33: 
 34:   const addItem = useMutation({
 35:     mutationFn: async () => {
 36:       const r = await fetch('/api/event-equipment', {
 37:         method: 'POST',
 38:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 39:         body: JSON.stringify({ eventId: event.id, name: newItemName, quantity: newItemQty }),
 40:       })
 41:       const j = await r.json()
 42:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
 43:       return j
 44:     },
 45:     onSuccess: () => {
 46:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['event-equipment', event.id] })
 47:       setNewItemName('')
 48:       setNewItemQty(1)
 49:       toast.success('Equipment added')
 50:     },
 51:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to add'),
 52:   })
 53: 
 54:   const removeItem = useMutation({
 55:     mutationFn: async (itemId: string) => {
 56:       const r = await fetch(`/api/event-equipment?id=${itemId}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
 57:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed')
 58:       return r.json()
 59:     },
 60:     onSuccess: () => {
 61:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['event-equipment', event.id] })
 62:       toast.success('Equipment removed')
 63:     },
 64:   })
 65: 
 66:   const claimMutation = useMutation({
 67:     mutationFn: async (args: { equipmentItemId: string; quantityClaimed: number; transportOffered: boolean }) => {
 68:       const r = await fetch('/api/equipment-claims', {
 69:         method: 'POST',
 70:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 71:         body: JSON.stringify(args),
 72:       })
 73:       const j = await r.json()
 74:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
 75:       return j
 76:     },
 77:     onSuccess: () => {
 78:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['event-equipment', event.id] })
 79:       toast.success('You\'re bringing this — the boss will be notified')
 80:     },
 81:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to claim'),
 82:   })
 83: 
 84:   const releaseClaim = useMutation({
 85:     mutationFn: async (claimId: string) => {
 86:       const r = await fetch(`/api/equipment-claims?id=${claimId}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
 87:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed')
 88:       return r.json()
 89:     },
 90:     onSuccess: () => {
 91:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['event-equipment', event.id] })
 92:       toast.success('Released — no longer bringing this')
 93:     },
 94:   })
 95: 
 96:   return (
 97:     <div className="rounded-md border border-border/40 bg-card/40 p-3 space-y-3">
 98:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
 99:         <Package className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
100:         <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground">
101:           Equipment needed
102:         </h3>
103:         {mode === 'admin' && (
104:           <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground/60 ml-auto">
105:             Add what needs to be there. Instructors claim items they'll bring.
106:           </span>
107:         )}
108:         {mode === 'instructor' && (
109:           <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground/60 ml-auto">
110:             Click "I'll bring" to claim an item. The boss will arrange to get it to you.
111:           </span>
112:         )}
113:       </div>
114: 
115:       {/* Equipment list */}
116:       {isLoading && <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">Loading…</p>}
117:       {(equipment ?? []).length === 0 && !isLoading && (
118:         <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground italic text-center py-2">
119:           {mode === 'admin' ? 'No equipment added yet.' : 'No equipment needed for this event.'}
120:         </p>
121:       )}
122: 
123:       {(equipment ?? []).map(item => {
124:         const totalClaimed = item.claims.reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.quantityClaimed, 0)
125:         const fullyClaimed = totalClaimed >= item.quantity
126:         const myClaim = myProfileId ? item.claims.find(c => c.profileId === myProfileId) : undefined
127: 
128:         return (
129:           <div
130:             key={item.id}
131:             className={cn(
132:               'rounded-md border p-2.5 space-y-2',
133:               fullyClaimed
134:                 ? 'border-emerald-500/30 bg-emerald-500/5'
135:                 : 'border-border/60 bg-muted/20',
136:             )}
137:           >
138:             {/* Item header */}
139:             <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
140:               <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
141:                 <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
142:                   <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{item.name}</p>
143:                   <span className={cn(
144:                     'text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-medium shrink-0',
145:                     fullyClaimed
146:                       ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300'
147:                       : 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300',
148:                   )}>
149:                     {totalClaimed}/{item.quantity}
150:                   </span>
151:                 </div>
152:                 {item.notes && (
153:                   <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{item.notes}</p>
154:                 )}
155:               </div>
156:               {/* Admin: delete */}
157:               {mode === 'admin' && (
158:                 <button
159:                   onClick={() => {
160:                     if (confirm(`Remove "${item.name}"?`)) removeItem.mutate(item.id)
161:                   }}
162:                   className="p-1 rounded hover:bg-rose-500/10 hover:text-rose-300 text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
163:                   aria-label={`Remove ${item.name}`}
164:                 >
165:                   <Trash2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
166:                 </button>
167:               )}
168:             </div>
169: 
170:             {/* Claims */}
171:             {item.claims.length > 0 && (
172:               <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
173:                 {item.claims.map(c => (
174:                   <span
175:                     key={c.id}
176:                     className={cn(
177:                       'inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] border',
178:                       c.profileId === myProfileId
179:                         ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/40'
180:                         : 'bg-muted/60 text-foreground/80 border-border/40',
181:                     )}
182:                     title={c.notes ?? undefined}
183:                   >
184:                     {c.transportOffered && <Truck className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />}
185:                     {c.profileName} ({c.quantityClaimed})
186:                     {c.profileId === myProfileId && mode === 'instructor' && (
187:                       <button
188:                         onClick={() => releaseClaim.mutate(c.id)}
189:                         className="hover:text-rose-300 ml-0.5"
190:                         aria-label="Release my claim"
191:                       >
192:                         <X className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
193:                       </button>
194:                     )}
195:                   </span>
196:                 ))}
197:               </div>
198:             )}
199: 
200:             {/* Instructor: claim button */}
201:             {mode === 'instructor' && !myClaim && (
202:               <ClaimForm
203:                 itemId={item.id}
204:                 maxQty={item.quantity - totalClaimed}
205:                 onSubmit={(qty, transport) => claimMutation.mutate({
206:                   equipmentItemId: item.id,
207:                   quantityClaimed: qty,
208:                   transportOffered: transport,
209:                 })}
210:                 disabled={claimMutation.isPending}
211:               />
212:             )}
213: 
214:             {/* Instructor: already claimed by me */}
215:             {mode === 'instructor' && myClaim && (
216:               <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[10px] text-emerald-300">
217:                 <Check className="h-3 w-3" />
218:                 You're bringing {myClaim.quantityClaimed}
219:                 {myClaim.transportOffered && ' (transporting)'}
220:               </div>
221:             )}
222:           </div>
223:         )
224:       })}
225: 
226:       {/* Admin: add new equipment */}
227:       {mode === 'admin' && (
228:         <div className="border-t border-border/40 pt-2 space-y-2">
229:           <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
230:             <input
231:               type="text"
232:               value={newItemName}
233:               onChange={e => setNewItemName(e.target.value)}
234:               placeholder="e.g. Drones (Tello EDU)"
235:               className="flex-1 px-2 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
236:               onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter' && newItemName.trim()) addItem.mutate() }}
237:             />
238:             <input
239:               type="number"
240:               min={1}
241:               value={newItemQty}
242:               onChange={e => setNewItemQty(Math.max(1, Number(e.target.value)))}
243:               className="w-16 px-2 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
244:               aria-label="Quantity"
245:             />
246:             <button
247:               onClick={() => newItemName.trim() && addItem.mutate()}
248:               disabled={!newItemName.trim() || addItem.isPending}
249:               className="px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[32px]"
250:             >
251:               <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
252:               Add
253:             </button>
254:           </div>
255:         </div>
256:       )}
257:     </div>
258:   )
259: }
260: 
261: function ClaimForm({ itemId, maxQty, onSubmit, disabled }: {
262:   itemId: string
263:   maxQty: number
264:   onSubmit: (qty: number, transport: boolean) => void
265:   disabled: boolean
266: }) {
267:   const [qty, setQty] = useState(Math.min(1, maxQty))
268:   const [transport, setTransport] = useState(true)
269: 
270:   // Clamp qty during render if maxQty shrinks (e.g. another instructor claimed while form was open)
271:   const effectiveQty = Math.min(qty, maxQty)
272:   if (maxQty <= 0) return null
273: 
274:   return (
275:     <div className="flex items-center gap-2 pt-1 border-t border-border/40">
276:       <button
277:         onClick={() => onSubmit(effectiveQty, transport)}
278:         disabled={disabled}
279:         className="px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[28px]"
280:       >
281:         <Truck className="h-3 w-3" />
282:         I'll bring
283:       </button>
284:       <input
285:         type="number"
286:         min={1}
287:         max={maxQty}
288:         value={effectiveQty}
289:         onChange={e => setQty(Math.max(1, Math.min(maxQty, Number(e.target.value))))}
290:         className="w-14 px-1.5 py-1 text-[11px] rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
291:         aria-label="Quantity you'll bring"
292:       />
293:       <label className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground cursor-pointer">
294:         <input
295:           type="checkbox"
296:           checked={transport}
297:           onChange={e => setTransport(e.target.checked)}
298:           className="h-3 w-3 rounded accent-emerald-500"
299:         />
300:         I can transport
301:       </label>
302:     </div>
303:   )
304: }
