File: src/components/scheduler/InstallAppMenuItem.tsx
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
  4: import { Download, X } from 'lucide-react'
  5: 
  6: type BeforeInstallPromptEvent = Event & {
  7:   prompt: () => Promise<void>
  8:   userChoice: Promise<{ outcome: 'accepted' | 'dismissed' }>
  9: }
 10: 
 11: /**
 12:  * "Install app" menu item for the account dropdown.
 13:  *
 14:  * Always shows a bottom-sheet with install instructions when tapped, so the
 15:  * button always responds (no dead taps). The instructions are tailored to
 16:  * the detected platform:
 17:  *
 18:  * - Android Chrome/Samsung (with beforeinstallprompt): tries the native
 19:  *   install prompt first; if that fails, falls back to manual instructions
 20:  * - iOS Safari: manual Share → Add to Home Screen instructions
 21:  * - Other: generic "Add to Home Screen" instructions
 22:  *
 23:  * Only renders on mobile (sm:hidden) and only when not already in
 24:  * standalone mode (i.e. PWA not yet installed).
 25:  *
 26:  * NOTE: For the native Android install prompt to fire, the app needs a
 27:  * service worker registered. See /sw.js (registered in layout.tsx).
 28:  */
 29: export function InstallAppMenuItem({ onAfterAction }: { onAfterAction?: () => void }) {
 30:   const [deferredPrompt, setDeferredPrompt] = useState<BeforeInstallPromptEvent | null>(null)
 31:   const [showInstructions, setShowInstructions] = useState(false)
 32: 
 33:   useEffect(() => {
 34:     const handler = (e: Event) => {
 35:       e.preventDefault()
 36:       setDeferredPrompt(e as BeforeInstallPromptEvent)
 37:     }
 38:     window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', handler)
 39:     return () => window.removeEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', handler)
 40:   }, [])
 41: 
 42:   // Detect platform
 43:   const isIOS = typeof navigator !== 'undefined' && (
 44:     /iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(navigator.userAgent) ||
 45:     (navigator.platform === 'MacIntel' && navigator.maxTouchPoints > 1)
 46:   )
 47:   const isAndroid = typeof navigator !== 'undefined' && /Android/i.test(navigator.userAgent)
 48: 
 49:   // Detect if already installed (standalone mode)
 50:   const isStandalone = typeof window !== 'undefined' &&
 51:     (window.matchMedia('(display-mode: standalone)').matches ||
 52:      (navigator as any).standalone === true)
 53: 
 54:   // Don't render if already installed
 55:   if (isStandalone) return null
 56: 
 57:   const handleClick = async () => {
 58:     // Close the account menu first
 59:     onAfterAction?.()
 60: 
 61:     // If we have a deferred prompt (Android Chrome with SW), try the native prompt
 62:     if (deferredPrompt) {
 63:       try {
 64:         await deferredPrompt.prompt()
 65:         const choice = await deferredPrompt.userChoice
 66:         if (choice.outcome === 'accepted') {
 67:           setDeferredPrompt(null)
 68:           return // installed — don't show instructions
 69:         }
 70:         // dismissed — fall through to show manual instructions
 71:       } catch {
 72:         // prompt failed — fall through to manual instructions
 73:       }
 74:     }
 75: 
 76:     // Always show instructions as fallback / for iOS
 77:     setShowInstructions(true)
 78:   }
 79: 
 80:   return (
 81:     <>
 82:       {/* Only render on mobile (sm:hidden) */}
 83:       <button
 84:         onClick={handleClick}
 85:         className="sm:hidden w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-xs hover:bg-muted flex items-center gap-2"
 86:       >
 87:         <Download className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
 88:         Install app
 89:       </button>
 90: 
 91:       {/* Instructions popover — always available as fallback */}
 92:       {showInstructions && (
 93:         <div
 94:           className="sm:hidden fixed inset-0 z-[60] flex items-end justify-center bg-black/50 p-0"
 95:           onClick={() => setShowInstructions(false)}
 96:         >
 97:           <div
 98:             className="bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-t-lg w-full max-w-md p-4 pb-6"
 99:             onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
100:           >
101:             <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
102:               <div>
103:                 <p className="text-sm font-semibold">Install RA Syncbot</p>
104:                 <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">Add to your home screen</p>
105:               </div>
106:               <button
107:                 onClick={() => setShowInstructions(false)}
108:                 className="p-1 rounded hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
109:                 aria-label="Close"
110:               >
111:                 <X className="h-4 w-4" />
112:               </button>
113:             </div>
114: 
115:             {isIOS ? (
116:               <ol className="space-y-3 text-xs text-foreground/90">
117:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
118:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">1.</span>
119:                   <span>Tap the <strong>Share</strong> button in Safari's toolbar (square with an up-arrow).</span>
120:                 </li>
121:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
122:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">2.</span>
123:                   <span>Scroll down and tap <strong>Add to Home Screen</strong>.</span>
124:                 </li>
125:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
126:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">3.</span>
127:                   <span>Tap <strong>Add</strong> — the RA Syncbot icon will appear on your home screen.</span>
128:                 </li>
129:               </ol>
130:             ) : isAndroid ? (
131:               <ol className="space-y-3 text-xs text-foreground/90">
132:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
133:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">1.</span>
134:                   <span>Tap the <strong>three-dot menu</strong> (⋮) in the top-right corner of your browser.</span>
135:                 </li>
136:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
137:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">2.</span>
138:                   <span>Tap <strong>Install app</strong> or <strong>Add to Home screen</strong>.</span>
139:                 </li>
140:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
141:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">3.</span>
142:                   <span>Tap <strong>Install</strong> — the RA Syncbot icon will appear on your home screen.</span>
143:                 </li>
144:               </ol>
145:             ) : (
146:               <ol className="space-y-3 text-xs text-foreground/90">
147:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
148:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">1.</span>
149:                   <span>Open your browser menu and look for <strong>Install app</strong> or <strong>Add to Home screen</strong>.</span>
150:                 </li>
151:                 <li className="flex gap-2">
152:                   <span className="font-semibold text-emerald-300 shrink-0">2.</span>
153:                   <span>Confirm — the RA Syncbot icon will appear on your home screen.</span>
154:                 </li>
155:               </ol>
156:             )}
157:           </div>
158:         </div>
159:       )}
160:     </>
161:   )
162: }

================
File: src/components/scheduler/NotificationBell.tsx
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
  4: import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import { toast } from 'sonner'
  6: import { Bell, Check, X } from 'lucide-react'
  7: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
  8: import { formatShortDate } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
  9: 
 10: type Notification = {
 11:   id: string
 12:   type: string
 13:   title: string
 14:   body: string | null
 15:   eventId: string | null
 16:   readAt: string | null
 17:   createdAt: string
 18:   read: boolean
 19: }
 20: 
 21: async function fetchNotifications(): Promise<{ notifications: Notification[]; unread: number }> {
 22:   const r = await fetch('/api/notifications')
 23:   if (!r.ok) return { notifications: [], unread: 0 }
 24:   return r.json()
 25: }
 26: 
 27: const TYPE_ICON: Record<string, string> = {
 28:   assignment_created: '📅',
 29:   assignment_removed: '❌',
 30:   opt_in_received: '⭐',
 31:   event_changed: '📝',
 32:   reminder: '⏰',
 33:   equipment_claimed: '📦',
 34: }
 35: 
 36: const TYPE_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
 37:   assignment_created: 'text-emerald-300',
 38:   assignment_removed: 'text-rose-300',
 39:   opt_in_received: 'text-teal-300',
 40:   event_changed: 'text-amber-300',
 41:   reminder: 'text-sky-300',
 42:   equipment_claimed: 'text-purple-300',
 43: }
 44: 
 45: export function NotificationBell() {
 46:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 47:   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)
 48:   const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
 49: 
 50:   const { data } = useQuery({
 51:     queryKey: ['notifications'],
 52:     queryFn: fetchNotifications,
 53:     refetchInterval: 30000, // poll every 30s for new notifications
 54:   })
 55: 
 56:   const markReadMutation = useMutation({
 57:     mutationFn: async (id?: string) => {
 58:       const url = id ? `/api/notifications/read?id=${id}` : '/api/notifications/read'
 59:       const r = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST' })
 60:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed')
 61:       return r.json()
 62:     },
 63:     onSuccess: () => {
 64:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['notifications'] })
 65:     },
 66:     onError: () => toast.error('Could not mark as read'),
 67:   })
 68: 
 69:   // Close on click outside
 70:   useEffect(() => {
 71:     const handleClick = (e: MouseEvent) => {
 72:       if (ref.current && !ref.current.contains(e.target as Node)) {
 73:         setOpen(false)
 74:       }
 75:     }
 76:     if (open) document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)
 77:     return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)
 78:   }, [open])
 79: 
 80:   const unread = data?.unread ?? 0
 81:   const notifications = data?.notifications ?? []
 82: 
 83:   return (
 84:     <div className="relative" ref={ref}>
 85:       <button
 86:         onClick={() => setOpen(o => !o)}
 87:         className="relative p-2 rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
 88:         aria-label={`Notifications${unread > 0 ? ` (${unread} unread)` : ''}`}
 89:         aria-expanded={open}
 90:       >
 91:         <Bell className="h-4 w-4" />
 92:         {unread > 0 && (
 93:           <span
 94:             className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 h-4 min-w-4 px-1 rounded-full bg-rose-500 text-white text-[9px] font-bold flex items-center justify-center"
 95:             aria-hidden="true"
 96:           >
 97:             {unread > 9 ? '9+' : unread}
 98:           </span>
 99:         )}
100:       </button>
101: 
102:       {open && (
103:         <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 z-50 w-80 max-w-[calc(100vw-1rem)] bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-md shadow-lg flex flex-col max-h-[70vh]">
104:           {/* Header */}
105:           <div className="px-3 py-2 border-b border-border/40 flex items-center justify-between">
106:             <p className="text-xs font-semibold">Notifications</p>
107:             {unread > 0 && (
108:               <button
109:                 onClick={() => markReadMutation.mutate(undefined)}
110:                 className="text-[10px] text-emerald-300 hover:text-emerald-200 flex items-center gap-1"
111:               >
112:                 <Check className="h-3 w-3" />
113:                 Mark all read
114:               </button>
115:             )}
116:           </div>
117: 
118:           {/* List */}
119:           <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto">
120:             {notifications.length === 0 ? (
121:               <div className="p-6 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">
122:                 <Bell className="h-6 w-6 mx-auto mb-2 opacity-30" />
123:                 No notifications yet
124:               </div>
125:             ) : (
126:               notifications.map(n => (
127:                 <button
128:                   key={n.id}
129:                   onClick={() => {
130:                     if (!n.read) markReadMutation.mutate(n.id)
131:                   }}
132:                   className={cn(
133:                     'w-full text-left px-3 py-2.5 border-b border-border/30 hover:bg-muted/40 transition-colors flex items-start gap-2',
134:                     !n.read && 'bg-emerald-500/[0.04]',
135:                   )}
136:                 >
137:                   <span className="text-base shrink-0 mt-0.5">
138:                     {TYPE_ICON[n.type] ?? '•'}
139:                   </span>
140:                   <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
141:                     <p className={cn('text-xs leading-tight', !n.read && 'font-medium', TYPE_COLOR[n.type] ?? '')}>
142:                       {n.title}
143:                     </p>
144:                     {n.body && (
145:                       <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 line-clamp-2">
146:                         {n.body}
147:                       </p>
148:                     )}
149:                     <p className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground/60 mt-1">
150:                       {formatRelativeTime(n.createdAt)}
151:                     </p>
152:                   </div>
153:                   {!n.read && (
154:                     <span className="h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-emerald-400 shrink-0 mt-1.5" aria-label="Unread" />
155:                   )}
156:                 </button>
157:               ))
158:             )}
159:           </div>
160:         </div>
161:       )}
162:     </div>
163:   )
164: }
165: 
166: function formatRelativeTime(iso: string): string {
167:   const now = Date.now()
168:   const then = new Date(iso).getTime()
169:   const diffMs = now - then
170:   const diffMin = Math.floor(diffMs / 60000)
171:   const diffHour = Math.floor(diffMin / 60)
172:   const diffDay = Math.floor(diffHour / 24)
173: 
174:   if (diffMin < 1) return 'just now'
175:   if (diffMin < 60) return `${diffMin}m ago`
176:   if (diffHour < 24) return `${diffHour}h ago`
177:   if (diffDay < 7) return `${diffDay}d ago`
178:   return formatShortDate(iso.slice(0, 10))
179: }

================
File: src/components/scheduler/SkillPicker.tsx
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
  4: import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import { toast } from 'sonner'
  6: import { Plus, X, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react'
  7: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
  8: import type { SkillItem } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
  9: 
 10: async function fetchSkills(): Promise<SkillItem[]> {
 11:   const r = await fetch('/api/skills')
 12:   if (!r.ok) return []
 13:   return r.json()
 14: }
 15: 
 16: type Props = {
 17:   selected: string[]
 18:   onChange: (skills: string[]) => void
 19:   /** If true, show a "Manage catalog" section with delete buttons (admin only) */
 20:   allowCatalogManagement?: boolean
 21:   label?: string
 22:   placeholder?: string
 23: }
 24: 
 25: /**
 26:  * Skill picker with reusable catalog.
 27:  * - Type to search existing skills
 28:  * - Click a skill to add it
 29:  * - Click "Add new skill" to create one in the catalog
 30:  * - X button on each chip to remove
 31:  * - (Admin) Trash icon to delete from catalog entirely
 32:  */
 33: export function SkillPicker({ selected, onChange, allowCatalogManagement = false, label = 'Skills', placeholder = 'Search skills…' }: Props) {
 34:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 35:   const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
 36:   const [showDropdown, setShowDropdown] = useState(false)
 37:   const [showCatalogManager, setShowCatalogManager] = useState(false)
 38:   const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
 39: 
 40:   const { data: skills } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['skills'], queryFn: fetchSkills })
 41: 
 42:   const createSkill = useMutation({
 43:     mutationFn: async (name: string) => {
 44:       const r = await fetch('/api/skills', {
 45:         method: 'POST',
 46:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 47:         body: JSON.stringify({ name }),
 48:       })
 49:       const j = await r.json()
 50:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
 51:       return j
 52:     },
 53:     onSuccess: () => {
 54:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['skills'] })
 55:     },
 56:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to create skill'),
 57:   })
 58: 
 59:   const deleteSkill = useMutation({
 60:     mutationFn: async (id: string) => {
 61:       const r = await fetch(`/api/skills?id=${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
 62:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed')
 63:       return r.json()
 64:     },
 65:     onSuccess: () => {
 66:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['skills'] })
 67:       toast.success('Skill removed from catalog')
 68:     },
 69:     onError: () => toast.error('Failed to delete skill'),
 70:   })
 71: 
 72:   // Close dropdown on click outside
 73:   useEffect(() => {
 74:     const handleClick = (e: MouseEvent) => {
 75:       if (ref.current && !ref.current.contains(e.target as Node)) {
 76:         setShowDropdown(false)
 77:       }
 78:     }
 79:     document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)
 80:     return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)
 81:   }, [])
 82: 
 83:   const filtered = (skills ?? []).filter(s =>
 84:     s.name.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase()) && !selected.includes(s.name)
 85:   )
 86: 
 87:   const exactMatch = (skills ?? []).some(s => s.name.toLowerCase() === query.toLowerCase().trim())
 88:   const canCreateNew = query.trim().length > 0 && !exactMatch && !selected.includes(query.trim())
 89: 
 90:   const addSkill = (name: string) => {
 91:     if (!selected.includes(name)) {
 92:       onChange([...selected, name])
 93:     }
 94:     setQuery('')
 95:     setShowDropdown(false)
 96:   }
 97: 
 98:   const removeSkill = (name: string) => {
 99:     onChange(selected.filter(s => s !== name))
100:   }
101: 
102:   return (
103:     <div className="space-y-2" ref={ref}>
104:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
105:         <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground">
106:           {label}
107:         </label>
108:         {allowCatalogManagement && (
109:           <button
110:             type="button"
111:             onClick={() => setShowCatalogManager(s => !s)}
112:             className="text-[10px] text-emerald-300 hover:text-emerald-200"
113:           >
114:             {showCatalogManager ? 'Hide catalog' : 'Manage catalog'}
115:           </button>
116:         )}
117:       </div>
118: 
119:       {/* Selected skills */}
120:       {selected.length > 0 && (
121:         <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
122:           {selected.map(s => (
123:             <span
124:               key={s}
125:               className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-md bg-muted/60 text-foreground/90 text-[11px] border border-border/40"
126:             >
127:               {s}
128:               <button
129:                 type="button"
130:                 onClick={() => removeSkill(s)}
131:                 className="hover:text-rose-300"
132:                 aria-label={`Remove ${s}`}
133:               >
134:                 <X className="h-3 w-3" />
135:               </button>
136:             </span>
137:           ))}
138:         </div>
139:       )}
140: 
141:       {/* Search + dropdown */}
142:       <div className="relative">
143:         <input
144:           type="text"
145:           value={query}
146:           onChange={e => { setQuery(e.target.value); setShowDropdown(true) }}
147:           onFocus={() => setShowDropdown(true)}
148:           onBlur={() => {
149:             // Delay so item clicks register before the dropdown closes
150:             setTimeout(() => setShowDropdown(false), 150)
151:           }}
152:           onKeyDown={e => {
153:             if (e.key === 'Escape') {
154:               setShowDropdown(false)
155:               setQuery('')
156:             }
157:           }}
158:           placeholder={placeholder}
159:           className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
160:         />
161:         {showDropdown && (filtered.length > 0 || canCreateNew) && (
162:           <div className="absolute z-30 top-full mt-1 left-0 right-0 bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-md shadow-lg max-h-48 overflow-y-auto">
163:             {filtered.map(s => (
164:               <button
165:                 key={s.id}
166:                 type="button"
167:                 onClick={() => addSkill(s.name)}
168:                 className="w-full text-left px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-muted/40 flex items-center justify-between"
169:               >
170:                 <span>{s.name}</span>
171:                 <Plus className="h-3 w-3 text-muted-foreground" />
172:               </button>
173:             ))}
174:             {canCreateNew && (
175:               <button
176:                 type="button"
177:                 onClick={() => {
178:                   createSkill.mutate(query.trim(), {
179:                     onSuccess: () => addSkill(query.trim()),
180:                   })
181:                 }}
182:                 className="w-full text-left px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300 flex items-center justify-between border-t border-border/40"
183:               >
184:                 <span>Create "{query.trim()}"</span>
185:                 <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
186:               </button>
187:             )}
188:           </div>
189:         )}
190:       </div>
191: 
192:       {/* Catalog manager (admin) */}
193:       {allowCatalogManagement && showCatalogManager && (
194:         <div className="rounded-md border border-border/40 bg-muted/20 p-2 max-h-40 overflow-y-auto">
195:           <p className="text-[9px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1.5">
196:             All skills in catalog ({(skills ?? []).length})
197:           </p>
198:           {(skills ?? []).length === 0 ? (
199:             <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground italic">No skills in catalog yet.</p>
200:           ) : (
201:             <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
202:               {(skills ?? []).map(s => (
203:                 <span
204:                   key={s.id}
205:                   className={cn(
206:                     'inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] border',
207:                     selected.includes(s.name)
208:                       ? 'bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/30'
209:                       : 'bg-muted/60 text-foreground/80 border-border/40',
210:                   )}
211:                 >
212:                   {s.name}
213:                   <button
214:                     type="button"
215:                     onClick={() => {
216:                       if (confirm(`Remove "${s.name}" from the catalog? This won't affect existing assignments.`)) {
217:                         deleteSkill.mutate(s.id)
218:                       }
219:                     }}
220:                     className="hover:text-rose-300"
221:                     aria-label={`Delete ${s.name} from catalog`}
222:                     title="Remove from catalog"
223:                   >
224:                     <Trash2 className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
225:                   </button>
226:                 </span>
227:               ))}
228:             </div>
229:           )}
230:         </div>
231:       )}
232:     </div>
233:   )
234: }

================
File: DEPLOYMENT.md
================
  1: # Deployment Guide
  2: 
  3: This guide walks you through deploying RA Syncbot from scratch on Vercel + Turso + Resend. Total cost on free tiers: $0.
  4: 
  5: Estimated setup time: 30–45 minutes.
  6: 
  7: ---
  8: 
  9: ## Prerequisites
 10: 
 11: - A [GitHub](https://github.com) account (to host the repo)
 12: - A [Vercel](https://vercel.com) account (free tier)
 13: - A [Turso](https://turso.tech) account (free tier)
 14: - A [Resend](https://resend.com) account (free tier, optional — for email notifications)
 15: - A domain name (optional — Vercel provides a free `*.vercel.app` subdomain)
 16: 
 17: ---
 18: 
 19: ## Step 1 — Push the code to GitHub
 20: 
 21: ```bash
 22: git init
 23: git add .
 24: git commit -m "Initial commit"
 25: git remote add origin https://github.com/<your-username>/ra-syncbot.git
 26: git push -u origin main
 27: ```
 28: 
 29: If you received this project as a zip, unzip it first and run the commands above from inside the project directory.
 30: 
 31: ---
 32: 
 33: ## Step 2 — Create the Turso database
 34: 
 35: 1. Sign up at [turso.tech](https://turso.tech) (free, no credit card).
 36: 2. Install the Turso CLI:
 37:    ```bash
 38:    curl -sSfL https://get.tur.so/install.sh | bash
 39:    turso auth login
 40:    ```
 41: 3. Create a database:
 42:    ```bash
 43:    turso db create ra-syncbot
 44:    ```
 45: 4. Get the connection URL:
 46:    ```bash
 47:    turso db show ra-syncbot --url
 48:    # → libsql://ra-syncbot-<your-org>.turso.io
 49:    ```
 50: 5. Create an auth token:
 51:    ```bash
 52:    turso db tokens create ra-syncbot
 53:    # → eyJhbGciOi... (long string)
 54:    ```
 55: 6. Save both values — you'll need them in Step 4.
 56: 
 57: ---
 58: 
 59: ## Step 3 — Initialize the database schema
 60: 
 61: The schema isn't included as a SQL file — it's created by the seed script.
 62: 
 63: 1. Clone the repo locally and install deps:
 64:    ```bash
 65:    git clone https://github.com/<your-username>/ra-syncbot.git
 66:    cd ra-syncbot
 67:    bun install
 68:    ```
 69: 2. Create a `.env` file:
 70:    ```bash
 71:    cp .env.example .env
 72:    ```
 73: 3. Edit `.env` and fill in:
 74:    ```
 75:    TURSO_URL=libsql://ra-syncbot-<your-org>.turso.io
 76:    TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN=eyJhbGciOi...
 77:    SESSION_PASSWORD=<generate a 32+ char random string>
 78:    ```
 79:    Generate a session password:
 80:    ```bash
 81:    openssl rand -hex 32
 82:    ```
 83: 4. Run the seed:
 84:    ```bash
 85:    bun run seed
 86:    ```
 87:    You should see output like:
 88:    ```
 89:    Seeding 20 staff profiles...
 90:    Seeding 17 events...
 91:    Seeding 33 preset assignments...
 92:    Creating admin user...
 93:    Done!
 94:    ```
 95: 
 96: > ⚠️ The seed script **wipes all existing data** before inserting. It is safe to run multiple times, but don't run it in production after you have real data.
 97: 
 98: ---
 99: 
100: ## Step 4 — Deploy to Vercel
101: 
102: 1. Go to [vercel.com/new](https://vercel.com/new) and sign in with GitHub.
103: 2. Import your `ra-syncbot` repository.
104: 3. Vercel auto-detects Next.js. **Don't override any build settings** — `vercel.json` in the repo already configures everything.
105: 4. Open **Environment Variables** and add:
106:    | Key | Value |
107:    |---|---|
108:    | `TURSO_URL` | `libsql://ra-syncbot-<your-org>.turso.io` |
109:    | `TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN` | (your Turso token) |
110:    | `SESSION_PASSWORD` | (your 32+ char secret) |
111:    | `NODE_ENV` | `production` |
112: 5. (Optional — email) Add:
113:    | Key | Value |
114:    |---|---|
115:    | `RESEND_API_KEY` | `re_...` (from Resend dashboard) |
116:    | `FROM_EMAIL` | `noreply@yourdomain.com` (must be a verified Resend domain) |
117:    | `ADMIN_EMAIL` | `you@example.com` (receives opt-in notifications) |
118: 6. Click **Deploy**. The first build takes ~2 minutes.
119: 
120: Once deployed, Vercel gives you a `*.vercel.app` URL. The app is now live.
121: 
122: ---
123: 
124: ## Step 5 — Configure your custom domain (optional)
125: 
126: 1. In the Vercel dashboard, go to **Project → Settings → Domains**.
127: 2. Add `ra-syncbot.com` (or your domain).
128: 3. Vercel shows you DNS records to add at your registrar:
129:    - `A` record: `@ → 76.76.21.21`
130:    - `CNAME` record: `www → cname.vercel-dns.com`
131: 4. Add the records at your domain registrar (Namecheap, GoDaddy, Cloudflare, etc.).
132: 5. Wait 5–60 minutes for DNS propagation. Vercel auto-provisions SSL.
133: 
134: ---
135: 
136: ## Step 6 — Configure Resend (optional, for email)
137: 
138: If you want email notifications (assignment alerts, opt-in receipts, daily reminders):
139: 
140: 1. Sign up at [resend.com](https://resend.com) (free, 100 emails/day).
141: 2. Go to **Domains → Add Domain**.
142: 3. Enter your domain (e.g. `ra-syncbot.com`).
143: 4. Resend gives you 3 DNS records to add:
144:    - `MX` record
145:    - `TXT` record (SPF)
146:    - `TXT` record (DKIM)
147: 5. Add them at your registrar and click **Verify** in Resend (usually takes 5–30 minutes).
148: 6. Go to **API Keys → Create API Key** → copy the `re_...` key.
149: 7. Add it to Vercel env vars (as `RESEND_API_KEY`) and redeploy.
150: 
151: **Without Resend configured**, the app works fine — email sending is silently skipped. The claim flow skips email verification in dev mode.
152: 
153: ---
154: 
155: ## Step 7 — Configure Vercel Cron (optional, for reminders + auto-archive)
156: 
157: Add a `crons` section to `vercel.json`:
158: 
159: ```json
160: {
161:   "framework": "nextjs",
162:   "buildCommand": "bun run build",
163:   "installCommand": "bun install",
164:   "functions": {
165:     "src/app/**/*.{ts,tsx}": { "maxDuration": 30 }
166:   },
167:   "crons": [
168:     { "path": "/api/reminders", "schedule": "0 8 * * *" },
169:     { "path": "/api/auto-archive", "schedule": "0 2 * * *" }
170:   ]
171: }
172: ```
173: 
174: - `0 8 * * *` — daily reminders at 08:00 UTC (04:00 AST Barbados)
175: - `0 2 * * *` — auto-archive past events at 02:00 UTC (22:00 AST previous day)
176: 
177: Commit and push — Vercel picks up the cron config on the next deploy.
178: 
179: > Vercel Cron on the free tier runs once per day per cron job. If you need more frequent runs, upgrade to Pro.
180: 
181: ---
182: 
183: ## Step 8 — Verify the deployment
184: 
185: 1. Visit your Vercel URL (or custom domain).
186: 2. Log in with the admin credentials created by the seed:
187:    - Email: `robotadventuresltd@gmail.com`
188:    - Password: `admin123`
189: 3. **Immediately change the password** via the account menu (top-right) → Change password.
190: 4. Walk through the tabs:
191:    - **Scheduler** — drag an instructor onto an event
192:    - **Calendar** — click an event chip
193:    - **Events** — edit an event
194:    - **Team** — view instructor profiles
195:    - **Invites** — create an invite link and open it in an incognito window to test the claim flow
196: 
197: ---
198: 
199: ## Troubleshooting
200: 
201: ### Build fails with "Cannot find module"
202: Run `bun install` locally to regenerate `bun.lock`, then commit and push.
203: 
204: ### 401 on every API call after deploying
205: You forgot to set `SESSION_PASSWORD` in Vercel env vars, or the seed didn't run. Re-run the seed locally with the same `SESSION_PASSWORD` you set in Vercel.
206: 
207: ### Drag-and-drop crashes on desktop (`Cannot access 'g' before initialization`)
208: This was a historical bug caused by Node's `crypto` module leaking into the client bundle. It's fixed — `session.ts` uses Web Crypto (`crypto.subtle`) and is marked `server-only`. If you see this error again, check that no API route imports from `src/lib/session.ts` directly in a way that gets bundled client-side.
209: 
210: ### Emails not sending
211: - Check that `RESEND_API_KEY` and `FROM_EMAIL` are set in Vercel env vars.
212: - Check that the `FROM_EMAIL` domain is **verified** in Resend.
213: - Check the Notifications tab in the admin UI for the send log.
214: 
215: ### Custom domain shows "404 Not Found"
216: - Vercel hasn't finished provisioning. Wait 5–10 minutes.
217: - DNS records aren't propagated. Check with `dig ra-syncbot.com`.
218: - You added the domain to Vercel but didn't add the DNS records at your registrar.
219: 
220: ### iCal feed returns 401
221: The iCal endpoint uses `?token=<userId>` as auth (not the session cookie). Get your userId from the account menu → "Subscribe to calendar" link. Don't share this link — anyone with it can see your schedule.
222: 
223: ---
224: 
225: ## Updating the deployment
226: 
227: ```bash
228: git pull
229: bun install        # if deps changed
230: bun run migrate    # run migrations to add new tables/columns (safe, idempotent)
231: bun run seed       # only if you need to wipe + reseed (usually you don't — destroys data)
232: git push           # Vercel auto-deploys on push to main
233: ```
234: 
235: **Always run `bun run migrate` after pulling** if there are new tables or columns. The migration script is idempotent — safe to run multiple times. It uses `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` and `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN` with duplicate-column detection.
236: 
237: The migration script (`scripts/migrate.ts`) handles:
238: - Adding `emailNotifications` column to `User`
239: - Adding `ackStatus` + `acknowledgedAt` columns to `Assignment`
240: - Creating `Skill`, `EquipmentCatalog`, `EventEquipment`, `EquipmentClaim`, `Notification`, `EmailQueue` tables
241: - Adding a unique index on `EquipmentClaim(equipmentItemId, profileId)`
242: - Seeding the skill catalog from existing `Profile.skills` + `EventSkill` data
243: 
244: ---
245: 
246: ## Backup
247: 
248: Turso free tier doesn't include automated backups, but you can dump the DB at any time:
249: 
250: ```bash
251: turso db shell ra-syncbot ".dump" > backup.sql
252: ```
253: 
254: To restore:
255: ```bash
256: turso db shell ra-syncbot < backup.sql
257: ```
258: 
259: Recommended cadence: weekly during the active camp season.

================
File: scripts/generate-icons.ts
================
  1: /**
  2:  * Generate all app icons from a source image.
  3:  *
  4:  * Two variants per size:
  5:  * - Transparent (for logo.png + "any" purpose icons) — checkerboard removed
  6:  * - Opaque (for "maskable" purpose icons) — solid background, required by PWA spec
  7:  *
  8:  * Run with: bun run scripts/generate-icons.ts
  9:  */
 10: 
 11: import sharp from 'sharp'
 12: import { readFileSync, writeFileSync } from 'fs'
 13: 
 14: const SRC = 'upload/Gemini_Generated_Image_amghq3amghq3amgh.png'
 15: const OUT = 'public'
 16: 
 17: const COLOR_TOLERANCE = 15
 18: const GREY_TOLERANCE = 8
 19: const Bg_COLOR = { r: 10, g: 10, b: 10 } // #0a0a0a — matches manifest background_color
 20: 
 21: async function main() {
 22:   const raw = readFileSync(SRC)
 23:   const meta = await sharp(raw).metadata()
 24:   console.log(`Source: ${meta.width}x${meta.height} ${meta.format}`)
 25: 
 26:   // Detect checkerboard greys
 27:   const { data, info } = await sharp(raw).raw().ensureAlpha().toBuffer({ resolveWithObject: true })
 28:   const cornerSamples: number[][] = []
 29:   const sampleSize = 20
 30:   for (const [cx, cy] of [[0,0], [info.width-1,0], [0,info.height-1], [info.width-1,info.height-1]]) {
 31:     for (let dy = 0; dy < sampleSize; dy++) {
 32:       for (let dx = 0; dx < sampleSize; dx++) {
 33:         const x = Math.min(info.width-1, Math.max(0, cx - sampleSize/2 + dx))
 34:         const y = Math.min(info.height-1, Math.max(0, cy - sampleSize/2 + dy))
 35:         const idx = (y * info.width + x) * 4
 36:         cornerSamples.push([data[idx], data[idx+1], data[idx+2]])
 37:       }
 38:     }
 39:   }
 40: 
 41:   const buckets = new Map<string, number[]>()
 42:   for (const [r, g, b] of cornerSamples) {
 43:     const isGrey = Math.abs(r-g) < GREY_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-b) < GREY_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(r-b) < GREY_TOLERANCE
 44:     if (!isGrey) continue
 45:     const key = `${Math.round(r/25)*25}`
 46:     if (!buckets.has(key)) buckets.set(key, [])
 47:     buckets.get(key)!.push(r)
 48:   }
 49:   const sorted = [...buckets.entries()].sort((a, b) => b[1].length - a[1].length)
 50:   const grey1 = sorted.length > 0 ? Math.round(sorted[0][1].reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / sorted[0][1].length) : null
 51:   const grey2 = sorted.length > 1 ? Math.round(sorted[1][1].reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / sorted[1][1].length) : null
 52:   console.log(`Detected checkerboard greys: ${grey1} and ${grey2}`)
 53: 
 54:   // Center-crop to square
 55:   const size = Math.min(meta.width!, meta.height!)
 56:   const left = Math.round((meta.width! - size) / 2)
 57:   const top = Math.round((meta.height! - size) / 2)
 58:   const cropped = sharp(raw).extract({ left, top, width: size, height: size })
 59: 
 60:   // Build transparent version (checkerboard removed → alpha=0)
 61:   const transparentBuffer = await removeCheckerboard(cropped, grey1, grey2)
 62: 
 63:   // Build opaque version (checkerboard replaced with solid background color)
 64:   const opaqueBuffer = await replaceCheckerboardWithBg(cropped, grey1, grey2)
 65: 
 66:   // ── Generate all target sizes ──
 67:   // Transparent icons (for UI + "any" purpose)
 68:   const transparentTargets = [
 69:     { name: 'logo.png', size: 512 },           // in-app header logo
 70:     { name: 'icon-any-192.png', size: 192 },    // PWA "any" purpose
 71:     { name: 'icon-any-512.png', size: 512 },    // PWA "any" purpose
 72:     { name: 'apple-touch-icon.png', size: 180 }, // iOS (opaque on iOS, but keep transparent for consistency)
 73:     { name: 'favicon-32.png', size: 32 },
 74:     { name: 'favicon-16.png', size: 16 },
 75:   ]
 76: 
 77:   // Opaque icons (for "maskable" purpose — must be fully opaque)
 78:   const opaqueTargets = [
 79:     { name: 'icon-maskable-192.png', size: 192 },
 80:     { name: 'icon-maskable-512.png', size: 512 },
 81:   ]
 82: 
 83:   console.log('\nTransparent icons:')
 84:   for (const t of transparentTargets) {
 85:     await sharp(transparentBuffer)
 86:       .resize(t.size, t.size, { fit: 'cover', position: 'center' })
 87:       .png({ palette: false, compressionLevel: 9 })  // force RGBA, not palette
 88:       .toFile(`${OUT}/${t.name}`)
 89:     console.log(`  ✓ ${t.name} (${t.size}x${t.size})`)
 90:   }
 91: 
 92:   console.log('\nOpaque (maskable) icons:')
 93:   for (const t of opaqueTargets) {
 94:     await sharp(opaqueBuffer)
 95:       .resize(t.size, t.size, { fit: 'cover', position: 'center' })
 96:       .png({ palette: false, compressionLevel: 9 })  // force RGBA
 97:       .flatten({ background: `rgb(${Bg_COLOR.r},${Bg_COLOR.g},${Bg_COLOR.b})` }) // ensure no alpha
 98:       .toFile(`${OUT}/${t.name}`)
 99:     console.log(`  ✓ ${t.name} (${t.size}x${t.size})`)
100:   }
101: 
102:   // Also generate the legacy-named icons for backward compat
103:   // icon-192.png and icon-512.png → use the opaque (maskable) versions
104:   // since the manifest references them for "any maskable" purpose
105:   await sharp(opaqueBuffer).resize(192, 192, { fit: 'cover' }).png({ palette: false }).flatten({ background: `rgb(${Bg_COLOR.r},${Bg_COLOR.g},${Bg_COLOR.b})` }).toFile(`${OUT}/icon-192.png`)
106:   await sharp(opaqueBuffer).resize(512, 512, { fit: 'cover' }).png({ palette: false }).flatten({ background: `rgb(${Bg_COLOR.r},${Bg_COLOR.g},${Bg_COLOR.b})` }).toFile(`${OUT}/icon-512.png`)
107:   console.log('  ✓ icon-192.png (opaque, for backward compat)')
108:   console.log('  ✓ icon-512.png (opaque, for backward compat)')
109: 
110:   // Build favicon.ico
111:   const png32 = readFileSync(`${OUT}/favicon-32.png`)
112:   const png16 = readFileSync(`${OUT}/favicon-16.png`)
113:   const ico = buildIco([
114:     { width: 32, height: 32, png: png32 },
115:     { width: 16, height: 16, png: png16 },
116:   ])
117:   writeFileSync(`${OUT}/favicon.ico`, ico)
118:   console.log('  ✓ favicon.ico')
119: 
120:   console.log('\n✓ All icons generated.')
121: }
122: 
123: async function removeCheckerboard(cropped: sharp.Sharp, grey1: number | null, grey2: number | null): Promise<Buffer> {
124:   if (grey1 === null || grey2 === null) {
125:     return cropped.raw().ensureAlpha().png().toBuffer()
126:   }
127:   const { data, info } = await cropped.raw().ensureAlpha().toBuffer({ resolveWithObject: true })
128:   const out = Buffer.from(data)
129:   for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i += 4) {
130:     const r = data[i], g = data[i+1], b = data[i+2]
131:     const isGrey = Math.abs(r-g) < GREY_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-b) < GREY_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(r-b) < GREY_TOLERANCE
132:     if (!isGrey) continue
133:     const m1 = Math.abs(r-grey1) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-grey1) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(b-grey1) < COLOR_TOLERANCE
134:     const m2 = Math.abs(r-grey2) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-grey2) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(b-grey2) < COLOR_TOLERANCE
135:     if (m1 || m2) out[i+3] = 0
136:   }
137:   return sharp(out, { raw: { width: info.width, height: info.height, channels: 4 } }).png().toBuffer()
138: }
139: 
140: async function replaceCheckerboardWithBg(cropped: sharp.Sharp, grey1: number | null, grey2: number | null): Promise<Buffer> {
141:   if (grey1 === null || grey2 === null) {
142:     return cropped.flatten({ background: `rgb(${Bg_COLOR.r},${Bg_COLOR.g},${Bg_COLOR.b})` }).png().toBuffer()
143:   }
144:   const { data, info } = await cropped.raw().ensureAlpha().toBuffer({ resolveWithObject: true })
145:   const out = Buffer.from(data)
146:   for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i += 4) {
147:     const r = data[i], g = data[i+1], b = data[i+2]
148:     const isGrey = Math.abs(r-g) < GREY_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-b) < GREY_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(r-b) < GREY_TOLERANCE
149:     if (!isGrey) continue
150:     const m1 = Math.abs(r-grey1) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-grey1) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(b-grey1) < COLOR_TOLERANCE
151:     const m2 = Math.abs(r-grey2) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(g-grey2) < COLOR_TOLERANCE && Math.abs(b-grey2) < COLOR_TOLERANCE
152:     if (m1 || m2) {
153:       out[i] = Bg_COLOR.r
154:       out[i+1] = Bg_COLOR.g
155:       out[i+2] = Bg_COLOR.b
156:       out[i+3] = 255 // fully opaque
157:     }
158:   }
159:   return sharp(out, { raw: { width: info.width, height: info.height, channels: 4 } }).png().toBuffer()
160: }
161: 
162: function buildIco(images: { width: number; height: number; png: Buffer }[]): Buffer {
163:   const HEADER_SIZE = 6
164:   const ENTRY_SIZE = 16
165:   const count = images.length
166:   const offset = HEADER_SIZE + ENTRY_SIZE * count
167:   const header = Buffer.alloc(HEADER_SIZE)
168:   header.writeUInt16LE(0, 0)
169:   header.writeUInt16LE(1, 2)
170:   header.writeUInt16LE(count, 4)
171:   let cursor = offset
172:   const entries: Buffer[] = []
173:   for (const img of images) {
174:     const entry = Buffer.alloc(ENTRY_SIZE)
175:     entry.writeUInt8(img.width === 256 ? 0 : img.width, 0)
176:     entry.writeUInt8(img.height === 256 ? 0 : img.height, 1)
177:     entry.writeUInt8(0, 2)
178:     entry.writeUInt8(0, 3)
179:     entry.writeUInt16LE(1, 4)
180:     entry.writeUInt16LE(32, 6)
181:     entry.writeUInt32LE(img.png.length, 8)
182:     entry.writeUInt32LE(cursor, 12)
183:     entries.push(entry)
184:     cursor += img.png.length
185:   }
186:   return Buffer.concat([header, ...entries, ...images.map(i => i.png)])
187: }
188: 
189: main().catch(e => { console.error(e); process.exit(1) })

File: src/app/api/auto-archive/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: 
 4: // POST /api/auto-archive — automatically archive events whose end date has passed
 5: // Called when the schedule is loaded. Safe to call repeatedly.
 6: export async function POST() {
 7:   try {
 8:     const today = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
 9:       timeZone: 'America/Barbados',
10:       year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
11:     }).format(new Date())
12: 
13:     const result = await db.execute({
14:       sql: `SELECT id, name, endDate FROM Event 
15:             WHERE status NOT IN ('Draft', 'Archived') 
16:             AND endDate < ?`,
17:       args: [today + 'T23:59:59.000Z'],
18:     })
19: 
20:     if (result.rows.length === 0) {
21:       return NextResponse.json({ archived: 0 })
22:     }
23: 
24:     for (const row of result.rows) {
25:       await db.execute({
26:         sql: "UPDATE Event SET status = 'Archived', updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?",
27:         args: [(row as any).id],
28:       })
29:     }
30: 
31:     return NextResponse.json({ archived: result.rows.length })
32:   } catch (e: any) {
33:     console.error('Auto-archive error:', e.message)
34:     return NextResponse.json({ archived: 0, error: e.message })
35:   }
36: }

================
File: src/app/api/ical/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: // GET /api/ical?token=<inviteToken>
 6: // Returns an iCal (.ics) feed of the user's assignments.
 7: // The token is the user's inviteToken (used as a simple auth mechanism for calendar apps).
 8: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 9:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
10:   const token = searchParams.get('token')
11: 
12:   if (!token) {
13:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing token' }, { status: 400 })
14:   }
15: 
16:   // Find the user by invite token OR user id (both work)
17:   const userResult = await db.execute({
18:     sql: `SELECT u.*, p.name as profileName FROM User u
19:           LEFT JOIN Profile p ON u.profileId = p.id
20:           WHERE (u.inviteToken = ? OR u.id = ?) AND u.claimedAt IS NOT NULL`,
21:     args: [token, token],
22:   })
23: 
24:   if (userResult.rows.length === 0) {
25:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid token' }, { status: 404 })
26:   }
27: 
28:   const user = userResult.rows[0] as any
29:   if (!user.profileId) {
30:     return new NextResponse('BEGIN:VCALENDAR\nVERSION:2.0\nPRODID:-//RA Syncbot//Scheduler//EN\nEND:VCALENDAR', {
31:       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/calendar; charset=utf-8' },
32:     })
33:   }
34: 
35:   // Get all assignments for this instructor
36:   const assignments = await db.execute({
37:     sql: `SELECT a.*, e.name as eventName, e.location, e.startTime, e.endTime,
38:           e.hostColor, e.setupDate, e.setupTime
39:           FROM Assignment a
40:           JOIN Event e ON a.eventId = e.id
41:           WHERE a.profileId = ?
42:           ORDER BY a.assignedDate ASC`,
43:     args: [user.profileId],
44:   })
45: 
46:   // Build iCal
47:   const lines: string[] = [
48:     'BEGIN:VCALENDAR',
49:     'VERSION:2.0',
50:     'PRODID:-//RA Syncbot//Scheduler//EN',
51:     'CALSCALE:GREGORIAN',
52:     'METHOD:PUBLISH',
53:     `X-WR-CALNAME:RA Syncbot Schedule`,
54:   ]
55: 
56:   for (const a of assignments.rows as any[]) {
57:     const date = String(a.assignedDate).slice(0, 10)
58:     const startTime = a.startTime || '09:00'
59:     const endTime = a.endTime || '15:00'
60: 
61:     const dtStart = `${date.replace(/-/g, '')}T${startTime.replace(':', '')}00`
62:     const dtEnd = `${date.replace(/-/g, '')}T${endTime.replace(':', '')}00`
63: 
64:     const summary = a.isAlternative ? `[ALT] ${a.eventName}` : a.eventName
65:     const location = a.location || ''
66:     const description = [
67:       `Event: ${a.eventName}`,
68:       a.shirtColor ? `Shirt: ${a.shirtColor}` : '',
69:       a.isAlternative ? 'Role: Alternative' : 'Role: Primary',
70:     ].filter(Boolean).join('\\n')
71: 
72:     lines.push(
73:       'BEGIN:VEVENT',
74:       `UID:${a.id}@robot-adventures.scheduler`,
75:       `DTSTAMP:${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[-:]/g, '').split('.')[0]}Z`,
76:       `DTSTART:${dtStart}`,
77:       `DTEND:${dtEnd}`,
78:       `SUMMARY:${summary}`,
79:       location ? `LOCATION:${location}` : '',
80:       `DESCRIPTION:${description}`,
81:       'END:VEVENT',
82:     )
83:   }
84: 
85:   lines.push('END:VCALENDAR')
86: 
87:   return new NextResponse(lines.join('\r\n'), {
88:     headers: {
89:       'Content-Type': 'text/calendar; charset=utf-8',
90:       'Content-Disposition': 'inline; filename="robot-adventures.ics"',
91:     },
92:   })
93: }

================
File: src/app/api/notifications/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: // GET /api/notifications — returns notifications for the current user (from Notification table)
 6: // Falls back to legacy computed notifications if the table doesn't exist yet.
 7: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 8:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 9:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
10: 
11:   try {
12:     const result = await db.execute({
13:       sql: `SELECT * FROM Notification WHERE userId = ? ORDER BY createdAt DESC LIMIT 50`,
14:       args: [user.id],
15:     })
16:     const notifications = (result.rows as any[]).map(n => ({
17:       id: n.id,
18:       type: n.type,
19:       title: n.title,
20:       body: n.body,
21:       eventId: n.eventId,
22:       assignmentId: n.assignmentId,
23:       readAt: n.readAt,
24:       createdAt: n.createdAt,
25:       read: !!n.readAt,
26:     }))
27:     const unread = notifications.filter(n => !n.read).length
28:     return NextResponse.json({ notifications, unread })
29:   } catch (e: any) {
30:     // Notification table doesn't exist yet — return empty
31:     return NextResponse.json({ notifications: [], unread: 0 })
32:   }
33: }

File: src/components/scheduler/PWAInstallPrompt.tsx
================
 1: 'use client'
 2: 
 3: import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
 4: import { Download, X } from 'lucide-react'
 5: 
 6: type BeforeInstallPromptEvent = Event & {
 7:   prompt: () => Promise<void>
 8:   userChoice: Promise<{ outcome: 'accepted' | 'dismissed' }>
 9: }
10: 
11: export function PWAInstallPrompt() {
12:   const [deferredPrompt, setDeferredPrompt] = useState<BeforeInstallPromptEvent | null>(null)
13:   const [showPrompt, setShowPrompt] = useState(false)
14: 
15:   useEffect(() => {
16:     const handler = (e: Event) => {
17:       e.preventDefault()
18:       setDeferredPrompt(e as BeforeInstallPromptEvent)
19:       // Check if already dismissed
20:       if (sessionStorage.getItem('pwa-prompt-dismissed') !== 'true') {
21:         setShowPrompt(true)
22:       }
23:     }
24:     window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', handler)
25:     return () => window.removeEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', handler)
26:   }, [])
27: 
28:   const handleInstall = async () => {
29:     if (!deferredPrompt) return
30:     await deferredPrompt.prompt()
31:     const choice = await deferredPrompt.userChoice
32:     if (choice.outcome === 'accepted') {
33:       setShowPrompt(false)
34:     }
35:     setDeferredPrompt(null)
36:   }
37: 
38:   const handleDismiss = () => {
39:     setShowPrompt(false)
40:     sessionStorage.setItem('pwa-prompt-dismissed', 'true')
41:   }
42: 
43:   if (!showPrompt || !deferredPrompt) return null
44: 
45:   return (
46:     <div className="fixed bottom-4 left-4 right-4 sm:left-auto sm:right-4 sm:w-80 z-50 bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-lg shadow-xl p-4">
47:       <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
48:         <div className="h-10 w-10 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-emerald-500 to-teal-600 flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold text-sm shrink-0">
49:           RA
50:         </div>
51:         <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
52:           <p className="text-sm font-semibold">Install RA Scheduler</p>
53:           <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
54:             Add to your home screen for quick access — works like a native app.
55:           </p>
56:           <div className="flex gap-2 mt-2">
57:             <button
58:               onClick={handleInstall}
59:               className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 flex items-center gap-1.5 min-h-[32px]"
60:             >
61:               <Download className="h-3 w-3" />
62:               Install
63:             </button>
64:             <button
65:               onClick={handleDismiss}
66:               className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px]"
67:             >
68:               Not now
69:             </button>
70:           </div>
71:         </div>
72:         <button
73:           onClick={handleDismiss}
74:           className="p-1 rounded hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
75:           aria-label="Dismiss"
76:         >
77:           <X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
78:         </button>
79:       </div>
80:     </div>
81:   )
82: }

 7: const buttonVariants = cva(
 8:   "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",

11:       variant: {

13:           "bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-xs hover:bg-primary/90",

15:           "bg-destructive text-white shadow-xs hover:bg-destructive/90 focus-visible:ring-destructive/20 dark:focus-visible:ring-destructive/40 dark:bg-destructive/60",
16:         outline:
17:           "border bg-background shadow-xs hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:bg-input/30 dark:border-input dark:hover:bg-input/50",
18:         secondary:
19:           "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground shadow-xs hover:bg-secondary/80",
20:         ghost:
21:           "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50",
22:         link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
23:       },
24:       size: {
25:         default: "h-9 px-4 py-2 has-[>svg]:px-3",
26:         sm: "h-8 rounded-md gap-1.5 px-3 has-[>svg]:px-2.5",
27:         lg: "h-10 rounded-md px-6 has-[>svg]:px-4",
28:         icon: "size-9",

30:     },

32:       variant: "default",
33:       size: "default",
34:     },

38: function Button({
39:   className,
40:   variant,
41:   size,
42:   asChild = false,
43:   ...props
44: }: React.ComponentProps<"button"> &
45:   VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> & {
46:     asChild?: boolean
47:   }) {
48:   const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"
49: 
50:   return (
51:     <Comp
52:       data-slot="button"
53:       className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
54:       {...props}
55:     />
56:   )
57: }
58:

 61:         data-slot="dialog-content"
 62:         className={cn(
 63:           "bg-background data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 fixed top-[50%] left-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 rounded-lg border p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 sm:max-w-lg",
 64:           className
 65:         )}
 66:         {...props}
 67:       >
 68:         {children}
 69:         {showCloseButton && (
 70:           <DialogPrimitive.Close
 71:             data-slot="dialog-close"
 72:             className="ring-offset-background focus:ring-ring data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground absolute top-4 right-4 rounded-xs opacity-70 transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:outline-hidden disabled:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:shrink-0 [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4"
 73:           >
 74:             <XIcon />
 75:             <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
 76:           </DialogPrimitive.Close>
 77:         )}
 78:       </DialogPrimitive.Content>
 79:     </DialogPortal>
 80:   )
 81: }
 82: 
 83: function DialogHeader({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
 84:   return (
 85:     <div
 86:       data-slot="dialog-header"
 87:       className={cn("flex flex-col gap-2 text-center sm:text-left", className)}
 88:       {...props}
 89:     />
 90:   )
 91: }
 92:

100:       )}

102:     />
103:   )
104: }
105:
