================
File: API.md
================
  1: # API Reference
  2: 
  3: All routes are under `/api`. Request bodies are JSON. Responses are JSON. All mutations require authentication via the `ra-session` cookie.
  4: 
  5: ## Authentication
  6: 
  7: | Header / Cookie | Required | Description |
  8: |---|---|---|
  9: | `Cookie: ra-session=<userId>.<hmac>` | Yes (for protected routes) | Set by `/api/auth/me` or `/api/auth/claim` |
 10: 
 11: ### Auth helper responses
 12: - `401 Unauthorized` — no session, or user not found
 13: - `403 Forbidden` — authenticated but not admin (admin routes only)
 14: 
 15: ---
 16: 
 17: ## Auth
 18: 
 19: ### `POST /api/auth/me`
 20: Login or refresh the current session.
 21: 
 22: **Request body**
 23: ```json
 24: { "email": "user@example.com", "password": "secret123" }
 25: ```
 26: **200 Response**
 27: ```json
 28: {
 29:   "user": {
 30:     "id": "uuid",
 31:     "name": "Jamie Smith",
 32:     "email": "user@example.com",
 33:     "role": "admin",
 34:     "profileId": "uuid" | null,
 35:     "profile": { "id": "uuid", "name": "...", "roleTier": "lead", "role": "...", "skills": "...", "unavailable": "..." } | null
 36:   }
 37: }
 38: ```
 39: **401 Response** — `{ "error": "Invalid email or password" }`
 40: 
 41: Sets `ra-session` cookie (httpOnly, 30-day expiry).
 42: 
 43: ---
 44: 
 45: ### `GET /api/auth/me`
 46: Return the currently authenticated user. Useful for refreshing on page load.
 47: 
 48: **200 Response** — same shape as the POST response, or `{ "user": null }` if not authenticated.
 49: 
 50: ---
 51: 
 52: ### `POST /api/auth/claim`
 53: Claim an invite. Two-step flow with email verification.
 54: 
 55: **Step 1 — request verification code**
 56: ```json
 57: { "token": "<inviteToken>", "name": "Jamie Smith", "email": "jamie@example.com", "password": "secret123" }
 58: ```
 59: **200 Response** — `{ "step": "verify", "message": "Verification code sent to your email." }`
 60: 
 61: **Step 2 — verify code and claim**
 62: ```json
 63: { "token": "<inviteToken>", "name": "Jamie Smith", "email": "jamie@example.com", "password": "secret123", "verifyCode": "123456" }
 64: ```
 65: **200 Response** — `{ "user": { ... } }` (same shape as login) and sets the session cookie.
 66: 
 67: **Error responses**
 68: - `400` — missing token, email, or password too short (<6 chars)
 69: - `404` — invalid invite token
 70: - `409` — email already in use
 71: - `410` — invite link expired or verification code expired
 72: - `401` — incorrect verification code
 73: 
 74: > **Note:** If `RESEND_API_KEY` is not set, the server skips email verification and claims the account immediately (dev mode).
 75: 
 76: ---
 77: 
 78: ### `POST /api/auth/logout`
 79: Clear the session cookie. No request body.
 80: 
 81: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
 82: 
 83: ---
 84: 
 85: ### `POST /api/auth/change-password`
 86: Change the current user's password. Requires authentication.
 87: 
 88: **Request body**
 89: ```json
 90: { "currentPassword": "old", "newPassword": "newpass123" }
 91: ```
 92: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
 93: **401 Response** — `{ "error": "Current password is incorrect" }`
 94: 
 95: ---
 96: 
 97: ## Schedule
 98: 
 99: ### `GET /api/schedule?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD`
100: Fetch all profiles, events, and assignments in the date range. This is the primary data fetch for the admin scheduler.
101: 
102: **Query params**
103: - `from` (optional, default `2026-06-01`) — ISO date
104: - `to` (optional, default `2026-09-30`) — ISO date
105: - `includeDrafts=1` (optional) — include Draft events (admin only)
106: 
107: **200 Response**
108: ```json
109: {
110:   "profiles": [ ProfileView ],
111:   "events":    [ EventView ],
112:   "assignments": [ AssignmentView ]
113: }
114: ```
115: 
116: See `src/lib/scheduler-types.ts` for the full type definitions.
117: 
118: **Filtering rules**
119: - Events: excludes `Draft` by default; includes `Confirmed`, `Tentative`, `Cancelled`, `Archived`
120: - Assignments: all assignments with `assignedDate` between `from` and `to`
121: - Profiles: all profiles (admin sees everyone; instructors should use `/api/profiles/me`)
122: 
123: ---
124: 
125: ## Assignments
126: 
127: ### `GET /api/assignments?eventId=<id>&date=YYYY-MM-DD`
128: Fetch assignments for a specific event+date. Used by the event detail drawer.
129: 
130: **200 Response** — `{ "assignments": [ AssignmentView ] }`
131: 
132: ---
133: 
134: ### `POST /api/assignments`
135: Create a new assignment. **Admin only.** Runs server-side conflict validation.
136: 
137: **Request body**
138: ```json
139: {
140:   "eventId": "uuid",
141:   "profileId": "uuid",
142:   "date": "2026-07-15",
143:   "isAlternative": false,
144:   "shirtColor": "Orange"
145: }
146: ```
147: **200 Response** — `{ "assignment": AssignmentView }`
148: **409 Response** — `{ "error": "Conflict: ...", "conflicts": [...] }`
149: 
150: Triggers `notifyAssignmentCreated` email if email is configured.
151: 
152: ---
153: 
154: ### `POST /api/assignments/bulk`
155: Create the same assignment across multiple dates. **Admin only.**
156: 
157: **Request body**
158: ```json
159: {
160:   "eventId": "uuid",
161:   "profileId": "uuid",
162:   "dates": ["2026-07-06", "2026-07-07", "2026-07-08"],
163:   "isAlternative": false
164: }
165: ```
166: **200 Response** — `{ "created": 3, "skipped": 0 }`
167: 
168: ---
169: 
170: ### `PATCH /api/assignments`
171: Update an existing assignment (e.g. change shirt color, toggle alternative). **Admin only.**
172: 
173: **Request body**
174: ```json
175: { "id": "uuid", "patch": { "shirtColor": "Blue", "isAlternative": false } }
176: ```
177: **200 Response** — `{ "assignment": AssignmentView }`
178: 
179: ---
180: 
181: ### `DELETE /api/assignments?id=<id>`
182: Remove an assignment. **Admin only.**
183: 
184: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
185: 
186: Triggers `notifyAssignmentRemoved` email if email is configured.
187: 
188: ---
189: 
190: ## Events
191: 
192: ### `GET /api/events`
193: List all events. **Admin only.**
194: 
195: **200 Response** — `{ "events": [ EventView ] }`
196: 
197: ---
198: 
199: ### `POST /api/events`
200: Create a new event. **Admin only.**
201: 
202: **Request body**
203: ```json
204: {
205:   "code": "WSB-1",
206:   "name": "Aerial Robotics",
207:   "host": "TVETC / WSB",
208:   "hostColor": "teal",
209:   "location": "SJPI",
210:   "description": "...",
211:   "startDate": "2026-07-06",
212:   "endDate": "2026-07-10",
213:   "startTime": "09:00",
214:   "endTime": "15:00",
215:   "status": "Confirmed",
216:   "specificDates": null,
217:   "ageRange": "10-16",
218:   "participantCount": 25,
219:   "requiredInstructors": 5,
220:   "setupDate": null,
221:   "setupTime": null,
222:   "notes": "",
223:   "requiredSkills": ["Aerial Robotics", "Python"]
224: }
225: ```
226: **200 Response** — `{ "event": EventView }`
227: 
228: ---
229: 
230: ### `PUT /api/events?id=<id>`
231: Update an event. **Admin only.** Accepts the same body as POST (all fields optional).
232: 
233: **200 Response** — `{ "event": EventView }`
234: 
235: ---
236: 
237: ### `DELETE /api/events?id=<id>`
238: Delete an event. **Admin only.** Also deletes all child assignments and EventSkill rows.
239: 
240: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
241: 
242: ---
243: 
244: ## Profiles
245: 
246: ### `GET /api/profiles`
247: List all staff profiles. **Admin only.**
248: 
249: **200 Response** — `{ "profiles": [ ProfileView ] }`
250: 
251: ---
252: 
253: ### `GET /api/profiles/me`
254: Get the current instructor's own profile. Used by the instructor view.
255: 
256: **200 Response** — `ProfileView` or `{ "error": "No profile linked" }` (404)
257: 
258: ---
259: 
260: ### `POST /api/profiles`
261: Create a new staff profile. **Admin only.**
262: 
263: **Request body**
264: ```json
265: {
266:   "name": "Jamie Smith",
267:   "sex": "F",
268:   "role": "Lead Instructor",
269:   "roleTier": "lead",
270:   "skills": "Robotics,Python",
271:   "available": null,
272:   "unavailable": null,
273:   "contractSigned": true,
274:   "notes": ""
275: }
276: ```
277: **200 Response** — `{ "profile": ProfileView }`
278: 
279: ---
280: 
281: ### `PUT /api/profiles?id=<id>`
282: Update a profile. **Admin only** (or the linked instructor updating their own unavailable dates).
283: 
284: **Request body** — partial Profile fields. Common use case:
285: ```json
286: { "unavailable": "2026-07-15,2026-07-22" }
287: ```
288: **200 Response** — `{ "profile": ProfileView }`
289: 
290: ---
291: 
292: ### `DELETE /api/profiles?id=<id>`
293: Delete a profile. **Admin only.**
294: 
295: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
296: 
297: ---
298: 
299: ## Opt-Ins
300: 
301: ### `GET /api/opt-ins`
302: List the current instructor's opt-ins. **Authenticated.**
303: 
304: **200 Response** — `[ OptInView ]`
305: 
306: ---
307: 
308: ### `POST /api/opt-ins`
309: Create or update an opt-in. **Authenticated.**
310: 
311: **Request body**
312: ```json
313: { "eventId": "uuid", "status": "interested", "note": "I love drones!" }
314: ```
315: `status` must be one of: `interested`, `available`, `unavailable`.
316: 
317: **200 Response** — `{ "optIn": OptInView }`
318: 
319: Triggers `notifyOptInReceived` email to the admin if email is configured.
320: 
321: ---
322: 
323: ## Invites
324: 
325: ### `GET /api/invites`
326: List all invites. **Admin only.**
327: 
328: **200 Response** — `{ "invites": [ InviteView ] }`
329: 
330: ---
331: 
332: ### `POST /api/invites`
333: Create a new invite. **Admin only.**
334: 
335: **Request body**
336: ```json
337: { "name": "Jamie Smith", "role": "instructor", "profileId": "uuid" }
338: ```
339: **200 Response** — `{ "invite": InviteView }` (includes `inviteToken` and a ready-to-share URL)
340: 
341: ---
342: 
343: ### `DELETE /api/invites?id=<id>`
344: Revoke an invite. **Admin only.** Only works on unclaimed invites.
345: 
346: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
347: 
348: ---
349: 
350: ## Notifications
351: 
352: ### `GET /api/notifications`
353: List recent email notifications sent. **Admin only.** Useful for auditing.
354: 
355: **200 Response** — `{ "notifications": [ { id, to, subject, sentAt, status } ] }`
356: 
357: ---
358: 
359: ## iCal
360: 
361: ### `GET /api/ical?token=<userId>`
362: Return an iCal calendar feed of the instructor's assignments. No session cookie required — the `token` (userId) acts as the auth.
363: 
364: **200 Response** — `Content-Type: text/calendar`
365: ```
366: BEGIN:VCALENDAR
367: VERSION:2.0
368: PRODID:-//RA Syncbot//Instructor Calendar//EN
369: BEGIN:VEVENT
370: UID:assignment-uuid@ra-syncbot.com
371: DTSTART:20260706T090000Z
372: DTEND:20260706T150000Z
373: SUMMARY:WSB — Aerial Robotics
374: LOCATION:SJPI
375: END:VEVENT
376: ...
377: END:VCALENDAR
378: ```
379: 
380: Instructors subscribe via their account menu → "Subscribe to calendar".
381: 
382: ---
383: 
384: ## Cron endpoints
385: 
386: These are intended to be called by Vercel Cron (or any external scheduler).
387: 
388: ### `POST /api/reminders`
389: Send reminder emails for assignments happening in 2 days, AND send the daily digest of pending notifications.
390: 
391: **200 Response** — `{ "reminders": N, "digests": N, "skipped": boolean }`
392: 
393: ### `POST /api/auto-archive`
394: Move all events whose `endDate` is in the past to `Archived` status.
395: 
396: **200 Response** — `{ "archived": N }`
397: 
398: ---
399: 
400: ## Notifications
401: 
402: ### `GET /api/notifications`
403: Return the current user's notifications (from the `Notification` table).
404: 
405: **200 Response**
406: ```json
407: {
408:   "notifications": [
409:     {
410:       "id": "uuid",
411:       "type": "assignment_created",
412:       "title": "New assignment: ...",
413:       "body": "...",
414:       "eventId": "uuid",
415:       "assignmentId": "uuid",
416:       "readAt": null,
417:       "createdAt": "2026-07-11T...",
418:       "read": false
419:     }
420:   ],
421:   "unread": 3
422: }
423: ```
424: 
425: ### `POST /api/notifications/read?id=<notificationId>`
426: Mark a single notification as read. If `id` is omitted, marks ALL of the user's notifications as read.
427: 
428: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
429: 
430: ### `POST /api/notifications/send-now`
431: **Admin only.** Flush all pending digest emails immediately. Useful when the admin has finished iterating on assignments and wants to notify instructors right away instead of waiting for the 8am digest.
432: 
433: **200 Response** — `{ "sent": N, "skipped": boolean }`
434: 
435: ---
436: 
437: ## Email preferences
438: 
439: ### `POST /api/auth/update-email-prefs`
440: Toggle email notifications for the current user. The notification bell is always on regardless of this setting.
441: 
442: **Request body** — `{ "emailNotifications": true }`
443: 
444: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true, "emailNotifications": true }`
445: 
446: ---
447: 
448: ## Skills (catalog)
449: 
450: ### `GET /api/skills`
451: List all skills in the catalog. **Authenticated.**
452: 
453: **200 Response** — `[ { "id": "uuid", "name": "Robotics", "createdAt": "..." } ]`
454: 
455: ### `POST /api/skills`
456: Create a new skill in the catalog. **Admin only.**
457: 
458: **Request body** — `{ "name": "Drone Piloting" }`
459: 
460: **201 Response** — `{ "id": "uuid", "name": "Drone Piloting" }`
461: 
462: ### `DELETE /api/skills?id=<id>`
463: Remove a skill from the catalog. **Admin only.** Does not affect existing assignments (skills are stored as text on Profile.skills and EventSkill.skillName).
464: 
465: **200 Response** — `{ "ok": true }`
466: 
467: ---
468: 
469: ## Equipment catalog
470: 
471: ### `GET /api/equipment`
472: List all equipment catalog items. **Authenticated.**
473: 
474: **200 Response** — `[ { "id": "uuid", "name": "Drone (Tello EDU)", "description": "..." } ]`
475: 
476: ### `POST /api/equipment`
477: Create a new equipment catalog item. **Admin only.**
478: 
479: **Request body** — `{ "name": "Drone (Tello EDU)", "description": "Educational drone" }`
480: 
481: ### `DELETE /api/equipment?id=<id>`
482: Remove from catalog. **Admin only.**
483: 
484: ---
485: 
486: ## Event equipment (per-event)
487: 
488: ### `GET /api/event-equipment?eventId=<id>`
489: List equipment items + their claims for a specific event.
490: 
491: **200 Response**
492: ```json
493: [
494:   {
495:     "id": "uuid",
496:     "eventId": "uuid",
497:     "name": "Drones",
498:     "quantity": 5,
499:     "notes": null,
500:     "claims": [
501:       {
502:         "id": "uuid",
503:         "equipmentItemId": "uuid",
504:         "profileId": "uuid",
505:         "profileName": "Nathan Reid",
506:         "quantityClaimed": 3,
507:         "transportOffered": true,
508:         "notes": null,
509:         "createdAt": "..."
510:       }
511:     ]
512:   }
513: ]
514: ```
515: 
516: ### `POST /api/event-equipment`
517: Add an equipment item to an event. **Admin only.**
518: 
519: **Request body** — `{ "eventId": "uuid", "name": "Drones", "quantity": 5, "notes": "Tello EDU" }`
520: 
521: ### `PATCH /api/event-equipment?id=<itemId>`
522: Update quantity/notes. **Admin only.**
523: 
524: ### `DELETE /api/event-equipment?id=<itemId>`
525: Remove an equipment item (cascades to its claims). **Admin only.**
526: 
527: ---
528: 
529: ## Equipment claims (instructor transport)
530: 
531: ### `GET /api/equipment-claims?equipmentItemId=<id>`
532: List claims for an equipment item.
533: 
534: ### `POST /api/equipment-claims`
535: Create or update a claim. Instructors say "I'll bring this" and optionally mark that they can transport it.
536: 
537: **Request body**
538: ```json
539: {
540:   "equipmentItemId": "uuid",
541:   "quantityClaimed": 2,
542:   "transportOffered": true,
543:   "notes": "I'll pick them up from the office"
544: }
545: ```
546: 
547: If the instructor already has a claim on this item, the existing claim is updated.
548: 
549: ### `DELETE /api/equipment-claims?id=<claimId>`
550: Release a claim. Instructors can only release their own claims; admins can release any.
551: 
552: ---
553: 
554: ## Seed (disabled in production)
555: 
556: ### `POST /api/seed`
557: Wipe and reseed the database. **Returns 403 in production.** In development, requires the `SESSION_PASSWORD` env var to match the request body.
558: 
559: **Request body** — `{ "confirm": "WIPE" }`
560: 
561: **200 Response (dev only)** — `{ "ok": true, "seeded": { "profiles": 20, "events": 17, "assignments": 33 } }`
562: 
563: > ⚠️ This endpoint is intentionally dangerous. Never enable it in production.

================
File: ARCHITECTURE.md
================
  1: # Architecture
  2: 
  3: This document describes the system design, data model, authentication flow, and deployment topology of RA Syncbot.
  4: 
  5: ---
  6: 
  7: ## High-Level Design
  8: 
  9: RA Syncbot is a single-page Next.js application served by Vercel. All state lives in Turso (libSQL/SQLite cloud). The browser never talks to Turso directly — every read/write goes through Next.js API routes that enforce auth and business rules.
 10: 
 11: ```
 12: ┌─────────────────┐     HTTPS     ┌──────────────────┐     libSQL     ┌─────────┐
 13: │  Browser (PWA)  │ ────────────► │  Next.js (Vercel)│ ─────────────► │  Turso  │
 14: │  React 19 + DnD │ ◄──────────── │  API routes + SSR│ ◄───────────── │  (SQL)  │
 15: └─────────────────┘                └──────────────────┘                 └─────────┘
 16:                                           │
 17:                                           │ fetch()
 18:                                           ▼
 19:                                    ┌──────────────┐
 20:                                    │   Resend     │  (email notifications)
 21:                                    └──────────────┘
 22: ```
 23: 
 24: There are no websockets, no background workers, and no message queues. Email notifications are fire-and-forget `fetch()` calls to Resend. Scheduled tasks (auto-archive, reminders) are triggered by Vercel Cron calling dedicated API endpoints.
 25: 
 26: ---
 27: 
 28: ## Application Layers
 29: 
 30: ### 1. Presentation (`src/components/scheduler/`)
 31: Pure React components. Each tab on the admin shell is its own component:
 32: - `CalendarGrid` — week view, the drag-and-drop surface
 33: - `CalendarView` — month view, read-only with clickable event chips
 34: - `EventDetailDrawer` — right-side drawer for editing assignments on a specific day
 35: - `RosterRail` — left-side list of instructors (draggable on desktop, tap-to-select on mobile)
 36: - `EventsManagerTab`, `TeamTab`, `ConflictSummaryTab`, `WorkloadTab`, `InvitesTab`
 37: - `InstructorView` — the instructor's 3-tab view (Assignments / Opt In / Calendar)
 38: - `LoginForm`, `ClaimInviteForm` (with email verification step)
 39: - `PrintLayout`, `PWAInstallPrompt`, `Accordion`, `HelpTooltip`
 40: 
 41: ### 2. State management
 42: - **Server state:** TanStack Query v5. Every list/detail fetch is a query; every mutation invalidates the relevant query keys.
 43: - **Local UI state:** React `useState` only — no global store. The `selected` event, current week, active tab, and tap-selected instructor are all local to `page.tsx` and passed down via props.
 44: - **No `useSyncExternalStore`** — it caused a TDZ crash that took a full session to diagnose. We use `useState + useEffect` for client-only state (claim token, mount detection).
 45: 
 46: ### 3. API layer (`src/app/api/`)
 47: Next.js App Router route handlers. Each route:
 48: 1. Reads the signed session cookie via `getAuthUser(req)` or `requireAdmin(req)`
 49: 2. Validates the request body
 50: 3. Executes SQL against Turso via `@libsql/client`
 51: 4. Returns JSON
 52: 
 53: All admin mutations are gated by `requireAdmin` which returns a 401/403 response if the caller is not an admin.
 54: 
 55: ### 4. Data layer (`src/lib/`)
 56: - **`db.ts`** — exports a single `db` client. Detects `TURSO_URL` in env; if present, connects to Turso, otherwise falls back to `file:./db/custom.db` for local dev.
 57: - **`session.ts`** — HMAC-signed cookies using Web Crypto API (`crypto.subtle`). The cookie payload is `userId.hmac(userId)` so it can't be tampered with. Marked `server-only` to prevent leaking into client bundles.
 58: - **`auth-helpers.ts`** — `getAuthUser`, `requireAdmin`, `requireAuth`. Wraps session reading + user lookup.
 59: - **`conflicts.ts`** — pure functions: `checkAvailability`, `checkTemporalOverlap`, `checkSkillMatch`, `checkFatigue`, `getMissingSkills`. No I/O — used both client-side (instant feedback) and server-side (validation).
 60: - **`email.ts`** — Resend API wrapper. `notifyAssignmentCreated`, `notifyAssignmentRemoved`, `notifyOptInReceived`, `sendReminders`. All silently no-op if `RESEND_API_KEY` is unset (dev mode).
 61: - **`scheduler-types.ts`** — shared TypeScript types + date helpers (`todayInBarbados`, `isPastDate`, `eventOnDate`, `isEventPast`). All date math uses ISO strings (`YYYY-MM-DD`) and explicit UTC to avoid timezone drift.
 62: 
 63: ---
 64: 
 65: ## Data Model
 66: 
 67: Twelve tables. All UUIDs are v4 strings. Timestamps are ISO strings stored as `datetime('now')`. Run `bun run migrate` to add new tables/columns to an existing database.
 68: 
 69: ### `User`
 70: Authentication account. Either an admin or an instructor.
 71: 
 72: | Column | Type | Notes |
 73: |---|---|---|
 74: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
 75: | `name` | TEXT | Display name |
 76: | `email` | TEXT UNIQUE | Login email; null until claimed |
 77: | `role` | TEXT | `'admin'` or `'instructor'` |
 78: | `passwordHash` | TEXT | bcrypt hash; null until claimed |
 79: | `profileId` | TEXT FK → Profile | Links auth account to staff profile |
 80: | `inviteToken` | TEXT UNIQUE | One-time token for the invite link |
 81: | `claimedAt` | DATETIME | Null until the invite is claimed |
 82: | `emailNotifications` | INTEGER | 1 (default) or 0 — per-user email toggle; bell always works |
 83: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | DATETIME | |
 84: 
 85: ### `Profile`
 86: A staff member's professional record. One Profile can be linked to one User.
 87: 
 88: | Column | Type | Notes |
 89: |---|---|---|
 90: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
 91: | `name` | TEXT | |
 92: | `sex` | TEXT NULL | |
 93: | `role` | TEXT | e.g. "Lead Instructor" |
 94: | `roleTier` | TEXT | `'lead'`, `'senior'`, `'junior'`, `'trainee'` |
 95: | `skills` | TEXT | Comma-separated skill names |
 96: | `available` | TEXT NULL | General availability notes |
 97: | `unavailable` | TEXT NULL | Comma-separated ISO dates the instructor can't work |
 98: | `contractSigned` | INTEGER | 0 or 1 |
 99: | `notes` | TEXT NULL | |
100: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | DATETIME | |
101: 
102: ### `Event`
103: A camp, workshop, or one-off session.
104: 
105: | Column | Type | Notes |
106: |---|---|---|
107: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
108: | `code` | TEXT NULL | Short code e.g. `WSB-1` |
109: | `name` | TEXT | |
110: | `host` | TEXT | Partner organization |
111: | `hostColor` | TEXT | One of: `teal`, `emerald`, `pink`, `rose`, `amber`, `slate`, `sky` |
112: | `location` | TEXT NULL | |
113: | `description` | TEXT NULL | |
114: | `startDate`, `endDate` | TEXT | ISO `YYYY-MM-DD` |
115: | `startTime`, `endTime` | TEXT | `HH:MM` 24h |
116: | `status` | TEXT | `Draft`, `Tentative`, `Confirmed`, `Cancelled`, `Archived` |
117: | `specificDates` | TEXT NULL | Comma-separated ISO dates (overrides start/end if set) |
118: | `ageRange` | TEXT NULL | |
119: | `participantCount` | INTEGER NULL | |
120: | `requiredInstructors` | INTEGER | |
121: | `setupDate` | TEXT NULL | Optional setup day before the event |
122: | `setupTime` | TEXT NULL | |
123: | `notes` | TEXT NULL | |
124: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | DATETIME | |
125: 
126: ### `Assignment`
127: A specific instructor assigned to a specific event on a specific date.
128: 
129: | Column | Type | Notes |
130: |---|---|---|
131: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
132: | `eventId` | TEXT FK → Event | |
133: | `profileId` | TEXT FK → Profile | |
134: | `assignedDate` | TEXT | ISO `YYYY-MM-DD` |
135: | `status` | TEXT | `'primary'` or `'alternative'` |
136: | `isAlternative` | INTEGER | 0 or 1 (denormalized for fast filtering) |
137: | `shirtColor` | TEXT NULL | e.g. `Orange`, `Blue`, `Purple`, `Grey` |
138: | `ackStatus` | TEXT NULL | `'confirmed'`, `'declined'`, or null (pending) — set by instructor |
139: | `acknowledgedAt` | TEXT NULL | When the instructor acknowledged |
140: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | DATETIME | |
141: 
142: ### `EventSkill`
143: Many-to-many join between events and skill names.
144: 
145: | Column | Type |
146: |---|---|
147: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) PK |
148: | `eventId` | TEXT FK → Event |
149: | `skillName` | TEXT |
150: 
151: ### `OptIn`
152: An instructor's interest/availability declaration on an event (not a date — the whole event).
153: 
154: | Column | Type | Notes |
155: |---|---|---|
156: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
157: | `userId` | TEXT FK → User | The instructor who opted in |
158: | `eventId` | TEXT FK → Event | |
159: | `status` | TEXT | `'interested'`, `'available'`, `'unavailable'` |
160: | `note` | TEXT NULL | |
161: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | DATETIME | |
162: 
163: ### `Skill`
164: Reusable skill catalog. Define once, reuse across events and profiles.
165: 
166: | Column | Type | Notes |
167: |---|---|---|
168: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
169: | `name` | TEXT UNIQUE | e.g. `Robotics`, `Python`, `Aerial Robotics` |
170: | `createdAt` | TEXT | |
171: 
172: Deleting a skill from the catalog does NOT cascade — existing `Profile.skills` (text) and `EventSkill.skillName` rows keep their values.
173: 
174: ### `EquipmentCatalog`
175: Reusable equipment catalog (optional — admins can also type equipment names directly per event).
176: 
177: | Column | Type | Notes |
178: |---|---|---|
179: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
180: | `name` | TEXT UNIQUE | e.g. `Drone (Tello EDU)` |
181: | `description` | TEXT NULL | |
182: | `createdAt` | TEXT | |
183: 
184: ### `EventEquipment`
185: Equipment needed for a specific event. Created by admin in the event detail drawer.
186: 
187: | Column | Type | Notes |
188: |---|---|---|
189: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
190: | `eventId` | TEXT FK → Event | CASCADE on delete |
191: | `name` | TEXT | e.g. `Drones`, `Laptops`, `Charger kit` |
192: | `quantity` | INTEGER | How many are needed |
193: | `notes` | TEXT NULL | |
194: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | TEXT | |
195: 
196: ### `EquipmentClaim`
197: An instructor's claim to bring part or all of an equipment item. Has a unique index on `(equipmentItemId, profileId)` — one claim per instructor per item.
198: 
199: | Column | Type | Notes |
200: |---|---|---|
201: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
202: | `equipmentItemId` | TEXT FK → EventEquipment | CASCADE on delete |
203: | `profileId` | TEXT FK → Profile | The instructor bringing it |
204: | `quantityClaimed` | INTEGER | How many they'll bring |
205: | `transportOffered` | INTEGER | 1 = can transport, 0 = needs dropoff |
206: | `notes` | TEXT NULL | e.g. "I'll pick them up from the office" |
207: | `createdAt`, `updatedAt` | TEXT | |
208: 
209: ### `Notification`
210: In-app notification bell entries. Created by `notifyUser()` in `email.ts`.
211: 
212: | Column | Type | Notes |
213: |---|---|---|
214: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
215: | `userId` | TEXT FK → User | CASCADE on delete |
216: | `type` | TEXT | `assignment_created`, `assignment_removed`, `opt_in_received`, `event_changed`, etc. |
217: | `title` | TEXT | Short headline |
218: | `body` | TEXT NULL | Longer description |
219: | `eventId` | TEXT NULL | Related event (makes notification clickable) |
220: | `assignmentId` | TEXT NULL | Related assignment |
221: | `readAt` | TEXT NULL | Null = unread |
222: | `createdAt` | TEXT | |
223: 
224: ### `EmailQueue`
225: Pending digest emails. Rows are created by `notifyUser()` with `urgency = 'digest'` or `'instant'`. Instant emails are sent immediately and marked `sentAt`; digest emails are sent in the 8am digest or when admin clicks "Send now".
226: 
227: | Column | Type | Notes |
228: |---|---|---|
229: | `id` | TEXT (UUID) | PK |
230: | `userId` | TEXT FK → User | CASCADE on delete |
231: | `type` | TEXT | Same as Notification.type |
232: | `subject` | TEXT | Email subject line |
233: | `body` | TEXT | HTML email body |
234: | `eventId` | TEXT NULL | |
235: | `urgency` | TEXT | `'instant'` or `'digest'` |
236: | `sentAt` | TEXT NULL | Null = pending; non-null = sent |
237: | `createdAt` | TEXT | |
238: 
239: ---
240: 
241: ## Authentication Flow
242: 
243: ### Invite + claim flow
244: ```
245: 1. Admin creates an invite in the Invites tab
246:    → POST /api/invites creates a User row with role='instructor', inviteToken=UUID,
247:      claimedAt=null, profileId=<selected profile>
248:    → Admin sends the invite link: https://ra-syncbot.com/?token=<inviteToken>
249: 
250: 2. Instructor opens the link
251:    → Client reads ?token= from URL
252:    → POST /api/auth/claim with { token, name, email, password }
253:    → Server validates token + email uniqueness
254:    → Server generates 6-digit code, stores in memory (10-min expiry)
255:    → Server emails code via Resend
256:    → Server returns { step: 'verify' }
257: 
258: 3. Instructor enters the 6-digit code
259:    → POST /api/auth/claim with { token, name, email, password, verifyCode }
260:    → Server validates code
261:    → Server hashes password with bcrypt
262:    → Server UPDATEs User: claimedAt=now, passwordHash=hash, email=email, name=name
263:    → Server emails welcome message
264:    → Server sets signed session cookie
265:    → Server returns { user: {...} }
266: 
267: 4. Subsequent requests
268:    → Browser sends cookie `ra-session=userId.hmac`
269:    → Server reads cookie, verifies HMAC, looks up User
270:    → If !claimedAt → 401
271: ```
272: 
273: ### Login flow (already-claimed instructors)
274: ```
275: 1. POST /api/auth/me with { email, password }
276: 2. Server looks up User by email
277: 3. Server compares bcrypt hash
278: 4. If match → set signed cookie, return { user: {...} }
279: 5. If no match → 401 { error: 'Invalid email or password' }
280: ```
281: 
282: ### Security properties
283: - Passwords are bcrypt-hashed (10 rounds) — never stored in plaintext.
284: - Session cookies are HMAC-signed with `SESSION_PASSWORD` (Web Crypto API).
285: - Cookies are `httpOnly`, `sameSite=lax`, `secure` in production.
286: - The HMAC secret must be ≥32 characters; rotate by changing `SESSION_PASSWORD` (invalidates all sessions).
287: - All admin routes call `requireAdmin(req)` which returns 401/403 early.
288: - The `/api/seed` endpoint is **disabled in production** (returns 403) to prevent accidental data wipes.
289: 
290: ---
291: 
292: ## Drag-and-Drop Design
293: 
294: ### Desktop
295: - `@dnd-kit/core` with `PointerSensor` (8px activation distance).
296: - The `RosterRail` renders each instructor as a `DraggableInstructor`.
297: - Each `DroppableEventCard` registers a per-day drop target (`drop-${eventId}-${date}`).
298: - Multi-day events expose a second "all days" target on the first day of the current week.
299: - `DragOverlay` renders a rotated preview of the dragged instructor card.
300: - On drop, `POST /api/assignments` creates the assignment after server-side conflict validation.
301: 
302: ### Mobile
303: - `useIsMobile()` returns `true` when viewport width < 768px.
304: - On mobile, `PointerSensor` activation distance is set to 9999 (effectively disabled).
305: - Instead, tapping an instructor in the roster selects them (visual highlight + floating bottom bar).
306: - Tapping an event card calls the same `POST /api/assignments` mutation.
307: - This avoids the broken mobile drag-drop experience that plagued earlier versions.
308: 
309: ---
310: 
311: ## Conflict Detection
312: 
313: Conflicts are computed by pure functions in `src/lib/conflicts.ts`. They run in two places:
314: 
315: 1. **Client-side** (instant feedback) — before dropping, the UI calls the functions and shows a toast warning if any conflict is detected.
316: 2. **Server-side** (validation) — the `POST /api/assignments` route re-runs the checks and returns 409 with details if any hard conflict exists.
317: 
318: ### Conflict types
319: | Conflict | Behavior |
320: |---|---|
321: | Double-booking | **Blocked** — instructor already assigned to another event on the same date |
322: | Unavailable date | **Blocked** — instructor marked the date as unavailable |
323: | Temporal overlap | **Blocked** — instructor's events on the same date have overlapping times |
324: | Fatigue (3+ consecutive days) | **Warning** — allowed but flagged in the Conflicts tab |
325: | Skill gap | **Informational** — instructor lacks a required skill; admin can still assign |
326: 
327: Soft conflicts (fatigue, skill gaps) are surfaced in the `ConflictSummaryTab` and as inline warnings on the calendar.
328: 
329: ---
330: 
331: ## Email + Notification System
332: 
333: All email is sent via Resend's REST API (`fetch()`, no SDK). The `sendEmail()` helper in `src/lib/email.ts` silently no-ops if `RESEND_API_KEY` is unset, so dev environments without email still work. All user-supplied values are HTML-escaped via `escapeHtml()` before interpolation into email bodies.
334: 
335: ### Smart digest system
336: 
337: Notifications have two urgency levels:
338: 
339: | Urgency | When | Behavior |
340: |---|---|---|
341: | `instant` | Event is within 72 hours, OR opt-in receipt, OR verification code | Email sent immediately + in-app notification created |
342: | `digest` | Event is >72 hours away | In-app notification created immediately; email queued for 8am AST digest |
343: 
344: This prevents email spam when the admin iterates on assignments during planning sessions. The admin can flush the digest queue at any time via the "Send now" button (paper airplane icon in the top bar) — `POST /api/notifications/send-now`.
345: 
346: ### Per-user email toggle
347: 
348: Each user has `emailNotifications` (default 1 = on). Instructors can toggle this via the mail icon in their top bar. When off:
349: - ✅ In-app bell notifications still work (always on)
350: - ❌ No emails sent (digest queue rows are still created but `sendDigests`/`sendAllPending` skip users with the toggle off)
351: - ✅ Verification codes + welcome emails bypass the toggle (transactional)
352: 
353: ### Notification bell
354: 
355: Both admins and instructors see a bell icon in the top bar. The `NotificationBell` component polls `/api/notifications` every 30 seconds. Unread count shows as a red badge. Click a notification to mark it read; "Mark all read" button clears all.
356: 
357: ### Triggered notifications
358: | Event | Recipient | Urgency | Type |
359: |---|---|---|---|
360: | Assignment created | Instructor | instant (if <72h) / digest (if >72h) | `assignment_created` |
361: | Assignment removed | Instructor | instant (if <72h) / digest (if >72h) | `assignment_removed` |
362: | Opt-in received | All admins | instant | `opt_in_received` |
363: | Daily reminder (cron) | Each instructor with assignment in 2 days | instant (direct send, not queued) | `reminder` |
364: | Verification code (claim flow) | Claiming instructor | instant (bypasses toggle) | n/a (direct send) |
365: | Welcome (post-claim) | New instructor | instant (bypasses toggle) | n/a (direct send) |
366: 
367: ### Vercel Cron
368: Two endpoints are intended to be hit by Vercel Cron:
369: - `POST /api/reminders` — sends 2-day reminders AND flushes the daily digest
370: - `POST /api/auto-archive` — moves past events to `Archived` status
371: 
372: Configure these in `vercel.json` (not currently set — add when going to production).
373: 
374: ---
375: 
376: ## Equipment + Skill Catalog
377: 
378: ### Skill catalog
379: - `Skill` table stores reusable skill names (define once, reuse everywhere)
380: - `SkillPicker` component replaces free-text inputs in Events + Team tabs
381: - Admins can manage the catalog (add/delete) from inside the picker via the "Manage catalog" link
382: - Deleting a skill does NOT cascade — existing `Profile.skills` (text) and `EventSkill.skillName` rows keep their values
383: 
384: ### Equipment coordination
385: - Admin adds equipment items per event via the `EquipmentSection` in the event detail drawer (admin mode)
386: - Each item has: name, quantity needed, optional notes
387: - Instructors claim items they'll bring: "I'll bring" button with quantity + "I can transport" checkbox
388: - Server-side validation: can't claim more than available (needed minus other instructors' claims)
389: - Unique index on `(equipmentItemId, profileId)` prevents duplicate claims
390: - Admin sees claims with truck icon (transport offered) per item
391: - The instructor event drawer shows the equipment section only if the instructor is assigned to the event
392: - Release a claim with the X button
393: 
394: ### Acknowledgment system
395: - Instructors see ✓ (confirm) / ✗ (decline) buttons on each assignment in the My Assignments tab
396: - `PATCH /api/assignments?id=<id>` with `{ ackStatus: 'confirmed' | 'declined' }` — instructors can only ack their own assignments
397: - Admin sees per-assignment ack status (✓ or ✗ declined) in the EventDetailDrawer
398: - Admin sees a summary: "X confirmed, Y declined, Z pending"
399: - Confirmed assignments get a green border; declined get a red border
400: 
401: ---
402: 
403: ## Deployment Topology
404: 
405: ```
406: ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
407: │  Vercel (Next.js, free tier)                             │
408: │  ├── Static assets served from CDN                       │
409: │  ├── API routes run as serverless functions (30s limit)  │
410: │  └── Custom domain: ra-syncbot.com                       │
411: └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
412:               │                          │
413:               ▼                          ▼
414:    ┌──────────────────┐       ┌──────────────────┐
415:    │  Turso (free)    │       │  Resend (free)   │
416:    │  Single DB       │       │  100 emails/day  │
417:    │  libSQL protocol │       │  REST API        │
418:    └──────────────────┘       └──────────────────┘
419: ```
420: 
421: ### Environment variables (production)
422: | Variable | Purpose |
423: |---|---|
424: | `TURSO_URL` | libsql:// connection string |
425: | `TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN` | Turso auth token |
426: | `SESSION_PASSWORD` | ≥32-char secret for HMAC cookie signing |
427: | `RESEND_API_KEY` | Resend API key (optional — skips email if unset) |
428: | `FROM_EMAIL` | Sender address (must be a verified Resend domain) |
429: | `ADMIN_EMAIL` | Receives opt-in notifications |
430: 
431: See [DEPLOYMENT.md](./DEPLOYMENT.md) for the full step-by-step setup.
432: 
433: ---
434: 
435: ## Known Constraints
436: 
437: - **30-second function timeout** on Vercel free tier. Long reports or bulk operations must stay under this.
438: - **Turso free tier** allows 9 GB storage and 1 billion row reads/month — far beyond what RA Syncbot needs.
439: - **Resend free tier** is 100 emails/day, 3,000/month. Daily reminders + assignment notifications should stay well under this for ~20 instructors.
440: - **In-memory verification codes** — the claim-flow verification codes are stored in a `Map` in the API route module. This resets on every cold start. For a more robust system, move these to a `VerificationCode` table with expiry.
441: - **No offline mode** — the app requires network to load schedule data. PWA installability is for the home-screen icon, not offline use.
442: 
443: ---
444: 
445: ## Design Decisions
446: 
447: ### Why raw SQL instead of an ORM?
448: Prisma's libSQL driver adapter had runtime issues on Vercel during initial development (mismatched binary deps, cold-start crashes). Raw SQL via `@libsql/client` is simpler, has zero cold-start overhead, and the queries are all straightforward CRUD. The trade-off is no type-safe schema — we compensate with the shared types in `scheduler-types.ts`.
449: 
450: ### Why HMAC cookies instead of JWT?
451: JWTs encode claims client-side, which means we'd need to handle expiry, refresh, and revocation. HMAC cookies are opaque to the client; the server looks up the user on every request. Simpler, safer for this use case, and the lookup cost is negligible against Turso's edge replicas.
452: 
453: ### Why Web Crypto instead of Node's `crypto`?
454: Node's `crypto` module (`createHmac`) leaked into the client bundle during initial development and caused a TDZ crash on desktop (`Cannot access 'g' before initialization`). Web Crypto (`crypto.subtle`) is isomorphic — it works in both Node 18+ and the browser — and never leaks into client bundles because it's only ever called from `server-only` modules.
455: 
456: ### Why `useState + useEffect` instead of `useSyncExternalStore`?
457: `useSyncExternalStore` was used to read the invite token from the URL without hydration mismatch. It triggered the same TDZ crash as `crypto` — likely a React 19 + Turbopack interaction. We reverted to `useState` initialized to `null` plus a `useEffect` that reads `window.location.search`. This causes one extra render but is rock-solid.

================
File: src/lib/export-utils.ts
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import {
  4:   hostColor,
  5:   formatTime,
  6:   formatPrettyDate,
  7:   formatShortDate,
  8:   eventOnDate,
  9:   addDaysISO,
 10:   SHIRT_COLOR_SWATCH,
 11:   type EventView,
 12:   type AssignmentView,
 13: } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
 14: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
 15: 
 16: type Props = {
 17:   weekStartISO: string
 18:   events: EventView[]
 19:   assignments: AssignmentView[]
 20: }
 21: 
 22: function weekDates(weekStartISO: string): string[] {
 23:   return Array.from({ length: 7 }, (_, i) => addDaysISO(weekStartISO, i))
 24: }
 25: 
 26: // Generate CSV string from the week's schedule
 27: export function generateCSV(weekStartISO: string, events: EventView[], assignments: AssignmentView[]): string {
 28:   const dates = weekDates(weekStartISO)
 29:   const rows: string[][] = []
 30: 
 31:   // Header row
 32:   rows.push(['Date', 'Day', 'Event', 'Host', 'Code', 'Start Time', 'End Time', 'Location', 'Status', 'Participants', 'Needed/Day', 'Assigned Today', 'Instructor', 'Role', 'Shirt', 'Type'])
 33: 
 34:   for (const dateISO of dates) {
 35:     const dayEvents = events.filter(e => eventOnDate(e, dateISO))
 36:     if (dayEvents.length === 0) {
 37:       const d = new Date(`${dateISO}T00:00:00.000Z`)
 38:       const dayName = d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'long', timeZone: 'UTC' })
 39:       rows.push([dateISO, dayName, '— No events —', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', ''])
 40:       continue
 41:     }
 42: 
 43:     for (const ev of dayEvents) {
 44:       const evAssignments = assignments.filter(a => a.eventId === ev.id && a.date === dateISO)
 45:       const primaries = evAssignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative)
 46:       const alts = evAssignments.filter(a => a.isAlternative)
 47:       const all = [...primaries, ...alts]
 48: 
 49:       const d = new Date(`${dateISO}T00:00:00.000Z`)
 50:       const dayName = d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'long', timeZone: 'UTC' })
 51: 
 52:       if (all.length === 0) {
 53:         rows.push([
 54:           dateISO, dayName, ev.name, ev.host, ev.code ?? '', ev.startTime, ev.endTime,
 55:           ev.location ?? '', ev.status, String(ev.participantCount ?? ''), String(ev.requiredInstructors), '0',
 56:           '— Unfilled —', '', '', '',
 57:         ])
 58:       } else {
 59:         for (const a of all) {
 60:           rows.push([
 61:             dateISO, dayName, ev.name, ev.host, ev.code ?? '', ev.startTime, ev.endTime,
 62:             ev.location ?? '', ev.status, String(ev.participantCount ?? ''), String(ev.requiredInstructors), String(primaries.length),
 63:             a.profileName, a.profileRoleTier, a.shirtColor ?? '',
 64:             a.isAlternative ? 'Alternative' : 'Primary',
 65:           ])
 66:         }
 67:       }
 68:     }
 69:   }
 70: 
 71:   // Convert to CSV with proper escaping
 72:   return rows.map(row =>
 73:     row.map(cell => {
 74:       const s = String(cell ?? '')
 75:       if (s.includes(',') || s.includes('"') || s.includes('\n')) {
 76:         return `"${s.replace(/"/g, '""')}"`
 77:       }
 78:       return s
 79:     }).join(',')
 80:   ).join('\n')
 81: }
 82: 
 83: // Download a string as a file
 84: export function downloadFile(filename: string, content: string, mimeType: string) {
 85:   const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mimeType })
 86:   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
 87:   const a = document.createElement('a')
 88:   a.href = url
 89:   a.download = filename
 90:   document.body.appendChild(a)
 91:   a.click()
 92:   document.body.removeChild(a)
 93:   URL.revokeObjectURL(url)
 94: }
 95: 
 96: // Export CSV
 97: export function exportCSV(weekStartISO: string, events: EventView[], assignments: AssignmentView[]) {
 98:   const csv = generateCSV(weekStartISO, events, assignments)
 99:   const dates = weekDates(weekStartISO)
100:   const filename = `robot-adventure-schedule-${dates[0]}-to-${dates[6]}.csv`
101:   downloadFile(filename, csv, 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;')
102: }

 2: # RA Syncbot — Environment Variables

 4: # Copy this file to .env and fill in your values.
 5: # Never commit .env to git!
 6: 
 7: # ── Database (REQUIRED for production) ────────────────────────────────────
 8: # Turso cloud database (libSQL). Get these from:
 9: #   turso db show your-db-name --url
10: #   turso db tokens create your-db-name
11: 
12: TURSO_URL=libsql://your-db-name.turso.io
13: TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN=your-turso-auth-token-here
14: 
15: # ── Database (OPTIONAL — local development fallback) ─────────────────────
16: # If TURSO_URL is not set, the app falls back to this local SQLite file.
17: # Only used in development.
18: 
19: DATABASE_URL=file:./db/custom.db
20: 
21: # ── Session (REQUIRED for production) ─────────────────────────────────────
22: # Used to HMAC-sign auth cookies via the Web Crypto API.
23: # Must be at least 32 characters. Generate one with:
24: #   openssl rand -hex 32
25: 
26: SESSION_PASSWORD=changeme-this-must-be-at-least-32-characters-long!!
27: 
28: # ── Email notifications (OPTIONAL — skip if not using) ───────────────────
29: # Get these from https://resend.com (free tier: 100 emails/day, 3000/month)
30: # If RESEND_API_KEY is not set, email notifications are silently skipped
31: # and the account-claim flow skips email verification (dev mode).
32: 
33: RESEND_API_KEY=re_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx
34: FROM_EMAIL=onboarding@resend.dev
35: 
36: # ── Admin notifications (OPTIONAL) ───────────────────────────────────────
37: # Receives an email when an instructor opts in to an event.
38: # If not set, opt-in notifications are skipped.
39: 
40: ADMIN_EMAIL=admin@yourdomain.com

================
File: CONTRIBUTING.md
================
  1: # Contributing
  2: 
  3: Thanks for working on RA Syncbot. This document covers local setup, code style, and the PR process.
  4: 
  5: ---
  6: 
  7: ## Local Development
  8: 
  9: ### Prerequisites
 10: - [Bun](https://bun.sh) 1.0+ (preferred) or Node.js 18+
 11: - A Turso account (free) — or use the local SQLite fallback
 12: 
 13: ### First-time setup
 14: 
 15: ```bash
 16: # 1. Clone
 17: git clone https://github.com/FamineDT246/RASchedule.git
 18: cd RASchedule
 19: 
 20: # 2. Install deps
 21: bun install
 22: 
 23: # 3. Configure env
 24: cp .env.example .env
 25: # Edit .env — at minimum set SESSION_PASSWORD (32+ chars)
 26: #   openssl rand -hex 32
 27: 
 28: # 4. (Optional) Seed the DB with demo data
 29: bun run seed
 30: 
 31: # 4b. (Existing deployments only) Run migrations to add new tables/columns
 32: bun run migrate
 33: 
 34: # 5. Start dev server
 35: bun run dev
 36: ```
 37: 
 38: Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000).
 39: 
 40: **Without Turso configured**, the app falls back to `file:./db/custom.db` (local SQLite). The seed script creates this file automatically.
 41: 
 42: ---
 43: 
 44: ## Project Layout
 45: 
 46: See [ARCHITECTURE.md](./ARCHITECTURE.md) for the full breakdown. Key directories:
 47: 
 48: ```
 49: src/
 50: ├── app/
 51: │   ├── api/             # Route handlers — one folder per resource
 52: │   ├── page.tsx         # Main app shell (auth gate, tabs, DnD)
 53: │   └── providers.tsx    # TanStack Query + theme + Sonner
 54: ├── components/
 55: │   ├── scheduler/       # App-specific components
 56: │   └── ui/              # Pruned shadcn/ui (10 components only)
 57: ├── hooks/
 58: │   └── use-is-mobile.ts
 59: └── lib/
 60:     ├── auth-helpers.ts  # requireAdmin / getAuthUser
 61:     ├── conflicts.ts     # Pure conflict-detection functions
 62:     ├── db.ts            # Turso client
 63:     ├── email.ts         # Resend wrapper
 64:     ├── scheduler-types.ts  # Shared types + date helpers
 65:     └── session.ts       # HMAC cookies (server-only)
 66: ```
 67: 
 68: ---
 69: 
 70: ## Code Style
 71: 
 72: ### TypeScript
 73: - **Strict mode** is on — no implicit `any`, no unchecked index access.
 74: - All shared types live in `src/lib/scheduler-types.ts`. Don't duplicate types inline.
 75: - Use `type` for unions and intersections; use `interface` only when you need declaration merging.
 76: - Prefer `unknown` over `any` for unknown API payloads; narrow with type guards.
 77: 
 78: ### React
 79: - **Function components only.** No class components.
 80: - **Hooks rule:** never call hooks conditionally. The scheduler sensors are always created (even on mobile) — we just set an impossible activation distance to disable them.
 81: - **No `useSyncExternalStore`** — it caused a TDZ crash in this project. Use `useState + useEffect` for client-only state.
 82: - **TanStack Query** for all server state. Don't use `useEffect` for data fetching.
 83: - Keep components under ~400 lines. Split larger components into sub-components in the same file.
 84: 
 85: ### Styling
 86: - **Tailwind CSS 4** — utility classes inline. No CSS modules.
 87: - Use the `cn()` helper from `src/lib/utils.ts` for conditional classes.
 88: - **WCAG 2.1 AA** is enforced:
 89:   - 16px base text, 12px absolute floor (enforced in `globals.css`)
 90:   - 44px minimum touch targets on mobile (enforced in `globals.css` `@media (pointer: coarse)`)
 91:   - All interactive elements must have an `aria-label` if their text content is ambiguous
 92: - Dark mode is via `next-themes` — use Tailwind's `dark:` variant, never hardcode colors.
 93: 
 94: ### API routes
 95: - Every route starts with `getAuthUser(req)` or `requireAdmin(req)`.
 96: - Validate the request body before touching the DB. Return `400` with a clear error message.
 97: - Run server-side conflict checks (don't trust the client) for assignment mutations.
 98: - Return `200` with the updated entity, not a generic `{ ok: true }`. The client uses the response to update the cache.
 99: - Use `crypto.randomUUID()` for IDs — never `Date.now()` or counter-based IDs.
100: 
101: ### SQL
102: - Raw SQL via `db.execute({ sql, args })`. **Always use `?` placeholders** — never string-interpolate user input.
103: - Column names are camelCase (matches the JS object shape). Table names are PascalCase.
104: - For complex queries, write the SQL as a template literal with the placeholders on separate lines for readability.
105: 
106: ### File naming
107: - Components: `PascalCase.tsx` (e.g. `EventDetailDrawer.tsx`)
108: - Hooks: `kebab-case.ts` (e.g. `use-is-mobile.ts`)
109: - Lib files: `kebab-case.ts` (e.g. `auth-helpers.ts`)
110: - API routes: `route.ts` inside a folder named after the resource
111: 
112: ---
113: 
114: ## Commit Conventions
115: 
116: Use [Conventional Commits](https://www.conventionalcommits.org/):
117: 
118: ```
119: <type>(<scope>): <subject>
120: 
121: <body — optional>
122: ```
123: 
124: Types: `feat`, `fix`, `docs`, `style`, `refactor`, `test`, `chore`.
125: 
126: Examples:
127: ```
128: feat(scheduler): add multi-day drop handle
129: fix(auth): prevent session cookie from leaking to client bundle
130: docs(api): document /api/opt-ins response shape
131: chore(deps): remove unused Radix packages
132: ```
133: 
134: ---
135: 
136: ## Pull Request Process
137: 
138: 1. **Branch** from `main`: `feat/<short-description>` or `fix/<short-description>`.
139: 2. **Commit** logically — one feature/fix per commit. Squash WIP commits before opening the PR.
140: 3. **Test locally:**
141:    ```bash
142:    bun run lint   # must pass with no errors
143:    bun run build  # must succeed
144:    ```
145: 4. **Open the PR** against `main`. Describe:
146:    - What changed and why
147:    - How to test it
148:    - Screenshots (if UI changes)
149: 5. **Review** — address feedback by pushing new commits (don't force-push during review).
150: 6. **Squash-merge** on approval.
151: 
152: ---
153: 
154: ## Testing
155: 
156: There's no automated test suite yet. Manual test checklist before merging:
157: 
158: - [ ] `bun run lint` passes
159: - [ ] `bun run build` succeeds
160: - [ ] Dev server starts without console errors
161: - [ ] Login works (admin + instructor)
162: - [ ] Drag-and-drop works on desktop (Chrome + Firefox)
163: - [ ] Tap-to-assign works on mobile (iOS Safari + Android Chrome)
164: - [ ] Esc closes drawers, modals, and tap selections
165: - [ ] Light/dark mode toggle works
166: - [ ] No `Cannot access 'g' before initialization` errors in console
167: 
168: ---
169: 
170: ## Known Pitfalls
171: 
172: ### Don't import `session.ts` from client code
173: `session.ts` is marked `server-only` and uses `crypto.subtle`. If you accidentally import it from a client component, the build will fail (good) or — worse — leak into the client bundle and cause a TDZ crash at runtime.
174: 
175: ### Don't use `useSyncExternalStore`
176: This caused a desktop-only crash that took a full session to diagnose. Use `useState + useEffect` instead, even at the cost of an extra render.
177: 
178: ### Don't run `bun run seed` against production
179: The seed script wipes all data. It's safe for local dev and for the initial Turso setup, but never run it against a DB with real data. The `/api/seed` endpoint is disabled in production (returns 403) as a safety net.
180: 
181: ### Don't add shadcn/ui components back without checking usage
182: The `src/components/ui/` directory was pruned from 40+ components down to 10. Each remaining component is actually used. If you need a new component, add it manually (don't run `npx shadcn add` — it pulls in deps we removed).
183: 
184: ### Don't change the auth cookie scheme without testing
185: The HMAC-signed cookie approach replaced iron-session (which had Vercel build issues) and a Node `crypto` version (which caused the desktop crash). Any change to `session.ts` needs testing on both desktop and mobile, in both light and dark mode.
186: 
187: ### Always run `bun run migrate` after pulling
188: If a PR adds new tables or columns, the migration script (`scripts/migrate.ts`) must be run against your local DB and the production Turso DB. The script is idempotent — safe to run multiple times. If you add a new table or column, add the migration to this script (don't rely on on-demand `CREATE TABLE` in API routes alone — that's a fallback, not the primary path).
189: 
190: ### Escape HTML in email templates
191: The `escapeHtml()` helper in `src/lib/email.ts` must be applied to every user-supplied value interpolated into HTML email bodies. Event names, user names, shirt colors — all can contain `<`, `>`, `&` characters that break email HTML or carry injection payloads. Never interpolate raw user input into email HTML.
192: 
193: ---
194: 
195: ## Getting Help
196: 
197: - Read [ARCHITECTURE.md](./ARCHITECTURE.md) for system design questions
198: - Read [API.md](./API.md) for endpoint specifics
199: - Read [DEPLOYMENT.md](./DEPLOYMENT.md) for infra setup
200: - Check `git log` for context on past decisions — commit messages explain why things were done

================
File: src/app/api/auth/change-password/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs'
 4: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 5: 
 6: // POST /api/auth/change-password
 7: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 8:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 9:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
10: 
11:   const body = await req.json()
12:   const { currentPassword, newPassword } = body as { currentPassword: string; newPassword: string }
13:   if (!currentPassword || !newPassword) {
14:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Current and new passwords are required' }, { status: 400 })
15:   }
16:   if (newPassword.length < 6) {
17:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'New password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })
18:   }
19: 
20:   if (!user.passwordHash) {
21:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No password set on account' }, { status: 400 })
22:   }
23: 
24:   const valid = await bcrypt.compare(currentPassword, user.passwordHash)
25:   if (!valid) {
26:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Current password is incorrect' }, { status: 401 })
27:   }
28: 
29:   const newHash = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 10)
30:   await db.execute({ sql: 'UPDATE User SET passwordHash = ? WHERE id = ?', args: [newHash, user.id] })
31: 
32:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
33: }

================
File: src/app/api/profiles/me/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: 
 5: function parseList(s: string | null | undefined): string[] {
 6:   if (!s) return []
 7:   return s.split(',').map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean)
 8: }
 9: 
10: // GET /api/profiles/me — returns the current user's linked profile
11: export async function GET(req: Request) {
12:   const user = await getAuthUser(req as any)
13:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
14:   if (!user.profileId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No profile linked' }, { status: 404 })
15: 
16:   const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Profile WHERE id = ?', args: [user.profileId] })
17:   if (result.rows.length === 0) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Profile not found' }, { status: 404 })
18: 
19:   const p = result.rows[0] as any
20:   return NextResponse.json({
21:     ...p,
22:     skillsList: parseList(p.skills),
23:     unavailableList: parseList(p.unavailable),
24:   })
25: }

File: src/app/providers.tsx
================
 1: 'use client'
 2: 
 3: import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
 4: import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query'
 5: import { ThemeProvider } from 'next-themes'
 6: import { Toaster as SonnerToaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner'
 7: 
 8: export function Providers({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
 9:   const [client] = useState(
10:     () =>
11:       new QueryClient({
12:         defaultOptions: {
13:           queries: {
14:             staleTime: 30_000,
15:             refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
16:             retry: 1,
17:           },
18:         },
19:       }),
20:   )
21: 
22:   // Register the service worker (required for PWA installability on Android)
23:   useEffect(() => {
24:     if (typeof window === 'undefined') return
25:     if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator)) return
26:     if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') return // skip in dev to avoid cache headaches
27: 
28:     navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js').catch((err) => {
29:       console.warn('[sw] registration failed:', err.message)
30:     })
31:   }, [])
32: 
33:   return (
34:     <ThemeProvider attribute="class" defaultTheme="dark" enableSystem={true} disableTransitionOnChange>
35:       <QueryClientProvider client={client}>
36:         {children}
37:         <SonnerToaster position="top-right" richColors closeButton />
38:       </QueryClientProvider>
39:     </ThemeProvider>
40:   )
41: }

 28: function weekDates(weekStartISO: string): string[] {
 29:   return Array.from({ length: 7 }, (_, i) => addDaysISO(weekStartISO, i))
 30: }
 31: 
 32: export function PrintLayout({ weekStartISO, events, assignments }: Props) {
 33:   const dates = weekDates(weekStartISO)
 34:   const todayISO = todayInBarbados()
 35: 
 36:   // Build per-day event+assignment data
 37:   const dayData = dates.map(dateISO => {
 38:     const dayEvents = events
 39:       .filter(e => eventOnDate(e, dateISO))
 40:       .map(ev => {
 41:         const evAssignments = assignments.filter(a => a.eventId === ev.id && a.date === dateISO)
 42:         const primaries = evAssignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative)
 43:         const alts = evAssignments.filter(a => a.isAlternative)
 44:         return { event: ev, primaries, alts }
 45:       })
 46:     return { dateISO, dayEvents }
 47:   })
 48: 
 49:   return (
 50:     <div className="print-layout p-8 bg-white text-black min-h-screen" id="print-root">

 56:             <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">
 57:               Week of {formatShortDate(dates[0])} – {formatShortDate(dates[6])}
 58:             </p>
 59:           </div>
 60:           <div className="text-right text-xs text-gray-500">
 61:             <p>Generated {new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'long', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' })}</p>
 62:             <p>Barbados time (AST)</p>
 63:           </div>
 64:         </div>
 65:       </div>
 66: 
 67:       {/* Summary stats */}
 68:       <div className="mb-6 grid grid-cols-4 gap-3 text-xs">
 69:         {(() => {
 70:           let totalSlots = 0, filledSlots = 0, eventsCount = 0
 71:           for (const { dayEvents } of dayData) {
 72:             for (const { event, primaries } of dayEvents) {
 73:               totalSlots += event.requiredInstructors
 74:               filledSlots += Math.min(primaries.length, event.requiredInstructors)
 75:               eventsCount++
 76:             }
 77:           }
 78:           return (
 79:             <>
 80:               <StatBox label="Events this week" value={eventsCount} />
 81:               <StatBox label="Instructor slots" value={totalSlots} />
 82:               <StatBox label="Filled" value={filledSlots} />
 83:               <StatBox label="Unfilled" value={totalSlots - filledSlots} highlight={totalSlots - filledSlots > 0} />
 84:             </>
 85:           )
 86:         })()}
 87:       </div>
 88: 
 89:       {/* Day-by-day schedule */}
 90:       <div className="space-y-4">
 91:         {dayData.map(({ dateISO, dayEvents }, idx) => {
 92:           const isToday = dateISO === todayISO
 93:           return (
 94:             <div key={dateISO} className={cn('break-inside-avoid', isToday && 'border-l-4 border-emerald-500 pl-3')}>

105:               </div>

222: function StatBox({ label, value, highlight }: { label: string; value: number; highlight?: boolean }) {

File: src/components/scheduler/RosterRail.tsx

  1: 'use client'

 13:   onToggleCollapsed: () => void
 14:   // Mobile tap-to-assign: when set, tapping an instructor selects them instead of dragging
 15:   tapSelectMode?: boolean
 16:   selectedProfileId?: string | null
 17:   onTapProfile?: (profileId: string) => void

 22: export function RosterRail({ profiles, collapsed, onToggleCollapsed, tapSelectMode, selectedProfileId, onTapProfile }: Props) {
 23:   const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
 24:   const [activeTiers, setActiveTiers] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
 25:   const [activeSkills, setActiveSkills] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
 26: 
 27:   const allSkills = useMemo(() => {
 28:     const s = new Set<string>()
 29:     profiles.forEach(p => p.skillsList.forEach(x => s.add(x)))
 30:     return Array.from(s).sort()
 31:   }, [profiles])
 32: 
 33:   const filtered = useMemo(() => {
 34:     return profiles.filter(p => {
 35:       if (query && !p.name.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())) return false
 36:       if (activeTiers.size && !activeTiers.has(p.roleTier)) return false
 37:       if (activeSkills.size && !p.skillsList.some(s => activeSkills.has(s))) return false
 38:       return true
 39:     })
 40:   }, [profiles, query, activeTiers, activeSkills])
 41: 
 42:   if (collapsed) {
 43:     return (
 44:       <aside
 45:         className="w-12 shrink-0 border-r border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex flex-col items-center py-3 gap-2"
 46:         aria-label="Roster (collapsed)"
 47:       >
 48:         <button
 49:           onClick={onToggleCollapsed}
 50:           className="p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
 51:           title="Expand roster"
 52:           aria-label="Expand roster"
 53:         >
 54:           <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
 55:         </button>
 56:         <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground -rotate-90 mt-4 whitespace-nowrap">
 57:           {filtered.length} staff
 58:         </div>
 59:       </aside>
 60:     )
 61:   }
 62: 
 63:   return (
 64:     <aside
 65:       className="w-64 sm:w-72 shrink-0 border-r border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex flex-col"
 66:       aria-label="Instructor roster"
 67:     >
 68:       <div className="p-3 border-b border-border/60 flex items-center justify-between">
 69:         <div>
 70:           <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">Roster</h2>
 71:           <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{filtered.length} of {profiles.length} staff</p>
 72:         </div>
 73:         <button
 74:           onClick={onToggleCollapsed}
 75:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
 76:           title="Collapse roster"
 77:         >
 78:           <ChevronLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
 79:         </button>
 80:       </div>
 81: 
 82:       <div className="p-3 space-y-2 border-b border-border/60">
 83:         <div className="relative">
 84:           <Search className="absolute left-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
 85:           <input
 86:             value={query}
 87:             onChange={e => setQuery(e.target.value)}
 88:             placeholder="Search name..."
 89:             className="w-full pl-7 pr-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
 90:           />
 91:         </div>
 92: 
 93:         <div className="space-y-1.5">
 94:           <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
 95:             <Filter className="h-2.5 w-2.5" /> Role
 96:           </div>
 97:           <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
 98:             {ROLE_TIERS.map(t => (
 99:               <button
100:                 key={t}
101:                 onClick={() => {
102:                   const next = new Set(activeTiers)
103:                   if (next.has(t)) next.delete(t); else next.add(t)
104:                   setActiveTiers(next)
105:                 }}
106:                 className={cn(
107:                   'px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] border transition-colors',
108:                   activeTiers.has(t)
109:                     ? roleColor(t)
110:                     : 'border-border/60 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/40',
111:                 )}
112:               >
113:                 {t}
114:               </button>
115:             ))}
116:           </div>
117:         </div>
118: 
119:         <div className="space-y-1.5">
120:           <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
121:             <Filter className="h-2.5 w-2.5" /> Skill
122:           </div>
123:           <div className="max-h-28 overflow-y-auto flex flex-wrap gap-1 pr-1">
124:             {allSkills.map(s => (
125:               <button
126:                 key={s}
127:                 onClick={() => {
128:                   const next = new Set(activeSkills)
129:                   if (next.has(s)) next.delete(s); else next.add(s)
130:                   setActiveSkills(next)
131:                 }}
132:                 className={cn(
133:                   'px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] border transition-colors',
134:                   activeSkills.has(s)
135:                     ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/40'
136:                     : 'border-border/60 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/40',
137:                 )}
138:               >
139:                 {s}
140:               </button>
141:             ))}
142:           </div>
143:         </div>
144: 
145:         {(activeTiers.size > 0 || activeSkills.size > 0 || query) && (
146:           <button
147:             onClick={() => { setQuery(''); setActiveTiers(new Set()); setActiveSkills(new Set()) }}
148:             className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground underline"
149:           >
150:             Clear filters
151:           </button>
152:         )}
153:       </div>
154: 
155:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-2 space-y-2">
156:         {filtered.map(p => (
157:           tapSelectMode ? (
158:             <button
159:               key={p.id}
160:               onClick={() => onTapProfile?.(p.id)}
161:               className={cn(
162:                 'w-full text-left rounded-lg border bg-card transition-all p-3 flex items-center gap-2',
163:                 selectedProfileId === p.id
164:                   ? 'border-emerald-400 ring-2 ring-emerald-400/40 bg-emerald-500/10'
165:                   : 'border-border/60 hover:border-foreground/30',
166:               )}
167:               aria-pressed={selectedProfileId === p.id}
168:             >
169:               <div className="h-9 w-9 rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br from-zinc-700 to-zinc-900 text-white text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
170:                 {p.name.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')}
171:               </div>
172:               <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
173:                 <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{p.name}</p>
174:                 <span className={cn(
175:                   'inline-block mt-0.5 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-medium border',
176:                   roleColor(p.roleTier),
177:                 )}>
178:                   {p.roleTier}
179:                 </span>
180:               </div>
181:               {selectedProfileId === p.id && (
182:                 <Check className="h-4 w-4 text-emerald-400 shrink-0" />
183:               )}
184:             </button>
185:           ) : (
186:             <DraggableInstructor key={p.id} profile={p} />
187:           )
188:         ))}
189:         {filtered.length === 0 && (
190:           <div className="text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground p-6">
191:             No staff match the filters.
192:           </div>
193:         )}
194:       </div>
195: 
196:       {tapSelectMode && (
197:         <div className="p-2 border-t border-border/60 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground text-center">
198:           {selectedProfileId
199:             ? 'Tap an event slot to assign'
200:             : 'Tap an instructor to select them'}
201:         </div>
202:       )}
203:     </aside>
204:   )
205: }

File: src/components/scheduler/WorkloadTab.tsx

  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useMemo } from 'react'
  4: import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import {
  6:   roleColor, formatShortDate, type ScheduleData,
  7: } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
  8: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
