 10: import { Accordion } from './Accordion'
 11: import { HelpTooltip } from './HelpTooltip'
 12: 
 13: async function fetchSchedule(): Promise<ScheduleData> {
 14:   const r = await fetch('/api/schedule?from=2026-06-01&to=2026-09-30')
 15:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load')
 16:   return r.json()
 17: }
 18: 
 19: export function WorkloadTab() {
 20:   const { data, isLoading } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['schedule'], queryFn: fetchSchedule })
 21: 
 22:   const workload = useMemo(() => {
 23:     if (!data) return []
 24: 
 25:     // Count assignments per instructor
 26:     const counts = new Map<string, { profile: any; total: number; primary: number; alt: number; days: Set<string>; events: Set<string> }>()
 27: 
 28:     for (const p of data.profiles) {
 29:       counts.set(p.id, { profile: p, total: 0, primary: 0, alt: 0, days: new Set(), events: new Set() })
 30:     }
 31: 
 32:     for (const a of data.assignments) {
 33:       const entry = counts.get(a.profileId)
 34:       if (!entry) continue
 35:       entry.total++
 36:       if (a.isAlternative) entry.alt++
 37:       else entry.primary++
 38:       entry.days.add(a.date)
 39:       entry.events.add(a.eventId)
 40:     }
 41: 
 42:     // Convert to array and sort by total assignments (most first)
 43:     const arr = Array.from(counts.values())
 44:       .filter(w => w.total > 0)
 45:       .sort((a, b) => b.total - a.total)
 46: 
 47:     // Also get instructors with 0 assignments
 48:     const unassigned = Array.from(counts.values())
 49:       .filter(w => w.total === 0)
 50:       .sort((a, b) => a.profile.name.localeCompare(b.profile.name))
 51: 
 52:     return { assigned: arr, unassigned }
 53:   }, [data])
 54: 
 55:   const stats = useMemo(() => {
 56:     if (!workload.assigned) return { total: 0, assigned: 0, unassigned: 0, avg: 0, max: 0 }
 57:     const total = workload.assigned.length + workload.unassigned.length
 58:     const assignedCount = workload.assigned.length
 59:     const unassignedCount = workload.unassigned.length
 60:     const totalAssignments = workload.assigned.reduce((sum, w) => sum + w.total, 0)
 61:     const avg = assignedCount > 0 ? Math.round(totalAssignments / assignedCount) : 0
 62:     const max = workload.assigned.length > 0 ? workload.assigned[0].total : 0
 63:     return { total, assigned: assignedCount, unassigned: unassignedCount, avg, max }
 64:   }, [workload])
 65: 
 66:   if (isLoading) {
 67:     return (
 68:       <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground">
 69:         <p className="text-sm">Loading workload data…</p>
 70:       </div>
 71:     )
 72:   }
 73: 
 74:   if (!data) return null
 75: 
 76:   return (
 77:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
 78:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex items-center gap-2">
 79:         <div>
 80:           <h2 className="text-base font-semibold">Instructor Workload</h2>
 81:           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Overview of assignments across the full summer</p>
 82:         </div>
 83:         <HelpTooltip text="Shows total assignments per instructor. Green bar = normal workload, Amber = above average, Red = busy (20+ days). Also shows days worked, events involved in, and alternatives. Unassigned instructors are listed separately at the bottom." />
 84:       </div>
 85: 
 86:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Workload summary">
 87:         <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
 88:           {/* Summary cards */}
 89:           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
 90:             <StatCard icon={<Users className="h-4 w-4" />} label="Total staff" value={stats.total} tone="neutral" />
 91:             <StatCard icon={<Calendar className="h-4 w-4" />} label="With assignments" value={stats.assigned} tone="good" />
 92:             <StatCard icon={<AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4" />} label="Unassigned" value={stats.unassigned} tone={stats.unassigned > 0 ? 'warn' : 'good'} />
 93:             <StatCard icon={<TrendingUp className="h-4 w-4" />} label="Avg per instructor" value={stats.avg} tone="neutral" />
 94:           </div>
 95: 
 96:           {/* Workload bars */}
 97:           <Accordion label="Assigned Instructors" labelClassName="bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/30" defaultOpen>
 98:             <div className="space-y-2 pt-2">
 99:               {workload.assigned.map((w, i) => {
100:                 const maxBar = stats.max || 1
101:                 const barWidth = (w.total / maxBar) * 100
102:                 const isOverworked = w.days.size > 20 // more than 20 working days
103:                 return (
104:                   <div key={w.profile.id} className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3">
105:                     <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
106:                       <div className="h-8 w-8 rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br from-zinc-700 to-zinc-900 text-white text-[10px] font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
107:                         {w.profile.name.split(' ').map((n: string) => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')}
108:                       </div>
109:                       <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
110:                         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
111:                           <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{w.profile.name}</p>
112:                           <span className={cn('text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', roleColor(w.profile.roleTier))}>
113:                             {w.profile.roleTier}
114:                           </span>
115:                           {isOverworked && (
116:                             <span className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border border-rose-500/30 flex items-center gap-0.5">
117:                               <AlertTriangle className="h-2 w-2" /> Busy
118:                             </span>
119:                           )}
120:                         </div>
121:                         {/* Workload bar */}
122:                         <div className="mt-1.5 flex items-center gap-2">
123:                           <div className="flex-1 h-2 bg-muted/40 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
124:                             <div
125:                               className={cn(
126:                                 'h-full rounded-full transition-all',
127:                                 isOverworked ? 'bg-rose-500' : w.total > stats.avg ? 'bg-amber-500' : 'bg-emerald-500',
128:                               )}
129:                               style={{ width: `${barWidth}%` }}
130:                             />
131:                           </div>
132:                           <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold tabular-nums shrink-0">{w.total}</span>
133:                         </div>
134:                         {/* Stats line */}
135:                         <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-1 flex items-center gap-3 flex-wrap">
136:                           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
137:                             <Calendar className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
138:                             {w.days.size} days
139:                           </span>
140:                           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
141:                             <Users className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
142:                             {w.events.size} events
143:                           </span>
144:                           {w.alt > 0 && (
145:                             <span className="text-amber-300">{w.alt} alt</span>
146:                           )}
147:                         </div>
148:                       </div>
149:                     </div>
150:                   </div>
151:                 )
152:               })}
153:             </div>
154:           </Accordion>
155: 
156:           {/* Unassigned */}
157:           {workload.unassigned.length > 0 && (
158:             <Accordion label={`Unassigned (${workload.unassigned.length})`} labelClassName="bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 border-amber-500/30">
159:               <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-2 pt-2">
160:                 {workload.unassigned.map((w) => (
161:                   <div key={w.profile.id} className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/60 p-2 flex items-center gap-2">
162:                     <div className="h-7 w-7 rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br from-zinc-700 to-zinc-900 text-white text-[9px] font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
163:                       {w.profile.name.split(' ').map((n: string) => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')}
164:                     </div>
165:                     <div className="min-w-0">
166:                       <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{w.profile.name}</p>
167:                       <span className={cn('text-[9px] px-1 py-0.5 rounded border', roleColor(w.profile.roleTier))}>
168:                         {w.profile.roleTier}
169:                       </span>
170:                     </div>
171:                   </div>
172:                 ))}
173:               </div>
174:             </Accordion>
175:           )}
176:         </div>
177:       </div>
178:     </div>
179:   )
180: }
181: 
182: function StatCard({ icon, label, value, tone }: {
183:   icon: React.ReactNode
184:   label: string
185:   value: number
186:   tone: 'good' | 'warn' | 'bad' | 'neutral'
187: }) {
188:   return (
189:     <div className={cn(
190:       'rounded-lg border p-3 flex items-center gap-2',
191:       tone === 'good' && 'border-emerald-500/30 bg-emerald-500/5',
192:       tone === 'warn' && 'border-amber-500/30 bg-amber-500/5',
193:       tone === 'bad' && 'border-rose-500/30 bg-rose-500/5',
194:       tone === 'neutral' && 'border-border/60',
195:     )}>
196:       <div className={cn(
197:         'h-8 w-8 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shrink-0',
198:         tone === 'good' && 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300',
199:         tone === 'warn' && 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300',
200:         tone === 'bad' && 'bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300',
201:         tone === 'neutral' && 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground',
202:       )}>
203:         {icon}
204:       </div>
205:       <div>
206:         <div className="text-lg font-bold tabular-nums">{value}</div>
207:         <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{label}</div>
208:       </div>
209:     </div>
210:   )
211: }

================
File: src/hooks/use-is-mobile.ts
================
 1: 'use client'
 2: 
 3: import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
 4: 
 5: // Returns true when the viewport is mobile-width (< 640px).
 6: // Uses useSyncExternalStore pattern to avoid hydration mismatch.
 7: export function useIsMobile(): boolean {
 8:   const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = useState(false)
 9:   useEffect(() => {
10:     const mq = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 639px)')
11:     const update = () => setIsMobile(mq.matches)
12:     update()
13:     mq.addEventListener('change', update)
14:     return () => mq.removeEventListener('change', update)
15:   }, [])
16:   return isMobile
17: }

================
File: src/lib/db.ts
================
 1: import { createClient } from '@libsql/client'
 2: 
 3: const globalForDb = globalThis as unknown as {
 4:   libsqlClient: ReturnType<typeof createClient> | undefined
 5: }
 6: 
 7: function createDbClient() {
 8:   const url = process.env.TURSO_URL || process.env.DATABASE_URL
 9:   if (!url) {
10:     throw new Error('DATABASE_URL or TURSO_URL environment variable is not set')
11:   }
12: 
13:   // Turso / libsql connection
14:   if (url.startsWith('libsql://')) {
15:     const authToken = process.env.TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN || process.env.DATABASE_AUTH_TOKEN
16:     return createClient({ url, authToken })
17:   }
18: 
19:   // Local SQLite
20:   return createClient({ url })
21: }
22: 
23: export const db = globalForDb.libsqlClient ?? createDbClient()
24: 
25: if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') globalForDb.libsqlClient = db

================
File: src/app/api/invites/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { requireAdmin } from "@/lib/auth-helpers"
 3: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 4: 
 5: // GET /api/invites
 6: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 7:   const authGet = await requireAdmin(req); if (authGet) return authGet;
 8:   const result = await db.execute({
 9:     sql: `SELECT u.*, p.name as profileName FROM User u LEFT JOIN Profile p ON u.profileId = p.id ORDER BY u.createdAt DESC`,
10:   })
11: 
12:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows.map((u: any) => ({
13:     id: u.id,
14:     name: u.name,
15:     email: u.email,
16:     role: u.role,
17:     profileId: u.profileId,
18:     profileName: u.profileName,
19:     inviteToken: u.inviteToken,
20:     claimedAt: u.claimedAt ? new Date(u.claimedAt).toISOString() : null,
21:     inviteExpiresAt: u.inviteExpiresAt ? new Date(u.inviteExpiresAt).toISOString() : null,
22:     createdAt: new Date(u.createdAt).toISOString(),
23:   })))
24: }
25: 
26: // POST /api/invites — create invite linked to existing staff
27: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
28:   const authPost = await requireAdmin(req); if (authPost) return authPost;
29:   const body = await req.json()
30:   const { name, profileId } = body as { name: string; profileId?: string }
31:   if (!name) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing name' }, { status: 400 })
32: 
33:   if (profileId) {
34:     const profile = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT id FROM Profile WHERE id = ?', args: [profileId] })
35:     if (profile.rows.length === 0) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Profile not found' }, { status: 404 })
36:   }
37: 
38:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
39:   const inviteToken = crypto.randomUUID()
40: 
41:   await db.execute({
42:     sql: `INSERT INTO User (id, name, role, profileId, inviteToken, createdAt, updatedAt)
43:           VALUES (?, ?, 'instructor', ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
44:     args: [id, name, profileId ?? null, inviteToken],
45:   })
46: 
47:   const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM User WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
48:   const u = result.rows[0] as any
49:   return NextResponse.json({
50:     id: u.id,
51:     name: u.name,
52:     inviteToken: u.inviteToken,
53:     profileId: u.profileId,
54:   }, { status: 201 })
55: }
56: 
57: // DELETE /api/invites?id=...
58: export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
59:   const authDel = await requireAdmin(req); if (authDel) return authDel;
60:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
61:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
62:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
63:   await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM User WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
64:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
65: }

================
File: src/app/api/opt-ins/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 4: import { notifyOptInReceived } from '@/lib/email'
 5: 
 6: // GET /api/opt-ins?eventId=...
 7: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 8:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 9:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
10: 
11:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
12:   const eventId = searchParams.get('eventId')
13: 
14:   let sql = `SELECT o.*, u.name as userName, u.profileId as userProfileId, p.name as userProfileName,
15:              e.name as eventName
16:              FROM OptIn o
17:              JOIN User u ON o.userId = u.id
18:              LEFT JOIN Profile p ON u.profileId = p.id
19:              JOIN Event e ON o.eventId = e.id`
20:   const args: unknown[] = []
21: 
22:   if (eventId) {
23:     sql += ' WHERE o.eventId = ?'
24:     args.push(eventId)
25:   } else if (user.role === 'instructor') {
26:     sql += ' WHERE o.userId = ?'
27:     args.push(user.id)
28:   }
29: 
30:   sql += ' ORDER BY o.createdAt DESC'
31: 
32:   const result = await db.execute({ sql, args })
33:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows.map((o: any) => ({
34:     id: o.id,
35:     userId: o.userId,
36:     userName: o.userName,
37:     userProfileId: o.userProfileId,
38:     userProfileName: o.userProfileName,
39:     eventId: o.eventId,
40:     eventName: o.eventName,
41:     status: o.status,
42:     note: o.note,
43:     createdAt: new Date(o.createdAt).toISOString(),
44:   })))
45: }
46: 
47: // POST /api/opt-ins — upsert
48: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
49:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
50:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
51:   if (user.role !== 'instructor') {
52:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Admins cannot opt in' }, { status: 403 })
53:   }
54: 
55:   const body = await req.json()
56:   const { eventId, status, note } = body as { eventId: string; status: string; note?: string }
57:   if (!eventId || !['interested', 'available', 'unavailable'].includes(status)) {
58:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid status' }, { status: 400 })
59:   }
60: 
61:   // Check if opt-in exists
62:   const existing = await db.execute({
63:     sql: 'SELECT id FROM OptIn WHERE userId = ? AND eventId = ?',
64:     args: [user.id, eventId],
65:   })
66: 
67:   if (existing.rows.length > 0) {
68:     const id = (existing.rows[0] as any).id
69:     await db.execute({
70:       sql: "UPDATE OptIn SET status = ?, note = ?, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?",
71:       args: [status, note ?? null, id],
72:     })
73:     // Email the admin
74:     const eventResult = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT name FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [eventId] })
75:     const eventName = eventResult.rows.length > 0 ? (eventResult.rows[0] as any).name : 'Unknown'
76:     notifyOptInReceived(user.name, status, eventName, eventId).catch(() => {})
77:     return NextResponse.json({ id, userId: user.id, eventId, status, note })
78:   } else {
79:     const id = crypto.randomUUID()
80:     await db.execute({
81:       sql: `INSERT INTO OptIn (id, userId, eventId, status, note, createdAt, updatedAt)
82:             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
83:       args: [id, user.id, eventId, status, note ?? null],
84:     })
85:     // Email the admin
86:     const eventResult = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT name FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [eventId] })
87:     const eventName = eventResult.rows.length > 0 ? (eventResult.rows[0] as any).name : 'Unknown'
88:     notifyOptInReceived(user.name, status, eventName, eventId).catch(() => {})
89:     return NextResponse.json({ id, userId: user.id, eventId, status, note }, { status: 201 })
90:   }
91: }

File: src/components/scheduler/HelpTooltip.tsx

 1: 'use client'
 2: 
 3: import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
 4: import { HelpCircle, X } from 'lucide-react'
 5: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
 6: 
 7: type Props = {
 8:   text: string
 9:   className?: string
10: }
11: 
12: export function HelpTooltip({ text, className }: Props) {
13:   const [show, setShow] = useState(false)
14:   const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
15: 
16:   // Close on click outside (for desktop absolute tooltip)
17:   useEffect(() => {
18:     if (!show) return
19:     const handleClick = (e: MouseEvent) => {
20:       if (ref.current && !ref.current.contains(e.target as Node)) {
21:         setShow(false)
22:       }
23:     }
24:     document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)
25:     return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)
26:   }, [show])
27: 
28:   return (
29:     <div className="relative inline-flex shrink-0" ref={ref}>
30:       <button
31:         onClick={() => setShow(s => !s)}
32:         className="p-1.5 rounded-md text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-muted/40 transition-colors min-h-[44px] min-w-[44px] flex items-center justify-center"
33:         aria-label="Help — click to toggle instructions"
34:         aria-expanded={show}
35:       >
36:         <HelpCircle className="h-5 w-5" />
37:       </button>
38:       {show && (
39:         <>
40:           {/* Mobile: fixed bottom sheet — no clipping */}
41:           <div
42:             className="sm:hidden fixed inset-x-0 bottom-0 z-50 bg-card border-t border-border/60 rounded-t-lg shadow-2xl p-4 max-h-[60vh] overflow-y-auto"
43:             role="tooltip"
44:             onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
45:           >
46:             <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-2">
47:               <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wide">How to use</span>
48:               <button
49:                 onClick={() => setShow(false)}
50:                 className="p-1 rounded hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
51:                 aria-label="Close help"
52:               >
53:                 <X className="h-4 w-4" />
54:               </button>
55:             </div>
56:             <p className="text-sm text-foreground leading-relaxed">{text}</p>
57:           </div>
58: 
59:           {/* Desktop: absolute positioned tooltip */}
60:           <div
61:             className={cn(
62:               "hidden sm:block absolute right-0 top-full mt-2 z-50 w-80 bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-md shadow-lg p-3 text-sm text-foreground leading-relaxed",
63:               className
64:             )}
65:             role="tooltip"
66:           >
67:             <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-1">
68:               <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wide">How to use</span>
69:               <button
70:                 onClick={() => setShow(false)}
71:                 className="p-0.5 rounded hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
72:                 aria-label="Close help"
73:               >
74:                 <X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
75:               </button>
76:             </div>
77:             {text}
78:           </div>
79:         </>
80:       )}
81:     </div>
82:   )
83: }

================
File: src/lib/email.ts

  1: /**
  2:  * Email notification service using Resend + digest queue.
  3:  *
  4:  * Two urgency levels:
  5:  *   - 'instant'  → sent immediately (opt-in receipts, verification codes, <72h assignment changes)
  6:  *   - 'digest'   → queued, sent in 8am AST digest or when admin clicks "Send now"
  7:  *
  8:  * Per-user email toggle (User.emailNotifications):
  9:  *   - 0 → no emails (notifications still appear in the bell)
 10:  *   - 1 → emails (default)
 11:  *   - Verification codes + welcome emails bypass the toggle (transactional)
 12:  *
 13:  * If RESEND_API_KEY is not set, everything is silently skipped (dev mode).
 14:  */
 15: 
 16: import "server-only"
 17: 
 18: const RESEND_API_KEY = process.env.RESEND_API_KEY
 19: const FROM_EMAIL = process.env.FROM_EMAIL || 'onboarding@resend.dev'
 20: const URGENT_HOURS = 72 // changes to events within this window fire instantly
 21: 
 22: // ---------- Low-level send ----------
 23: 
 24: /** Escape user-supplied text for safe interpolation into HTML email bodies. */
 25: function escapeHtml(s: string): string {
 26:   return String(s)
 27:     .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
 28:     .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
 29:     .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
 30:     .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
 31:     .replace(/'/g, '&#039;')
 32: }
 33: 
 34: export async function sendEmail(to: string, subject: string, html: string) {
 35:   if (!RESEND_API_KEY) {
 36:     console.log('[email] Skipped (no RESEND_API_KEY):', subject, '→', to)
 37:     return false
 38:   }
 39:   try {
 40:     const res = await fetch('https://api.resend.com/emails', {
 41:       method: 'POST',
 42:       headers: {
 43:         'Authorization': `Bearer ${RESEND_API_KEY}`,
 44:         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
 45:       },
 46:       body: JSON.stringify({ from: FROM_EMAIL, to, subject, html }),
 47:     })
 48:     if (!res.ok) {
 49:       console.error('[email] Failed:', await res.text())
 50:       return false
 51:     }
 52:     return true
 53:   } catch (e: any) {
 54:     console.error('[email] Error:', e.message)
 55:     return false
 56:   }
 57: }
 58: 
 59: // ---------- User lookup helpers ----------
 60: 
 61: async function getUserEmailAndPrefs(userId: string): Promise<{ email: string | null; emailNotifications: boolean } | null> {
 62:   const { db } = await import('./db')
 63:   const r = await db.execute({
 64:     sql: 'SELECT email, emailNotifications FROM User WHERE id = ?',
 65:     args: [userId],
 66:   })
 67:   if (r.rows.length === 0) return null
 68:   const u = r.rows[0] as any
 69:   return {
 70:     email: u.email ?? null,
 71:     emailNotifications: u.emailNotifications === null || u.emailNotifications === undefined ? true : !!u.emailNotifications,
 72:   }
 73: }
 74: 
 75: async function getUserIdByProfileId(profileId: string): Promise<string | null> {
 76:   const { db } = await import('./db')
 77:   const r = await db.execute({
 78:     sql: 'SELECT id FROM User WHERE profileId = ?',
 79:     args: [profileId],
 80:   })
 81:   if (r.rows.length === 0) return null
 82:   return (r.rows[0] as any).id
 83: }
 84: 
 85: async function getAdminUserIds(): Promise<string[]> {
 86:   const { db } = await import('./db')
 87:   const r = await db.execute({ sql: "SELECT id FROM User WHERE role = 'admin'" })
 88:   return r.rows.map((u: any) => u.id)
 89: }
 90: 
 91: // ---------- Event date urgency check ----------
 92: 
 93: async function isEventUrgent(eventId: string): Promise<boolean> {
 94:   const { db } = await import('./db')
 95:   const r = await db.execute({
 96:     sql: 'SELECT startDate FROM Event WHERE id = ?',
 97:     args: [eventId],
 98:   })
 99:   if (r.rows.length === 0) return false
100:   const startDate = String((r.rows[0] as any).startDate).slice(0, 10)
101:   // Today in Barbados
102:   const today = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
103:     timeZone: 'America/Barbados', year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
104:   }).format(new Date())
105:   const diffMs = new Date(startDate + 'T00:00:00.000Z').getTime() - new Date(today + 'T00:00:00.000Z').getTime()
106:   const diffHours = diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60)
107:   return diffHours >= 0 && diffHours <= URGENT_HOURS * 24
108: }
109: 
110: // ---------- Notification + Email queue ----------
111: 
112: /**
113:  * Create an in-app notification AND queue an email if appropriate.
114:  * Called by assignment/opt-in handlers.
115:  *
116:  * @param userId     recipient user
117:  * @param type       notification type ('assignment_created' | 'assignment_removed' | 'opt_in_received' | 'event_changed')
118:  * @param title      short title
119:  * @param body       longer body (optional)
120:  * @param eventId    related event (optional, makes notification clickable)
121:  * @param assignmentId  related assignment (optional)
122:  * @param urgency    'instant' | 'digest' (default 'digest')
123:  * @param alwaysEmail  if true, ignore user's emailNotifications toggle (for transactional emails)
124:  */
125: export async function notifyUser(opts: {
126:   userId: string
127:   type: string
128:   title: string
129:   body?: string | null
130:   eventId?: string | null
131:   assignmentId?: string | null
132:   urgency?: 'instant' | 'digest'
133:   alwaysEmail?: boolean
134:   emailSubject?: string
135:   emailHtml?: string
136: }) {
137:   const { db } = await import('./db')
138:   const { userId, type, title, body, eventId, assignmentId, urgency = 'digest', alwaysEmail = false } = opts
139: 
140:   // 1. Always create the in-app notification (bell)
141:   await db.execute({
142:     sql: `INSERT INTO Notification (id, userId, type, title, body, eventId, assignmentId, readAt, createdAt)
143:           VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NULL, datetime('now'))`,
144:     args: [crypto.randomUUID(), userId, type, title, body ?? null, eventId ?? null, assignmentId ?? null],
145:   }).catch(() => {
146:     // Notification table might not exist yet (pre-migration). Silently skip.
147:     console.log('[notify] Notification table missing — skipping in-app notification')
148:   })
149: 
150:   // 2. Queue the email if user has email notifications on (or alwaysEmail=true)
151:   const prefs = await getUserEmailAndPrefs(userId)
152:   if (!prefs || !prefs.email) return // no email address → can't email
153:   if (!alwaysEmail && !prefs.emailNotifications) return // user opted out
154: 
155:   // Capture the queue row id so we can reliably mark it sent (datetime('now') has
156:   // 1-second precision and would otherwise fail to match after the sendEmail HTTP call)
157:   const emailQueueId = crypto.randomUUID()
158:   await db.execute({
159:     sql: `INSERT INTO EmailQueue (id, userId, type, subject, body, eventId, urgency, sentAt, createdAt)
160:           VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NULL, datetime('now'))`,
161:     args: [
162:       emailQueueId,
163:       userId,
164:       type,
165:       opts.emailSubject ?? title,
166:       opts.emailHtml ?? `<p>${body ?? title}</p>`,
167:       eventId ?? null,
168:       urgency,
169:     ],
170:   }).catch(() => {
171:     console.log('[notify] EmailQueue table missing — skipping email queue')
172:   })
173: 
174:   // 3. If urgency is 'instant', send immediately and mark the row sent by id
175:   if (urgency === 'instant') {
176:     await sendEmail(prefs.email, opts.emailSubject ?? title, opts.emailHtml ?? `<p>${body ?? title}</p>`)
177:     await db.execute({
178:       sql: "UPDATE EmailQueue SET sentAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?",
179:       args: [emailQueueId],
180:     }).catch(() => {})
181:   }
182: }
183: 
184: // ---------- High-level notification helpers ----------
185: 
186: export async function notifyAssignmentCreated(profileId: string, eventName: string, date: string, shirtColor: string | null, eventId: string | null) {
187:   const userId = await getUserIdByProfileId(profileId)
188:   if (!userId) return
189: 
190:   const urgent = eventId ? await isEventUrgent(eventId) : false
191:   const title = `New assignment: ${eventName}`
192:   const body = `You've been assigned to ${eventName} on ${date}${shirtColor ? `. Shirt: ${shirtColor}` : ''}.`
193:   const html = `<h2>📅 New Assignment</h2><p><strong>${escapeHtml(eventName)}</strong> on ${escapeHtml(date)}${shirtColor ? `<br>Shirt: ${escapeHtml(shirtColor)}` : ''}</p>`
194: 
195:   await notifyUser({
196:     userId,
197:     type: 'assignment_created',
198:     title,
199:     body,
200:     eventId,
201:     urgency: urgent ? 'instant' : 'digest',
202:     emailSubject: title,
203:     emailHtml: html,
204:   })
205: }
206: 
207: export async function notifyAssignmentRemoved(profileId: string, eventName: string, date: string, eventId: string | null) {
208:   const userId = await getUserIdByProfileId(profileId)
209:   if (!userId) return
210: 
211:   const urgent = eventId ? await isEventUrgent(eventId) : false
212:   const title = `Assignment removed: ${eventName}`
213:   const body = `Your assignment to ${eventName} on ${date} has been removed.`
214:   const html = `<p>Your assignment to <strong>${escapeHtml(eventName)}</strong> on ${escapeHtml(date)} has been removed.</p>`
215: 
216:   await notifyUser({
217:     userId,
218:     type: 'assignment_removed',
219:     title,
220:     body,
221:     eventId,
222:     urgency: urgent ? 'instant' : 'digest',
223:     emailSubject: title,
224:     emailHtml: html,
225:   })
226: }
227: 
228: export async function notifyOptInReceived(userName: string, status: string, eventName: string, eventId: string | null) {
229:   // Notify all admins
230:   const adminIds = await getAdminUserIds()
231:   const title = `${userName} ${status}: ${eventName}`
232:   const body = `${userName} marked themselves as ${status} for ${eventName}.`
233:   const html = `<p><strong>${escapeHtml(userName)}</strong> marked themselves as <strong>${escapeHtml(status)}</strong> for ${escapeHtml(eventName)}.</p>`
234: 
235:   await Promise.all(adminIds.map(adminId =>
236:     notifyUser({
237:       userId: adminId,
238:       type: 'opt_in_received',
239:       title,
240:       body,
241:       eventId,
242:       urgency: 'instant', // opt-ins are always instant — instructors expect immediate feedback
243:       emailSubject: title,
244:       emailHtml: html,
245:     })
246:   ))
247: }
248: 
249: // ---------- Digest + manual send ----------
250: 
251: /**
252:  * Send all pending digest emails for a user.
253:  * Groups by user, concatenates body into a single digest email.
254:  */
255: export async function sendDigests() {
256:   if (!RESEND_API_KEY) return { sent: 0, skipped: true }
257:   const { db } = await import('./db')
258: 
259:   // Find users with pending digest emails
260:   const pending = await db.execute({
261:     sql: `SELECT DISTINCT userId FROM EmailQueue WHERE sentAt IS NULL AND urgency = 'digest'`,
262:   })
263: 
264:   let sent = 0
265:   for (const row of pending.rows as any[]) {
266:     const userId = row.userId
267:     const prefs = await getUserEmailAndPrefs(userId)
268:     if (!prefs || !prefs.email || !prefs.emailNotifications) continue
269: 
270:     // Get all pending digest items for this user
271:     const items = await db.execute({
272:       sql: `SELECT * FROM EmailQueue WHERE userId = ? AND sentAt IS NULL AND urgency = 'digest' ORDER BY createdAt ASC`,
273:       args: [userId],
274:     })
275: 
276:     if (items.rows.length === 0) continue
277: 
278:     // Build digest email
279:     const html = `<div style="font-family: sans-serif; max-width: 500px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 20px;">
280:       <h2 style="color: #10b981;">RA Syncbot — Daily Digest</h2>
281:       <p>You have ${items.rows.length} update${items.rows.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}:</p>
282:       <ul>
283:         ${items.rows.map((i: any) => `<li><strong>${escapeHtml(i.subject)}</strong><br><span style="color: #666; font-size: 12px;">${escapeHtml(i.body)}</span></li>`).join('')}
284:       </ul>
285:       <p style="color: #666; font-size: 11px; margin-top: 20px;">Log in to <a href="https://ra-syncbot.com">ra-syncbot.com</a> to view details.</p>
286:     </div>`
287: 
288:     const success = await sendEmail(prefs.email, `RA Syncbot — ${items.rows.length} update${items.rows.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} today`, html)
289:     if (success) {
290:       // Mark all as sent
291:       await db.execute({
292:         sql: "UPDATE EmailQueue SET sentAt = datetime('now') WHERE userId = ? AND sentAt IS NULL AND urgency = 'digest'",
293:         args: [userId],
294:       })
295:       sent++
296:     }
297:   }
298: 
299:   return { sent, skipped: false }
300: }
301: 
302: /**
303:  * Send ALL pending emails (digest + instant) immediately.
304:  * Called when admin clicks "Send pending notifications now".
305:  */
306: export async function sendAllPending() {
307:   if (!RESEND_API_KEY) return { sent: 0, skipped: true }
308:   const { db } = await import('./db')
309: 
310:   const pending = await db.execute({
311:     sql: `SELECT DISTINCT userId FROM EmailQueue WHERE sentAt IS NULL`,
312:   })
313: 
314:   let sent = 0
315:   for (const row of pending.rows as any[]) {
316:     const userId = row.userId
317:     const prefs = await getUserEmailAndPrefs(userId)
318:     if (!prefs || !prefs.email || !prefs.emailNotifications) continue
319: 
320:     const items = await db.execute({
321:       sql: `SELECT * FROM EmailQueue WHERE userId = ? AND sentAt IS NULL ORDER BY createdAt ASC`,
322:       args: [userId],
323:     })
324: 
325:     if (items.rows.length === 0) continue
326: 
327:     const html = `<div style="font-family: sans-serif; max-width: 500px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 20px;">
328:       <h2 style="color: #10b981;">RA Syncbot — Update</h2>
329:       <p>You have ${items.rows.length} update${items.rows.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}:</p>
330:       <ul>
331:         ${items.rows.map((i: any) => `<li><strong>${escapeHtml(i.subject)}</strong><br><span style="color: #666; font-size: 12px;">${escapeHtml(i.body)}</span></li>`).join('')}
332:       </ul>
333:     </div>`
334: 
335:     const success = await sendEmail(prefs.email, `RA Syncbot — ${items.rows.length} update${items.rows.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`, html)
336:     if (success) {
337:       await db.execute({
338:         sql: "UPDATE EmailQueue SET sentAt = datetime('now') WHERE userId = ? AND sentAt IS NULL",
339:         args: [userId],
340:       })
341:       sent++
342:     }
343:   }
344: 
345:   return { sent, skipped: false }
346: }
347: 
348: // ---------- Reminders (unchanged behavior, instant) ----------
349: 
350: export async function sendReminders() {
351:   if (!RESEND_API_KEY) return { sent: 0, skipped: true }
352:   const { db } = await import('./db')
353:   const today = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
354:     timeZone: 'America/Barbados', year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
355:   }).format(new Date())
356:   const d = new Date(today + 'T00:00:00.000Z')
357:   d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 2)
358:   const targetDate = d.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
359: 
360:   const assignments = await db.execute({
361:     sql: `SELECT a.*, e.name as eventName, e.location, e.startTime, e.id as eventId, u.email, u.id as userId, u.emailNotifications, p.name as profileName
362:           FROM Assignment a JOIN Event e ON a.eventId = e.id
363:           JOIN User u ON u.profileId = a.profileId JOIN Profile p ON p.id = a.profileId
364:           WHERE a.assignedDate = ? AND u.email IS NOT NULL`,
365:     args: [targetDate + 'T00:00:00.000Z'],
366:   })
367: 
368:   let sent = 0
369:   for (const a of assignments.rows as any[]) {
370:     const emailOn = a.emailNotifications === null || a.emailNotifications === undefined ? true : !!a.emailNotifications
371:     if (!emailOn) continue
372:     const html = `<h2>⏰ Reminder</h2><p>You're assigned to <strong>${escapeHtml(a.eventName)}</strong> on ${escapeHtml(targetDate)} at ${escapeHtml(a.startTime)}.${a.location ? ` Location: ${escapeHtml(a.location)}.` : ''}${a.shirtColor ? ` Shirt: ${escapeHtml(a.shirtColor)}.` : ''}</p>`
373:     const success = await sendEmail(a.email, `Reminder: ${a.eventName} in 2 days`, html)
374:     if (success) sent++
375:   }
376:   return { sent, skipped: false }
377: }

File: src/app/api/auth/claim/route.ts
================
  1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
  2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
  3: import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs'
  4: import { saveSessionToResponse } from '@/lib/session'
  5: import { sendEmail } from '@/lib/email'
  6: 
  7: // POST /api/auth/claim — claim an invite with password + email verification
  8: //
  9: // Flow:
 10: // 1. Instructor opens invite link, enters name + email + password
 11: // 2. We create the account but mark it as "unverified"
 12: // 3. We send a verification email with a link containing a verification token
 13: // 4. Instructor clicks the link → account is verified → they can log in
 14: //
 15: // If RESEND_API_KEY is not set, we skip verification (dev mode) and
 16: // claim the account immediately.
 17: 
 18: const verifyCodes = new Map<string, { email: string; code: string; expires: number }>()
 19: 
 20: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 21:   const body = await req.json()
 22:   const { token, name, email, password, verifyCode } = body as {
 23:     token: string
 24:     name?: string
 25:     email: string
 26:     password: string
 27:     verifyCode?: string
 28:   }
 29:   if (!token) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing token' }, { status: 400 })
 30:   if (!email) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Email is required' }, { status: 400 })
 31:   if (!password || password.length < 6) {
 32:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })
 33:   }
 34: 
 35:   const result = await db.execute({
 36:     sql: 'SELECT * FROM User WHERE inviteToken = ?',
 37:     args: [token],
 38:   })
 39: 
 40:   if (result.rows.length === 0) {
 41:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid invite token' }, { status: 404 })
 42:   }
 43: 
 44:   const user = result.rows[0] as any
 45:   if (user.inviteExpiresAt && new Date(user.inviteExpiresAt) < new Date()) {
 46:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invite link has expired' }, { status: 410 })
 47:   }
 48: 
 49:   // Check email uniqueness
 50:   if (email !== user.email) {
 51:     const existing = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT id FROM User WHERE email = ?', args: [email] })
 52:     if (existing.rows.length > 0) {
 53:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Email already in use' }, { status: 409 })
 54:     }
 55:   }
 56: 
 57:   // Step 1: If no verifyCode, send verification email
 58:   if (!verifyCode) {
 59:     // Generate a 6-digit code
 60:     const code = String(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000))
 61:     const expires = Date.now() + 10 * 60 * 1000 // 10 minutes
 62: 
 63:     // Store the code (keyed by invite token + email)
 64:     const key = `${token}:${email}`
 65:     verifyCodes.set(key, { email, code, expires })
 66: 
 67:     // Send verification email
 68:     await sendEmail(
 69:       email,
 70:       'Your RA Syncbot verification code',
 71:       `<div style="font-family: sans-serif; max-width: 400px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 20px;">
 72:         <h2 style="color: #10b981;">Email Verification</h2>
 73:         <p>Your verification code is:</p>
 74:         <p style="font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold; letter-spacing: 8px; color: #10b981; text-align: center; margin: 20px 0;">${code}</p>
 75:         <p style="color: #666; font-size: 12px;">This code expires in 10 minutes. If you didn't request this, ignore this email.</p>
 76:       </div>`,
 77:     )
 78: 
 79:     return NextResponse.json({
 80:       step: 'verify',
 81:       message: 'Verification code sent to your email. Enter it to complete account setup.',
 82:     })
 83:   }
 84: 
 85:   // Step 2: Verify the code
 86:   const key = `${token}:${email}`
 87:   const stored = verifyCodes.get(key)
 88:   if (!stored) {
 89:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No verification code was sent. Please start again.' }, { status: 400 })
 90:   }
 91:   if (Date.now() > stored.expires) {
 92:     verifyCodes.delete(key)
 93:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Verification code has expired. Please start again.' }, { status: 410 })
 94:   }
 95:   if (stored.code !== verifyCode) {
 96:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Incorrect verification code' }, { status: 401 })
 97:   }
 98: 
 99:   // Code verified — create the account
100:   verifyCodes.delete(key)
101: 
102:   const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10)
103:   const updates: string[] = ['claimedAt = datetime(\'now\')', 'passwordHash = ?', 'email = ?']
104:   const args: unknown[] = [passwordHash, email]
105:   if (name) { updates.push('name = ?'); args.push(name) }
106:   args.push(user.id)
107: 
108:   await db.execute({
109:     sql: `UPDATE User SET ${updates.join(', ')} WHERE id = ?`,
110:     args,
111:   })
112: 
113:   // Send welcome email
114:   await sendEmail(
115:     email,
116:     'Welcome to RA Syncbot!',
117:     `<div style="font-family: sans-serif; max-width: 400px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 20px;">
118:       <h2 style="color: #10b981;">Welcome to RA Syncbot!</h2>
119:       <p>Hi ${name || user.name},</p>
120:       <p>Your account has been verified and is ready to go. You can now:</p>
121:       <ul>
122:         <li>View your camp schedule</li>
123:         <li>Opt in to events you'd like to work</li>
124:         <li>Set your availability</li>
125:         <li>Subscribe to your calendar</li>
126:       </ul>
127:       <p>Login at any time using your email and password.</p>
128:     </div>`,
129:   )
130: 
131:   const res = NextResponse.json({
132:     user: {
133:       id: user.id,
134:       name: name || user.name,
135:       email,
136:       role: user.role,
137:       profileId: user.profileId,
138:     },
139:   })
140:   await saveSessionToResponse(res, { userId: user.id })
141:   return res
142: }

================
File: src/components/scheduler/LoginForm.tsx
================
 1: 'use client'
 2: 
 3: import { useState } from 'react'
 4: import { toast } from 'sonner'
 5: import { AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react'
 6: 
 7: type Props = {
 8:   onLoggedIn: () => void
 9: }
10: 
11: export function LoginForm({ onLoggedIn }: Props) {
12:   const [email, setEmail] = useState('')
13:   const [password, setPassword] = useState('')
14:   const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
15: 
16:   const submit = async () => {
17:     if (!email || !password) {
18:       toast.error('Email and password are required')
19:       return
20:     }
21:     setSubmitting(true)
22:     try {
23:       const r = await fetch('/api/auth/me', {
24:         method: 'POST',
25:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
26:         body: JSON.stringify({ email, password }),
27:       })
28:       const j = await r.json()
29:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Login failed')
30:       toast.success('Logged in')
31:       onLoggedIn()
32:     } catch (e: any) {
33:       toast.error(e.message || 'Login failed')
34:     } finally {
35:       setSubmitting(false)
36:     }
37:   }
38: 
39:   return (
40:     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background p-6">
41:       <div className="max-w-sm w-full">
42:         <div className="text-center mb-6">
43:           <img src="/logo.png" alt="RA Syncbot" className="h-16 w-16 mx-auto mb-3 rounded-xl object-cover" />
44:           <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold">RA Syncbot</h1>
45:           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
46:             Sign in to the camp scheduler
47:           </p>
48:         </div>
49: 
50:         <div className="space-y-3 bg-card/80 border border-border/60 rounded-lg p-4">
51:           <div>
52:             <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
53:               Email
54:             </label>
55:             <input
56:               value={email}
57:               onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)}
58:               type="email"
59:               placeholder="you@example.com"
60:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
61:               onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && submit()}
62:             />
63:           </div>
64:           <div>
65:             <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
66:               Password
67:             </label>
68:             <input
69:               value={password}
70:               onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)}
71:               type="password"
72:               placeholder="••••••••"
73:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
74:               onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && submit()}
75:             />
76:           </div>
77:           <button
78:             onClick={submit}
79:             disabled={submitting}
80:             className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 min-h-[40px]"
81:           >
82:             {submitting ? 'Signing in…' : 'Sign in'}
83:           </button>
84:         </div>
85: 
86:         <div className="mt-4 flex items-start gap-2 p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
87:           <AlertCircle className="h-3 w-3 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
88:           <span>
89:             Staff: use the invite link your boss sent you. Admin: use your email and password.
90:           </span>
91:         </div>
92:       </div>
93:     </div>
94:   )
95: }

================
File: src/components/scheduler/TeamTab.tsx
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useMemo } from 'react'
  4: import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import { toast } from 'sonner'
  6: import {
  7:   roleColor,
  8:   type ProfileView,
  9: } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
 10: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
 11: import {
 12:   Plus, Pencil, Trash2, X, Save, User, CheckCircle2, AlertCircle,
 13:   LayoutGrid, List, Star, Calendar,
 14: } from 'lucide-react'
 15: import { Accordion } from './Accordion'
 16: import { HelpTooltip } from './HelpTooltip'
 17: import { SkillPicker } from './SkillPicker'
 18: 
 19: type Profile = ProfileView & {
 20:   _assignmentCount?: number
 21: }
 22: 
 23: async function fetchProfiles(): Promise<Profile[]> {
 24:   const r = await fetch('/api/profiles')
 25:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load staff')
 26:   return r.json()
 27: }
 28: 
 29: const ROLE_TIERS = ['Chief', 'Senior', 'Junior', 'Assistant', 'Intern'] as const
 30: 
 31: export function TeamTab() {
 32:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 33:   const { data: profiles, isLoading } = useQuery({
 34:     queryKey: ['profiles-list'],
 35:     queryFn: fetchProfiles,
 36:   })
 37:   const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'directory' | 'edit'>('directory')
 38:   const [editing, setEditing] = useState<Profile | null>(null)
 39:   const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false)
 40: 
 41:   const deleteMutation = useMutation({
 42:     mutationFn: async (id: string) => {
 43:       const r = await fetch(`/api/profiles?id=${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
 44:       if (!r.ok) {
 45:         const j = await r.json()
 46:         throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed to delete')
 47:       }
 48:       return r.json()
 49:     },
 50:     onSuccess: () => {
 51:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['profiles-list'] })
 52:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
 53:       toast.success('Staff member removed')
 54:     },
 55:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to delete'),
 56:   })
 57: 
 58:   const handleDelete = (profile: Profile) => {
 59:     toast(`Remove ${profile.name}?`, {
 60:       description: 'Their assignments will also be removed. This cannot be undone.',
 61:       duration: 8000,
 62:       action: {
 63:         label: 'Remove',
 64:         onClick: () => deleteMutation.mutate(profile.id),
 65:       },
 66:     })
 67:   }
 68: 
 69:   const grouped = useMemo(() => {
 70:     if (!profiles) return {} as Record<string, Profile[]>
 71:     const g: Record<string, Profile[]> = {}
 72:     for (const p of profiles) {
 73:       (g[p.roleTier] ?? (g[p.roleTier] = [])).push(p)
 74:     }
 75:     return g
 76:   }, [profiles])
 77: 
 78:   const total = profiles?.length ?? 0
 79:   const signed = profiles?.filter(p => p.contractSigned).length ?? 0
 80: 
 81:   return (
 82:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
 83:       {/* Header */}
 84:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
 85:         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
 86:           <div className="min-w-0">
 87:             <h2 className="text-base font-semibold">Team</h2>
 88:             <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{total} staff · {signed} contracts signed · {total - signed} pending</p>
 89:           </div>
 90:           <HelpTooltip text="Directory shows staff cards (read-only). Switch to Edit mode to add/edit/remove staff. Each staff member has a role tier (Chief/Senior/Junior/Assistant/Intern), skills, availability window, and unavailable dates. Use the Invites tab to create login accounts for staff." />
 91:         </div>
 92:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0">
 93:           {/* View toggle */}
 94:           <div className="flex rounded-md border border-border/60 overflow-hidden">
 95:             <button
 96:               onClick={() => setViewMode('directory')}
 97:               className={cn(
 98:                 'px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[32px]',
 99:                 viewMode === 'directory'
100:                   ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300'
101:                   : 'text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted',
102:               )}
103:               aria-pressed={viewMode === 'directory'}
104:               title="Directory view"
105:             >
106:               <LayoutGrid className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
107:               <span className="hidden sm:inline">Directory</span>
108:             </button>
109:             <button
110:               onClick={() => setViewMode('edit')}
111:               className={cn(
112:                 'px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[32px] border-l border-border/60',
113:                 viewMode === 'edit'
114:                   ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300'
115:                   : 'text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted',
116:               )}
117:               aria-pressed={viewMode === 'edit'}
118:               title="Edit view"
119:             >
120:               <List className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
121:               <span className="hidden sm:inline">Edit</span>
122:             </button>
123:           </div>
124:           {viewMode === 'edit' && (
125:             <button
126:               onClick={() => setCreating(true)}
127:               className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 flex items-center gap-1.5 min-h-[32px]"
128:             >
129:               <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
130:               <span className="hidden sm:inline">Add staff</span>
131:             </button>
132:           )}
133:         </div>
134:       </div>
135: 
136:       {/* Content */}
137:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Team directory">
138:         {isLoading && (
139:           <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8">Loading team…</p>
140:         )}
141: 
142:         {viewMode === 'directory' ? (
143:           <DirectoryView grouped={grouped} />
144:         ) : (
145:           <EditView grouped={grouped} onEdit={p => setEditing(p)} onDelete={handleDelete} />
146:         )}
147:       </div>
148: 
149:       {(editing || creating) && (
150:         <StaffEditDrawer
151:           profile={editing}
152:           onClose={() => { setEditing(null); setCreating(false) }}
153:           onSaved={() => {
154:             setEditing(null)
155:             setCreating(false)
156:             qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['profiles-list'] })
157:             qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
158:           }}
159:         />
160:       )}
161:     </div>
162:   )
163: }
164: 
165: // ---------- Directory (read-only card grid) ----------
166: 
167: function DirectoryView({ grouped }: { grouped: Record<string, Profile[]> }) {
168:   return (
169:     <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
170:       {ROLE_TIERS.map(tier => {
171:         const list = grouped[tier]
172:         if (!list || list.length === 0) return null
173:         return (
174:           <Accordion
175:             key={tier}
176:             label={tier}
177:             count={list.length}
178:             labelClassName={roleColor(tier)}
179:             defaultOpen={tier === 'Chief' || tier === 'Senior'}
180:           >
181:             <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-3 pt-2">
182:               {list.map(p => <StaffCard key={p.id} profile={p} />)}
183:             </div>
184:           </Accordion>
185:         )
186:       })}
187:     </div>
188:   )
189: }
