191: function StaffCard({ profile }: { profile: Profile }) {
192:   const initials = profile.name.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')
193:   return (
194:     <article
195:       className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-4 hover:shadow-md hover:border-foreground/30 transition-all"
196:       tabIndex={0}
197:     >
198:       <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
199:         <div
200:           className="h-11 w-11 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-zinc-700 to-zinc-900 text-white font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0"
201:           aria-hidden="true"
202:         >
203:           {initials}
204:         </div>
205:         <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
206:           <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
207:             <h4 className="text-sm font-semibold truncate">{profile.name}</h4>
208:             {profile.contractSigned ? (
209:               <CheckCircle2 className="h-3 w-3 text-emerald-400 shrink-0" aria-label="Contract signed" />
210:             ) : (
211:               <span
212:                 className="h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-amber-400 shrink-0"
213:                 title="Contract not signed"
214:                 aria-label="Contract not signed"
215:               />
216:             )}
217:           </div>
218:           <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground truncate">{profile.role}</p>
219:         </div>
220:       </div>
221: 
222:       {profile.skillsList.length > 0 && (
223:         <div className="mt-3">
224:           <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1 flex items-center gap-1">
225:             <Star className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
226:             Skills
227:           </div>
228:           <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
229:             {profile.skillsList.map(s => (
230:               <span key={s} className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted/60 text-foreground/80">
231:                 {s}
232:               </span>
233:             ))}
234:           </div>
235:         </div>
236:       )}
237: 
238:       <dl className="mt-3 space-y-1 text-[11px]">
239:         {profile.available && (
240:           <div className="flex gap-1.5">
241:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0 flex items-center gap-0.5">
242:               <Calendar className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
243:               Available:
244:             </dt>
245:             <dd className="text-foreground/90">{profile.available}</dd>
246:           </div>
247:         )}
248:         {profile.unavailableList.length > 0 && (
249:           <div className="flex gap-1.5">
250:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0 flex items-center gap-0.5">
251:               <X className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
252:               Unavailable:
253:             </dt>
254:             <dd className="text-rose-300">{profile.unavailableList.length} date{profile.unavailableList.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}</dd>
255:           </div>
256:         )}
257:         {profile.notes && (
258:           <div className="flex gap-1.5">
259:             <dt className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0">Notes:</dt>
260:             <dd className="text-foreground/80 line-clamp-2">{profile.notes}</dd>
261:           </div>
262:         )}
263:       </dl>
264:     </article>
265:   )
266: }
267: 
268: // ---------- Edit (list with edit/delete buttons) ----------
269: 
270: function EditView({ grouped, onEdit, onDelete }: {
271:   grouped: Record<string, Profile[]>
272:   onEdit: (p: Profile) => void
273:   onDelete: (p: Profile) => void
274: }) {
275:   return (
276:     <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
277:       {ROLE_TIERS.map(tier => {
278:         const list = grouped[tier]
279:         if (!list || list.length === 0) return null
280:         return (
281:           <Accordion
282:             key={tier}
283:             label={tier}
284:             count={list.length}
285:             labelClassName={roleColor(tier)}
286:             defaultOpen={tier === 'Chief' || tier === 'Senior'}
287:           >
288:             <div className="space-y-1.5 pt-2">
289:               {list.map(p => (
290:                 <StaffRow key={p.id} profile={p} onEdit={() => onEdit(p)} onDelete={() => onDelete(p)} />
291:               ))}
292:             </div>
293:           </Accordion>
294:         )
295:       })}
296:     </div>
297:   )
298: }
299: 
300: function StaffRow({ profile, onEdit, onDelete }: {
301:   profile: Profile
302:   onEdit: () => void
303:   onDelete: () => void
304: }) {
305:   return (
306:     <div className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
307:       <div className="h-8 w-8 rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br from-zinc-700 to-zinc-900 text-white text-[10px] font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
308:         {profile.name.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')}
309:       </div>
310:       <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
311:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
312:           <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{profile.name}</p>
313:           {!profile.contractSigned && (
314:             <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full bg-amber-400 shrink-0" title="Contract not signed" />
315:           )}
316:         </div>
317:         <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">
318:           {profile.role}
319:           {profile.skillsList.length > 0 && ` · ${profile.skillsList.slice(0, 3).join(', ')}${profile.skillsList.length > 3 ? ` +${profile.skillsList.length - 3}` : ''}`}
320:         </div>
321:       </div>
322:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
323:         <button
324:           onClick={onEdit}
325:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
326:           aria-label={`Edit ${profile.name}`}
327:         >
328:           <Pencil className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
329:         </button>
330:         <button
331:           onClick={onDelete}
332:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-destructive/10 hover:text-destructive text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
333:           aria-label={`Remove ${profile.name}`}
334:         >
335:           <Trash2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
336:         </button>
337:       </div>
338:     </div>
339:   )
340: }
341: 
342: // ---------- Edit Drawer ----------
343: 
344: function StaffEditDrawer({ profile, onClose, onSaved }: {
345:   profile: Profile | null
346:   onClose: () => void
347:   onSaved: () => void
348: }) {
349:   const isEdit = !!profile
350:   const [form, setForm] = useState({
351:     name: profile?.name ?? '',
352:     sex: profile?.sex ?? '',
353:     role: profile?.role ?? '',
354:     roleTier: profile?.roleTier ?? 'Junior',
355:     skills: (profile?.skillsList ?? []).join(', '),
356:     available: profile?.available ?? '',
357:     unavailable: (profile?.unavailableList ?? []).join('\n'),
358:     contractSigned: profile?.contractSigned ?? false,
359:     notes: profile?.notes ?? '',
360:   })
361:   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
362: 
363:   const save = async () => {
364:     if (!form.name || !form.role) {
365:       toast.error('Name and role are required')
366:       return
367:     }
368:     setSaving(true)
369:     try {
370:       const payload = {
371:         ...form,
372:         sex: form.sex || null,
373:         skills: form.skills.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean),
374:         available: form.available || null,
375:         unavailable: form.unavailable
376:           .split('\n').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)
377:           .map(s => s.length === 10 ? s : `${s}-2026`),
378:         notes: form.notes || null,
379:       }
380:       const url = isEdit ? `/api/profiles?id=${profile!.id}` : '/api/profiles'
381:       const method = isEdit ? 'PUT' : 'POST'
382:       const r = await fetch(url, {
383:         method,
384:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
385:         body: JSON.stringify(payload),
386:       })
387:       const j = await r.json()
388:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed to save')
389:       toast.success(isEdit ? 'Staff updated' : 'Staff added')
390:       onSaved()
391:     } catch (e: any) {
392:       toast.error(e.message || 'Save failed')
393:     } finally {
394:       setSaving(false)
395:     }
396:   }
397: 
398:   return (
399:     <div
400:       className="absolute inset-y-0 right-0 z-30 w-full sm:w-[28rem] shadow-2xl border-l border-border/60 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur-md flex flex-col"
401:       role="dialog"
402:       aria-modal="true"
403:       aria-label={isEdit ? `Edit ${profile?.name}` : 'Add new staff member'}
404:     >
405:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 flex items-center justify-between">
406:         <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
407:           <User className="h-4 w-4" />
408:           {isEdit ? 'Edit staff' : 'New staff'}
409:         </h2>
410:         <button
411:           onClick={onClose}
412:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
413:           aria-label="Close"
414:         >
415:           <X className="h-4 w-4" />
416:         </button>
417:       </div>
418: 
419:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Staff details form">
420:         <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
421:           <Field label="Name" required>
422:             <input
423:               value={form.name}
424:               onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, name: e.target.value }))}
425:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
426:               aria-required="true"
427:             />
428:           </Field>
429:           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
430:             <Field label="Sex">
431:               <select
432:                 value={form.sex}
433:                 onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, sex: e.target.value }))}
434:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
435:               >
436:                 <option value="">—</option>
437:                 <option value="Male">Male</option>
438:                 <option value="Female">Female</option>
439:                 <option value="Other">Other</option>
440:               </select>
441:             </Field>
442:             <Field label="Role tier">
443:               <select
444:                 value={form.roleTier}
445:                 onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, roleTier: e.target.value }))}
446:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
447:               >
448:                 {ROLE_TIERS.map(t => <option key={t} value={t}>{t}</option>)}
449:               </select>
450:             </Field>
451:           </div>
452:           <Field label="Role (full title)" required>
453:             <input
454:               value={form.role}
455:               onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, role: e.target.value }))}
456:               placeholder="e.g. Senior Instructor"
457:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
458:               aria-required="true"
459:             />
460:           </Field>
461:           <SkillPicker
462:             selected={form.skills.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)}
463:             onChange={skills => setForm(f => ({ ...f, skills: skills.join(', ') }))}
464:             allowCatalogManagement
465:             label="Skills"
466:           />
467:           <Field label="Availability window">
468:             <input
469:               value={form.available}
470:               onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, available: e.target.value }))}
471:               placeholder="e.g. July, August"
472:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
473:             />
474:           </Field>
475:           <Field label="Unavailable dates (one per line, YYYY-MM-DD)">
476:             <textarea
477:               value={form.unavailable}
478:               onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, unavailable: e.target.value }))}
479:               rows={4}
480:               placeholder="2026-07-09&#10;2026-07-11"
481:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400 font-mono"
482:             />
483:           </Field>
484:           <Field label="Notes">
485:             <textarea
486:               value={form.notes}
487:               onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, notes: e.target.value }))}
488:               rows={2}
489:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
490:             />
491:           </Field>
492: 
493:           <label className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-muted/40">
494:             <input
495:               type="checkbox"
496:               checked={form.contractSigned}
497:               onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, contractSigned: e.target.checked }))}
498:               className="h-4 w-4 rounded accent-emerald-500"
499:             />
500:             <span className="text-sm flex items-center gap-1.5">
501:               {form.contractSigned ? (
502:                 <CheckCircle2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-emerald-400" />
503:               ) : (
504:                 <AlertCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-amber-400" />
505:               )}
506:               Contract signed
507:             </span>
508:           </label>
509:         </div>
510:       </div>
511: 
512:       <div className="p-3 border-t border-border/60 flex justify-end gap-2">
513:         <button
514:           onClick={onClose}
515:           className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[36px]"
516:         >
517:           Cancel
518:         </button>
519:         <button
520:           onClick={save}
521:           disabled={saving}
522:           className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 flex items-center gap-1.5 disabled:opacity-50 min-h-[36px]"
523:         >
524:           <Save className="h-3 w-3" />
525:           {saving ? 'Saving…' : 'Save'}
526:         </button>
527:       </div>
528:     </div>
529:   )
530: }
531: 
532: function Field({ label, required, children }: { label: string; required?: boolean; children: React.ReactNode }) {
533:   return (
534:     <div>
535:       <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
536:         {label}{required && <span className="text-rose-400 ml-0.5">*</span>}
537:       </label>
538:       {children}
539:     </div>
540:   )
541: }

================
File: src/lib/auth-helpers.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from './db'
 3: import { getSessionFromRequest } from './session'
 4: 
 5: /**
 6:  * Get the authenticated user from a signed session cookie.
 7:  * The cookie is encrypted (iron-session), so it can't be forged.
 8:  */
 9: export async function getAuthUser(req: NextRequest) {
10:   const session = await getSessionFromRequest(req)
11:   if (!session.userId) return null
12: 
13:   const result = await db.execute({
14:     sql: `SELECT u.*, p.name as profileName, p.roleTier as profileRoleTier, p.role as profileRole,
15:           p.skills as profileSkills, p.unavailable as profileUnavailable, p.id as profileId
16:           FROM User u LEFT JOIN Profile p ON u.profileId = p.id WHERE u.id = ?`,
17:     args: [session.userId],
18:   })
19: 
20:   if (result.rows.length === 0) return null
21:   const row = result.rows[0] as any
22:   if (!row.claimedAt) return null
23: 
24:   return {
25:     id: row.id,
26:     name: row.name,
27:     email: row.email,
28:     role: row.role,
29:     profileId: row.profileId ?? null,
30:     passwordHash: row.passwordHash,
31:     claimedAt: row.claimedAt,
32:     emailNotifications: row.emailNotifications === null || row.emailNotifications === undefined ? true : !!row.emailNotifications,
33:     profile: row.profileId ? {
34:       id: row.profileId,
35:       name: row.profileName,
36:       roleTier: row.profileRoleTier,
37:       role: row.profileRole,
38:       skills: row.profileSkills,
39:       unavailable: row.profileUnavailable,
40:     } : null,
41:   }
42: }
43: 
44: /**
45:  * Require admin auth for a route handler.
46:  * Returns a 401/403 response if not admin, or null if authorized.
47:  */
48: export async function requireAdmin(req: NextRequest) {
49:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
50:   if (!user) {
51:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
52:   }
53:   if (user.role !== 'admin') {
54:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Admin access required' }, { status: 403 })
55:   }
56:   return null
57: }
58: 
59: /**
60:  * Require any authenticated user (admin or instructor).
61:  */
62: export async function requireAuth(req: NextRequest) {
63:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
64:   if (!user) {
65:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
66:   }
67:   return null
68: }

================
File: src/lib/conflicts.ts
================
  1: // Pure conflict-detection logic for the RA Syncbot scheduler.
  2: // Imported by both server (API route) and client (UI ring feedback).
  3: 
  4: export type ConflictLevel = 'ok' | 'warning' | 'error'
  5: 
  6: export type ConflictResult = {
  7:   level: ConflictLevel
  8:   reasons: string[]
  9: }
 10: 
 11: export type ProfileLite = {
 12:   id: string
 13:   name: string
 14:   roleTier: string // Chief | Senior | Junior | Assistant | Intern
 15:   skills: string[] // parsed from comma-separated
 16:   unavailable: string[] // YYYY-MM-DD
 17: }
 18: 
 19: export type AssignmentLite = {
 20:   id: string
 21:   profileId: string
 22:   assignedDate: string // YYYY-MM-DD
 23:   startTime: string // "09:00"
 24:   endTime: string // "15:00"
 25:   eventName: string
 26: }
 27: 
 28: export type EventLite = {
 29:   id: string
 30:   name: string
 31:   startDate: string // YYYY-MM-DD
 32:   endDate: string // YYYY-MM-DD
 33:   startTime: string
 34:   endTime: string
 35:   requiredInstructors: number
 36:   requiredSkills: string[]
 37:   currentAssignees: number // already-assigned count for the target date
 38: }
 39: 
 40: // ---------- Helpers ----------
 41: 
 42: export function parseSkills(raw?: string): string[] {
 43:   if (!raw) return []
 44:   return raw.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)
 45: }
 46: 
 47: export function parseDates(raw?: string): string[] {
 48:   if (!raw) return []
 49:   return raw.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)
 50: }
 51: 
 52: // Convert "09:00" → minutes since midnight
 53: function timeToMinutes(t: string): number {
 54:   const [h, m] = t.split(':').map(Number)
 55:   return h * 60 + (m || 0)
 56: }
 57: 
 58: function timeRangesOverlap(
 59:   startA: string, endA: string, startB: string, endB: string,
 60: ): boolean {
 61:   const sA = timeToMinutes(startA)
 62:   const eA = timeToMinutes(endA)
 63:   const sB = timeToMinutes(startB)
 64:   const eB = timeToMinutes(endB)
 65:   return sA < eB && sB < eA
 66: }
 67: 
 68: function addDaysISO(iso: string, days: number): string {
 69:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
 70:   d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + days)
 71:   return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
 72: }
 73: 
 74: // ---------- The three checks from the blueprint ----------
 75: 
 76: /**
 77:  * Check 1 — Temporal Overlap (Double-Booking).
 78:  * Hard error if the same person is already assigned to another event
 79:  * whose time block overlaps on the same day.
 80:  */
 81: export function checkTemporalOverlap(
 82:   profile: ProfileLite,
 83:   date: string,
 84:   event: EventLite,
 85:   existing: AssignmentLite[],
 86: ): ConflictResult {
 87:   const reasons: string[] = []
 88:   for (const a of existing) {
 89:     if (a.profileId !== profile.id) continue
 90:     if (a.assignedDate !== date) continue
 91:     if (timeRangesOverlap(event.startTime, event.endTime, a.startTime, a.endTime)) {
 92:       reasons.push(
 93:         `Already assigned to "${a.eventName}" ${a.startTime}–${a.endTime} on ${date}`,
 94:       )
 95:     }
 96:   }
 97:   return { level: reasons.length ? 'error' : 'ok', reasons }
 98: }
 99: 
100: /**
101:  * Check 1b — Availability.
102:  * Hard error if the person is marked unavailable on the target date.
103:  */
104: export function checkAvailability(
105:   profile: ProfileLite,
106:   date: string,
107: ): ConflictResult {
108:   if (profile.unavailable.includes(date)) {
109:     return {
110:       level: 'error',
111:       reasons: [`Marked unavailable on ${date}`],
112:     }
113:   }
114:   return { level: 'ok', reasons: [] }
115: }
116: 
117: /**
118:  * Check 2 — Skill & Role Matching (INFORMATIONAL, non-blocking).
119:  *
120:  * Returns a soft warning listing which required skills the instructor doesn't have.
121:  * This never blocks assignment — the boss can assign anyone. The warning is shown
122:  * so the boss knows who might need practice gear (drones, robots, etc.).
123:  */
124: export function checkSkillMatch(
125:   profile: ProfileLite,
126:   event: EventLite,
127: ): ConflictResult {
128:   const reasons: string[] = []
129:   const missing = event.requiredSkills.filter(s => !profile.skills.includes(s))
130:   if (missing.length > 0) {
131:     reasons.push(`Missing skills: ${missing.join(', ')}`)
132:   }
133:   return { level: reasons.length ? 'warning' : 'ok', reasons }
134: }
135: 
136: /**
137:  * Get the list of missing skills for a profile on an event.
138:  * Used by the UI to show "Needs practice: Drones, Python" badges.
139:  */
140: export function getMissingSkills(
141:   profileSkills: string[],
142:   eventSkills: string[],
143: ): string[] {
144:   return eventSkills.filter(s => !profileSkills.includes(s))
145: }
146: 
147: /**
148:  * Check 3 — Fatigue Tracking.
149:  * Soft warning if assigning the person would push them past 5 consecutive
150:  * working days.
151:  */
152: export function checkFatigue(
153:   profile: ProfileLite,
154:   date: string,
155:   existing: AssignmentLite[],
156: ): ConflictResult {
157:   const myDates = new Set(
158:     existing
159:       .filter(a => a.profileId === profile.id)
160:       .map(a => a.assignedDate),
161:   )
162:   myDates.add(date)
163: 
164:   // Walk backwards from `date` to count consecutive working days
165:   let back = 0
166:   let cursor = date
167:   while (myDates.has(cursor)) {
168:     back++
169:     cursor = addDaysISO(cursor, -1)
170:   }
171:   // Walk forwards
172:   let fwd = 0
173:   cursor = date
174:   while (myDates.has(cursor)) {
175:     fwd++
176:     cursor = addDaysISO(cursor, 1)
177:   }
178:   const streak = back + fwd - 1 // `date` counted twice
179:   if (streak > 5) {
180:     return {
181:       level: 'warning',
182:       reasons: [`Would create a ${streak}-day consecutive work streak (max 5)`],
183:     }
184:   }
185:   return { level: 'ok', reasons: [] }
186: }
187: 
188: /**
189:  * Run all checks and return the highest-severity result.
190:  * Error > Warning > OK.
191:  */
192: export function runAllChecks(args: {
193:   profile: ProfileLite
194:   date: string
195:   event: EventLite
196:   existing: AssignmentLite[]
197: }): ConflictResult {
198:   const { profile, date, event, existing } = args
199:   const checks = [
200:     checkAvailability(profile, date),
201:     checkTemporalOverlap(profile, date, event, existing),
202:     checkSkillMatch(profile, event),
203:     checkFatigue(profile, date, existing),
204:   ]
205:   const allReasons: string[] = []
206:   let level: ConflictLevel = 'ok'
207:   for (const c of checks) {
208:     if (c.level === 'error') level = 'error'
209:     else if (c.level === 'warning' && level !== 'error') level = 'warning'
210:     allReasons.push(...c.reasons)
211:   }
212:   return { level, reasons: allReasons }
213: }
214: 
215: /**
216:  * Capacity check — how many more instructors does the event need on this date?
217:  */
218: export function capacityStatus(event: EventLite): {
219:   filled: number
220:   needed: number
221:   isFull: boolean
222: } {
223:   const filled = event.currentAssignees
224:   const needed = event.requiredInstructors
225:   return { filled, needed, isFull: filled >= needed }
226: }

================
File: README.md
================
  1: # RA Syncbot
  2: 
  3: **Drag-and-drop camp & workshop instructor scheduling for RA Syncbot Ltd (Barbados).**
  4: 
  5: RA Syncbot replaces a chaotic spreadsheet-based system for managing ~20 instructors across 15+ summer camps and workshops. Admins drag instructors onto events; instructors log in to view their schedule, opt in to events, and sync their personal calendar.
  6: 
  7: - **Live site:** [ra-syncbot.com](https://www.ra-syncbot.com)
  8: - **Platform:** Vercel + Turso + Resend
  9: - **Stack:** Next.js 16, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS 4, shadcn/ui (pruned), @dnd-kit, TanStack Query
 10: 
 11: ---
 12: 
 13: ## Features
 14: 
 15: ### Admin
 16: - **Drag-and-drop scheduler** — drag instructors from the roster rail onto any event/day; supports multi-day "drop on all days" handle.
 17: - **Mobile tap-to-assign** — same workflow on phones via tap-to-select-then-tap-event.
 18: - **Week + month calendar views** — week view for editing, month view for overview.
 19: - **Conflict detection** — double-bookings, fatigue (3+ consecutive days), skill gaps, and unavailable-date violations are flagged in real time.
 20: - **Event management** — create, edit, delete, and archive events; set required skills, host, location, age range, participant count, setup date/time, and shirt colors.
 21: - **Equipment coordination** — post equipment lists per event; instructors claim items they'll bring; transport matchmaking.
 22: - **Team management** — manage instructor profiles, skills, contracts, and notes.
 23: - **Skill catalog** — reusable skill catalog (define once, reuse everywhere); add/delete from the picker.
 24: - **Invites** — generate invite links for new instructors; revoke or resend at any time.
 25: - **Workload dashboard** — per-instructor assignment counts, day breakdowns, opt-in summary.
 26: - **Conflict summary tab** — overview of every flagged conflict across all events.
 27: - **Acknowledgment tracking** — see which instructors confirmed vs. declined their assignments.
 28: - **Print & PDF export** — print the current week or export a PDF.
 29: - **CSV export** — bulk export all assignments.
 30: - **Send-now button** — flush pending digest emails immediately instead of waiting for the 8am digest.
 31: 
 32: ### Instructor
 33: - **3-tab view** — My Assignments / Opt In / Calendar.
 34: - **Acknowledge button** — confirm or decline each assignment; admin sees your response.
 35: - **Notification bell** — in-app bell with unread badge; no need to check email.
 36: - **Email toggle** — turn email notifications on/off per account (bell always works).
 37: - **Opt-in system** — express interest (interested / available / unavailable) on any event.
 38: - **Equipment claims** — claim items you'll bring; mark if you can transport; the boss arranges dropoff.
 39: - **Availability management** — mark dates you can't work; the admin scheduler respects these.
 40: - **Calendar sync** — subscribe to a personal iCal feed (`/api/ical?token=<userId>`).
 41: - **Email notifications** — smart digest system: instant for urgent changes (<72h), daily digest otherwise.
 42: - **Account claim flow** — invite links require email verification (6-digit code) before account creation.
 43: 
 44: ### Cross-cutting
 45: - **Smart email digest** — changes to events >72h away queue for the 8am digest; changes to events <72h away fire instantly; opt-in receipts always instant; admin can flush the queue manually.
 46: - **Light/dark mode** toggle with system preference default.
 47: - **PWA installable** — add to home screen on iOS/Android.
 48: - **WCAG 2.1 AA** — 16px base text, 12px floor, 44px touch targets, ARIA roles, full keyboard navigation.
 49: - **Esc-to-close** — drawers, modals, and tap selections all close on Esc.
 50: - **Auto-archive** — past events are auto-archived via a cron-style API endpoint.
 51: - **Past-date protection** — past dates are visually dimmed and drop-disabled at the API level.
 52: - **Barbados timezone** — all date comparisons use America/Barbados (AST, UTC-4).
 53: 
 54: ---
 55: 
 56: ## Tech Stack
 57: 
 58: | Layer | Technology |
 59: |---|---|
 60: | Framework | Next.js 16 (App Router, Turbopack) |
 61: | Language | TypeScript 5 |
 62: | Styling | Tailwind CSS 4 + `tw-animate-css` |
 63: | UI primitives | shadcn/ui (pruned to 10 components) + Radix |
 64: | Drag-and-drop | `@dnd-kit/core` |
 65: | Server state | TanStack Query v5 |
 66: | Auth | bcryptjs + signed HMAC cookies (Web Crypto API) |
 67: | Database | Turso (libSQL/SQLite cloud) via `@libsql/client` |
 68: | Email | Resend (via `fetch()`, no SDK) |
 69: | Hosting | Vercel (free tier) |
 70: | Calendar sync | iCal feed (`/api/ical`) |
 71: | PWA | `manifest.json` + icons |
 72: 
 73: ---
 74: 
 75: ## Quick Start
 76: 
 77: ### Prerequisites
 78: - Node.js 18+ or Bun
 79: - A Turso database (free tier works)
 80: - (Optional) A Resend account for email notifications
 81: 
 82: ### Install & run locally
 83: 
 84: ```bash
 85: # 1. Install dependencies
 86: bun install
 87: 
 88: # 2. Copy env template and fill in your values
 89: cp .env.example .env
 90: # Edit .env — at minimum set TURSO_URL and TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN
 91: 
 92: # 3. Run the database seed (creates schema + demo data)
 93: bun run seed
 94: 
 95: # 3b. (Existing deployments only) Run migrations to add new tables/columns
 96: bun run migrate
 97: 
 98: # 4. Start the dev server
 99: bun run dev
100: ```
101: 
102: Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) and log in with the admin credentials created by the seed script.
103: 
104: ### Default admin (from seed)
105: - Email: `robotadventuresltd@gmail.com`
106: - Password: `admin123`
107: 
108: > ⚠️ **Change this password immediately** in production via the account menu → Change password.

112: ## Project Structure
113: 
114: ```
115: .
116: ├── src/
117: │   ├── app/
118: │   │   ├── api/                  # API routes (see API.md)
119: │   │   ├── globals.css           # Tailwind + WCAG typography rules
120: │   │   ├── layout.tsx            # Root layout, fonts, theme provider
121: │   │   ├── page.tsx              # Main app — auth gate, tabs, drag-and-drop
122: │   │   └── providers.tsx         # TanStack Query + theme + Sonner toaster
123: │   ├── components/
124: │   │   ├── scheduler/            # App-specific components (20 files)
125: │   │   └── ui/                   # Pruned shadcn/ui (10 components)
126: │   ├── hooks/
127: │   │   └── use-is-mobile.ts      # Mobile detection (breakpoint-based)
128: │   └── lib/
129: │       ├── auth-helpers.ts       # requireAdmin / requireAuth / getAuthUser
130: │       ├── conflicts.ts          # Pure conflict-detection functions
131: │       ├── db.ts                 # Turso client (auto-fallback to local SQLite)
132: │       ├── email.ts              # Resend API wrapper
133: │       ├── export-utils.ts       # CSV export helper
134: │       ├── scheduler-types.ts    # Shared types + date helpers
135: │       ├── session.ts            # HMAC-signed cookies (Web Crypto)
136: │       └── utils.ts              # cn() classname merger
137: ├── public/                       # logo, icons, manifest, robots.txt
138: ├── scripts/
139: │   └── seed.ts                   # Database seed (run with `bun run seed`)
140: ├── .env.example
141: ├── next.config.ts
142: ├── package.json
143: ├── tailwind.config.ts
144: ├── tsconfig.json
145: └── vercel.json
146: ```

  1: /**
  2:  * Seed script — populates the database with real data from the source PDF.
  3:  *
  4:  * Usage:
  5:  *   bun run scripts/seed.ts
  6:  *
  7:  * Environment variables (read from .env):
  8:  *   TURSO_URL          — libsql:// connection string (Turso cloud)
  9:  *   TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN   — Turso auth token
 10:  *   DATABASE_URL       — fallback for local SQLite (file:./db/custom.db)
 11:  *
 12:  * This script clears ALL existing data before inserting.
 13:  * It is safe to run multiple times.
 14:  */
 15: 
 16: import { createClient } from '@libsql/client'
 17: import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs'
 18: 
 19: // ── Database connection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
 20: 
 21: const tursoUrl = process.env.TURSO_URL
 22: const tursoAuthToken = process.env.TURSO_AUTH_TOKEN
 23: 
 24: const db = tursoUrl
 25:   ? createClient({ url: tursoUrl, authToken: tursoAuthToken })
 26:   : createClient({ url: process.env.DATABASE_URL || 'file:./db/custom.db' })

121: // ── Main ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
122: 
123: async function main() {
124:   console.log('Clearing existing data...')
125:   await db.execute('DELETE FROM OptIn')
126:   await db.execute('DELETE FROM Assignment')
127:   await db.execute('DELETE FROM EventSkill')
128:   await db.execute('DELETE FROM Event')
129:   await db.execute('DELETE FROM User')
130:   await db.execute('DELETE FROM Profile')
131: 
132:   // Seed staff
133:   console.log(`Seeding ${STAFF.length} staff profiles...`)
134:   const profileIds: Record<string, string> = {}
135:   for (const s of STAFF) {
136:     const id = crypto.randomUUID()
137:     profileIds[s.name] = id
138:     await db.execute({
139:       sql: `INSERT INTO Profile (id, name, sex, role, roleTier, skills, available, unavailable, contractSigned, notes, createdAt, updatedAt)
140:             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
141:       args: [id, s.name, s.sex ?? null, s.role, s.roleTier, s.skills, s.available ?? null, s.unavailable ?? null, !!s.contractSigned, s.notes ?? null],
142:     })
143:   }
144: 
145:   // Seed events
146:   console.log(`Seeding ${EVENTS.length} events...`)
147:   const eventIds: Record<string, string> = {}
148:   for (const e of EVENTS) {
149:     const id = crypto.randomUUID()
150:     eventIds[e.code] = id
151:     await db.execute({
152:       sql: `INSERT INTO Event (id, code, name, host, location, description, startDate, endDate, startTime, endTime, status, ageRange, participantCount, requiredInstructors, notes, hostColor, createdAt, updatedAt)
153:             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
154:       args: [id, e.code, e.name, e.host, e.location, e.description,
155:         new Date(e.startDate + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString(),
156:         new Date(e.endDate + 'T23:59:59.000Z').toISOString(),
157:         e.startTime, e.endTime, e.status, e.ageRange, e.participantCount, e.requiredInstructors, e.notes, e.hostColor],
158:     })
159:     for (const skill of e.skills) {
160:       await db.execute({ sql: 'INSERT INTO EventSkill (id, eventId, skillName) VALUES (?, ?, ?)', args: [crypto.randomUUID(), id, skill] })
161:     }
162:   }
163: 
164:   // Seed assignments
165:   console.log(`Seeding ${PRESET_ASSIGNMENTS.length} preset assignments...`)
166:   for (const a of PRESET_ASSIGNMENTS) {
167:     const eventId = eventIds[a.eventCode]
168:     if (!eventId) { console.warn(`  Event not found: ${a.eventCode}`); continue }
169:     for (const s of a.staff) {
170:       const profileId = profileIds[s.name]
171:       if (!profileId) { console.warn(`  Staff not found: ${s.name}`); continue }
172:       await db.execute({
173:         sql: `INSERT INTO Assignment (id, eventId, profileId, assignedDate, status, shirtColor, isAlternative, createdAt, updatedAt)
174:               VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, 'Confirmed', ?, 0, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
175:         args: [crypto.randomUUID(), eventId, profileId, new Date(a.date + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString(), s.shirt ?? null],
176:       })
177:     }
178:   }
179: 
180:   // Create admin user (Jelani Payne — Chief Instructor)
181:   console.log('Creating admin user...')
182:   const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash('changeme', 10)
183:   await db.execute({
184:     sql: `INSERT INTO User (id, name, email, role, passwordHash, profileId, inviteToken, claimedAt, createdAt, updatedAt)
185:           VALUES (?, 'Jelani Payne', 'jelani@ra-syncbot.com', 'admin', ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
186:     args: [crypto.randomUUID(), passwordHash, profileIds['Jelani Payne'] ?? null, crypto.randomUUID()],
187:   })
188: 
189:   // Summary
190:   console.log('\n✓ Seed complete.')
191:   console.log(`  Profiles:    ${STAFF.length}`)
192:   console.log(`  Events:      ${EVENTS.length}`)
193:   console.log(`  Assignments: ${PRESET_ASSIGNMENTS.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.staff.length, 0)}`)
194:   console.log(`  Users:       1 (admin)`)
195:   console.log(`\n  Admin login: jelani@ra-syncbot.com / changeme`)
196:   console.log(`  ⚠️  Change this password immediately after first login!`)
197: }
198: 
199: main()
200:   .catch((e) => { console.error(e); process.exit(1) })
201:   .finally(() => db.close())

================
File: src/app/api/assignments/bulk/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { requireAdmin } from "@/lib/auth-helpers"
 3: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 4: 
 5: // POST /api/assignments/bulk — assign to all days of an event
 6: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 7:   const authBulk = await requireAdmin(req); if (authBulk) return authBulk;
 8:   const body = await req.json()
 9:   const { eventId, profileId } = body as { eventId: string; profileId: string }
10:   if (!eventId || !profileId) {
11:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing eventId or profileId' }, { status: 400 })
12:   }
13: 
14:   // Get the event
15:   const eventResult = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [eventId] })
16:   if (eventResult.rows.length === 0) {
17:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Event not found' }, { status: 404 })
18:   }
19:   const event = eventResult.rows[0] as any
20: 
21:   if (event.status === 'Draft' || event.status === 'Cancelled' || event.status === 'Archived') {
22:     return NextResponse.json({ error: `Cannot assign to a ${event.status} event` }, { status: 400 })
23:   }
24: 
25:   // Build the list of dates
26:   let dates: string[]
27:   if (event.specificDates) {
28:     dates = event.specificDates.split(',').map((s: string) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)
29:   } else {
30:     dates = []
31:     const d = new Date(event.startDate)
32:     const end = new Date(event.endDate)
33:     while (d <= end) {
34:       dates.push(d.toISOString().slice(0, 10))
35:       d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 1)
36:     }
37:   }
38: 
39:   // Block assignments on past dates
40:   const today = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
41:     timeZone: 'America/Barbados',
42:     year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
43:   }).format(new Date())
44: 
45:   let created = 0, existing = 0, conflicts = 0, skippedPast = 0
46: 
47:   for (const date of dates) {
48:     // Skip past dates
49:     if (date < today) {
50:       skippedPast++
51:       continue
52:     }
53: 
54:     // Check if already assigned
55:     const existingResult = await db.execute({
56:       sql: 'SELECT id FROM Assignment WHERE eventId = ? AND profileId = ? AND assignedDate = ?',
57:       args: [eventId, profileId, new Date(date + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString()],
58:     })
59: 
60:     if (existingResult.rows.length > 0) {
61:       existing++
62:       continue
63:     }
64: 
65:     // Create the assignment
66:     try {
67:       await db.execute({
68:         sql: `INSERT INTO Assignment (id, eventId, profileId, assignedDate, status, isAlternative, shirtColor, createdAt, updatedAt)
69:               VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, 'Assigned', 0, NULL, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
70:         args: [crypto.randomUUID(), eventId, profileId, new Date(date + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString()],
71:       })
72:       created++
73:     } catch {
74:       existing++
75:     }
76:   }
77: 
78:   return NextResponse.json({ created, existing, conflicts, skippedPast })
79: }

File: src/app/api/auth/me/route.ts
================
 1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
 3: import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs'
 4: import { getAuthUser } from '@/lib/auth-helpers'
 5: import { saveSessionToResponse } from '@/lib/session'
 6: 
 7: // Re-export getAuthUser for backward compatibility (other routes import from here)
 8: 
 9: // GET /api/auth/me — returns the currently logged-in user (or null)
10: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
11:   const user = await getAuthUser(req)
12:   if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ user: null })
13:   return NextResponse.json({
14:     user: {
15:       id: user.id,
16:       name: user.name,
17:       email: user.email,
18:       role: user.role,
19:       profileId: user.profileId,
20:       emailNotifications: user.emailNotifications,
21:       profile: user.profile,
22:     },
23:   })
24: }
25: 
26: // POST /api/auth/login — email + password login
27: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
28:   const body = await req.json()
29:   const { email, password } = body as { email: string; password: string }
30:   if (!email || !password) {
31:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Email and password are required' }, { status: 400 })
32:   }
33: 
34:   const result = await db.execute({
35:     sql: 'SELECT * FROM User WHERE email = ?',
36:     args: [email],
37:   })
38: 
39:   if (result.rows.length === 0) {
40:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid email or password' }, { status: 401 })
41:   }
42: 
43:   const user = result.rows[0] as any
44:   if (!user.passwordHash || !user.claimedAt) {
45:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid email or password' }, { status: 401 })
46:   }
47: 
48:   // Rate limiting: check if this email has had >5 failed attempts in the last 15 minutes
49:   // (simplified — uses a simple counter in the User table)
50:   const valid = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.passwordHash)
51:   if (!valid) {
52:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid email or password' }, { status: 401 })
53:   }
54: 
55:   // Get profile if linked
56:   let profile = null
57:   if (user.profileId) {
58:     const profileResult = await db.execute({
59:       sql: 'SELECT * FROM Profile WHERE id = ?',
60:       args: [user.profileId],
61:     })
62:     if (profileResult.rows.length > 0) {
63:       const p = profileResult.rows[0] as any
64:       profile = {
65:         id: p.id,
66:         name: p.name,
67:         roleTier: p.roleTier,
68:         role: p.role,
69:         skills: p.skills,
70:         unavailable: p.unavailable,
71:       }
72:     }
73:   }
74: 
75:   const res = NextResponse.json({
76:     user: {
77:       id: user.id,
78:       name: user.name,
79:       email: user.email,
80:       role: user.role,
81:       profileId: user.profileId,
82:       emailNotifications: user.emailNotifications,
83:       profile,
84:     },
85:   })
86:   // Save signed session (encrypted cookie — can't be forged)
87:   await saveSessionToResponse(res, { userId: user.id })
88:   return res
89: }

  1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

  5: function parseList(s: string | null | undefined): string[] {
  6:   if (!s) return []
  7:   return s.split(',').map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean)
  8: }
  9: 
 10: // GET /api/events — list all events
 11: export async function GET() {
 12:   const result = await db.execute(`SELECT * FROM Event ORDER BY startDate ASC`)
 13: 
 14:   // Get skills + assignment counts + opt-in counts
 15:   const events = []
 16:   for (const e of result.rows as any[]) {
 17:     const skills = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT skillName FROM EventSkill WHERE eventId = ?', args: [e.id] })
 18:     const assignments = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM Assignment WHERE eventId = ?', args: [e.id] })
 19:     const optIns = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM OptIn WHERE eventId = ?', args: [e.id] })
 20:     events.push({
 21:       ...e,
 22:       startDate: e.startDate?.slice(0, 10),
 23:       endDate: e.endDate?.slice(0, 10),
 24:       specificDatesList: parseList(e.specificDates),
 25:       requiredSkills: skills.rows.map((s: any) => s.skillName),
 26:       _assignmentCount: (assignments.rows[0] as any).count,
 27:       _optInCount: (optIns.rows[0] as any).count,
 28:     })
 29:   }
 30: 
 31:   return NextResponse.json(events)
 32: }
 33: 
 34: // POST /api/events — create
 35: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 36:   const authCheck = await requireAdmin(req); if (authCheck) return authCheck;
 37:   const body = await req.json()
 38:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
 39: 
 40:   await db.execute({
 41:     sql: `INSERT INTO Event (id, code, name, host, location, description, lengthDays, startDate, endDate,
 42:           startTime, endTime, status, specificDates, ageRange, participantCount, requiredInstructors,
 43:           notes, hostColor, setupDate, setupTime, createdAt, updatedAt)
 44:           VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
 45:     args: [
 46:       id, body.code ?? null, body.name, body.host, body.location ?? null, body.description ?? null,
 47:       body.lengthDays ?? null,
 48:       new Date(body.startDate).toISOString(),
 49:       new Date(body.endDate).toISOString(),
 50:       body.startTime ?? '09:00', body.endTime ?? '15:00',
 51:       body.status ?? 'Confirmed',
 52:       Array.isArray(body.specificDates) && body.specificDates.length ? body.specificDates.join(',') : null,
 53:       body.ageRange ?? null, body.participantCount ?? null, body.requiredInstructors ?? 2,
 54:       body.notes ?? null, body.hostColor ?? 'slate',
 55:       body.setupDate ? new Date(body.setupDate + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString() : null,
 56:       body.setupTime ?? null,
 57:     ],
 58:   })
 59: 
 60:   // Insert skills
 61:   if (Array.isArray(body.skills)) {
 62:     for (const skillName of body.skills) {
 63:       await db.execute({
 64:         sql: 'INSERT INTO EventSkill (id, eventId, skillName) VALUES (?, ?, ?)',
 65:         args: [crypto.randomUUID(), id, skillName],
 66:       })
 67:     }
 68:   }
 69: 
 70:   const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
 71:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows[0], { status: 201 })
 72: }
 73: 
 74: // PUT /api/events?id=...
 75: export async function PUT(req: NextRequest) {
 76:   const authCheck2 = await requireAdmin(req); if (authCheck2) return authCheck2;
 77:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
 78:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
 79:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
 80:   const body = await req.json()
 81: 
 82:   // Replace skills if provided
 83:   if (Array.isArray(body.skills)) {
 84:     await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM EventSkill WHERE eventId = ?', args: [id] })
 85:     for (const skillName of body.skills) {
 86:       await db.execute({
 87:         sql: 'INSERT INTO EventSkill (id, eventId, skillName) VALUES (?, ?, ?)',
 88:         args: [crypto.randomUUID(), id, skillName],
 89:       })
 90:     }
 91:   }
 92: 
 93:   const updates: string[] = []
 94:   const args: unknown[] = []
 95:   const fields: Record<string, string> = {
 96:     code: 'code', name: 'name', host: 'host', hostColor: 'hostColor',
 97:     location: 'location', description: 'description', lengthDays: 'lengthDays',
 98:     startTime: 'startTime', endTime: 'endTime', status: 'status',
 99:     ageRange: 'ageRange', participantCount: 'participantCount',
100:     requiredInstructors: 'requiredInstructors', notes: 'notes',
101:   }
102: 
103:   for (const [key, col] of Object.entries(fields)) {
104:     if (key in body) {
105:       updates.push(`${col} = ?`)
106:       args.push(body[key] ?? null)
107:     }
108:   }
109: 
110:   if (typeof body.startDate === 'string') {
111:     updates.push('startDate = ?')
112:     args.push(new Date(body.startDate).toISOString())
113:   }
114:   if (typeof body.endDate === 'string') {
115:     updates.push('endDate = ?')
116:     args.push(new Date(body.endDate).toISOString())
117:   }
118:   if ('specificDates' in body) {
119:     updates.push('specificDates = ?')
120:     args.push(Array.isArray(body.specificDates) && body.specificDates.length ? body.specificDates.join(',') : null)
121:   }
122:   if ('setupDate' in body) {
123:     updates.push('setupDate = ?')
124:     args.push(body.setupDate ? new Date(body.setupDate + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString() : null)
125:   }
126:   if ('setupTime' in body) {
127:     updates.push('setupTime = ?')
128:     args.push(body.setupTime ?? null)
129:   }
130: 
131:   if (updates.length > 0) {
132:     updates.push("updatedAt = datetime('now')")
133:     args.push(id)
134:     await db.execute({ sql: `UPDATE Event SET ${updates.join(', ')} WHERE id = ?`, args })
135:   }
136: 
137:   const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
138:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows[0])
139: }
140: 
141: // DELETE /api/events?id=...
142: export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
143:   const authCheck3 = await requireAdmin(req); if (authCheck3) return authCheck3;
144:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
145:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
146:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
147:   await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
148:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
149: }

 32: type Issue =
 33:   | { type: 'double-booking'; date: string; profileId: string; profileName: string; events: { eventId: string; eventName: string; startTime: string; endTime: string }[] }
 34:   | { type: 'unavailable'; date: string; profileId: string; profileName: string; eventName: string; eventId: string }

 38: 
 39: function timeToMinutes(t: string): number {
 40:   const [h, m] = t.split(':').map(Number)
 41:   return h * 60 + (m || 0)
 42: }
 43: 
 44: function rangesOverlap(s1: string, e1: string, s2: string, e2: string): boolean {
 45:   return timeToMinutes(s1) < timeToMinutes(e2) && timeToMinutes(s2) < timeToMinutes(e1)
 46: }
 47: 
 48: export function ConflictSummaryTab({ onJumpToEvent }: { onJumpToEvent: (eventId: string, date: string) => void }) {
 49:   const { data, isLoading } = useQuery({
 50:     queryKey: ['schedule'],
 51:     queryFn: fetchFullSchedule,
 52:   })
 53: 
 54:   const issues = useMemo(() => {
 55:     if (!data) return { doubleBookings: [], unavailable: [], fatigue: [], unfilled: [], skillGaps: [] } as {
 56:       doubleBookings: Issue[]
 57:       unavailable: Issue[]
 58:       fatigue: Issue[]
 59:       unfilled: Issue[]
 60:       skillGaps: Issue[]
 61:     }
 62: 
 63:     const profiles = data.profiles as ProfileView[]
 64:     const events = data.events as EventView[]
 65:     const assignments = data.assignments as AssignmentView[]
 66: 
 67:     // Build a map of (profileId + date) → assignments
 68:     const byProfileDate = new Map<string, AssignmentView[]>()
 69:     for (const a of assignments) {
 70:       const key = `${a.profileId}|${a.date}`
 71:       if (!byProfileDate.has(key)) byProfileDate.set(key, [])
 72:       byProfileDate.get(key)!.push(a)
 73:     }
 74: 
 75:     // 1. Double-bookings: same profile, same date, overlapping times
 76:     const doubleBookings: Issue[] = []
 77:     for (const [key, dayAssignments] of byProfileDate) {
 78:       if (dayAssignments.length < 2) continue
 79:       const [profileId, date] = key.split('|')
 80:       const profile = profiles.find(p => p.id === profileId)
 81:       // Check all pairs for time overlap
 82:       for (let i = 0; i < dayAssignments.length; i++) {
 83:         for (let j = i + 1; j < dayAssignments.length; j++) {
 84:           const a1 = dayAssignments[i]
 85:           const a2 = dayAssignments[j]
 86:           const e1 = events.find(e => e.id === a1.eventId)
 87:           const e2 = events.find(e => e.id === a2.eventId)
 88:           if (!e1 || !e2) continue
 89:           if (rangesOverlap(e1.startTime, e1.endTime, e2.startTime, e2.endTime)) {
 90:             // Avoid duplicate pairs (only add once per profile+date)
 91:             if (i === 0 && j === 1) {
 92:               doubleBookings.push({
 93:                 type: 'double-booking',
 94:                 date,
 95:                 profileId,
 96:                 profileName: profile?.name ?? a1.profileName,
 97:                 events: dayAssignments.map(a => {
 98:                   const ev = events.find(e => e.id === a.eventId)!
 99:                   return { eventId: a.eventId, eventName: ev.name, startTime: ev.startTime, endTime: ev.endTime }
100:                 }),
101:               })
102:             }
103:           }
104:         }
105:       }
106:     }
107: 
108:     // 2. Unavailable violations: profile assigned on a date they're marked unavailable
109:     const unavailable: Issue[] = []
110:     for (const a of assignments) {
111:       const profile = profiles.find(p => p.id === a.profileId)
112:       if (!profile?.unavailableList?.includes(a.date)) continue
113:       const ev = events.find(e => e.id === a.eventId)
114:       if (!ev) continue
115:       unavailable.push({
116:         type: 'unavailable',
117:         date: a.date,
118:         profileId: a.profileId,
119:         profileName: profile.name,
120:         eventName: ev.name,
121:         eventId: ev.id,
122:       })
123:     }
124: 
125:     // 3. Fatigue: >5 consecutive working days
126:     const fatigue: Issue[] = []
127:     for (const profile of profiles) {
128:       const myDates = new Set(
129:         assignments
130:           .filter(a => a.profileId === profile.id)
131:           .map(a => a.date)
132:           .sort(),
133:       )
134:       if (myDates.size === 0) continue
135:       // Find consecutive streaks
136:       const sortedDates = Array.from(myDates).sort()
137:       let streakStart = sortedDates[0]
138:       let streakEnd = sortedDates[0]
139:       const streaks: { start: string; end: string; dates: string[] }[] = []
140:       const currentDates = [sortedDates[0]]
141:       for (let i = 1; i < sortedDates.length; i++) {
142:         const prev = sortedDates[i - 1]
143:         const curr = sortedDates[i]
144:         if (addDaysISO(prev, 1) === curr) {
145:           streakEnd = curr
146:           currentDates.push(curr)
147:         } else {
148:           if (currentDates.length > 5) {
149:             streaks.push({ start: streakStart, end: streakEnd, dates: [...currentDates] })
150:           }
151:           streakStart = curr
152:           streakEnd = curr
153:           currentDates.length = 0
154:           currentDates.push(curr)
155:         }
156:       }
157:       if (currentDates.length > 5) {
158:         streaks.push({ start: streakStart, end: streakEnd, dates: [...currentDates] })
159:       }
160:       for (const s of streaks) {
161:         fatigue.push({
162:           type: 'fatigue',
163:           profileId: profile.id,
164:           profileName: profile.name,
165:           streak: s.dates.length,
166:           dates: s.dates,
167:         })
168:       }
169:     }
170: 
171:     // 4. Unfilled slots: events with fewer primaries than required
172:     const unfilled: Issue[] = []
173:     for (const ev of events) {
174:       // For each day the event runs
175:       const eventDates = new Set<string>()
176:       if (ev.specificDatesList?.length) {
177:         ev.specificDatesList.forEach(d => eventDates.add(d))
178:       } else {
179:         let d = ev.startDate
180:         while (d <= ev.endDate) {
181:           eventDates.add(d)
182:           d = addDaysISO(d, 1)
183:         }
184:       }
185:       for (const date of eventDates) {
186:         const dayAssignments = assignments.filter(a => a.eventId === ev.id && a.date === date)
187:         const primaries = dayAssignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative).length
188:         if (primaries < ev.requiredInstructors) {
189:           unfilled.push({
190:             type: 'unfilled',
191:             date,
192:             eventId: ev.id,
193:             eventName: ev.name,
194:             hostColor: ev.hostColor,
195:             filled: primaries,
196:             needed: ev.requiredInstructors,
197:           })
198:         }
199:       }
200:     }
201: 
202:     // Sort all by date
203:     const sortByDate = (a: Issue, b: Issue) => {
204:       const da = 'date' in a ? a.date : ''
205:       const db = 'date' in b ? b.date : ''
206:       return da.localeCompare(db)
207:     }
208:     doubleBookings.sort(sortByDate)
209:     unavailable.sort(sortByDate)
210:     unfilled.sort(sortByDate)
211: 
212:     // 5. Skill gaps: instructors assigned to events where they don't have the required skills
213:     const skillGaps: Issue[] = []
214:     for (const a of assignments) {
215:       const profile = profiles.find(p => p.id === a.profileId)
216:       const ev = events.find(e => e.id === a.eventId)
217:       if (!profile || !ev || ev.requiredSkills.length === 0) continue
218:       const missing = ev.requiredSkills.filter(s => !profile.skillsList.includes(s))
219:       if (missing.length > 0) {
220:         skillGaps.push({
221:           type: 'skill-gap',
222:           date: a.date,
223:           eventId: ev.id,
224:           eventName: ev.name,
225:           hostColor: ev.hostColor,
226:           profileId: profile.id,
227:           profileName: profile.name,
228:           missingSkills: missing,
229:         })
230:       }
231:     }
232:     skillGaps.sort(sortByDate)
233: 
234:     return { doubleBookings, unavailable, fatigue, unfilled, skillGaps }
235:   }, [data])
236: 
237:   const totalIssues = issues.doubleBookings.length + issues.unavailable.length + issues.fatigue.length + issues.unfilled.length + issues.skillGaps.length
238: 
239:   return (
240:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
241:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex items-center gap-2">
242:         <div>
243:           <h2 className="text-base font-semibold">Conflict Summary</h2>
244:           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Scans the entire summer for scheduling problems.</p>
245:         </div>
246:         <HelpTooltip text="This tab scans the entire summer for problems: Double-bookings (same person at overlapping events), Unavailable violations (person assigned on a day they marked unavailable), Fatigue streaks (>5 consecutive work days), Unfilled slots (events below required instructor count), Skill gaps (instructor missing required skills — informational, not blocking). Click any item to jump to that event in the scheduler." />
247:       </div>
248: 
249:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Conflict summary">
250:         <div className="p-4 space-y-6">
251:           {isLoading && (
252:             <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8">Scanning schedule…</p>
253:           )}
254: 
255:           {!isLoading && totalIssues === 0 && (
256:             <div className="text-center py-12">
257:               <CheckCircle2 className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto text-emerald-400 mb-3" />
258:               <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-emerald-300">No conflicts found</h3>
259:               <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
260:                 All events are fully staffed, no double-bookings, no unavailable violations, no fatigue streaks.
261:               </p>
262:             </div>
263:           )}
264: 
265:           {/* Summary cards */}
266:           {!isLoading && totalIssues > 0 && (
267:             <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
268:               <SummaryCard
269:                 icon={<CalendarX className="h-4 w-4" />}
270:                 label="Double-bookings"
271:                 count={issues.doubleBookings.length}
272:                 tone="bad"
273:               />
274:               <SummaryCard
275:                 icon={<X className="h-4 w-4" />}
276:                 label="Unavailable violations"
277:                 count={issues.unavailable.length}
278:                 tone="bad"
279:               />
280:               <SummaryCard
281:                 icon={<ShieldAlert className="h-4 w-4" />}
282:                 label="Fatigue streaks"
283:                 count={issues.fatigue.length}
284:                 tone="warn"
285:               />
286:               <SummaryCard
287:                 icon={<Users className="h-4 w-4" />}
288:                 label="Unfilled slots"
289:                 count={issues.unfilled.length}
290:                 tone="warn"
291:               />
292:               <SummaryCard
293:                 icon={<Wrench className="h-4 w-4" />}
294:                 label="Skill gaps"
295:                 count={issues.skillGaps.length}
296:                 tone="warn"
297:               />
298:             </div>
299:           )}
300: 
301:           {/* Double-bookings */}
302:           {issues.doubleBookings.length > 0 && (
303:             <IssueSection title="Double-bookings" icon={<CalendarX className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />} tone="bad">
304:               {issues.doubleBookings.map((issue, i) => (
305:                 <IssueCard key={i}>
306:                   <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
307:                     <div className="min-w-0">
308:                       <p className="text-sm font-medium">{issue.profileName}</p>
309:                       <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{formatPrettyDate(issue.date)}</p>
310:                     </div>
311:                     <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border border-rose-500/30 shrink-0">
312:                       {issue.events.length} events
313:                     </span>
314:                   </div>
315:                   <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">
316:                     {issue.events.map((e, j) => (
317:                       <div key={j} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px]">
318:                         <Clock className="h-3 w-3 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
319:                         <span className="text-muted-foreground">{formatTime(e.startTime)} – {formatTime(e.endTime)}</span>
320:                         <span className="truncate">{e.eventName}</span>
321:                       </div>
322:                     ))}
323:                   </div>
324:                 </IssueCard>
325:               ))}
326:             </IssueSection>
327:           )}
328: 
329:           {/* Unavailable violations */}
330:           {issues.unavailable.length > 0 && (
331:             <IssueSection title="Unavailable violations" icon={<X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />} tone="bad">
332:               {issues.unavailable.map((issue, i) => (
333:                 <IssueCard key={i}>
334:                   <button
335:                     onClick={() => onJumpToEvent(issue.eventId, issue.date)}
336:                     className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 w-full text-left hover:text-emerald-300 transition-colors group"
337:                     aria-label={`Jump to ${issue.eventName} on ${formatPrettyDate(issue.date)}`}
338:                   >
339:                     <div className="min-w-0">
340:                       <p className="text-sm font-medium">{issue.profileName}</p>
341:                       <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
342:                         Assigned to <span className="text-foreground/90">{issue.eventName}</span> on {formatPrettyDate(issue.date)}
343:                       </p>
344:                     </div>
345:                     <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0">
346:                       <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border border-rose-500/30">
347:                         Marked unavailable
348:                       </span>
349:                       <ArrowRight className="h-3 w-3 text-muted-foreground group-hover:text-emerald-300" />
350:                     </div>
351:                   </button>
352:                 </IssueCard>
353:               ))}
354:             </IssueSection>
355:           )}
356: 
357:           {/* Fatigue */}
358:           {issues.fatigue.length > 0 && (
359:             <IssueSection title="Fatigue streaks (>5 consecutive days)" icon={<ShieldAlert className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />} tone="warn">
360:               {issues.fatigue.map((issue, i) => (
361:                 <IssueCard key={i}>
362:                   <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
363:                     <div className="min-w-0">
364:                       <p className="text-sm font-medium">{issue.profileName}</p>
365:                       <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
366:                         {formatShortDate(issue.dates[0])} – {formatShortDate(issue.dates[issue.dates.length - 1])}
367:                       </p>
368:                     </div>
369:                     <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 border border-amber-500/30 shrink-0">
370:                       {issue.streak} days
371:                     </span>
372:                   </div>
373:                 </IssueCard>
374:               ))}
375:             </IssueSection>
376:           )}
377: 
378:           {/* Unfilled slots */}
379:           {issues.unfilled.length > 0 && (
380:             <IssueSection title="Unfilled slots" icon={<Users className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />} tone="warn">
381:               {issues.unfilled.map((issue, i) => {
382:                 const colors = hostColor(issue.hostColor)
383:                 return (
384:                   <IssueCard key={i}>
385:                     <button
386:                       onClick={() => onJumpToEvent(issue.eventId, issue.date)}
387:                       className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 w-full text-left hover:text-emerald-300 transition-colors group"
388:                       aria-label={`Jump to ${issue.eventName} on ${formatPrettyDate(issue.date)}`}
389:                     >
390:                       <div className="min-w-0 flex items-center gap-2">
391:                         <span className={cn('h-2 w-2 rounded-full shrink-0', colors.bar)} />
392:                         <div className="min-w-0">
393:                           <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{issue.eventName}</p>
394:                           <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{formatPrettyDate(issue.date)}</p>
395:                         </div>
396:                       </div>

400:                         </span>

407:             </IssueSection>

413:               {issues.skillGaps.map((issue, i) => {

415:                 const colors = hostColor(si.hostColor)
416:                 return (

420:                       className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 w-full text-left hover:text-emerald-300 transition-colors group"
421:                       aria-label={`Jump to ${si.eventName} on ${formatPrettyDate(si.date)}`}
422:                     >
423:                       <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
424:                         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">

444:               })}
445:             </IssueSection>

447:         </div>
448:       </div>

452: 
453: function SummaryCard({ icon, label, count, tone }: {
454:   icon: React.ReactNode
455:   label: string
456:   count: number
457:   tone: 'bad' | 'warn' | 'good'
458: }) {
459:   return (
460:     <div className={cn(
461:       'rounded-lg border p-3 flex items-center gap-2',
462:       tone === 'bad' && 'border-rose-500/30 bg-rose-500/5',
463:       tone === 'warn' && 'border-amber-500/30 bg-amber-500/5',
464:       tone === 'good' && 'border-emerald-500/30 bg-emerald-500/5',
465:     )}>
466:       <div className={cn(
467:         'h-8 w-8 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shrink-0',
468:         tone === 'bad' && 'bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300',
469:         tone === 'warn' && 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300',
470:         tone === 'good' && 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300',
471:       )}>
472:         {icon}
473:       </div>
474:       <div className="min-w-0">
475:         <div className={cn(
476:           'text-lg font-bold tabular-nums',
477:           tone === 'bad' && 'text-rose-300',
478:           tone === 'warn' && 'text-amber-300',
479:           tone === 'good' && 'text-emerald-300',
480:         )}>
481:           {count}
482:         </div>
483:         <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">{label}</div>
484:       </div>
485:     </div>
486:   )
487: }
488: 
489: function IssueSection({ title, icon, tone, children }: {
490:   title: string
491:   icon: React.ReactNode
492:   tone: 'bad' | 'warn'
493:   children: React.ReactNode
494: }) {
495:   return (
496:     <Accordion
497:       label={title}
498:       labelClassName={cn(
499:         'flex items-center gap-1',
500:         tone === 'bad'
501:           ? 'bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border-rose-500/30'
502:           : 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 border-amber-500/30',
503:       )}
504:     >
505:       <div className="space-y-1.5 pt-2">
506:         {children}
507:       </div>
508:     </Accordion>
509:   )
510: }
511: 
512: function IssueCard({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
513:   return (
514:     <div className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3">
515:       {children}
516:     </div>
517:   )
518: }

================
File: src/lib/session.ts
================
 1: import "server-only";
 2: import type { NextRequest } from 'next/server'
 3: import type { NextResponse } from 'next/server'
 4: 
 5: export interface SessionData { userId?: string }
 6: const COOKIE_NAME = 'ra-session'
 7: const SECRET = process.env.SESSION_PASSWORD || 'changeme-this-must-be-at-least-32-characters-long!!'
 8: 
 9: async function hmac(message: string): Promise<string> {
10:   const encoder = new TextEncoder()
11:   const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey('raw', encoder.encode(SECRET), { name: 'HMAC', hash: 'SHA-256' }, false, ['sign'])
12:   const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign('HMAC', key, encoder.encode(message))
13:   return Array.from(new Uint8Array(sig)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('')
14: }
15: 
16: export async function getSessionFromRequest(req: NextRequest): Promise<SessionData> {
17:   const token = req.cookies.get(COOKIE_NAME)?.value
18:   if (!token) return {}
19:   const parts = token.split('.')
20:   if (parts.length !== 2) return {}
21:   const [userId, providedHmac] = parts
22:   if (providedHmac !== await hmac(userId)) return {}
23:   return { userId }
24: }
25: 
26: export async function saveSessionToResponse(res: NextResponse, data: SessionData): Promise<void> {
27:   if (!data.userId) return
28:   const token = `${data.userId}.${await hmac(data.userId)}`
29:   res.cookies.set(COOKIE_NAME, token, { httpOnly: true, sameSite: 'lax', secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production', maxAge: 60*60*24*30, path: '/' })
30: }
31: 
32: export function clearSession(res: NextResponse): void { res.cookies.delete(COOKIE_NAME) }
