File: src/components/scheduler/CalendarView.tsx
================
  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useMemo } from 'react'
  4: import {
  5:   hostColor, formatTime, eventOnDate, todayInBarbados, isPastDate,
  6:   addDaysISO, type EventView, type AssignmentView, type ProfileView,
  7: } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
  8: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
  9: import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, Users, MapPin, Clock } from 'lucide-react'
 10: import { HelpTooltip } from './HelpTooltip'
 11: 
 12: type Props = {
 13:   events: EventView[]
 14:   assignments: AssignmentView[]
 15:   profiles?: ProfileView[]
 16:   /** If provided, highlights this instructor's assignments */
 17:   myProfileId?: string
 18:   /** Read-only mode (instructors can't click to edit) */
 19:   readOnly?: boolean
 20:   onSelect?: (eventId: string, date: string) => void
 21: }
 22: 
 23: const MONTH_NAMES = [
 24:   'January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June',
 25:   'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December',
 26: ]
 27: const WEEKDAY_LABELS = ['Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat', 'Sun']
 28: 
 29: function getMonthDates(year: number, month: number): string[] {
 30:   const firstDay = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month, 1))
 31:   const lastDay = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month + 1, 0))
 32: 
 33:   // Find the Monday on or before the first day
 34:   const start = new Date(firstDay)
 35:   const dayOfWeek = start.getUTCDay() // 0=Sun
 36:   const offset = dayOfWeek === 0 ? 6 : dayOfWeek - 1
 37:   start.setUTCDate(start.getUTCDate() - offset)
 38: 
 39:   // Find the Sunday on or after the last day
 40:   const end = new Date(lastDay)
 41:   const endDayOfWeek = end.getUTCDay()
 42:   const endOffset = endDayOfWeek === 0 ? 0 : 7 - endDayOfWeek
 43:   end.setUTCDate(end.getUTCDate() + endOffset)
 44: 
 45:   const dates: string[] = []
 46:   const d = new Date(start)
 47:   while (d <= end) {
 48:     dates.push(d.toISOString().slice(0, 10))
 49:     d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 1)
 50:   }
 51:   return dates
 52: }
 53: 
 54: export function CalendarView({ events, assignments, profiles, myProfileId, readOnly, onSelect }: Props) {
 55:   const todayISO = todayInBarbados()
 56:   const [currentMonth, setCurrentMonth] = useState(() => {
 57:     // Default to the month of the first event, or current month
 58:     if (events.length > 0) {
 59:       const d = new Date(events[0].startDate + 'T00:00:00.000Z')
 60:       return { year: d.getUTCFullYear(), month: d.getUTCMonth() }
 61:     }
 62:     const d = new Date()
 63:     return { year: d.getUTCFullYear(), month: d.getUTCMonth() }
 64:   })
 65: 
 66:   const dates = useMemo(
 67:     () => getMonthDates(currentMonth.year, currentMonth.month),
 68:     [currentMonth],
 69:   )
 70: 
 71:   const prevMonth = () => {
 72:     setCurrentMonth(m => {
 73:       const d = new Date(Date.UTC(m.year, m.month - 1, 1))
 74:       return { year: d.getUTCFullYear(), month: d.getUTCMonth() }
 75:     })
 76:   }
 77: 
 78:   const nextMonth = () => {
 79:     setCurrentMonth(m => {
 80:       const d = new Date(Date.UTC(m.year, m.month + 1, 1))
 81:       return { year: d.getUTCFullYear(), month: d.getUTCMonth() }
 82:     })
 83:   }
 84: 
 85:   const jumpToday = () => {
 86:     const d = new Date()
 87:     setCurrentMonth({ year: d.getUTCFullYear(), month: d.getMonth() })
 88:   }
 89: 
 90:   // Group dates into weeks (rows of 7)
 91:   const weeks: string[][] = []
 92:   for (let i = 0; i < dates.length; i += 7) {
 93:     weeks.push(dates.slice(i, i + 7))
 94:   }
 95: 
 96:   return (
 97:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
 98:       {/* Month navigator */}
 99:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 gap-2">
100:         <div className="min-w-0 flex items-center gap-1.5">
101:           <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">
102:             {MONTH_NAMES[currentMonth.month]} {currentMonth.year}
103:           </h2>
104:           <HelpTooltip text="This is the full month calendar view. Each colored chip is an event on that date. The X/Y number shows how many instructors are assigned vs needed. Click any event to see details. Use the arrows to navigate between months. Past dates are dimmed." />
105:           <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground hidden sm:block">
106:             {events.length} events total
107:           </p>
108:         </div>
109:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
110:           <button
111:             onClick={jumpToday}
112:             className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px]"
113:           >
114:             Today
115:           </button>
116:           <button
117:             onClick={prevMonth}
118:             className="p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
119:             aria-label="Previous month"
120:           >
121:             <ChevronLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
122:           </button>
123:           <button
124:             onClick={nextMonth}
125:             className="p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
126:             aria-label="Next month"
127:           >
128:             <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
129:           </button>
130:         </div>
131:       </div>
132: 
133:       {/* Scrollable calendar */}
134:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Month calendar">
135:         {/* Weekday header */}
136:         <div className="grid grid-cols-7 sticky top-0 bg-card/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-10 border-b border-border/60">
137:           {WEEKDAY_LABELS.map(wd => (
138:             <div
139:               key={wd}
140:               className="p-2 text-center text-[10px] font-medium text-muted-foreground border-r border-border/40 last:border-r-0"
141:             >
142:               {wd}
143:             </div>
144:           ))}
145:         </div>
146: 
147:         {/* Calendar grid */}
148:         <div className="grid grid-cols-7">
149:           {dates.map((dateISO, i) => {
150:             const dayEvents = events.filter(e => eventOnDate(e, dateISO))
151:             const isInMonth = new Date(dateISO + 'T00:00:00.000Z').getUTCMonth() === currentMonth.month
152:             const isToday = dateISO === todayISO
153:             const isPast = isPastDate(dateISO)
154:             const dayNum = new Date(dateISO + 'T00:00:00.000Z').getUTCDate()
155: 
156:             return (
157:               <div
158:                 key={dateISO}
159:                 className={cn(
160:                   'min-h-[90px] sm:min-h-[120px] border-r border-b border-border/40 last:border-r-0 p-1 sm:p-1.5 flex flex-col gap-0.5',
161:                   !isInMonth && 'bg-muted/5',
162:                   isToday && 'bg-emerald-500/[0.08] ring-1 ring-emerald-400/30 ring-inset',
163:                   isPast && !isToday && 'bg-zinc-500/[0.03]',
164:                 )}
165:               >
166:                 <div className={cn(
167:                   'text-[10px] sm:text-xs font-semibold tabular-nums mb-0.5',
168:                   !isInMonth && 'text-muted-foreground/30',
169:                   isToday && 'text-emerald-400',
170:                   isPast && !isToday && isInMonth && 'text-muted-foreground/50',
171:                 )}>
172:                   {dayNum}
173:                 </div>
174:                 {dayEvents.map(ev => {
175:                   const colors = hostColor(ev.hostColor)
176:                   const dayAssignments = assignments.filter(a => a.eventId === ev.id && a.date === dateISO)
177:                   const primaries = dayAssignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative).length
178:                   const myAssignment = myProfileId
179:                     ? dayAssignments.find(a => a.profileId === myProfileId)
180:                     : undefined
181:                   const isArchived = ev.status === 'Archived'
182: 
183:                   return (
184:                     <button
185:                       key={ev.id}
186:                       onClick={() => onSelect?.(ev.id, dateISO)}
187:                       className={cn(
188:                         'text-left rounded px-1 py-0.5 text-[9px] sm:text-[10px] leading-tight truncate transition-all border cursor-pointer hover:scale-[1.02] hover:shadow-sm',
189:                         isPast ? 'opacity-60' : '',
190:                         isArchived ? 'opacity-60' : '',
191:                         myAssignment ? 'ring-1 ring-emerald-400' : '',
192:                         colors.chip,
193:                       )}
194:                       title={`${ev.name} — ${formatTime(ev.startTime)}${ev.location ? ' @ ' + ev.location : ''}${dayAssignments.length ? ` (${primaries}/${ev.requiredInstructors} instructors)` : ''}${myAssignment ? ' — YOU ARE ASSIGNED' : ''}`}
195:                     >
196:                       <div className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
197:                         <span className={cn('h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full shrink-0', colors.dot)} />
198:                         <span className="truncate font-medium">{ev.name}</span>
199:                       </div>
200:                       <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-0.5">
201:                         {!readOnly && (
202:                           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5 opacity-70">
203:                             <Users className="h-2 w-2" />
204:                             {primaries}/{ev.requiredInstructors}
205:                           </span>
206:                         )}
207:                         {myAssignment && (
208:                           <span className="text-emerald-300 font-bold ml-auto">★</span>
209:                         )}
210:                       </div>
211:                       {readOnly && myAssignment && (
212:                         <span className="text-emerald-300 text-[9px] font-bold">★ You're in</span>
213:                       )}
214:                     </button>
215:                   )
216:                 })}
217:               </div>
218:             )
219:           })}
220:         </div>
221:       </div>
222:     </div>
223:   )
224: }

 31: 
 32: export function EventDetailDrawer({
 33:   event, date, assignments, profiles, onClose, onRemove, onUpdateAssignment, onBulkShirtColor,
 34: }: Props) {
 35:   if (!event || !date) return null
 36:   const colors = hostColor(event.hostColor)
 37:   const primaryAssignments = assignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative)
 38:   const altAssignments = assignments.filter(a => a.isAlternative)
 39:   const filled = primaryAssignments.length
 40:   const needed = event.requiredInstructors
 41:   const isFull = filled >= needed
 42:   const isPast = isPastDate(date)
 43: 
 44:   return (
 45:     <div className="absolute inset-y-0 right-0 z-30 w-full sm:w-96 shadow-2xl border-l border-border/60 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur-md flex flex-col">
 46:       <div className={cn('h-1', colors.bar)} />
 47:       {isPast && (
 48:         <div className="px-4 py-2 bg-zinc-500/10 border-b border-zinc-500/30 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] text-zinc-300">
 49:           <Lock className="h-3 w-3 shrink-0" />
 50:           Past date — assignments are locked (read only)
 51:         </div>
 52:       )}
 53:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
 54:         <div className="min-w-0">
 55:           <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{event.code ?? 'No code'}</p>
 56:           <h2 className="text-base font-semibold leading-tight">{event.name}</h2>
 57:           <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 mt-1 flex-wrap">
 58:             <span className={cn('text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', colors.chip)}>
 59:               {event.host}
 60:             </span>
 61:             <span className={cn('text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', EVENT_STATUS_COLOR[event.status] ?? EVENT_STATUS_COLOR.Confirmed)}>
 62:               {event.status}
 63:             </span>
 64:           </div>
 65:         </div>
 66:         <button
 67:           onClick={onClose}
 68:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
 69:           title="Close"
 70:         >
 71:           <X className="h-4 w-4" />
 72:         </button>
 73:       </div>
 74: 
 75:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Event details">
 76:         <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
 77:           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-xs">
 78:             <DetailRow icon={<Calendar className="h-3 w-3" />} label="Date" value={formatPrettyDate(date)} />
 79:             <DetailRow icon={<Clock className="h-3 w-3" />} label="Time" value={`${formatTime(event.startTime)} – ${formatTime(event.endTime)}`} />
 80:             <DetailRow icon={<MapPin className="h-3 w-3" />} label="Location" value={event.location ?? 'TBD'} />
 81:             <DetailRow icon={<Users className="h-3 w-3" />} label="Participants" value={event.participantCount?.toString() ?? 'TBD'} />
 82:             <DetailRow icon={<GraduationCap className="h-3 w-3" />} label="Age range" value={event.ageRange ?? 'TBD'} />
 83:             <DetailRow icon={<Tag className="h-3 w-3" />} label="Required" value={`${needed} instructors`} />
 84:           </div>
 85: 
 86:           {event.description && (
 87:             <div>
 88:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1">Description</h3>
 89:               <p className="text-xs leading-relaxed">{event.description}</p>
 90:             </div>
 91:           )}
 92: 
 93:           {event.requiredSkills.length > 0 && (
 94:             <div>
 95:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1">
 96:                 Skills <span className="normal-case text-muted-foreground/60">(informational — not enforced)</span>
 97:               </h3>
 98:               <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
 99:                 {event.requiredSkills.map(s => (
100:                   <span key={s} className="text-[11px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted/60 text-foreground/80">
101:                     {s}
102:                   </span>
103:                 ))}
104:               </div>
105:             </div>
106:           )}
107: 
108:           <div>
109:             <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
110:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground">
111:                 Primary ({filled}/{needed})
112:               </h3>
113:               <span className={cn(
114:                 'text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-medium',
115:                 isFull ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300' : 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300',
116:               )}>
117:                 {isFull ? 'Full' : `${needed - filled} more needed`}
118:               </span>
119:             </div>
120:             {/* Acknowledgment summary */}
121:             {primaryAssignments.length > 0 && (
122:               <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2 text-[10px]">
123:                 {(() => {
124:                   const confirmed = primaryAssignments.filter(a => a.ackStatus === 'confirmed').length
125:                   const declined = primaryAssignments.filter(a => a.ackStatus === 'declined').length
126:                   const pending = primaryAssignments.length - confirmed - declined
127:                   return (
128:                     <>
129:                       {confirmed > 0 && (
130:                         <span className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border border-emerald-500/30">
131:                           ✓ {confirmed} confirmed
132:                         </span>
133:                       )}
134:                       {declined > 0 && (
135:                         <span className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border border-rose-500/30">
136:                           ✗ {declined} declined
137:                         </span>
138:                       )}
139:                       {pending > 0 && (
140:                         <span className="px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 border border-amber-500/30">
141:                           ⏳ {pending} pending
142:                         </span>
143:                       )}
144:                     </>
145:                   )
146:                 })()}
147:               </div>
148:             )}
149:             <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/70 mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">
150:               <Shirt className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
151:               Shirt color is set per day per event — change it for each instructor below.
152:             </p>
153:             {/* Bulk shirt color assign */}
154:             {!isPast && onBulkShirtColor && primaryAssignments.length > 0 && (
155:               <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2 p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40">
156:                 <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground whitespace-nowrap">Set all shirts:</span>
157:                 <select
158:                   value=""
159:                   onChange={e => { if (e.target.value) onBulkShirtColor(event.id, date, e.target.value) }}
160:                   className="text-[11px] bg-background border border-border/60 rounded px-2 py-1 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400 text-foreground"
161:                   title="Set shirt color for all instructors on this day"
162:                 >
163:                   <option value="">Choose color…</option>
164:                   {SHIRT_COLORS.map(c => (
165:                     <option key={c} value={c}>{c}</option>
166:                   ))}
167:                 </select>
168:               </div>
169:             )}
170:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
171:               {primaryAssignments.length === 0 && altAssignments.length === 0 && (
172:                 <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground p-3 border border-dashed border-border/60 rounded-md text-center">
173:                   No instructors assigned. Drag from the roster.
174:                 </div>
175:               )}
176:               {primaryAssignments.map(a => (
177:                 <AssignmentRow
178:                   key={a.id}
179:                   assignment={a}
180:                   event={event}
181:                   profile={profiles.find(p => p.id === a.profileId)}
182:                   profiles={profiles}
183:                   onRemove={onRemove}
184:                   onUpdate={onUpdateAssignment}
185:                   isPast={isPast}
186:                 />
187:               ))}
188:             </div>
189:           </div>
190: 
191:           {altAssignments.length > 0 && (
192:             <div>
193:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-amber-300 mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">
194:                 <Shield className="h-3 w-3" />
195:                 Alternatives ({altAssignments.length})
196:               </h3>
197:               <div className="space-y-1.5">
198:                 {altAssignments.map(a => (
199:                   <AssignmentRow
200:                     key={a.id}
201:                     assignment={a}
202:                     event={event}
203:                     profile={profiles.find(p => p.id === a.profileId)}
204:                     profiles={profiles}
205:                     onRemove={onRemove}
206:                     onUpdate={onUpdateAssignment}
207:                     isPast={isPast}
208:                   />
209:                 ))}
210:               </div>
211:             </div>
212:           )}
213: 
214:           {event.notes && (
215:             <div>
216:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1">Notes</h3>
217:               <p className="text-xs leading-relaxed text-muted-foreground">{event.notes}</p>
218:             </div>
219:           )}
220: 
221:           {/* Equipment coordination */}
222:           <EquipmentSection event={event} mode="admin" />
223: 
224:           {/* Opt-ins section */}
225:           {event.optIns && (event.optIns.interested.length + event.optIns.available.length + event.optIns.unavailable.length > 0) && (
226:             <OptInsSection optIns={event.optIns} />
227:           )}
228:         </div>
229:       </div>
230:     </div>
231:   )

234: function OptInsSection({ optIns }: { optIns: NonNullable<EventView['optIns']> }) {
235:   const total = optIns.interested.length + optIns.available.length + optIns.unavailable.length
236:   return (
237:     <div>
238:       <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">
239:         <Star className="h-3 w-3" />
240:         Opt-ins ({total})
241:       </h3>
242:       <div className="space-y-2">
243:         {optIns.available.length > 0 && (
244:           <OptInGroup label="Available" color="emerald" entries={optIns.available} />
245:         )}
246:         {optIns.interested.length > 0 && (
247:           <OptInGroup label="Interested" color="teal" entries={optIns.interested} />
248:         )}
249:         {optIns.unavailable.length > 0 && (
250:           <OptInGroup label="Can't make it" color="rose" entries={optIns.unavailable} />
251:         )}
252:       </div>
253:     </div>
254:   )
255: }
256: 
257: function OptInGroup({ label, color, entries }: {
258:   label: string
259:   color: 'emerald' | 'teal' | 'rose'
260:   entries: { id: string; userName: string; userProfileName: string | null; note: string | null }[]
261: }) {
262:   const colorClasses = {
263:     emerald: 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/30',
264:     teal: 'bg-teal-500/15 text-teal-300 border-teal-500/30',
265:     rose: 'bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border-rose-500/30',
266:   }
267:   return (
268:     <div>
269:       <div className={cn('inline-block text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border mb-1', colorClasses[color])}>
270:         {label} ({entries.length})
271:       </div>
272:       <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
273:         {entries.map(e => (
274:           <span
275:             key={e.id}
276:             className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] bg-muted/60 text-foreground/90"
277:             title={e.note ?? undefined}
278:           >
279:             {e.userProfileName ?? e.userName}
280:             {e.note && <span className="text-muted-foreground">· {e.note}</span>}
281:           </span>
282:         ))}
283:       </div>
284:     </div>
285:   )
286: }
287: 
288: function DetailRow({ icon, label, value }: { icon: React.ReactNode; label: string; value: string }) {
289:   return (
290:     <div className="p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40">
291:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mb-0.5">
292:         {icon}
293:         {label}
294:       </div>
295:       <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{value}</p>
296:     </div>
297:   )
298: }

300: function AssignmentRow({
301:   assignment, event, profile, profiles, onRemove, onUpdate, isPast,
302: }: {
303:   assignment: AssignmentView
304:   event: EventView
305:   profile?: ProfileView
306:   profiles: ProfileView[]
307:   onRemove: (id: string) => void
308:   onUpdate: (id: string, patch: { isAlternative?: boolean; shirtColor?: string | null }) => void
309:   isPast?: boolean
310: }) {
311:   return (
312:     <div
313:       className={cn(
314:         'flex items-center gap-2 p-2 rounded-md border',
315:         assignment.isAlternative
316:           ? 'bg-amber-500/5 border-amber-500/30 border-dashed'
317:           : 'bg-muted/40 border-border/40',
318:       )}
319:     >
320:       <div className="h-7 w-7 rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br from-zinc-700 to-zinc-900 text-white text-[10px] font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
321:         {assignment.profileName.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')}
322:       </div>
323:       <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
324:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
325:           <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{assignment.profileName}</p>
326:           {assignment.ackStatus === 'confirmed' && (
327:             <span className="text-[9px] px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border border-emerald-500/30 shrink-0">
328:               ✓
329:             </span>
330:           )}
331:           {assignment.ackStatus === 'declined' && (
332:             <span className="text-[9px] px-1 py-0.5 rounded bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 border border-rose-500/30 shrink-0" title="Instructor declined this assignment">
333:               ✗ declined
334:             </span>
335:           )}
336:         </div>
337:         <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{assignment.profileRoleTier}</p>
338:         {/* Skill match indicator */}
339:         {(() => {
340:           const p = profiles.find(p => p.id === assignment.profileId)
341:           if (!p) return null
342:           const missing = event.requiredSkills.filter(s => !p.skillsList.includes(s))
343:           if (missing.length === 0) return null
344:           return (
345:             <div className="mt-1 flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap">
346:               <span className="text-[9px] text-amber-300 flex items-center gap-0.5">
347:                 <Wrench className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
348:                 Needs practice: {missing.join(', ')}
349:               </span>
350:             </div>
351:           )
352:         })()}
353:       </div>
354: 
355:       {/* Shirt color picker — disabled for past dates */}
356:       {!isPast && (
357:         <div className="flex items-center gap-0.5 shrink-0">
358:           <Shirt className="h-3 w-3 text-muted-foreground" />
359:           <select
360:             value={assignment.shirtColor ?? ''}
361:             onChange={e => onUpdate(assignment.id, { shirtColor: e.target.value || null })}
362:             className="text-[11px] bg-background border border-border/60 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400 cursor-pointer text-foreground"
363:             title="Shirt color for this day"
364:           >
365:             <option value="">—</option>
366:             {SHIRT_COLORS.map(c => (
367:               <option key={c} value={c}>{c}</option>
368:             ))}
369:           </select>
370:           {assignment.shirtColor && SHIRT_COLOR_SWATCH[assignment.shirtColor] && (
371:             <span className={cn('h-3.5 w-3.5 rounded-full border border-border/40', SHIRT_COLOR_SWATCH[assignment.shirtColor])} />
372:           )}
373:         </div>
374:       )}
375:       {isPast && assignment.shirtColor && (
376:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
377:           <Shirt className="h-3 w-3" />
378:           {assignment.shirtColor}
379:         </div>
380:       )}
381: 
382:       {/* Alt toggle — disabled for past dates */}
383:       {!isPast && (
384:         <button
385:           onClick={() => onUpdate(assignment.id, { isAlternative: !assignment.isAlternative })}
386:           className={cn(
387:             'shrink-0 p-1 rounded',
388:             assignment.isAlternative
389:               ? 'text-amber-300 bg-amber-500/10'
390:               : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-amber-300 hover:bg-amber-500/10',
391:           )}
392:           title={assignment.isAlternative ? 'Make primary' : 'Make alternative'}
393:         >
394:           <Shield className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
395:         </button>
396:       )}
397: 
398:       {/* Remove — disabled for past dates */}
399:       {!isPast && (
400:         <button
401:           onClick={() => onRemove(assignment.id)}
402:           className="shrink-0 p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-destructive/10 hover:text-destructive text-muted-foreground"
403:           title="Remove from event"
404:         >
405:           <Trash2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
406:         </button>
407:       )}
408:     </div>
409:   )
410: }

 30: async function fetchInvites(): Promise<Invite[]> {

 32:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load invites')

 38:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load profiles')
 39:   return r.json()
 40: }

 42: function inviteUrl(token: string): string {
 43:   if (typeof window === 'undefined') return `/?token=${token}`
 44:   return `${window.location.origin}/?token=${token}`
 45: }

 47: export function InvitesTab() {
 48:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 49:   const { data: invites } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['invites'], queryFn: fetchInvites })
 50:   const { data: profiles } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['profiles-list'], queryFn: fetchProfiles })
 51:   const [showCreate, setShowCreate] = useState(false)
 52: 
 53:   const createMutation = useMutation({
 54:     mutationFn: async (args: { name: string; profileId?: string }) => {
 55:       const r = await fetch('/api/invites', {
 56:         method: 'POST',
 57:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 58:         body: JSON.stringify(args),
 59:       })
 60:       const j = await r.json()
 61:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed to create invite')
 62:       return j
 63:     },
 64:     onSuccess: () => {
 65:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['invites'] })
 66:       toast.success('Invite created')
 67:       setShowCreate(false)
 68:     },
 69:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to create invite'),
 70:   })
 71: 
 72:   const deleteMutation = useMutation({
 73:     mutationFn: async (id: string) => {
 74:       const r = await fetch(`/api/invites?id=${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
 75:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to delete')
 76:       return r.json()
 77:     },
 78:     onSuccess: () => {
 79:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['invites'] })
 80:       toast.success('Invite revoked')
 81:     },
 82:     onError: () => toast.error('Failed to revoke invite'),
 83:   })
 84: 
 85:   const copyLink = async (token: string) => {
 86:     const url = inviteUrl(token)
 87:     try {
 88:       await navigator.clipboard.writeText(url)
 89:       toast.success('Invite link copied', { description: url })
 90:     } catch {
 91:       toast.error('Could not copy — copy manually', { description: url })
 92:     }
 93:   }
 94: 
 95:   const shareWhatsApp = (token: string, name: string) => {
 96:     const url = inviteUrl(token)
 97:     const msg = `Hi ${name}! You're invited to join the RA Syncbot camp scheduler. Click here to claim your account and see the camp schedule:\n\n${url}`
 98:     window.open(`https://wa.me/?text=${encodeURIComponent(msg)}`, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer')
 99:   }
100: 
101:   const shareEmail = (token: string, name: string) => {
102:     const url = inviteUrl(token)
103:     const subject = 'Your RA Syncbot scheduler invite'
104:     const body = `Hi ${name},\n\nYou're invited to join the RA Syncbot camp scheduler. Click the link below to claim your account and see the camp schedule:\n\n${url}\n\nOnce you claim your account, you'll be able to opt in to events you'd like to work and see your assignments.\n\nThanks!`
105:     window.location.href = `mailto:?subject=${encodeURIComponent(subject)}&body=${encodeURIComponent(body)}`
106:   }
107: 
108:   return (
109:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
110:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
111:         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
112:           <div>
113:             <h2 className="text-base font-semibold">Instructor Invites</h2>
114:             <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Generate invite links for staff to opt in and view their schedule.</p>
115:           </div>
116:           <HelpTooltip text="Generate invite links for staff. Click New invite, select a staff member, then copy the link and send via WhatsApp or email. The instructor opens the link, enters their email + password, receives a verification code, and can then log in. They can only see their own schedule and opt in to events." />
117:         </div>
118:         <button
119:           onClick={() => setShowCreate(true)}
120:           className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 flex items-center gap-1.5"
121:         >
122:           <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
123:           New invite
124:         </button>
125:       </div>
126: 
127:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Invites list">
128:         <div className="p-4 space-y-2">
129:           {invites?.length === 0 && (
130:             <div className="text-center p-8 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
131:               No invites yet. Click <strong>New invite</strong> to generate one for an instructor.
132:             </div>
133:           )}
134:           {invites?.map(inv => (
135:             <div key={inv.id} className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
136:               <div className={cn(
137:                 'h-9 w-9 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shrink-0',
138:                 inv.claimedAt
139:                   ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300'
140:                   : 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300',
141:               )}>
142:                 {inv.claimedAt ? <CheckCircle2 className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Clock className="h-4 w-4" />}
143:               </div>

145:                 <div className="flex items-center gap-2">

147:                   {inv.profileName && (
148:                     <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">

151:                   )}

229: function CreateInviteDrawer({ profiles, invitedProfileIds, onClose, onCreate, creating }: {
230:   profiles: Profile[]
231:   invitedProfileIds: Set<string>
232:   onClose: () => void
233:   onCreate: (name: string, profileId?: string) => void
234:   creating: boolean
235: }) {
236:   // Filter out staff who already have invites linked
237:   const available = profiles.filter(p => !invitedProfileIds.has(p.id))
238:   const [profileId, setProfileId] = useState<string>(available[0]?.id ?? '')
239: 
240:   const canCreate = !!profileId
241: 
242:   const submit = () => {
243:     const p = profiles.find(p => p.id === profileId)
244:     if (p) onCreate(p.name, p.id)
245:   }
246: 
247:   return (
248:     <div
249:       className="absolute inset-y-0 right-0 z-30 w-full sm:w-96 shadow-2xl border-l border-border/60 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur-md flex flex-col"
250:       role="dialog"
251:       aria-modal="true"
252:       aria-label="Create new invite"
253:     >
254:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 flex items-center justify-between">
255:         <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">New invite</h2>
256:         <button
257:           onClick={onClose}
258:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-w-[36px] min-h-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
259:           aria-label="Close"
260:         >
261:           <X className="h-4 w-4" />
262:         </button>
263:       </div>
264:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-4">
265:         {available.length === 0 ? (
266:           <div className="text-center py-8">
267:             <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
268:               All staff members already have invites.
269:             </p>
270:             <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-1">
271:               Add new staff in the Team tab first, then come back to create their invite.
272:             </p>
273:           </div>

282:                 onChange={e => setProfileId(e.target.value)}

 36: const WEEKDAYS = ['Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat', 'Sun']

 38: function weekDates(weekStartISO: string): string[] {
 39:   const d = new Date(`${weekStartISO}T00:00:00.000Z`)
 40:   const out: string[] = []
 41:   for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
 42:     out.push(d.toISOString().slice(0, 10))
 43:     d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 1)
 44:   }
 45:   return out
 46: }
 47: 
 48: export function CalendarGrid({
 49:   weekStartISO, events, assignments, selected, onSelect, onPrevWeek, onNextWeek, onJumpToday, onPrint,
 50:   tapAssignMode, hasSelectedProfile,
 51: }: Props) {
 52:   const dates = weekDates(weekStartISO)
 53:   const todayISO = todayInBarbados()
 54:   // Mobile: track which day is in focus (defaults to today if in this week, else first day)
 55:   const [mobileDayIdx, setMobileDayIdx] = useState(() => {
 56:     const todayIdx = dates.indexOf(todayISO)
 57:     return todayIdx >= 0 ? todayIdx : 0
 58:   })
 59: 
 60:   const renderDayColumn = (dateISO: string, idx: number, dates: string[]) => {
 61:     const dayEvents = events.filter(e => eventOnDate(e, dateISO))
 62:     const dayAssignments = assignments.filter(a => a.date === dateISO)
 63:     const isToday = dateISO === todayISO
 64:     const isPast = isPastDate(dateISO)
 65:     const weekday = formatWeekday(dateISO)
 66:     const dayNum = formatDayNum(dateISO)
 67:     return (
 68:       <div
 69:         key={dateISO}
 70:         className={cn(
 71:           'flex flex-col border-r border-border/40 last:border-r-0 min-w-0 overflow-y-auto',
 72:           isToday && 'bg-emerald-500/[0.04]',
 73:           isPast && !isToday && 'bg-zinc-500/[0.03]',
 74:         )}
 75:         role="region"
 76:         aria-label={`${weekday} ${dayNum}${isPast ? ' (past)' : ''}`}
 77:       >
 78:         <div className={cn(
 79:           'p-2 border-b border-border/40 sticky top-0 backdrop-blur-sm bg-card/80 z-10',
 80:           isToday && 'bg-emerald-500/10',
 81:           isPast && !isToday && 'bg-zinc-500/5',
 82:         )}>
 83:           <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
 84:             <span className={cn(
 85:               'text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide',
 86:               isPast ? 'text-muted-foreground/50' : 'text-muted-foreground',
 87:             )}>{weekday}</span>
 88:             <span className={cn(
 89:               'text-sm font-semibold tabular-nums',
 90:               isToday && 'text-emerald-400',
 91:             )}>
 92:               {dayNum}
 93:             </span>
 94:           </div>
 95:         </div>
 96:         <div className="p-1.5 space-y-2 flex-1">
 97:           {dayEvents.length === 0 && (
 98:             <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground text-center py-2 opacity-50">
 99:               No events
100:             </div>
101:           )}
102:           {dayEvents.map(ev => {
103:             const evAssignments = dayAssignments.filter(a => a.eventId === ev.id)
104:             const isSelected = selected?.eventId === ev.id && selected?.date === dateISO
105:             const isMultiDay = ev.endDate > dateISO
106:             const isFirstDayThisWeek = ev.startDate === dateISO || dateISO === dates[0]
107:             const showMultiDayHandle = isMultiDay && isFirstDayThisWeek
108:             return (
109:               <DroppableEventCard
110:                 key={ev.id}
111:                 event={ev}
112:                 date={dateISO}
113:                 assignments={evAssignments}
114:                 selected={!!isSelected}
115:                 onSelect={(eventId, date) => onSelect(eventId, date)}
116:                 showMultiDayHandle={showMultiDayHandle && !tapAssignMode}
117:                 tapAssignMode={tapAssignMode}
118:                 highlightTapTarget={tapAssignMode && hasSelectedProfile}
119:               />
120:             )
121:           })}
122:         </div>
123:       </div>
124:     )
125:   }
126: 
127:   return (
128:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-w-0">
129:       {/* Week navigator */}
130:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 gap-2">
131:         <div className="min-w-0 flex items-center gap-1.5">
132:           <div className="min-w-0">
133:             <h2 className="text-base font-semibold truncate">
134:               Week of {formatShortDate(weekStartISO)}
135:             </h2>
136:             <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">
137:               {formatShortDate(dates[0])} – {formatShortDate(dates[6])}
138:             </p>
139:           </div>
140:           <HelpTooltip text="DRAG instructors from the left roster onto event cards to assign them. Each card shows X/Y (assigned/needed). Use CSV to export to Excel, PDF to print. '↧ all days' assigns to all days of a multi-day event at once. Past dates are locked (read-only). On mobile: tap an instructor, then tap an event to assign." />
141:         </div>
142:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
143:           {/* Export dropdown */}
144:           <div className="relative group">
145:             <button
146:               onClick={() => exportCSV(weekStartISO, events, assignments)}
147:               className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px] flex items-center gap-1.5"
148:               aria-label="Export schedule as CSV"
149:               title="Export as CSV"
150:             >
151:               <Download className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
152:               <span className="hidden sm:inline">CSV</span>

160:           >

173:             title="Previous week"
174:             aria-label="Previous week"

183:           >

================
File: src/app/api/assignments/route.ts
================
  1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
  2: import { requireAdmin, getAuthUser } from "@/lib/auth-helpers"
  3: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
  4: import { notifyAssignmentCreated, notifyAssignmentRemoved } from '@/lib/email'
  5: 
  6: // GET /api/assignments?eventId=...&profileId=...&date=YYYY-MM-DD
  7: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  8:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
  9:   const eventId = searchParams.get('eventId')
 10:   const profileId = searchParams.get('profileId')
 11:   const date = searchParams.get('date')
 12: 
 13:   let sql = `SELECT a.*, p.name as profileName, p.roleTier as profileRoleTier,
 14:              e.name as eventName, e.hostColor as eventHostColor, e.startTime, e.endTime
 15:              FROM Assignment a
 16:              JOIN Profile p ON a.profileId = p.id
 17:              JOIN Event e ON a.eventId = e.id`
 18:   const conditions: string[] = []
 19:   const args: unknown[] = []
 20: 
 21:   if (eventId) { conditions.push('a.eventId = ?'); args.push(eventId) }
 22:   if (profileId) { conditions.push('a.profileId = ?'); args.push(profileId) }
 23:   if (date) { conditions.push('a.assignedDate = ?'); args.push(new Date(date + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString()) }
 24: 
 25:   if (conditions.length > 0) sql += ' WHERE ' + conditions.join(' AND ')
 26:   sql += ' ORDER BY a.assignedDate ASC'
 27: 
 28:   const result = await db.execute({ sql, args })
 29:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows.map((a: any) => ({
 30:     ...a,
 31:     assignedDate: a.assignedDate,
 32:   })))
 33: }
 34: 
 35: // POST /api/assignments — create single assignment
 36: export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
 37:   const authPost = await requireAdmin(req); if (authPost) return authPost;
 38:   const body = await req.json()
 39:   const { eventId, profileId, date, overrideFlag, isAlternative, shirtColor } = body as {
 40:     eventId: string; profileId: string; date: string
 41:     overrideFlag?: boolean; isAlternative?: boolean; shirtColor?: string | null
 42:   }
 43: 
 44:   if (!eventId || !profileId || !date) {
 45:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing eventId, profileId or date' }, { status: 400 })
 46:   }
 47: 
 48:   // Block assignments on past dates
 49:   const today = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
 50:     timeZone: 'America/Barbados',
 51:     year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
 52:   }).format(new Date())
 53:   if (date < today) {
 54:     return NextResponse.json(
 55:       { error: 'Cannot assign to a past date. That day has already passed.' },
 56:       { status: 400 },
 57:     )
 58:   }
 59: 
 60:   const id = crypto.randomUUID()
 61:   await db.execute({
 62:     sql: `INSERT INTO Assignment (id, eventId, profileId, assignedDate, status, isAlternative, shirtColor, createdAt, updatedAt)
 63:           VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, 'Assigned', ?, ?, datetime('now'), datetime('now'))`,
 64:     args: [id, eventId, profileId, new Date(date + 'T00:00:00.000Z').toISOString(),
 65:            !!isAlternative, shirtColor ?? null],
 66:   })
 67: 
 68:   const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Assignment WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
 69: 
 70:   // Send email notification (fire-and-forget)
 71:   const eventResult = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT name FROM Event WHERE id = ?', args: [eventId] })
 72:   const eventName = eventResult.rows.length > 0 ? (eventResult.rows[0] as any).name : 'Unknown event'
 73:   notifyAssignmentCreated(profileId, eventName, date, shirtColor ?? null, eventId).catch(() => {})
 74: 
 75:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows[0], { status: 201 })
 76: }
 77: 
 78: // PATCH /api/assignments?id=...
 79: // Admin: can update isAlternative, shirtColor, status
 80: // Instructor: can only update acknowledgedAt + ackStatus on their own assignments
 81: export async function PATCH(req: NextRequest) {
 82:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
 83:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
 84:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
 85:   const body = await req.json()
 86: 
 87:   // Check if this is an acknowledgment (instructor action)
 88:   if ('ackStatus' in body) {
 89:     const user = await getAuthUser(req)
 90:     if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not authenticated' }, { status: 401 })
 91:     if (!user.profileId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No profile linked' }, { status: 400 })
 92: 
 93:     // Verify the assignment belongs to this instructor
 94:     const assignment = await db.execute({
 95:       sql: 'SELECT profileId FROM Assignment WHERE id = ?',
 96:       args: [id],
 97:     })
 98:     if (assignment.rows.length === 0) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 })
 99:     if ((assignment.rows[0] as any).profileId !== user.profileId) {
100:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not your assignment' }, { status: 403 })
101:     }
102: 
103:     const ackStatus = body.ackStatus as string
104:     if (!['confirmed', 'declined'].includes(ackStatus)) {
105:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'ackStatus must be "confirmed" or "declined"' }, { status: 400 })
106:     }
107: 
108:     try {
109:       await db.execute({
110:         sql: "UPDATE Assignment SET ackStatus = ?, acknowledgedAt = datetime('now'), updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?",
111:         args: [ackStatus, id],
112:       })
113:     } catch (e: any) {
114:       // Column might not exist — try ALTER TABLE
115:       try {
116:         await db.execute({ sql: 'ALTER TABLE Assignment ADD COLUMN ackStatus TEXT' })
117:         await db.execute({ sql: 'ALTER TABLE Assignment ADD COLUMN acknowledgedAt TEXT' })
118:         await db.execute({
119:           sql: "UPDATE Assignment SET ackStatus = ?, acknowledgedAt = datetime('now'), updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?",
120:           args: [ackStatus, id],
121:         })
122:       } catch (e2: any) {
123:         return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to acknowledge' }, { status: 500 })
124:       }
125:     }
126: 
127:     const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Assignment WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
128:     return NextResponse.json(result.rows[0])
129:   }
130: 
131:   // Admin-only field updates
132:   const authPatch = await requireAdmin(req); if (authPatch) return authPatch;
133: 
134:   const updates: string[] = []
135:   const args: unknown[] = []
136:   if (typeof body.isAlternative === 'boolean') { updates.push('isAlternative = ?'); args.push(body.isAlternative) }
137:   if ('shirtColor' in body) { updates.push('shirtColor = ?'); args.push(body.shirtColor ?? null) }
138:   if (typeof body.status === 'string') { updates.push('status = ?'); args.push(body.status) }
139: 
140:   if (updates.length === 0) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No fields to update' }, { status: 400 })
141: 
142:   updates.push("updatedAt = datetime('now')")
143:   args.push(id)
144: 
145:   await db.execute({ sql: `UPDATE Assignment SET ${updates.join(', ')} WHERE id = ?`, args })
146:   const result = await db.execute({ sql: 'SELECT * FROM Assignment WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
147:   return NextResponse.json(result.rows[0])
148: }
149: 
150: // DELETE /api/assignments?id=...
151: export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
152:   const authDel = await requireAdmin(req); if (authDel) return authDel;
153:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
154:   const id = searchParams.get('id')
155:   if (!id) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing id' }, { status: 400 })
156: 
157:   // Get assignment info before deleting (for email notification)
158:   const existing = await db.execute({
159:     sql: `SELECT a.profileId, a.assignedDate, a.eventId, e.name as eventName FROM Assignment a JOIN Event e ON a.eventId = e.id WHERE a.id = ?`,
160:     args: [id],
161:   })
162: 
163:   await db.execute({ sql: 'DELETE FROM Assignment WHERE id = ?', args: [id] })
164: 
165:   // Send email notification (fire-and-forget)
166:   if (existing.rows.length > 0) {
167:     const a = existing.rows[0] as any
168:     notifyAssignmentRemoved(a.profileId, a.eventName, String(a.assignedDate).slice(0, 10), a.eventId).catch(() => {})
169:   }
170: 
171:   return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
172: }

  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useDroppable } from '@dnd-kit/core'
  4: import {
  5:   hostColor,
  6:   formatTime,
  7:   SHIRT_COLOR_SWATCH,
  8:   isPastDate,
  9:   type EventView,
 10:   type AssignmentView,
 11: } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
 12: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
 13: import { MapPin, Clock, Users, AlertTriangle, Shield, Star, Wrench } from 'lucide-react'
 14: 
 15: type Props = {
 16:   event: EventView
 17:   date: string
 18:   assignments: AssignmentView[]
 19:   selected: boolean
 20:   onSelect: (eventId: string, date: string) => void
 21:   /** When true, this card renders as a "drop on all days" target (used on the first
 22:    *  day a multi-day event appears in the current week). */
 23:   showMultiDayHandle?: boolean
 24:   // Mobile tap-to-assign: when true, card is not droppable (tap only)
 25:   tapAssignMode?: boolean
 26:   // When true + tapAssignMode, highlight this card as a valid tap target
 27:   highlightTapTarget?: boolean
 28: }
 29: 
 30: export function DroppableEventCard({
 31:   event, date, assignments, selected, onSelect, showMultiDayHandle,
 32:   tapAssignMode, highlightTapTarget,
 33: }: Props) {
 34:   const isPast = isPastDate(date)
 35:   const isCancelled = event.status === 'Cancelled'
 36:   const isArchived = event.status === 'Archived'
 37:   // Read-only when past, cancelled, or archived (can't drop, but still selectable for details)
 38:   const isReadOnly = isPast || isCancelled || isArchived
 39:   // Per-day drop target (disabled in tap mode or when read-only)
 40:   const { setNodeRef, isOver } = useDroppable({
 41:     id: `drop-${event.id}-${date}`,
 42:     data: { type: 'event-drop', eventId: event.id, date },
 43:     disabled: tapAssignMode || isReadOnly,
 44:   })
 45: 
 46:   const primaryCount = assignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative).length
 47:   const altCount = assignments.length - primaryCount
 48:   const filled = primaryCount
 49:   const needed = event.requiredInstructors
 50:   const isFull = filled >= needed
 51:   const isTentative = event.status === 'Tentative'
 52:   const colors = hostColor(event.hostColor)
 53: 
 54:   // Opt-in counts
 55:   const optIns = event.optIns
 56:   const optInTotal = (optIns?.interested.length ?? 0) + (optIns?.available.length ?? 0)
 57: 
 58:   return (
 59:     <div
 60:       ref={setNodeRef}
 61:       onClick={() => onSelect(event.id, date)}
 62:       className={cn(
 63:         'relative rounded-lg border bg-card/95 backdrop-blur-sm transition-all',
 64:         isReadOnly ? 'cursor-default opacity-60' : 'cursor-pointer hover:shadow-md hover:border-foreground/30',
 65:         selected && 'ring-2 ring-emerald-400 ring-offset-1 ring-offset-background',
 66:         isOver && 'ring-2 ring-emerald-400 scale-[1.02]',
 67:         highlightTapTarget && !isReadOnly && 'ring-2 ring-emerald-400/60 animate-pulse cursor-pointer',
 68:         isCancelled || isArchived
 69:           ? 'border-rose-500/40 opacity-60'
 70:           : isPast
 71:             ? 'border-zinc-600/40 opacity-60'
 72:             : isFull
 73:               ? 'border-emerald-500/40'
 74:               : 'border-amber-500/30',
 75:       )}
 76:       role="button"
 77:       tabIndex={0}
 78:       aria-label={`${event.name} on ${date}, ${filled} of ${needed} instructors assigned${altCount ? `, ${altCount} alternatives` : ''}${optInTotal ? `, ${optInTotal} opt-ins` : ''}${isReadOnly ? '. Read only' : ''}${highlightTapTarget && !isReadOnly ? '. Tap to assign selected instructor' : ''}`}
 79:       onKeyDown={(e) => {
 80:         if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
 81:           e.preventDefault()
 82:           onSelect(event.id, date)
 83:         }
 84:       }}
 85:     >
 86:       <div className={cn('h-1 rounded-t-lg', isCancelled || isArchived ? 'bg-rose-500' : isPast ? 'bg-zinc-600' : colors.bar)} />
 87: 
 88:       <div className="p-2.5 space-y-2">
 89:         <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-1.5">
 90:           <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
 91:             <p className={cn('text-xs font-semibold leading-tight truncate', isCancelled && 'line-through')}>
 92:               {event.name}
 93:             </p>
 94:             <span className={cn('inline-block mt-0.5 text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', colors.chip)}>
 95:               {event.host}
 96:             </span>
 97:           </div>
 98:           <div
 99:             className={cn(
100:               'shrink-0 flex items-center gap-0.5 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-semibold tabular-nums',
101:               isFull ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300' : 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300',
102:             )}
103:             title={`${filled}/${needed} primary instructors${altCount ? ` + ${altCount} alternative${altCount > 1 ? 's' : ''}` : ''}`}
104:           >
105:             <Users className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
106:             {filled}/{needed}
107:             {altCount > 0 && <span className="text-amber-400">+{altCount}</span>}
108:           </div>
109:         </div>
110: 
111:         <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
112:           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
113:             <Clock className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
114:             {formatTime(event.startTime)}
115:           </span>
116:           {event.location && (
117:             <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5 truncate" title={event.location}>
118:               <MapPin className="h-2.5 w-2.5 shrink-0" />
119:               <span className="truncate">{event.location}</span>
120:             </span>
121:           )}
122:         </div>
123: 
124:         {isTentative && (
125:           <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-amber-300">
126:             <AlertTriangle className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
127:             Tentative — dates not finalized
128:           </div>
129:         )}
130: 
131:         {assignments.length > 0 && (
132:           <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
133:             {assignments.map(a => (
134:               <span
135:                 key={a.id}
136:                 className={cn(
137:                   'inline-flex items-center gap-0.5 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] max-w-[120px]',
138:                   a.isAlternative
139:                     ? 'bg-amber-500/10 text-amber-300 border border-dashed border-amber-500/40'
140:                     : 'bg-muted/80 text-foreground/90',
141:                 )}
142:                 title={a.isAlternative ? `${a.profileName} (Alternative)` : a.profileName}
143:               >
144:                 {a.isAlternative && <Shield className="h-2 w-2 shrink-0" />}
145:                 <span className="truncate">{a.profileName.split(' ')[0]}</span>
146:                 {a.shirtColor && SHIRT_COLOR_SWATCH[a.shirtColor] && (
147:                   <span
148:                     className={cn('h-2 w-2 rounded-full shrink-0', SHIRT_COLOR_SWATCH[a.shirtColor])}
149:                     title={`Shirt: ${a.shirtColor}`}
150:                   />
151:                 )}
152:               </span>
153:             ))}
154:           </div>
155:         )}
156: 
157:         {/* Opt-in indicator + multi-day drop handle */}
158:         <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-1 pt-1 border-t border-border/40">
159:           {optInTotal > 0 ? (
160:             <span
161:               className="flex items-center gap-0.5 text-[9px] text-emerald-300"
162:               title={`${optIns?.interested.length ?? 0} interested, ${optIns?.available.length ?? 0} available`}
163:             >
164:               <Star className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
165:               {optInTotal} opt-in{optInTotal > 1 ? 's' : ''}
166:             </span>
167:           ) : (
168:             <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground/50">No opt-ins yet</span>
169:           )}
170:           {showMultiDayHandle && !isReadOnly && <MultiDayHandle eventId={event.id} />}
171:         </div>
172:       </div>
173:     </div>
174:   )
175: }
176: 
177: // Separate component to satisfy the lint rule about not accessing refs during render.
178: function MultiDayHandle({ eventId }: { eventId: string }) {
179:   const { setNodeRef, isOver } = useDroppable({
180:     id: `drop-multi-${eventId}`,
181:     data: { type: 'event-drop-all', eventId },
182:   })
183:   return (
184:     <button
185:       ref={setNodeRef as any}
186:       onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
187:       className={cn(
188:         'text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border transition-colors',
189:         isOver
190:           ? 'bg-emerald-500/20 border-emerald-400 text-emerald-300'
191:           : 'border-border/60 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/40',
192:       )}
193:       title="Drag an instructor here to assign them to ALL days of this event"
194:       aria-label="Drop zone: assign to all days of this event"
195:     >
196:       ↧ all days
197:     </button>
198:   )
199: }

================
File: src/components/scheduler/EventsManagerTab.tsx

  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useMemo } from 'react'
  4: import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import { toast } from 'sonner'
  6: import {
  7:   hostColor, EVENT_STATUS_COLOR, formatShortDate, formatTime,
  8:   type EventView,
  9: } from '@/lib/scheduler-types'
 10: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
 11: import {
 12:   Plus, Pencil, Trash2, X, Calendar, Clock, Users, MapPin, Tag, Save, AlertCircle,
 13: } from 'lucide-react'
 14: import { Accordion } from './Accordion'
 15: import { HelpTooltip } from './HelpTooltip'
 16: import { SkillPicker } from './SkillPicker'
 17: import { EquipmentSection } from './EquipmentSection'
 18: 
 19: type EventRow = EventView & {
 20:   _assignmentCount?: number
 21:   _optInCount?: number
 22: }
 23: 
 24: const HOST_COLOR_OPTIONS = ['teal', 'emerald', 'amber', 'pink', 'rose', 'slate']
 25: const STATUS_OPTIONS = ['Draft', 'Tentative', 'Confirmed', 'Cancelled', 'Archived']
 26: 
 27: async function fetchEvents(): Promise<EventRow[]> {
 28:   const r = await fetch('/api/events')
 29:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load events')
 30:   const data = await r.json()
 31:   return data.map((e: any) => ({
 32:     ...e,
 33:     specificDatesList: e.specificDatesList ?? (e.specificDates ? e.specificDates.split(',').map((s: string) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : []),
 34:   }))
 35: }
 36: 
 37: export function EventsManagerTab() {
 38:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 39:   const { data: events, isLoading } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['events'], queryFn: fetchEvents })
 40:   const [editing, setEditing] = useState<EventRow | null>(null)
 41:   const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false)
 42: 
 43:   const deleteMutation = useMutation({
 44:     mutationFn: async (id: string) => {
 45:       const r = await fetch(`/api/events?id=${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
 46:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to delete')
 47:       return r.json()
 48:     },
 49:     onSuccess: () => {
 50:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['events'] })
 51:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
 52:       toast.success('Event deleted')
 53:     },
 54:     onError: () => toast.error('Failed to delete event'),
 55:   })
 56: 
 57:   const grouped = useMemo(() => {
 58:     if (!events) return { Confirmed: [], Tentative: [], Draft: [], Cancelled: [] } as Record<string, EventRow[]>
 59:     const g: Record<string, EventRow[]> = { Confirmed: [], Tentative: [], Draft: [], Cancelled: [] }
 60:     for (const e of events) {
 61:       (g[e.status] ?? (g[e.status] = [])).push(e)
 62:     }
 63:     return g
 64:   }, [events])
 65: 
 66:   return (
 67:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
 68:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
 69:         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
 70:           <div>
 71:             <h2 className="text-base font-semibold">Event Management</h2>
 72:             <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Set status, dates, and required instructor counts.</p>
 73:           </div>
 74:           <HelpTooltip text="Create and manage events here. Set status: Draft (hidden from calendar, dates TBD), Tentative (visible with warning), Confirmed (normal), Cancelled (greyed out), Archived (hidden). Use the Recurring checkbox for weekly events. Use the Setup day checkbox to add a setup date where staff can be assigned to prepare equipment." />
 75:         </div>
 76:         <button
 77:           onClick={() => setCreating(true)}
 78:           className="px-3 py-2 text-sm rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 flex items-center gap-1.5 min-h-[44px]"
 79:         >
 80:           <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
 81:           New event
 82:         </button>
 83:       </div>
 84: 
 85:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Events list">
 86:         <div className="p-4 space-y-6">
 87:           {isLoading && <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Loading…</p>}
 88:           {STATUS_OPTIONS.map(status => {
 89:             const list = grouped[status] ?? []
 90:             if (list.length === 0) return null
 91:             return (
 92:               <Accordion
 93:                 key={status}
 94:                 label={status}
 95:                 count={list.length}
 96:                 labelClassName={EVENT_STATUS_COLOR[status]}
 97:                 defaultOpen={status === 'Draft' || status === 'Archived'}
 98:               >
 99:                 {list.map(ev => (
100:                   <EventListItem
101:                     key={ev.id}
102:                     event={ev}
103:                     onEdit={() => setEditing(ev)}
104:                     onDelete={() => {
105:                       toast(`Delete "${ev.name}"?`, {
106:                         description: 'This cannot be undone.',
107:                         duration: 8000,
108:                         action: {
109:                           label: 'Delete',
110:                           onClick: () => deleteMutation.mutate(ev.id),
111:                         },
112:                       })
113:                     }}
114:                   />
115:                 ))}
116:               </Accordion>
117:             )
118:           })}
119:         </div>
120:       </div>
121: 
122:       {(editing || creating) && (
123:         <EventEditDrawer
124:           event={editing}
125:           onClose={() => { setEditing(null); setCreating(false) }}
126:           onSaved={() => {
127:             setEditing(null)
128:             setCreating(false)
129:             qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['events'] })
130:             qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
131:           }}
132:         />
133:       )}
134:     </div>
135:   )
136: }
137: 
138: function EventListItem({ event, onEdit, onDelete }: {
139:   event: EventRow
140:   onEdit: () => void
141:   onDelete: () => void
142: }) {
143:   const colors = hostColor(event.hostColor)
144:   return (
145:     <div className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
146:       <div className={cn('h-10 w-1 rounded-full shrink-0', colors.bar)} />
147:       <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
148:         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
149:           <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{event.name}</p>
150:           {event.code && <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{event.code}</span>}
151:         </div>
152:         <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-0.5 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground flex-wrap">
153:           <span className={cn('px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', colors.chip)}>{event.host}</span>
154:           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
155:             <Calendar className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
156:             {formatShortDate(event.startDate)}{event.endDate !== event.startDate && ` – ${formatShortDate(event.endDate)}`}
157:           </span>
158:           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
159:             <Clock className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
160:             {formatTime(event.startTime)}
161:           </span>
162:           <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
163:             <Users className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
164:             {event._assignmentCount ?? 0} assignments
165:           </span>
166:           <span className="text-muted-foreground/70">
167:             {event.requiredInstructors} needed/day
168:           </span>
169:           {event._optInCount && event._optInCount > 0 && (
170:             <span className="text-emerald-400">+{event._optInCount} opt-in{event._optInCount > 1 ? 's' : ''}</span>
171:           )}
172:           {event.specificDatesList && event.specificDatesList.length > 0 && (
173:             <span className="text-teal-300">
174:               {event.specificDatesList.length} specific date{event.specificDatesList.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}
175:             </span>
176:           )}
177:         </div>
178:       </div>
179:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
180:         <button
181:           onClick={onEdit}
182:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
183:           title="Edit"
184:         >
185:           <Pencil className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
186:         </button>
187:         <button
188:           onClick={onDelete}
189:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-destructive/10 hover:text-destructive text-muted-foreground"
190:           title="Delete"
191:         >
192:           <Trash2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
193:         </button>
194:       </div>
195:     </div>
196:   )
197: }
198: 
199: function EventEditDrawer({ event, onClose, onSaved }: {
200:   event: EventRow | null
201:   onClose: () => void
202:   onSaved: () => void
203: }) {
204:   const isEdit = !!event
205:   const [form, setForm] = useState(() => ({
206:     code: event?.code ?? '',
207:     name: event?.name ?? '',
208:     host: event?.host ?? '',
209:     hostColor: event?.hostColor ?? 'slate',
210:     location: event?.location ?? '',
211:     description: event?.description ?? '',
212:     status: event?.status ?? 'Draft',
213:     startDate: event?.startDate ?? '2026-07-06',
214:     endDate: event?.endDate ?? '2026-07-10',
215:     startTime: event?.startTime ?? '09:00',
216:     endTime: event?.endTime ?? '15:00',
217:     requiredInstructors: event?.requiredInstructors ?? 2,
218:     ageRange: event?.ageRange ?? '',
219:     participantCount: event?.participantCount ?? '',
220:     specificDates: (event?.specificDatesList ?? []).join('\n'),
221:     notes: event?.notes ?? '',
222:     skills: (event?.requiredSkills ?? []).join(', '),
223:     // Setup date (optional)
224:     hasSetup: !!(event as any)?.setupDate,
225:     setupDate: (event as any)?.setupDate ? String(event.setupDate).slice(0, 10) : '',
226:     setupTime: (event as any)?.setupTime ?? '14:00',
227:     // Recurrence fields
228:     recurring: false,
229:     recurringDays: [] as number[], // 0=Mon .. 6=Sun
230:     recurringWeeks: 6,
231:   }))
232:   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
233: 
234:   // Generate preview dates from recurrence pattern
235:   const recurringPreview = useMemo(() => {
236:     if (!form.recurring || form.recurringDays.length === 0 || !form.startDate) return []
237:     const dates: string[] = []
238:     const start = new Date(`${form.startDate}T00:00:00.000Z`)
239:     // Find the first matching day on or after startDate
240:     let cursor = new Date(start)
241:     // Walk forward up to recurringWeeks * 7 days to find all matching days
242:     const maxDays = form.recurringWeeks * 7 + 7
243:     for (let i = 0; i < maxDays; i++) {
244:       const dayOfWeek = cursor.getUTCDay() // 0=Sun .. 6=Sat
245:       // Convert to Monday-based: 0=Mon .. 6=Sun
246:       const mondayBased = dayOfWeek === 0 ? 6 : dayOfWeek - 1
247:       if (form.recurringDays.includes(mondayBased)) {
248:         dates.push(cursor.toISOString().slice(0, 10))
249:       }
250:       if (dates.length >= form.recurringWeeks) break
251:       cursor.setUTCDate(cursor.getUTCDate() + 1)
252:     }
253:     return dates
254:   }, [form.recurring, form.recurringDays, form.recurringWeeks, form.startDate])
255: 
256:   const WEEKDAY_LABELS = ['Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat', 'Sun']
257: 
258:   const toggleRecurringDay = (day: number) => {
259:     setForm(f => ({
260:       ...f,
261:       recurringDays: f.recurringDays.includes(day)
262:         ? f.recurringDays.filter(d => d !== day)
263:         : [...f.recurringDays, day].sort(),
264:     }))
265:   }
266: 
267:   const save = async () => {
268:     if (!form.name || !form.host) {
269:       toast.error('Name and host are required')
270:       return
271:     }
272:     setSaving(true)
273:     try {
274:       // If recurring is on, use the generated dates as specificDates and ignore manual entry
275:       const specificDates = form.recurring
276:         ? recurringPreview
277:         : form.specificDates
278:             .split('\n').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)
279:             .map(s => s.length === 10 ? s : `${s}-2026`)
280: 
281:       const payload = {
282:         code: form.code || null,
283:         name: form.name,
284:         host: form.host,
285:         hostColor: form.hostColor,
286:         location: form.location || null,
287:         description: form.description || null,
288:         status: form.status,
289:         startDate: form.startDate,
290:         endDate: form.recurring && recurringPreview.length > 0
291:           ? recurringPreview[recurringPreview.length - 1]
292:           : form.endDate,
293:         startTime: form.startTime,
294:         endTime: form.endTime,
295:         requiredInstructors: form.requiredInstructors,
296:         ageRange: form.ageRange || null,
297:         participantCount: form.participantCount === '' ? null : Number(form.participantCount),
298:         specificDates,
299:         notes: form.notes || null,
300:         skills: form.skills.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean),
301:         setupDate: form.hasSetup && form.setupDate ? form.setupDate : null,
302:         setupTime: form.hasSetup && form.setupTime ? form.setupTime : null,
303:       }
304:       const url = isEdit ? `/api/events?id=${event!.id}` : '/api/events'
305:       const method = isEdit ? 'PUT' : 'POST'
306:       const r = await fetch(url, {
307:         method,
308:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
309:         body: JSON.stringify(payload),
310:       })
311:       if (!r.ok) {
312:         const j = await r.json()
313:         throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed to save')
314:       }
315:       toast.success(isEdit ? 'Event updated' : 'Event created')
316:       onSaved()
317:     } catch (e: any) {
318:       toast.error(e.message || 'Save failed')
319:     } finally {
320:       setSaving(false)
321:     }
322:   }
323: 
324:   return (
325:     <div className="absolute inset-y-0 right-0 z-30 w-full sm:w-[28rem] shadow-2xl border-l border-border/60 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur-md flex flex-col">
326:       <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/60 flex items-center justify-between">
327:         <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">{isEdit ? 'Edit event' : 'New event'}</h2>
328:         <button
329:           onClick={onClose}
330:           className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
331:           title="Close"
332:         >
333:           <X className="h-4 w-4" />
334:         </button>
335:       </div>
336:       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Event details form">
337:         <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
338:           <Field label="Name" required>
339:             <input value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, name: e.target.value }))}
340:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400" />
341:           </Field>
342:           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
343:             <Field label="Code">
344:               <input value={form.code} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, code: e.target.value }))}
345:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400" />
346:             </Field>
347:             <Field label="Status">
348:               <select value={form.status} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, status: e.target.value }))}
349:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400">
350:                 {STATUS_OPTIONS.map(s => <option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
351:               </select>
352:             </Field>
353:           </div>
354:           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
355:             <Field label="Host" required>
356:               <input value={form.host} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, host: e.target.value }))}
357:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400" />
358:             </Field>

360:               <select value={form.hostColor} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, hostColor: e.target.value }))}
361:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400">
362:                 {HOST_COLOR_OPTIONS.map(c => <option key={c} value={c}>{c}</option>)}
363:               </select>

478:                           key={d}
479:                           className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300 border border-emerald-500/30 font-mono"
480:                         >
481:                           {d}
482:                         </span>
483:                       ))}
