518:                     />
519:                   </Field>
520:                   <Field label="Setup time">
521:                     <input
522:                       type="time"
523:                       value={form.setupTime}
524:                       onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, setupTime: e.target.value }))}
525:                       className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
526:                     />
527:                   </Field>
528:                 </div>
529:                 <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">Set status, dates, and required instructor counts. Draft events don't appear on the calendar.</p>
530:         <HelpTooltip text="Create and manage events here. Set status: Draft (hidden from calendar, dates TBD), Tentative (visible with warning), Confirmed (normal), Cancelled (greyed out), Archived (hidden). Use the Recurring checkbox for weekly events. Use the Setup day checkbox to add a setup date where staff can be assigned to prepare equipment." />
531:         <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground hidden">
532:                   Staff assigned to this event on the setup date will be setting up equipment, not teaching.
533:                 </p>
534:               </div>
535:             )}
536:           </div>
537: 
538:           {/* Manual specific dates — hidden when recurring is on */}
539:           {!form.recurring && (
540:             <Field label="Specific dates (one per line, YYYY-MM-DD) — overrides the start/end range">
541:               <textarea value={form.specificDates} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, specificDates: e.target.value }))} rows={3}
542:                 placeholder="2026-07-15&#10;2026-07-17"
543:                 className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400 font-mono" />
544:             </Field>
545:           )}
546:           <SkillPicker
547:             selected={form.skills.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)}
548:             onChange={skills => setForm(f => ({ ...f, skills: skills.join(', ') }))}
549:             allowCatalogManagement
550:             label="Skills (informational only)"
551:           />
552:           <Field label="Notes">
553:             <textarea value={form.notes} onChange={e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, notes: e.target.value }))} rows={2}
554:               className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400" />
555:           </Field>
556: 
557:           {form.status === 'Draft' && (
558:             <div className="flex items-start gap-2 p-2 rounded-md bg-zinc-500/10 border border-zinc-500/30 text-[10px] text-zinc-300">
559:               <AlertCircle className="h-3 w-3 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
560:               <span>Draft events do not appear on the calendar. Set status to Tentative or Confirmed when dates are firm.</span>
561:             </div>
562:           )}
563: 
564:           {/* Equipment section — only when editing an existing event */}
565:           {isEdit && event && (
566:             <EquipmentSection event={event} mode="admin" />
567:           )}
568:           {!isEdit && (
569:             <div className="flex items-start gap-2 p-2 rounded-md bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/30 text-[10px] text-emerald-200">
570:               <AlertCircle className="h-3 w-3 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
571:               <span>Save the event first, then reopen it to add equipment and assign instructors.</span>
572:             </div>
573:           )}
574:         </div>
575:       </div>
576:       <div className="p-3 border-t border-border/60 flex justify-end gap-2">
577:         <button onClick={onClose} className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground">
578:           Cancel
579:         </button>
580:         <button onClick={save} disabled={saving}
581:           className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 flex items-center gap-1.5 disabled:opacity-50">
582:           <Save className="h-3 w-3" />
583:           {saving ? 'Saving…' : 'Save'}
584:         </button>
585:       </div>
586:     </div>
587:   )
588: }
589: 
590: function Field({ label, required, children }: { label: string; required?: boolean; children: React.ReactNode }) {
591:   return (
592:     <div>
593:       <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
594:         {label}{required && <span className="text-rose-400 ml-0.5">*</span>}
595:       </label>
596:       {children}
597:     </div>
598:   )
599: }

File: src/components/scheduler/StatsBar.tsx

  1: 'use client'
  2: 
  3: import { useState, useSyncExternalStore } from 'react'
  4: import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query'
  5: import { useTheme } from 'next-themes'
  6: import { toast } from 'sonner'
  7: import { Users, AlertTriangle, CheckCircle2, CalendarDays, ChevronDown, KeyRound, LogOut, User, Sun, Moon, Send } from 'lucide-react'
  8: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
  9: import { NotificationBell } from './NotificationBell'
 10: import { InstallAppMenuItem } from './InstallAppMenuItem'
 11: 
 12: type Props = {
 13:   totalSlots: number
 14:   filledSlots: number
 15:   conflictCount: number
 16:   weekLabel: string
 17:   userName?: string
 18:   userEmail?: string | null
 19:   onChangePassword: () => void
 20:   onLogout: () => void
 21: }
 22: 
 23: export function StatsBar({
 24:   totalSlots, filledSlots, conflictCount, weekLabel,
 25:   userName, userEmail, onChangePassword, onLogout,
 26: }: Props) {
 27:   const { theme, setTheme } = useTheme()
 28:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 29:   const mounted = useSyncExternalStore(() => () => {}, () => true, () => false)
 30:   const [menuOpen, setMenuOpen] = useState(false)
 31: 
 32:   const sendNowMutation = useMutation({
 33:     mutationFn: async () => {
 34:       const r = await fetch('/api/notifications/send-now', { method: 'POST' })
 35:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed')
 36:       return r.json()
 37:     },
 38:     onSuccess: (data: any) => {
 39:       toast.success(`Sent ${data.sent} digest email${data.sent !== 1 ? 's' : ''}${data.skipped ? ' (skipped — no API key)' : ''}`)
 40:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['notifications'] })
 41:     },
 42:     onError: () => toast.error('Failed to send notifications'),
 43:   })
 44: 
 45:   const fillPct = totalSlots === 0 ? 0 : Math.round((filledSlots / totalSlots) * 100)
 46:   const stats = [
 47:     { icon: <CalendarDays className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />, label: 'Current week', value: weekLabel, tone: 'neutral' as const },
 48:     { icon: <Users className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />, label: 'Instructors assigned', value: `${filledSlots} / ${totalSlots}`, tone: 'neutral' as const },
 49:     { icon: <CheckCircle2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />, label: 'Fill rate', value: `${fillPct}%`, tone: fillPct >= 80 ? 'good' : fillPct >= 50 ? 'warn' : 'bad' },
 50:     { icon: <AlertTriangle className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />, label: 'Conflict warnings', value: String(conflictCount), tone: conflictCount === 0 ? 'good' : 'bad' },
 51:   ]
 52:   return (
 53:     <header
 54:       className="border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 px-3 sm:px-4 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between gap-2 sm:gap-4"
 55:       role="banner"
 56:     >
 57:       <div className="flex items-center gap-2 sm:gap-3 min-w-0">
 58:         <img src="/logo.png" alt="RA Syncbot" className="h-8 w-8 sm:h-9 sm:w-9 rounded-lg object-cover shrink-0" />
 59:         <div className="min-w-0 hidden sm:block">
 60:           <h1 className="text-base font-semibold leading-tight truncate">RA Syncbot</h1>
 61:           <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">
 62:             Barbados time (AST)
 63:           </p>
 64:         </div>
 65:       </div>
 66: 
 67:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1 sm:gap-1.5 overflow-x-auto flex-1" role="group" aria-label="Schedule statistics">
 68:         {stats.map((s, i) => (
 69:           <div
 70:             key={i}
 71:             className={cn(
 72:               'flex items-center gap-1 sm:gap-1.5 px-2 sm:px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md border text-xs whitespace-nowrap shrink-0',
 73:               s.tone === 'good' && 'bg-emerald-500/10 border-emerald-500/30 text-emerald-300',
 74:               s.tone === 'warn' && 'bg-amber-500/10 border-amber-500/30 text-amber-300',
 75:               s.tone === 'bad' && 'bg-rose-500/10 border-rose-500/30 text-rose-300',
 76:               s.tone === 'neutral' && 'bg-muted/40 border-border/60 text-foreground/80',
 77:             )}
 78:             aria-label={`${s.label}: ${s.value}`}
 79:           >
 80:             {s.icon}
 81:             <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground hidden md:inline">{s.label}</span>
 82:             <span className="font-semibold tabular-nums">{s.value}</span>
 83:           </div>
 84:         ))}
 85:       </div>
 86: 
 87:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0">
 88:         {/* Theme toggle */}
 89:         {mounted && (
 90:           <button
 91:             onClick={() => setTheme(theme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark')}
 92:             className="p-2 rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px] flex items-center justify-center"
 93:             aria-label="Toggle theme"
 94:             title={theme === 'dark' ? 'Switch to light mode' : 'Switch to dark mode'}
 95:           >
 96:             {theme === 'dark' ? <Sun className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> : <Moon className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
 97:           </button>
 98:         )}
 99: 
100:         {/* Send pending notifications now (admin) */}
101:         <button
102:           onClick={() => sendNowMutation.mutate()}
103:           disabled={sendNowMutation.isPending}
104:           className="p-2 rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px] flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50"
105:           aria-label="Send pending notification emails now"
106:           title="Send all pending digest emails immediately (instead of waiting for the 8am digest)"
107:         >
108:           <Send className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
109:         </button>
110: 
111:         {/* Notifications */}
112:         <NotificationBell />
113: 
114:         {/* User menu */}
115:         <div className="relative">
116:           <button
117:             onClick={() => setMenuOpen(o => !o)}
118:             className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px]"
119:             aria-label="User menu"
120:             aria-expanded={menuOpen}
121:           >
122:             <User className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
123:             <span className="hidden sm:inline truncate max-w-[100px]">{userName ?? 'Account'}</span>
124:             <ChevronDown className="h-3 w-3" />
125:           </button>
126:           {menuOpen && (
127:             <>
128:               <div className="fixed inset-0 z-40" onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)} />
129:               <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 z-50 w-48 bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-md shadow-lg py-1">
130:                 <div className="px-3 py-2 border-b border-border/40">
131:                   <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{userName}</p>
132:                   <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">{userEmail}</p>
133:                 </div>
134:                 <button
135:                   onClick={() => { setMenuOpen(false); onChangePassword() }}
136:                   className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-xs hover:bg-muted flex items-center gap-2"
137:                 >
138:                   <KeyRound className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
139:                   Change password
140:                 </button>
141:                 <InstallAppMenuItem onAfterAction={() => setMenuOpen(false)} />
142:                 <button
143:                   onClick={() => { setMenuOpen(false); onLogout() }}
144:                   className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-xs hover:bg-muted text-rose-300 flex items-center gap-2"
145:                 >
146:                   <LogOut className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
147:                   Log out
148:                 </button>
149:               </div>
150:             </>
151:           )}
152:         </div>
153:       </div>
154:     </header>
155:   )
156: }

================
File: src/app/api/schedule/route.ts
================
  1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
  2: import { db } from '@/lib/db'
  3: 
  4: function parseList(s: string | null | undefined): string[] {
  5:   if (!s) return []
  6:   return s.split(',').map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean)
  7: }
  8: 
  9: // GET /api/schedule?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD
 10: export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
 11:   const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
 12:   const fromStr = searchParams.get('from')
 13:   const toStr = searchParams.get('to')
 14:   const includeDrafts = searchParams.get('includeDrafts') === '1'
 15: 
 16:   const from = fromStr || '2026-06-01'
 17:   const to = toStr || '2026-09-30'
 18: 
 19:   // Fetch profiles
 20:   const profileResult = await db.execute(
 21:     `SELECT * FROM Profile ORDER BY roleTier ASC, name ASC`
 22:   )
 23:   const profiles = profileResult.rows.map((p: any) => ({
 24:     ...p,
 25:     skillsList: parseList(p.skills),
 26:     unavailableList: parseList(p.unavailable),
 27:   }))
 28: 
 29:   // Fetch events (exclude Draft and Archived unless includeDrafts=1)
 30:   const eventQuery = includeDrafts
 31:     ? `SELECT * FROM Event WHERE 
 32:        (startDate >= ? AND startDate <= ?) OR 
 33:        (endDate >= ? AND endDate <= ?) OR 
 34:        (startDate <= ? AND endDate >= ?) 
 35:        ORDER BY startDate ASC`
 36:     : `SELECT * FROM Event WHERE status != 'Draft' AND (
 37:        (startDate >= ? AND startDate <= ?) OR 
 38:        (endDate >= ? AND endDate <= ?) OR 
 39:        (startDate <= ? AND endDate >= ?) 
 40:        ) ORDER BY startDate ASC`
 41:   const eventArgs = [from, to, from, to, from, to]
 42:   const eventResult = await db.execute({ sql: eventQuery, args: eventArgs })
 43:   const eventIds = eventResult.rows.map((e: any) => e.id)
 44: 
 45:   // Fetch skills for events
 46:   let eventSkills: Record<string, string[]> = {}
 47:   if (eventIds.length > 0) {
 48:     const placeholders = eventIds.map(() => '?').join(',')
 49:     const skillResult = await db.execute({
 50:       sql: `SELECT * FROM EventSkill WHERE eventId IN (${placeholders})`,
 51:       args: eventIds,
 52:     })
 53:     for (const s of skillResult.rows as any[]) {
 54:       if (!eventSkills[s.eventId]) eventSkills[s.eventId] = []
 55:       eventSkills[s.eventId].push(s.skillName)
 56:     }
 57:   }
 58: 
 59:   // Fetch opt-ins
 60:   let optInsByEvent: Record<string, any> = {}
 61:   if (eventIds.length > 0) {
 62:     const placeholders = eventIds.map(() => '?').join(',')
 63:     const optInResult = await db.execute({
 64:       sql: `SELECT o.*, u.name as userName, u.profileId as userProfileId, p.name as userProfileName
 65:             FROM OptIn o 
 66:             JOIN User u ON o.userId = u.id
 67:             LEFT JOIN Profile p ON u.profileId = p.id
 68:             WHERE o.eventId IN (${placeholders})`,
 69:       args: eventIds,
 70:     })
 71:     for (const o of optInResult.rows as any[]) {
 72:       if (!optInsByEvent[o.eventId]) {
 73:         optInsByEvent[o.eventId] = { interested: [], available: [], unavailable: [] }
 74:       }
 75:       const entry = {
 76:         id: o.id, status: o.status, note: o.note,
 77:         userId: o.userId, userName: o.userName,
 78:         userProfileId: o.userProfileId, userProfileName: o.userProfileName,
 79:       }
 80:       ;(optInsByEvent[o.eventId] as any)[o.status]?.push(entry)
 81:     }
 82:   }
 83: 
 84:   // Fetch assignments
 85:   const assignmentResult = await db.execute({
 86:     sql: `SELECT a.*, p.name as profileName, p.roleTier as profileRoleTier, 
 87:           e.name as eventName, e.hostColor as eventHostColor
 88:           FROM Assignment a
 89:           JOIN Profile p ON a.profileId = p.id
 90:           JOIN Event e ON a.eventId = e.id
 91:           WHERE a.assignedDate >= ? AND a.assignedDate <= ?
 92:           ORDER BY a.assignedDate ASC`,
 93:     args: [from, to],
 94:   })
 95: 
 96:   return NextResponse.json({
 97:     profiles,
 98:     events: eventResult.rows.map((e: any) => ({
 99:       ...e,
100:       startDate: e.startDate?.slice(0, 10),
101:       endDate: e.endDate?.slice(0, 10),
102:       specificDatesList: parseList(e.specificDates),
103:       requiredSkills: eventSkills[e.id] ?? [],
104:       setupDate: e.setupDate ? String(e.setupDate).slice(0, 10) : null,
105:       setupTime: e.setupTime ?? null,
106:       optIns: optInsByEvent[e.id] ?? { interested: [], available: [], unavailable: [] },
107:     })),
108:     assignments: assignmentResult.rows.map((a: any) => ({
109:       id: a.id,
110:       eventId: a.eventId,
111:       profileId: a.profileId,
112:       date: a.assignedDate?.slice(0, 10),
113:       status: a.status,
114:       isAlternative: !!a.isAlternative,
115:       shirtColor: a.shirtColor,
116:       ackStatus: a.ackStatus ?? null,
117:       acknowledgedAt: a.acknowledgedAt ?? null,
118:       profileName: a.profileName,
119:       profileRoleTier: a.profileRoleTier,
120:       eventName: a.eventName,
121:       eventHostColor: a.eventHostColor,
122:     })),
123:   })
124: }

212: // ---------- Date helpers ----------
213: 
214: // All date comparisons use America/Barbados time (AST, UTC-4).
215: const BBD_TZ = 'America/Barbados'
216: 
217: export function todayInBarbados(): string {
218:   const fmt = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
219:     timeZone: BBD_TZ,
220:     year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit',
221:   })
222:   return fmt.format(new Date())
223: }
224: 
225: // Is this date in the past (before today in Barbados)?
226: export function isPastDate(iso: string): boolean {
227:   return iso < todayInBarbados()
228: }
229: 
230: // Is this date today in Barbados?
231: export function isToday(iso: string): boolean {
232:   return iso === todayInBarbados()
233: }
234: 
235: // Is this event fully in the past (endDate is before today)?
236: export function isEventPast(endDate: string): boolean {
237:   return endDate < todayInBarbados()
238: }
239: 
240: export function isoWeekdaysInRange(fromISO: string, toISO: string): string[] {
241:   const out: string[] = []
242:   const d = new Date(`${fromISO}T00:00:00.000Z`)
243:   const end = new Date(`${toISO}T00:00:00.000Z`)
244:   while (d <= end) {
245:     out.push(d.toISOString().slice(0, 10))
246:     d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 1)
247:   }
248:   return out
249: }
250: 
251: export function startOfWeekISO(iso: string): string {
252:   // Monday-based week start
253:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
254:   const day = d.getUTCDay() // 0=Sun .. 6=Sat
255:   const offset = (day === 0 ? 6 : day - 1)
256:   d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() - offset)
257:   return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
258: }
259: 
260: export function addDaysISO(iso: string, days: number): string {
261:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
262:   d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + days)
263:   return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
264: }
265: 
266: export function formatPrettyDate(iso: string): string {
267:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
268:   return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
269:     weekday: 'short', month: 'short', day: 'numeric',
270:     timeZone: 'UTC',
271:   })
272: }
273: 
274: export function formatShortDate(iso: string): string {
275:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
276:   return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
277:     month: 'short', day: 'numeric', timeZone: 'UTC',
278:   })
279: }
280: 
281: export function formatWeekday(iso: string): string {
282:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
283:   return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short', timeZone: 'UTC' })
284: }
285: 
286: export function formatDayNum(iso: string): string {
287:   const d = new Date(`${iso}T00:00:00.000Z`)
288:   return String(d.getUTCDate())
289: }
290: 
291: // 24-hour "09:00" → "9:00 AM"
292: export function formatTime(t: string): string {
293:   const [h, m] = t.split(':').map(Number)
294:   const ampm = h >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM'
295:   const hh = h % 12 === 0 ? 12 : h % 12
296:   return `${hh}:${String(m || 0).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`
297: }
298: 
299: // Does the event fall on the given date?
300: // Also returns true if the date matches the event's optional setup date.
301: // Draft events don't show on the calendar. Archived events DO show (dimmed) for history.
302: export function eventOnDate(ev: EventView, dateISO: string): boolean {
303:   // Draft events never show on the calendar
304:   if (ev.status === 'Draft') return false
305:   // Check setup date
306:   if (ev.setupDate && ev.setupDate === dateISO) return true
307:   // Cancelled + Archived events still show (dimmed) so the boss can see history
308:   if (ev.specificDatesList && ev.specificDatesList.length > 0) {
309:     return ev.specificDatesList.includes(dateISO)
310:   }
311:   return ev.startDate <= dateISO && ev.endDate >= dateISO
312: }

 20: type OptInMap = Record<string, { status: string; note: string | null }>

 22: async function fetchSchedule() {
 23:   const r = await fetch('/api/schedule?from=2026-06-01&to=2026-09-30')
 24:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load schedule')
 25:   return r.json()
 26: }
 27: 
 28: async function fetchMyOptIns(): Promise<OptInMap> {
 29:   const r = await fetch('/api/opt-ins')
 30:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load opt-ins')
 31:   const list = await r.json()
 32:   const map: OptInMap = {}
 33:   for (const o of list) {
 34:     map[o.eventId] = { status: o.status, note: o.note }
 35:   }
 36:   return map
 37: }
 38: 
 39: async function fetchMyProfile() {
 40:   const profileId = 'me' // The API will use the cookie to find the user's profile
 41:   const r = await fetch('/api/profiles/me')
 42:   if (!r.ok) return null
 43:   return r.json()
 44: }
 45: 
 46: export function InstructorView({ user }: { user: AuthUser }) {
 47:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 48:   const { data } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['schedule'], queryFn: fetchSchedule })
 49:   const { data: optIns } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['my-opt-ins'], queryFn: fetchMyOptIns })
 50:   const { data: myProfile } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['my-profile'], queryFn: fetchMyProfile })
 51:   const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'assignments' | 'events' | 'calendar'>('assignments')
 52:   const [selectedEvent, setSelectedEvent] = useState<EventView | null>(null)
 53: 
 54:   // Close event drawer with Esc
 55:   useEffect(() => {
 56:     const handleEsc = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
 57:       if (e.key === 'Escape' && selectedEvent) setSelectedEvent(null)
 58:     }
 59:     window.addEventListener('keydown', handleEsc)
 60:     return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleEsc)
 61:   }, [selectedEvent])
 62: 
 63:   const optInMutation = useMutation({
 64:     mutationFn: async (args: { eventId: string; status: string }) => {
 65:       const r = await fetch('/api/opt-ins', {
 66:         method: 'POST',
 67:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 68:         body: JSON.stringify(args),
 69:       })
 70:       const j = await r.json()
 71:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
 72:       return j
 73:     },
 74:     onSuccess: () => {
 75:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['my-opt-ins'] })
 76:       toast.success('Preference saved')
 77:     },
 78:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to save preference'),
 79:   })
 80: 
 81:   const ackMutation = useMutation({
 82:     mutationFn: async (args: { id: string; ackStatus: 'confirmed' | 'declined' }) => {
 83:       const r = await fetch(`/api/assignments?id=${args.id}`, {
 84:         method: 'PATCH',
 85:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 86:         body: JSON.stringify({ ackStatus: args.ackStatus }),
 87:       })
 88:       const j = await r.json()
 89:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
 90:       return j
 91:     },
 92:     onSuccess: (_data, vars) => {
 93:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
 94:       toast.success(vars.ackStatus === 'confirmed' ? 'Assignment confirmed' : 'Assignment declined — the boss has been notified')
 95:     },
 96:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to acknowledge'),
 97:   })
 98: 
 99:   // My assignments = assignments where profileId matches the linked profile
100:   const myProfileId = user.profile?.id
101:   const myAssignments = useMemo(() => {
102:     if (!data || !myProfileId) return []
103:     return (data.assignments as AssignmentView[])
104:       .filter(a => a.profileId === myProfileId)
105:       .sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date))
106:   }, [data, myProfileId])
107: 
108:   // Split into upcoming and past (based on Barbados timezone)
109:   const { upcomingAssignments, pastAssignments } = useMemo(() => {
110:     const today = todayInBarbados()
111:     return {
112:       upcomingAssignments: myAssignments.filter(a => a.date >= today),
113:       pastAssignments: myAssignments.filter(a => a.date < today),
114:     }
115:   }, [myAssignments])
116: 
117:   // Available events to opt in to (Confirmed + Tentative, exclude Draft/Cancelled)
118:   const optableEvents = useMemo(() => {
119:     if (!data) return []
120:     return (data.events as EventView[])
121:       .filter(e => e.status === 'Confirmed' || e.status === 'Tentative')
122:       .sort((a, b) => a.startDate.localeCompare(b.startDate))
123:   }, [data])
124: 
125:   return (
126:     <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
127:       {/* Tab navigation */}
128:       <nav
129:         className="border-b border-border/60 bg-card/30 flex items-center gap-1 px-2 sm:px-3 overflow-x-auto"
130:         role="tablist"
131:         aria-label="Instructor views"
132:         style={{ WebkitOverflowScrolling: 'touch' }}
133:       >
134:         <button
135:           role="tab"
136:           aria-selected={viewMode === 'assignments'}
137:           onClick={() => setViewMode('assignments')}
138:           className={cn(
139:             'px-3 sm:px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors whitespace-nowrap min-h-[44px] flex items-center shrink-0',
140:             viewMode === 'assignments'
141:               ? 'border-emerald-400 text-foreground'
142:               : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
143:           )}
144:         >
145:           <Calendar className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5 inline" />
146:           My Assignments
147:           {myAssignments.length > 0 && (
148:             <span className="ml-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">({myAssignments.length})</span>
149:           )}
150:         </button>
151:         <button
152:           role="tab"
153:           aria-selected={viewMode === 'events'}
154:           onClick={() => setViewMode('events')}
155:           className={cn(
156:             'px-3 sm:px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors whitespace-nowrap min-h-[44px] flex items-center shrink-0',
157:             viewMode === 'events'
158:               ? 'border-emerald-400 text-foreground'
159:               : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
160:           )}
161:         >
162:           <Star className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5 inline" />
163:           Opt In
164:           {optableEvents.length > 0 && (
165:             <span className="ml-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">({optableEvents.length})</span>
166:           )}
167:         </button>
168:         <button
169:           role="tab"
170:           aria-selected={viewMode === 'calendar'}
171:           onClick={() => setViewMode('calendar')}
172:           className={cn(
173:             'px-3 sm:px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors whitespace-nowrap min-h-[44px] flex items-center shrink-0',
174:             viewMode === 'calendar'
175:               ? 'border-emerald-400 text-foreground'
176:               : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
177:           )}
178:         >
179:           <CalendarDays className="h-4 w-4 mr-1.5 inline" />
180:           Calendar
181:         </button>
182:       </nav>
183: 
184:       {viewMode === 'calendar' && data ? (
185:         <CalendarView
186:           events={data.events}
187:           assignments={data.assignments}
188:           myProfileId={user.profile?.id}
189:           readOnly
190:           onSelect={(eventId, date) => {
191:             const ev = data.events.find(e => e.id === eventId)
192:             if (ev) setSelectedEvent(ev)
193:           }}
194:         />
195:       ) : viewMode === 'assignments' ? (
196:         <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="My assignments">
197:           <div className="p-3 sm:p-4 space-y-4">
198:             {/* Upcoming assignments */}
199:             <Accordion
200:               label={`Upcoming Assignments (${upcomingAssignments.length})`}
201:               labelClassName="bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/30"
202:               defaultOpen
203:             >
204:               {upcomingAssignments.length === 0 ? (
205:                 <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground p-4 text-center">
206:                   {user.profile
207:                     ? 'No upcoming assignments. Go to the Opt In tab to express interest in events.'
208:                     : 'No staff profile linked. Ask the boss to link your account.'}
209:                 </div>
210:               ) : (
211:                 <div className="space-y-2 pt-2">
212:                   {upcomingAssignments.map(a => (
213:                     <AssignmentCard
214:                       key={a.id}
215:                       assignment={a}
216:                       event={data?.events.find((e: EventView) => e.id === a.eventId)}
217:                       onView={setSelectedEvent}
218:                       onAck={(ackStatus) => ackMutation.mutate({ id: a.id, ackStatus })}
219:                       ackPending={ackMutation.isPending}
220:                     />
221:                   ))}
222:                 </div>
223:               )}
224:             </Accordion>
225: 
226:             {/* Past assignments */}
227:             {pastAssignments.length > 0 && (
228:               <Accordion
229:                 label={`Past Assignments (${pastAssignments.length})`}
230:                 labelClassName="bg-zinc-500/15 text-zinc-300 border-zinc-500/30"
231:                 defaultOpen={false}
232:               >
233:                 <div className="space-y-2 pt-2">
234:                   {pastAssignments.map(a => (
235:                     <AssignmentCard
236:                       key={a.id}
237:                       assignment={a}
238:                       event={data?.events.find((e: EventView) => e.id === a.eventId)}
239:                       onView={setSelectedEvent}
240:                       onAck={(ackStatus) => ackMutation.mutate({ id: a.id, ackStatus })}
241:                       ackPending={ackMutation.isPending}
242:                       isPast
243:                     />
244:                   ))}
245:                 </div>
246:               </Accordion>
247:             )}
248: 
249:             {/* Availability section */}
250:             {user.profile && (
251:               <AvailabilitySection
252:                 profileId={user.profile.id}
253:                 initialUnavailable={myProfile?.unavailableList ?? user.profile.unavailable?.split(',').map((s: string) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) ?? []}
254:               />
255:             )}
256:           </div>
257:         </div>
258:       ) : viewMode === 'events' ? (
259:         <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto" role="region" aria-label="Events to opt in to">
260:           <div className="p-3 sm:p-4">
261:             {optableEvents.length === 0 ? (
262:               <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground p-4 text-center">
263:                 No events available for opt-in right now.
264:               </div>
265:             ) : (
266:               <CarouselGroup
267:                 items={optableEvents.map(ev => {
268:                   const colors = hostColor(ev.hostColor)
269:                   const optIn = optIns?.[ev.id]
270:                   const isAssigned = myAssignments.some(a => a.eventId === ev.id)
271:                   return (
272:                     <div
273:                       key={ev.id}
274:                       onClick={() => setSelectedEvent(ev)}
275:                       className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3 cursor-pointer hover:border-foreground/30 transition-all flex flex-col gap-2 h-full"
276:                     >
277:                       <div className={cn('h-1 rounded-full', colors.bar)} />
278:                       <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
279:                         <div className={cn('h-8 w-1 rounded-full shrink-0', colors.bar)} />
280:                         <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
281:                           <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{ev.name}</p>
282:                           <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
283:                             <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
284:                               <Calendar className="h-3 w-3" />
285:                               {formatShortDate(ev.startDate)}{ev.endDate !== ev.startDate && ` – ${formatShortDate(ev.endDate)}`}
286:                             </span>
287:                             <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
288:                               <Clock className="h-3 w-3" />
289:                               {formatTime(ev.startTime)}
290:                             </span>
291:                           </div>
292:                           {ev.location && (
293:                             <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 flex items-center gap-0.5 truncate">
294:                               <MapPin className="h-3 w-3" />
295:                               {ev.location}
296:                             </div>
297:                           )}
298:                         </div>
299:                       </div>
300:                       {isAssigned ? (
301:                         <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-emerald-300 bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/30 rounded px-2 py-1">
302:                           <Check className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
303:                           You&apos;re assigned to this event
304:                         </div>
305:                       ) : (
306:                         <div className="flex gap-1.5" onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
307:                           <OptInButton
308:                             active={optIn?.status === 'interested'}
309:                             color="active:bg-teal-500/20 bg-teal-500/10 text-teal-300 border-teal-500/40"
310:                             onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); optInMutation.mutate({ eventId: ev.id, status: 'interested' }) }}
311:                             icon={<Star className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
312:                             label="Interested"
313:                           />
314:                           <OptInButton
315:                             active={optIn?.status === 'available'}
316:                             color="active:bg-emerald-500/20 bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300 border-emerald-500/40"
317:                             onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); optInMutation.mutate({ eventId: ev.id, status: 'available' }) }}
318:                             icon={<Check className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
319:                             label="Available"
320:                           />
321:                           <OptInButton
322:                             active={optIn?.status === 'unavailable'}
323:                             color="active:bg-rose-500/20 bg-rose-500/10 text-rose-300 border-rose-500/40"
324:                             onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); optInMutation.mutate({ eventId: ev.id, status: 'unavailable' }) }}
325:                             icon={<X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
326:                             label="Can&apos;t"
327:                           />
328:                         </div>
329:                       )}
330:                       <p className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground/50 text-center">Tap for details</p>
331:                     </div>
332:                   )
333:                 })}
334:               />
335:             )}
336:           </div>
337:         </div>
338:       ) : null}
339: 
340:       {/* Event details drawer */}
341:       {selectedEvent && (
342:         <InstructorEventDrawer
343:           event={selectedEvent}
344:           optIn={optIns?.[selectedEvent.id]}
345:           isAssigned={myAssignments.some(a => a.eventId === selectedEvent.id)}
346:           onOptIn={(status) => optInMutation.mutate({ eventId: selectedEvent.id, status })}
347:           onClose={() => setSelectedEvent(null)}
348:           myProfileId={user.profile?.id}
349:         />
350:       )}
351:     </div>
352:   )
353: }
354: 
355: // ---------- Assignment card (used in both upcoming + past accordions) ----------
356: 
357: function AssignmentCard({ assignment: a, event: ev, onView, onAck, ackPending, isPast }: {
358:   assignment: AssignmentView
359:   event: EventView | undefined
360:   onView: (event: EventView) => void
361:   onAck: (ackStatus: 'confirmed' | 'declined') => void
362:   ackPending: boolean
363:   isPast?: boolean
364: }) {
365:   if (!ev) return null
366:   const colors = hostColor(ev.hostColor)
367:   const acked = a.ackStatus === 'confirmed'
368:   const declined = a.ackStatus === 'declined'
369:   return (
370:     <div
371:       className={cn(
372:         'rounded-lg border p-3 flex items-center gap-3 transition-all',
373:         a.isAlternative
374:           ? 'border-amber-500/30 border-dashed bg-amber-500/5'
375:           : 'border-border/60 bg-card/80',
376:         isPast && 'opacity-70',
377:         acked && 'border-emerald-500/40 bg-emerald-500/5',
378:         declined && 'border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/5',
379:       )}
380:     >
381:       <button
382:         onClick={() => onView(ev)}
383:         className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1 min-w-0 text-left"
384:         aria-label={`View details for ${ev.name}`}
385:       >
386:         <div className={cn('h-8 w-1 rounded-full shrink-0', colors.bar)} />
387:         <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
388:           <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
389:             <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{ev.name}</p>
390:             {a.isAlternative && (
391:               <span className="text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 flex items-center gap-0.5 shrink-0">
392:                 <Shield className="h-3 w-3" /> Alt
393:               </span>
394:             )}
395:             {acked && (
396:               <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 flex items-center gap-0.5 shrink-0">
397:                 <Check className="h-2.5 w-2.5" /> Confirmed
398:               </span>
399:             )}
400:             {declined && (
401:               <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-300 flex items-center gap-0.5 shrink-0">
402:                 <X className="h-2.5 w-2.5" /> Declined
403:               </span>
404:             )}
405:           </div>
406:           <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
407:             <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
408:               <Calendar className="h-3 w-3" />
409:               {formatPrettyDate(a.date)}
410:             </span>
411:             <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
412:               <Clock className="h-3 w-3" />
413:               {formatTime(ev.startTime)}
414:             </span>
415:             {a.shirtColor && (
416:               <span className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
417:                 <Shirt className="h-3 w-3" />
418:                 {a.shirtColor}
419:               </span>
420:             )}
421:           </div>
422:         </div>
423:       </button>
424:       {/* Acknowledge buttons (hidden for past or already-acked assignments) */}
425:       {!isPast && !acked && !declined && (
426:         <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
427:           <button
428:             onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onAck('confirmed') }}
429:             disabled={ackPending}
430:             className="p-2 rounded-md border border-emerald-500/40 bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300 hover:bg-emerald-500/20 min-h-[36px] min-w-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
431:             aria-label="Confirm assignment — I'll be there"
432:             title="Confirm — I'll be there"
433:           >
434:             <Check className="h-4 w-4" />
435:           </button>
436:           <button
437:             onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onAck('declined') }}
438:             disabled={ackPending}
439:             className="p-2 rounded-md border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/10 text-rose-300 hover:bg-rose-500/20 min-h-[36px] min-w-[36px] flex items-center justify-center"
440:             aria-label="Decline assignment — I can't make it"
441:             title="Decline — I can't make it"
442:           >
443:             <X className="h-4 w-4" />
444:           </button>
445:         </div>
446:       )}
447:     </div>
448:   )
449: }
450: 
451: // ---------- Carousel (5 items per group, horizontal scroll on each group) ----------
452: 
453: function CarouselGroup({ items, itemsPerGroup = 5 }: { items: React.ReactNode[]; itemsPerGroup?: number }) {
454:   // Split items into groups of itemsPerGroup; each group is a horizontal scroll row
455:   const groups: React.ReactNode[][] = []
456:   for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i += itemsPerGroup) {
457:     groups.push(items.slice(i, i + itemsPerGroup))
458:   }
459:   if (groups.length === 0) {
460:     return (
461:       <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground p-4 text-center border border-dashed border-border/60 rounded-md">
462:         No items to display.
463:       </div>
464:     )
465:   }
466: 
467:   return (
468:     <div className="space-y-4">
469:       {groups.map((group, gi) => (
470:         <div
471:           key={gi}
472:           className="flex gap-3 overflow-x-auto pb-2 snap-x snap-mandatory"
473:           style={{ scrollbarWidth: 'thin', WebkitOverflowScrolling: 'touch' }}
474:         >
475:           {group.map((item, ii) => (
476:             <div key={ii} className="min-w-[280px] sm:min-w-[320px] snap-start shrink-0">
477:               {item}
478:             </div>
479:           ))}
480:         </div>
481:       ))}
482:     </div>
483:   )
484: }
485: 
486: // ---------- Event details drawer (instructor view) ----------
487: 
488: function InstructorEventDrawer({ event, optIn, isAssigned, onOptIn, onClose, myProfileId }: {
489:   event: EventView
490:   optIn?: { status: string; note: string | null }
491:   isAssigned: boolean
492:   onOptIn: (status: 'interested' | 'available' | 'unavailable') => void
493:   onClose: () => void
494:   myProfileId?: string | null
495: }) {
496:   const colors = hostColor(event.hostColor)
497:   return (
498:     <div
499:       className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-end sm:items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-0 sm:p-4"
500:       onClick={onClose}
501:       role="dialog"
502:       aria-modal="true"
503:       aria-label={event.name}
504:     >
505:       <div
506:         className="bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-t-lg sm:rounded-lg max-w-md w-full max-h-[85vh] overflow-y-auto"
507:         onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
508:       >
509:         <div className={cn('h-1 rounded-t-lg', colors.bar)} />
510:         <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
511:           <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
512:             <div className="min-w-0">
513:               <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{event.code ?? 'No code'}</p>
514:               <h2 className="text-base font-semibold leading-tight">{event.name}</h2>
515:               <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 mt-1 flex-wrap">
516:                 <span className={cn('text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', colors.chip)}>
517:                   {event.host}
518:                 </span>
519:                 <span className={cn('text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border', EVENT_STATUS_COLOR[event.status] ?? EVENT_STATUS_COLOR.Confirmed)}>
520:                   {event.status}
521:                 </span>
522:               </div>
523:             </div>
524:             <button
525:               onClick={onClose}
526:               className="p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
527:               aria-label="Close"
528:             >
529:               <XIcon className="h-4 w-4" />
530:             </button>
531:           </div>
532: 
533:           <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-xs">
534:             <div className="p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40">
535:               <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mb-0.5">
536:                 <Calendar className="h-3 w-3" />
537:                 Dates
538:               </div>
539:               <p className="text-xs font-medium">
540:                 {formatShortDate(event.startDate)}{event.endDate !== event.startDate && ` – ${formatShortDate(event.endDate)}`}
541:               </p>
542:             </div>
543:             <div className="p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40">
544:               <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mb-0.5">
545:                 <Clock className="h-3 w-3" />
546:                 Time
547:               </div>
548:               <p className="text-xs font-medium">{formatTime(event.startTime)} – {formatTime(event.endTime)}</p>
549:             </div>
550:             {event.location && (
551:               <div className="p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40">
552:                 <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mb-0.5">
553:                   <MapPin className="h-3 w-3" />
554:                   Location
555:                 </div>
556:                 <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{event.location}</p>
557:               </div>
558:             )}
559:             <div className="p-2 rounded-md bg-muted/30 border border-border/40">
560:               <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mb-0.5">
561:                 <Users className="h-3 w-3" />
562:                 Instructors
563:               </div>
564:               <p className="text-xs font-medium">{event.requiredInstructors} needed</p>
565:             </div>
566:           </div>
567: 
568:           {event.description && (
569:             <div>
570:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1">Description</h3>
571:               <p className="text-xs leading-relaxed">{event.description}</p>
572:             </div>
573:           )}
574: 
575:           {event.requiredSkills.length > 0 && (
576:             <div>
577:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1">Skills</h3>
578:               <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
579:                 {event.requiredSkills.map(s => (
580:                   <span key={s} className="text-[11px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded bg-muted/60 text-foreground/80">
581:                     {s}
582:                   </span>
583:                 ))}
584:               </div>
585:             </div>
586:           )}
587: 
588:           {event.notes && (
589:             <div>
590:               <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-1">Notes</h3>
591:               <p className="text-xs leading-relaxed text-muted-foreground">{event.notes}</p>
592:             </div>
593:           )}
594: 
595:           {/* Equipment coordination (instructor view — only if assigned) */}
596:           {isAssigned && (
597:             <EquipmentSection event={event} mode="instructor" myProfileId={myProfileId} />
598:           )}
599: 
600:           {/* Opt-in section */}
601:           <div className="pt-2 border-t border-border/40">
602:             {isAssigned ? (
603:               <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-emerald-300 bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/30 rounded-md px-3 py-2">
604:                 <Check className="h-4 w-4" />
605:                 You&apos;re assigned to this event
606:               </div>
607:             ) : (
608:               <>
609:                 <p className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground mb-2">
610:                   Your preference {optIn && `(currently: ${optIn.status})`}
611:                 </p>
612:                 <div className="flex gap-2">
613:                   <button
614:                     onClick={() => onOptIn('interested')}
615:                     className={cn(
616:                       'flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 text-xs rounded-md border transition-colors min-h-[40px]',
617:                       optIn?.status === 'interested'
618:                         ? 'bg-teal-500/15 border-teal-500/40 text-teal-300'
619:                         : 'border-border/60 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/40',
620:                     )}
621:                   >
622:                     <Star className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
623:                     Interested
624:                   </button>
625:                   <button
626:                     onClick={() => onOptIn('available')}
627:                     className={cn(
628:                       'flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 text-xs rounded-md border transition-colors min-h-[40px]',
629:                       optIn?.status === 'available'
630:                         ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 border-emerald-500/40 text-emerald-300'
631:                         : 'border-border/60 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/40',
632:                     )}
633:                   >
634:                     <Check className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
635:                     Available
636:                   </button>
637:                   <button
638:                     onClick={() => onOptIn('unavailable')}
639:                     className={cn(
640:                       'flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 text-xs rounded-md border transition-colors min-h-[40px]',
641:                       optIn?.status === 'unavailable'
642:                         ? 'bg-rose-500/15 border-rose-500/40 text-rose-300'
643:                         : 'border-border/60 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/40',
644:                     )}
645:                   >
646:                     <X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
647:                     Can&apos;t
648:                   </button>
649:                 </div>
650:               </>
651:             )}
652:           </div>
653:         </div>
654:       </div>
655:     </div>
656:   )
657: }
658: 
659: // ---------- Availability section ----------
660: 
661: function AvailabilitySection({ profileId, initialUnavailable }: {
662:   profileId: string
663:   initialUnavailable: string[]
664: }) {
665:   const qc = useQueryClient()
666:   const [unavailable, setUnavailable] = useState<string[]>(initialUnavailable)
667:   const [newDate, setNewDate] = useState('')
668:   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
669: 
670:   const addDate = () => {
671:     if (!newDate) return
672:     if (unavailable.includes(newDate)) {
673:       toast.error('That date is already in your unavailable list')
674:       return
675:     }
676:     setUnavailable([...unavailable, newDate].sort())
677:     setNewDate('')
678:   }
679: 
680:   const removeDate = (date: string) => {
681:     setUnavailable(unavailable.filter(d => d !== date))
682:   }
683: 
684:   const save = async () => {
685:     setSaving(true)
686:     try {
687:       const r = await fetch(`/api/profiles?id=${profileId}`, {
688:         method: 'PUT',
689:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
690:         body: JSON.stringify({ unavailable }),
691:       })
692:       const j = await r.json()
693:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed to save')
694:       toast.success('Availability updated')
695:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['my-profile'] })
696:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
697:     } catch (e: any) {
698:       toast.error(e.message || 'Save failed')
699:     } finally {
700:       setSaving(false)
701:     }
702:   }
703: 
704:   const hasChanges = JSON.stringify(unavailable.sort()) !== JSON.stringify(initialUnavailable.sort())
705: 
706:   return (
707:     <section aria-label="My availability">
708:       <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
709:         <h3 className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5">
710:           <Calendar className="h-3 w-3" />
711:           My Availability
712:         </h3>
713:         {hasChanges && (
714:           <button
715:             onClick={save}
716:             disabled={saving}
717:             className="px-2.5 py-1 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 min-h-[28px]"
718:           >
719:             {saving ? 'Saving…' : 'Save changes'}
720:           </button>
721:         )}
722:       </div>
723:       <div className="rounded-lg border border-border/60 bg-card/80 p-3 space-y-3">
724:         <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
725:           Add dates you can&apos;t work. The boss will see these when assigning you to events, and the scheduler will block assignments on these dates.
726:         </p>
727: 
728:         {/* Add date */}
729:         <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
730:           <input
731:             type="date"
732:             value={newDate}
733:             onChange={e => setNewDate(e.target.value)}
734:             className="px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
735:           />
736:           <button
737:             onClick={addDate}
738:             disabled={!newDate}
739:             className="px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[36px]"
740:           >
741:             <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
742:             Add date
743:           </button>
744:         </div>
745: 
746:         {/* Unavailable dates list */}
747:         {unavailable.length === 0 ? (
748:           <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground italic text-center py-2">
749:             No unavailable dates set — you&apos;re available every day.
750:           </div>
751:         ) : (
752:           <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
753:             {unavailable.map(date => (
754:               <span
755:                 key={date}
756:                 className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-md bg-rose-500/10 border border-rose-500/30 text-rose-300 text-[11px]"
757:               >
758:                 <Calendar className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
759:                 {formatPrettyDate(date)}
760:                 <button
761:                   onClick={() => removeDate(date)}
762:                   className="ml-1 hover:text-rose-100"
763:                   aria-label={`Remove ${date}`}
764:                 >
765:                   <X className="h-3 w-3" />
766:                 </button>
767:               </span>
768:             ))}
769:           </div>
770:         )}
771:       </div>
772:     </section>
773:   )
774: }

799: // ---------- Claim form (shown when visiting with a token but not yet claimed) ----------
800: 
801: export function ClaimInviteForm({ token, onClaimed }: { token: string; onClaimed: () => void }) {
802:   const [name, setName] = useState('')
803:   const [email, setEmail] = useState('')
804:   const [password, setPassword] = useState('')
805:   const [confirmPassword, setConfirmPassword] = useState('')
806:   const [verifyCode, setVerifyCode] = useState('')
807:   const [step, setStep] = useState<'details' | 'verify'>('details')
808:   const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
809: 
810:   const submit = async () => {
811:     if (!email) {
812:       toast.error('Email is required')
813:       return
814:     }
815:     if (!password || password.length < 6) {
816:       toast.error('Password must be at least 6 characters')
817:       return
818:     }
819:     if (password !== confirmPassword) {
820:       toast.error('Passwords do not match')
821:       return
822:     }
823:     setSubmitting(true)
824:     try {
825:       if (step === 'details') {
826:         // Step 1: send verification code
827:         const r = await fetch('/api/auth/claim', {
828:           method: 'POST',
829:           headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
830:           body: JSON.stringify({ token, name, email, password }),
831:         })
832:         const j = await r.json()
833:         if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
834:         if (j.step === 'verify') {
835:           setStep('verify')
836:           toast.success('Verification code sent to your email')
837:         } else {
838:           // No verification needed (dev mode) — account claimed
839:           toast.success('Account claimed')
840:           onClaimed()
841:         }
842:       } else {
843:         // Step 2: verify code + claim
844:         const r = await fetch('/api/auth/claim', {
845:           method: 'POST',
846:           headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
847:           body: JSON.stringify({ token, name, email, password, verifyCode }),
848:         })
849:         const j = await r.json()
850:         if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed to claim')
851:         toast.success('Account verified!')
852:         onClaimed()
853:       }
854:     } catch (e: any) {
855:       toast.error(e.message || 'Claim failed')
856:     } finally {
857:       setSubmitting(false)
858:     }
859:   }
860: 
861:   return (
862:     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background p-6">
863:       <div className="max-w-sm w-full">
864:         <div className="text-center mb-6">
865:           <img src="/logo.png" alt="RA Syncbot" className="h-16 w-16 mx-auto mb-3 rounded-xl object-cover" />
866:           <h1 className="text-lg font-semibold">You&apos;re invited!</h1>
867:           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
868:             {step === 'details'
869:               ? 'Claim your account to view the camp schedule and opt in to events.'
870:               : 'Enter the 6-digit code we sent to your email.'}
871:           </p>
872:         </div>
873: 
874:         <div className="space-y-3 bg-card/80 border border-border/60 rounded-lg p-4">
875:           {step === 'details' ? (
876:             <>
877:               <div className="flex items-start gap-2 p-2 rounded-md bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/30 text-[10px] text-emerald-200">
878:                 <AlertCircle className="h-3 w-3 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
879:                 <span>Set a password you&apos;ll remember — you&apos;ll use it with your email to log in next time. We&apos;ll send a verification code to your email.</span>
880:               </div>
881: 
882:               <div>
883:                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
884:                   Your name (optional)
885:                 </label>
886:                 <input
887:                   value={name}
888:                   onChange={e => setName(e.target.value)}
889:                   placeholder="e.g. Jamie Smith"
890:                   className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
891:                 />
892:               </div>
893:               <div>
894:                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
895:                   Email (required)
896:                 </label>
897:                 <input
898:                   value={email}
899:                   onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)}
900:                   type="email"
901:                   placeholder="you@example.com"
902:                   className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
903:                 />
904:               </div>
905:               <div>
906:                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
907:                   Password (min 6 characters)
908:                 </label>
909:                 <input
910:                   value={password}
911:                   onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)}
912:                   type="password"
913:                   placeholder="••••••••"
914:                   className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
915:                 />
916:               </div>
917:               <div>
918:                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
919:                   Confirm password
920:                 </label>
921:                 <input
922:                   value={confirmPassword}
923:                   onChange={e => setConfirmPassword(e.target.value)}
924:                   type="password"
925:                   placeholder="••••••••"
926:                   className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-emerald-400"
927:                   onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && submit()}
928:                 />
929:               </div>
930:               <button
931:                 onClick={submit}
932:                 disabled={submitting}
933:                 className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 min-h-[40px]"
934:               >
935:                 {submitting ? 'Sending code…' : 'Send verification code'}
936:               </button>
937:             </>
938:           ) : (
939:             <>
940:               <div className="flex items-start gap-2 p-2 rounded-md bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/30 text-[10px] text-emerald-200">
941:                 <AlertCircle className="h-3 w-3 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
942:                 <span>Enter the 6-digit code sent to <strong>{email}</strong>. The code expires in 10 minutes.</span>
943:               </div>
944:               <div>
945:                 <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
946:                   Verification code
947:                 </label>
948:                 <input
949:                   value={verifyCode}
950:                   onChange={e => setVerifyCode(e.target.value)}
951:                   type="text"
952:                   inputMode="numeric"
953:                   maxLength={6}
954:                   placeholder="123456"
955:                   className="w-full px-2 py-3 text-center text-2xl tracking-[0.5em] rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400 font-mono"
956:                   onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && submit()}
957:                   autoFocus
958:                 />
959:               </div>
960:               <button
961:                 onClick={submit}
962:                 disabled={submitting || verifyCode.length !== 6}
963:                 className="w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 min-h-[40px]"
964:               >
965:                 {submitting ? 'Verifying…' : 'Verify & claim account'}
966:               </button>
967:               <button
968:                 onClick={() => { setStep('details'); setVerifyCode('') }}
969:                 className="w-full px-3 py-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
970:               >
971:                 ← Back to details
972:               </button>
973:             </>
974:           )}
975:         </div>
976:       </div>
977:     </div>
978:   )
979: }

 39: async function fetchSchedule(): Promise<ScheduleData> {
 40:   // Auto-archive past events + send reminders (fire-and-forget)
 41:   fetch('/api/auto-archive', { method: 'POST' }).catch(() => {})
 42:   fetch('/api/reminders', { method: 'POST' }).catch(() => {})

 44:   if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load schedule')

 48: async function fetchMe(): Promise<{ user: AuthUser | null }> {
 49:   const r = await fetch('/api/auth/me')
 50:   if (!r.ok) return { user: null }
 51:   return r.json()
