 54: type Tab = 'scheduler' | 'calendar' | 'events' | 'team' | 'conflicts' | 'workload' | 'invites'
 55: 
 56: export default function Home() {
 57:   const qc = useQueryClient()
 58: 
 59:   // Auth state
 60:   const { data: meData, refetch: refetchMe } = useQuery({ queryKey: ['me'], queryFn: fetchMe })
 61:   const user = meData?.user ?? null
 62: 
 63:   const [claimToken, setClaimToken] = useState<string | null>(null)
 64:   const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false)
 65:   useEffect(() => {
 66:     setMounted(true)
 67:     if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
 68:       const url = new URL(window.location.href)
 69:       const t = url.searchParams.get('token')
 70:       if (t) setClaimToken(t)
 71:     }
 72:   }, [])
 73: 
 74:   // Active tab
 75:   const [tab, setTab] = useState<Tab>('scheduler')
 76: 
 77:   // Scheduler state
 78:   const [weekStart, setWeekStart] = useState<string>(() => startOfWeekISO('2026-07-06'))
 79:   const [weekPinned, setWeekPinned] = useState(false)
 80:   const [rosterCollapsed, setRosterCollapsed] = useState(false)
 81:   const [selected, setSelected] = useState<{ eventId: string; date: string } | null>(null)
 82:   const [activeDrag, setActiveDrag] = useState<{ profileId: string } | null>(null)
 83:   const [printMode, setPrintMode] = useState(false)
 84:   const [showChangePassword, setShowChangePassword] = useState(false)
 85:   const [tapSelectedProfileId, setTapSelectedProfileId] = useState<string | null>(null)
 86:   const isMobile = useIsMobile()
 87: 
 88:   // Prevent back button from accidentally leaving the app.
 89:   // Push a dummy history state on mount; when user presses back, we intercept it
 90:   // and show a toast instead of navigating away.
 91:   useEffect(() => {
 92:     // Only run in browser
 93:     if (typeof window === 'undefined') return
 94:     // Push a state so there's something to go "back" to
 95:     window.history.pushState({ app: true }, '', window.location.href)
 96: 
 97:     const handlePopState = (e: PopStateEvent) => {
 98:       // User pressed back — re-push the state so they stay in the app
 99:       window.history.pushState({ app: true }, '', window.location.href)
100:       // Show a toast telling them to press back again to leave
101:       toast('Press back again to exit', {
102:         description: 'Use the tabs to navigate within the app.',
103:         duration: 3000,
104:       })
105:     }
106: 
107:     window.addEventListener('popstate', handlePopState)
108:     return () => window.removeEventListener('popstate', handlePopState)
109:   }, [])
110: 
111:   // Close drawers/modals with Esc key
112:   // Priority: event drawer → change password modal → tap selection
113:   useEffect(() => {
114:     const handleEsc = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
115:       if (e.key !== 'Escape') return
116:       if (selected) { setSelected(null); return }
117:       if (showChangePassword) { setShowChangePassword(false); return }
118:       if (tapSelectedProfileId) { setTapSelectedProfileId(null); return }
119:     }
120:     window.addEventListener('keydown', handleEsc)
121:     return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleEsc)
122:   }, [selected, showChangePassword, tapSelectedProfileId])
123: 
124:   // Print handler — renders PrintLayout to a portal, triggers window.print(), then cleans up
125:   const handlePrint = useCallback(() => {
126:     setPrintMode(true)
127:     document.body.classList.add('printing')
128:     // Wait for the print layout to render, then trigger print
129:     setTimeout(() => {
130:       window.print()
131:       // Cleanup after print dialog closes
132:       const cleanup = () => {
133:         setPrintMode(false)
134:         document.body.classList.remove('printing')
135:         window.removeEventListener('afterprint', cleanup)
136:       }
137:       window.addEventListener('afterprint', cleanup)
138:       // Fallback cleanup in case afterprint doesn't fire
139:       setTimeout(() => {
140:         setPrintMode(false)
141:         document.body.classList.remove('printing')
142:       }, 2000)
143:     }, 300)
144:   }, [])
145: 
146:   // Jump from Conflicts tab to an event in the Scheduler
147:   const handleJumpToEvent = useCallback((eventId: string, date: string) => {
148:     setTab('scheduler')
149:     setWeekPinned(true)
150:     setWeekStart(startOfWeekISO(date))
151:     setSelected({ eventId, date })
152:   }, [])
153: 
154:   const { data, isLoading, error } = useQuery({
155:     queryKey: ['schedule'],
156:     queryFn: fetchSchedule,
157:     enabled: !user || user.role === 'admin', // instructors use a different view
158:   })
159: 
160:   // On mobile, we use tap-to-assign instead of drag-drop.
161:   // The sensors are always created (hooks rule), but on mobile we set an impossible
162:   // activation distance so drag never triggers.
163:   const sensors = useSensors(
164:     useSensor(PointerSensor, {
165:       activationConstraint: { distance: isMobile ? 9999 : 8 },
166:     }),
167:     useSensor(TouchSensor, {
168:       activationConstraint: { delay: 250, tolerance: 8 },
169:       disabled: isMobile,
170:     }),
171:   )
172: 
173:   // Auto-jump to the first event's week on first admin load.
174:   const effectiveWeekStart = !weekPinned && data?.events?.length
175:     ? startOfWeekISO(data.events[0].startDate)
176:     : weekStart
177:   const setWeek = useCallback((next: string | ((prev: string) => string)) => {
178:     setWeekPinned(true)
179:     setWeekStart(next)
180:   }, [])
181: 
182:   // ---- mutations ----
183:   const assignMutation = useMutation({
184:     mutationFn: async (args: { eventId: string; profileId: string; date: string; overrideFlag?: boolean }) => {
185:       const r = await fetch('/api/assignments', {
186:         method: 'POST',
187:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
188:         body: JSON.stringify(args),
189:       })
190:       const json = await r.json()
191:       if (!r.ok) throw { status: r.status, body: json }
192:       return json
193:     },
194:     onSuccess: (_data, vars) => {
195:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
196:       toast.success(`Assigned`, { description: vars.date })
197:     },
198:     onError: (err: any, vars) => {
199:       const conflict = err?.body?.conflict
200:       if (conflict?.level === 'error') {
201:         toast.error(`Cannot assign — ${conflict.reasons.join('; ')}`)
202:       } else if (conflict?.level === 'warning') {
203:         // Only fatigue warnings reach here now (skill-match was removed)
204:         toast(`Warning: ${conflict.reasons.join('; ')}`, {
205:           description: 'Click to override and assign anyway.',
206:           duration: 8000,
207:           action: {
208:             label: 'Override',
209:             onClick: () => assignMutation.mutate({ ...vars, overrideFlag: true }),
210:           },
211:         })
212:       } else {
213:         toast.error(err?.body?.error || 'Failed to assign')
214:       }
215:     },
216:   })
217: 
218:   const removeMutation = useMutation({
219:     mutationFn: async (id: string) => {
220:       const r = await fetch(`/api/assignments?id=${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
221:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to remove')
222:       return r.json()
223:     },
224:     onSuccess: () => {
225:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
226:       toast.success('Removed from event')
227:     },
228:     onError: () => toast.error('Failed to remove'),
229:   })
230: 
231:   const patchAssignmentMutation = useMutation({
232:     mutationFn: async (args: { id: string; patch: { isAlternative?: boolean; shirtColor?: string | null } }) => {
233:       const r = await fetch(`/api/assignments?id=${args.id}`, {
234:         method: 'PATCH',
235:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
236:         body: JSON.stringify(args.patch),
237:       })
238:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Failed to update')
239:       return r.json()
240:     },
241:     onSuccess: () => {
242:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
243:     },
244:     onError: () => toast.error('Failed to update assignment'),
245:   })
246: 
247:   // Multi-day assignment: drop onto the "↧ all days" handle
248:   const bulkAssignMutation = useMutation({
249:     mutationFn: async (args: { eventId: string; profileId: string }) => {
250:       const r = await fetch('/api/assignments/bulk', {
251:         method: 'POST',
252:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
253:         body: JSON.stringify(args),
254:       })
255:       const j = await r.json()
256:       if (!r.ok && r.status !== 409) throw { status: r.status, body: j }
257:       return { status: r.status, body: j }
258:     },
259:     onSuccess: (res: any) => {
260:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['schedule'] })
261:       const { created, existing, conflicts, details } = res.body
262:       const parts: string[] = []
263:       if (created) parts.push(`${created} day${created > 1 ? 's' : ''} assigned`)
264:       if (existing) parts.push(`${existing} already assigned`)
265:       if (conflicts) parts.push(`${conflicts} conflict${conflicts > 1 ? 's' : ''} skipped`)
266:       toast.success(`Multi-day assign: ${parts.join(' · ')}`)
267:       // If there were conflicts, show the details
268:       if (conflicts > 0) {
269:         const conflictDetails = details
270:           .filter((d: any) => d.status === 'conflict')
271:           .map((d: any) => `${d.date}: ${d.conflict?.reasons.join('; ')}`)
272:           .join('\n')
273:         toast.warning('Conflicts skipped', { description: conflictDetails, duration: 10000 })
274:       }
275:     },
276:     onError: (err: any) => {
277:       toast.error(err?.body?.error || 'Failed to bulk assign')
278:     },
279:   })
280: 
281:   const logoutMutation = useMutation({
282:     mutationFn: async () => fetch('/api/auth/logout', { method: 'POST' }).then(r => r.json()),
283:     onSuccess: () => {
284:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['me'] })
285:       setTab('scheduler')
286:       toast.success('Logged out')
287:     },
288:   })
289: 
290:   const changePasswordMutation = useMutation({
291:     mutationFn: async (args: { currentPassword: string; newPassword: string }) => {
292:       const r = await fetch('/api/auth/change-password', {
293:         method: 'POST',
294:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
295:         body: JSON.stringify(args),
296:       })
297:       const j = await r.json()
298:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error(j.error || 'Failed')
299:       return j
300:     },
301:     onSuccess: () => {
302:       toast.success('Password changed')
303:       setShowChangePassword(false)
304:     },
305:     onError: (e: any) => toast.error(e.message || 'Failed to change password'),
306:   })
307: 
308:   // Tap-to-assign (mobile): when an instructor is selected and an event slot is tapped,
309:   // assign the instructor to that event+date.
310:   const handleTapAssign = useCallback((eventId: string, date: string) => {
311:     if (!tapSelectedProfileId) {
312:       // No instructor selected — just open the event drawer
313:       setSelected({ eventId, date })
314:       return
315:     }
316:     assignMutation.mutate({
317:       eventId,
318:       profileId: tapSelectedProfileId,
319:       date,
320:     })
321:     setTapSelectedProfileId(null)
322:   }, [tapSelectedProfileId, assignMutation])
323: 
324:   // ---- dnd handlers ----
325:   const onDragStart = (e: { active: { data: { current: any } } }) => {
326:     const d = e.active.data.current
327:     if (d?.type === 'profile') setActiveDrag({ profileId: d.profileId })
328:   }
329:   const onDragEnd = (e: { over?: { data: { current: any } } | null; active: { data: { current: any } } }) => {
330:     setActiveDrag(null)
331:     const overData = e.over?.data.current
332:     const activeData = e.active.data.current
333:     if (!overData || !activeData || activeData.type !== 'profile') return
334: 
335:     if (overData.type === 'event-drop-all') {
336:       // Multi-day assignment
337:       bulkAssignMutation.mutate({
338:         eventId: overData.eventId,
339:         profileId: activeData.profileId,
340:       })
341:     } else if (overData.type === 'event-drop') {
342:       // Single-day assignment
343:       assignMutation.mutate({
344:         eventId: overData.eventId,
345:         profileId: activeData.profileId,
346:         date: overData.date,
347:       })
348:     }
349:   }
350: 
351:   // ---- derived values ----
352:   const weekDates = useMemo(
353:     () => Array.from({ length: 7 }, (_, i) => addDaysISO(effectiveWeekStart, i)),
354:     [effectiveWeekStart],
355:   )
356: 
357:   const weekEvents = useMemo(() => {
358:     if (!data) return []
359:     return data.events.filter(ev =>
360:       weekDates.some(d => ev.startDate <= d && ev.endDate >= d),
361:     )
362:   }, [data, weekDates])
363: 
364:   const weekAssignments = useMemo(() => {
365:     if (!data) return []
366:     const set = new Set(weekDates)
367:     return data.assignments.filter(a => set.has(a.date))
368:   }, [data, weekDates])
369: 
370:   const { totalSlots, filledSlots, conflictCount } = useMemo(() => {
371:     if (!data) return { totalSlots: 0, filledSlots: 0, conflictCount: 0 }
372:     let total = 0, filled = 0, conflicts = 0
373:     for (const ev of weekEvents) {
374:       const eventDaysThisWeek = weekDates.filter(d => ev.startDate <= d && ev.endDate >= d)
375:       for (const d of eventDaysThisWeek) {
376:         total += ev.requiredInstructors
377:         const dayAssignments = weekAssignments.filter(a => a.eventId === ev.id && a.date === d)
378:         const primaries = dayAssignments.filter(a => !a.isAlternative).length
379:         filled += Math.min(primaries, ev.requiredInstructors)
380:         if (primaries > ev.requiredInstructors) conflicts += primaries - ev.requiredInstructors
381:       }
382:     }
383:     return { totalSlots: total, filledSlots: filled, conflictCount: conflicts }
384:   }, [data, weekEvents, weekAssignments, weekDates])
385: 
386:   const selectedEvent = selected ? data?.events.find(e => e.id === selected.eventId) ?? null : null
387:   const selectedAssignments = selected
388:     ? data?.assignments.filter(a => a.eventId === selected.eventId && a.date === selected.date) ?? []
389:     : []
390:   const selectedProfile = activeDrag ? data?.profiles.find(p => p.id === activeDrag.profileId) ?? null : null
391: 
392:   // ---- CLAIM FLOW ----
393:   // If the URL has ?token=..., show the claim form (or instructor view if already claimed).
394:   // Wait for mount to avoid hydration mismatch.
395:   if (mounted && claimToken) {
396:     if (user && (user.role === 'instructor' || user.role === 'admin')) {
397:       // Already claimed — show appropriate view
398:       if (user.role === 'instructor') {
399:         return (
400:           <div className="h-screen flex flex-col bg-background">
401:             <InstructorTopBar user={user} onLogout={() => logoutMutation.mutate()} onChangePassword={() => setShowChangePassword(true)} />
402:             <InstructorView user={user} />
403:           </div>
404:         )
405:       }
406:       // Admin with token in URL — just clear it and show admin view
407:       // (falls through to admin view below)
408:     } else {
409:       return (
410:         <ClaimInviteForm
411:           token={claimToken}
412:           onClaimed={() => {
413:             setClaimToken('')
414:             if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
415:               const url = new URL(window.location.href)
416:               url.searchParams.delete('token')
417:               window.history.replaceState({}, '', url.toString())
418:             }
419:             refetchMe()
420:           }}
421:         />
422:       )
423:     }
424:   }
425: 
426:   // ---- LOGIN REQUIRED ----
427:   // After mount, if no user is logged in, show the login form.
428:   // This closes the security hole where logout → admin view.
429:   if (mounted && !user) {
430:     return <LoginForm onLoggedIn={() => refetchMe()} />
431:   }
432: 
433:   // ---- INSTRUCTOR VIEW ----
434:   if (mounted && user && user.role === 'instructor') {
435:     return (
436:       <div className="h-screen flex flex-col bg-background">
437:         <InstructorTopBar user={user} onLogout={() => logoutMutation.mutate()} onChangePassword={() => setShowChangePassword(true)} />
438:         <InstructorView user={user} />
439:         {showChangePassword && (
440:           <ChangePasswordModal
441:             onClose={() => setShowChangePassword(false)}
442:             onSubmit={(current, next) => changePasswordMutation.mutate({ currentPassword: current, newPassword: next })}
443:             saving={changePasswordMutation.isPending}
444:           />
445:         )}
446:       </div>
447:     )
448:   }
449: 
450:   // ---- ADMIN VIEW (only shown when user.role === 'admin') ----
451:   if (mounted && user && user.role !== 'admin') {
452:     // Safety net — shouldn't happen, but logout if it does
453:     return <LoginForm onLoggedIn={() => refetchMe()} />
454:   }
455: 
456:   // ---- ADMIN VIEW (default — also covers the boss who hasn't logged in) ----
457:   if (isLoading) {
458:     return (
459:       <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background text-muted-foreground">
460:         <div className="text-center">
461:           <div className="h-8 w-8 mx-auto mb-3 border-2 border-emerald-400 border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
462:           <p className="text-sm">Loading schedule…</p>
463:         </div>
464:       </div>
465:     )
466:   }
467: 
468:   if (error || !data) {
469:     return (
470:       <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background">
471:         <div className="text-center max-w-sm p-6">
472:           <p className="text-sm text-rose-400 mb-2">Failed to load schedule</p>
473:           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-4">{String(error)}</p>
474:           <button
475:             onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
476:             className="px-3 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600"
477:           >
478:             Reload page
479:           </button>
480:         </div>
481:       </div>
482:     )
483:   }
484: 
485:   return (
486:     <DndContext
487:       sensors={sensors}
488:       onDragStart={onDragStart}
489:       onDragEnd={onDragEnd as any}
490:       onDragCancel={() => setActiveDrag(null)}
491:     >
492:       <div className="h-screen flex flex-col bg-background overflow-hidden">
493:         {/* Skip link for keyboard users */}
494:         <a
495:           href="#main-content"
496:           className="sr-only focus:not-sr-only focus:absolute focus:top-2 focus:left-2 focus:z-50 focus:px-3 focus:py-1.5 focus:rounded-md focus:bg-emerald-500 focus:text-white focus:text-sm"
497:         >
498:           Skip to main content
499:         </a>
500:         <StatsBar
501:           totalSlots={totalSlots}
502:           filledSlots={filledSlots}
503:           conflictCount={conflictCount}
504:           weekLabel={formatShortDate(effectiveWeekStart)}
505:           userName={user?.name}
506:           userEmail={user?.email}
507:           onChangePassword={() => setShowChangePassword(true)}
508:           onLogout={() => logoutMutation.mutate()}
509:         />
510: 
511:         {/* Tab nav — horizontal scroll on mobile */}
512:         <nav
513:           className="border-b border-border/60 bg-card/30 flex items-center gap-1 px-2 sm:px-3 overflow-x-auto"
514:           role="tablist"
515:           aria-label="Main navigation"
516:           style={{ WebkitOverflowScrolling: 'touch', scrollbarWidth: 'none' }}
517:         >
518:           <TabButton active={tab === 'scheduler'} onClick={() => setTab('scheduler')}>
519:             Scheduler
520:           </TabButton>
521:           <TabButton active={tab === 'calendar'} onClick={() => setTab('calendar')}>
522:             Calendar
523:           </TabButton>
524:           <TabButton active={tab === 'events'} onClick={() => setTab('events')}>
525:             Events
526:             <span className="ml-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
527:               ({data.events.length})
528:             </span>
529:           </TabButton>
530:           <TabButton active={tab === 'team'} onClick={() => setTab('team')}>
531:             Team
532:           </TabButton>
533:           <TabButton active={tab === 'conflicts'} onClick={() => setTab('conflicts')}>
534:             Conflicts
535:           </TabButton>
536:           <TabButton active={tab === 'workload'} onClick={() => setTab('workload')}>
537:             Workload
538:           </TabButton>
539:           <TabButton active={tab === 'invites'} onClick={() => setTab('invites')}>
540:             Invites
541:           </TabButton>
542:         </nav>
543: 
544:         <div className="flex-1 flex min-h-0 relative" id="main-content" role="main">
545:           {tab === 'scheduler' && (
546:             <>
547:               <RosterRail
548:                 profiles={data.profiles}
549:                 collapsed={rosterCollapsed}
550:                 onToggleCollapsed={() => setRosterCollapsed(c => !c)}
551:                 tapSelectMode={isMobile}
552:                 selectedProfileId={tapSelectedProfileId}
553:                 onTapProfile={(id) => setTapSelectedProfileId(id === tapSelectedProfileId ? null : id)}
554:               />
555:               <CalendarGrid
556:                 weekStartISO={effectiveWeekStart}
557:                 events={weekEvents}
558:                 assignments={weekAssignments}
559:                 selected={selected}
560:                 onSelect={isMobile ? handleTapAssign : (eventId, date) => setSelected({ eventId, date })}
561:                 onPrevWeek={() => setWeek(w => addDaysISO(w, -7))}
562:                 onNextWeek={() => setWeek(w => addDaysISO(w, 7))}
563:                 onJumpToday={() => setWeek(startOfWeekISO(todayInBarbados()))}
564:                 onPrint={handlePrint}
565:                 tapAssignMode={isMobile}
566:                 hasSelectedProfile={!!tapSelectedProfileId}
567:               />
568: 
569:               {/* Mobile: floating selected-instructor bar */}
570:               {isMobile && tapSelectedProfileId && (
571:                 <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-20 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur-md border-t border-border/60 p-3 flex items-center justify-between gap-2 shadow-lg">
572:                   <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
573:                     <div className="h-8 w-8 rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br from-emerald-500 to-teal-600 text-white text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
574:                       {data.profiles.find(p => p.id === tapSelectedProfileId)?.name.split(' ').map((n: string) => n[0]).slice(0, 2).join('')}
575:                     </div>
576:                     <div className="min-w-0">
577:                       <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">
578:                         {data.profiles.find(p => p.id === tapSelectedProfileId)?.name}
579:                       </p>
580:                       <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">Tap an event to assign</p>
581:                     </div>
582:                   </div>
583:                   <button
584:                     onClick={() => setTapSelectedProfileId(null)}
585:                     className="p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground shrink-0"
586:                     aria-label="Cancel selection"
587:                   >
588:                     <X className="h-4 w-4" />
589:                   </button>
590:                 </div>
591:               )}
592:             </>
593:           )}
594: 
595:           {tab === 'calendar' && (
596:             <CalendarView
597:               events={data.events}
598:               assignments={data.assignments}
599:               profiles={data.profiles}
600:               onSelect={(eventId, date) => setSelected({ eventId, date })}
601:             />
602:           )}
603:           {tab === 'events' && <EventsManagerTab />}
604:           {tab === 'team' && <TeamTab />}
605:           {tab === 'conflicts' && <ConflictSummaryTab onJumpToEvent={handleJumpToEvent} />}
606:           {tab === 'workload' && <WorkloadTab />}
607:           {tab === 'invites' && <InvitesTab />}
608: 
609:           {/* Event detail drawer — shared by Scheduler + Calendar tabs */}
610:           {(tab === 'scheduler' || tab === 'calendar') && (
611:             <AnimatePresence>
612:               {selectedEvent && (
613:                 <motion.div
614:                   key="drawer"
615:                   initial={{ x: 400, opacity: 0 }}
616:                   animate={{ x: 0, opacity: 1 }}
617:                   exit={{ x: 400, opacity: 0 }}
618:                   transition={{ type: 'spring', stiffness: 320, damping: 32 }}
619:                   className="absolute inset-y-0 right-0 z-30"
620:                 >
621:                   <EventDetailDrawer
622:                     event={selectedEvent}
623:                     date={selected?.date ?? null}
624:                     assignments={selectedAssignments}
625:                     profiles={data.profiles}
626:                     onClose={() => setSelected(null)}
627:                     onRemove={(id) => removeMutation.mutate(id)}
628:                     onUpdateAssignment={(id, patch) => patchAssignmentMutation.mutate({ id, patch })}
629:                     onBulkShirtColor={(eventId, date, shirtColor) => {
630:                       const dayAssignments = data.assignments.filter(
631:                         a => a.eventId === eventId && a.date === date && !a.isAlternative
632:                       )
633:                       for (const a of dayAssignments) {
634:                         patchAssignmentMutation.mutate({ id: a.id, patch: { shirtColor } })
635:                       }
636:                       toast.success(`Set all shirts to ${shirtColor}`)
637:                     }}
638:                   />
639:                 </motion.div>
640:               )}
641:             </AnimatePresence>
642:           )}
643:         </div>
644:       </div>
645: 
646:       <DragOverlay dropAnimation={{ duration: 180, easing: 'cubic-bezier(0.18, 0.67, 0.6, 1.22)' }}>
647:         {selectedProfile ? (
648:           <div className="w-64 pointer-events-none opacity-90 rotate-2">
649:             <DraggableInstructor profile={selectedProfile} />
650:           </div>
651:         ) : null}
652:       </DragOverlay>
653: 
654:       {/* Print portal — rendered outside the main layout, shown only when printing */}
655:       {printMode && data && (
656:         <div id="print-portal">
657:           <PrintLayout
658:             weekStartISO={effectiveWeekStart}
659:             events={weekEvents}
660:             assignments={weekAssignments}
661:           />
662:         </div>
663:       )}
664: 
665:       {/* Change password modal */}
666:       {showChangePassword && (
667:         <ChangePasswordModal
668:           onClose={() => setShowChangePassword(false)}
669:           onSubmit={(current, next) => changePasswordMutation.mutate({ currentPassword: current, newPassword: next })}
670:           saving={changePasswordMutation.isPending}
671:         />
672:       )}
673: 
674:       <PWAInstallPrompt />
675:     </DndContext>
676:   )
677: }
678: 
679: function TabButton({ active, onClick, children }: {
680:   active: boolean
681:   onClick: () => void
682:   children: React.ReactNode
683: }) {
684:   return (
685:     <button
686:       role="tab"
687:       aria-selected={active}
688:       onClick={onClick}
689:       className={`px-3 sm:px-4 py-2.5 text-xs sm:text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors whitespace-nowrap min-h-[44px] flex items-center shrink-0 ${
690:         active
691:           ? 'border-emerald-400 text-foreground'
692:           : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
693:       }`}
694:     >
695:       {children}
696:     </button>
697:   )
698: }
699: 
700: function InstructorTopBar({ user, onLogout, onChangePassword }: {
701:   user: AuthUser
702:   onLogout: () => void
703:   onChangePassword: () => void
704: }) {
705:   const [menuOpen, setMenuOpen] = useState(false)
706:   const { theme, setTheme } = useTheme()
707:   const qc = useQueryClient()
708:   const [emailOn, setEmailOn] = useState<boolean>(user.emailNotifications ?? true)
709: 
710:   const toggleEmails = async () => {
711:     const newValue = !emailOn
712:     setEmailOn(newValue)
713:     try {
714:       const r = await fetch('/api/auth/update-email-prefs', {
715:         method: 'POST',
716:         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
717:         body: JSON.stringify({ emailNotifications: newValue }),
718:       })
719:       if (!r.ok) throw new Error()
720:       toast.success(`Email notifications ${newValue ? 'on' : 'off'}`)
721:       qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['me'] })
722:     } catch {
723:       setEmailOn(!newValue) // revert
724:       toast.error('Failed to update email preferences')
725:     }
726:   }
727: 
728:   return (
729:     <header className="border-b border-border/60 bg-card/40 px-3 sm:px-4 py-2 flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
730:       <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
731:         <img src="/logo.png" alt="RA Syncbot" className="h-8 w-8 sm:h-9 sm:w-9 rounded-lg object-cover shrink-0" />
732:         <div className="min-w-0">
733:           <h1 className="text-sm sm:text-base font-semibold leading-tight truncate">
734:             Hi {user.name.split(' ')[0]}
735:           </h1>
736:           <p className="text-[9px] sm:text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">
737:             {user.profile ? 'Opt in to events below' : 'No profile linked'}
738:           </p>
739:         </div>
740:       </div>
741:       <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0">
742:         {/* Theme toggle */}
743:         <button
744:           onClick={() => setTheme(theme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark')}
745:           className="p-2 rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[32px] flex items-center justify-center"
746:           aria-label="Toggle theme"
747:           title={theme === 'dark' ? 'Switch to light mode' : 'Switch to dark mode'}
748:         >
749:           {theme === 'dark' ? <Sun className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> : <Moon className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
750:         </button>
751: 
752:         {/* Email toggle */}
753:         <button
754:           onClick={toggleEmails}
755:           className={cn(
756:             'p-2 rounded-md border min-h-[32px] flex items-center justify-center',
757:             emailOn
758:               ? 'border-emerald-500/40 bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-300'
759:               : 'border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground',
760:           )}
761:           aria-label={`Email notifications ${emailOn ? 'on' : 'off'}`}
762:           title={emailOn ? 'Email notifications on — click to turn off' : 'Email notifications off — click to turn on'}
763:         >
764:           <Mail className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
765:         </button>
766: 
767:         {/* Notification bell */}
768:         <NotificationBell />
769: 
770:         {/* Account menu */}
771:         <div className="relative">
772:           <button
773:             onClick={() => setMenuOpen(o => !o)}
774:             className="px-2 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1 min-h-[32px]"
775:             aria-label="Account menu"
776:             aria-expanded={menuOpen}
777:           >
778:             <User className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
779:             <ChevronDown className="h-3 w-3" />
780:           </button>
781:           {menuOpen && (
782:             <>
783:               <div className="fixed inset-0 z-40" onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)} />
784:               <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 z-50 w-48 bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-md shadow-lg py-1">
785:                 <div className="px-3 py-2 border-b border-border/40">
786:                   <p className="text-xs font-medium truncate">{user.name}</p>
787:                   <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate">{user.email}</p>
788:                 </div>
789:                 <button
790:                   onClick={() => { setMenuOpen(false); onChangePassword() }}
791:                   className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-xs hover:bg-muted flex items-center gap-2"
792:                 >
793:                   <KeyRound className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
794:                   Change password
795:                 </button>
796:                 <a
797:                   href={`/api/ical?token=${user.id}`}
798:                   target="_blank"
799:                   rel="noopener noreferrer"
800:                   className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-xs hover:bg-muted flex items-center gap-2"
801:                   onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)}
802:                 >
803:                   <CalendarDays className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
804:                   Subscribe to calendar
805:                 </a>
806:                 <InstallAppMenuItem onAfterAction={() => setMenuOpen(false)} />
807:                 <button
808:                   onClick={() => { setMenuOpen(false); onLogout() }}
809:                   className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-xs hover:bg-muted text-rose-300 flex items-center gap-2"
810:                 >
811:                   <LogOut className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
812:                   Log out
813:                 </button>
814:               </div>
815:             </>
816:           )}
817:         </div>
818:       </div>
819:     </header>
820:   )
821: }
822: 
823: function ChangePasswordModal({ onClose, onSubmit, saving }: {
824:   onClose: () => void
825:   onSubmit: (current: string, next: string) => void
826:   saving: boolean
827: }) {
828:   const [current, setCurrent] = useState('')
829:   const [next, setNext] = useState('')
830:   const [confirm, setConfirm] = useState('')
831: 
832:   const canSubmit = current && next.length >= 6 && next === confirm && !saving
833: 
834:   return (
835:     <div
836:       className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4"
837:       onClick={onClose}
838:       role="dialog"
839:       aria-modal="true"
840:       aria-label="Change password"
841:     >
842:       <div
843:         className="bg-card border border-border/60 rounded-lg p-6 max-w-sm w-full space-y-3"
844:         onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
845:       >
846:         <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">Change Password</h2>
847:         <div>
848:           <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
849:             Current password
850:           </label>
851:           <input
852:             type="password"
853:             value={current}
854:             onChange={e => setCurrent(e.target.value)}
855:             className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
856:           />
857:         </div>
858:         <div>
859:           <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
860:             New password (min 6 characters)
861:           </label>
862:           <input
863:             type="password"
864:             value={next}
865:             onChange={e => setNext(e.target.value)}
866:             className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
867:           />
868:         </div>
869:         <div>
870:           <label className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wide text-muted-foreground block mb-1">
871:             Confirm new password
872:           </label>
873:           <input
874:             type="password"
875:             value={confirm}
876:             onChange={e => setConfirm(e.target.value)}
877:             onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && canSubmit && onSubmit(current, next)}
878:             className="w-full px-2 py-1.5 text-sm rounded-md bg-background border border-border/60 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"
879:           />
880:         </div>
881:         <div className="flex justify-end gap-2 pt-2">
882:           <button
883:             onClick={onClose}
884:             className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md border border-border/60 hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground min-h-[36px]"
885:           >
886:             Cancel
887:           </button>
888:           <button
889:             onClick={() => canSubmit && onSubmit(current, next)}
890:             disabled={!canSubmit}
891:             className="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-emerald-500 text-white hover:bg-emerald-600 disabled:opacity-50 min-h-[36px]"
892:           >
893:             {saving ? 'Saving…' : 'Change password'}
894:           </button>
895:         </div>
896:       </div>
897:     </div>
898:   )
899: }
